atha śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate

śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ // śrīgaurīśaṃkarābhyāṃ namaḥ // atha saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate

vyāsa uvāca |

namasśivāya somāya sagaṇāya sasūnave |
pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityantahetave || 1 ||

śaktirapratimā yasya hyaiśvaryyaṃ cāpi sarvagam |
svāmitvaṃ ca vibhutvaṃ ca svabhāvaṃ saṃpracakṣate || 2 ||

tamajaṃ viśvakarmāṇaṃ śāśvataṃ śivamavyayam |
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ śivam || 3 ||

dharmakṣetre mahātīrthe gaṃgākālindisaṃgame |
prayāge naimiṣāraṇye brahmalokasya vartmani || 4 ||

munayaśśaṃsitātmānaḥ satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ |
mahaujaso mahābhāgā mahāsatraṃ vitenire || 5 ||

tatra satraṃ samākarṇya teṣāmakliṣṭakarmaṇām |
sākṣātsatyavatīsūnorvedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ || 6 ||

śiṣyo mahātmā medhāvī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ |
pañcāvayavayuktasya vākyasya guṇadoṣavit || 7 ||

uttarottaravaktā ca bruvato .api bṛhaspateḥ |
madhuraḥ śravaṇānāṃ ca manojñapadaparvaṇām || 8 ||

kathānāṃ nipuṇo vaktā kālavinnayavitkaviḥ |
ājagāma sa taṃ deśaṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ || 9 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtamāyāntaṃ munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ |
tasmai sāma ca pūjāṃ ca yathāvatpratyapādayan || 10 ||

pratigṛhya satāṃ pūjāṃ munibhiḥ pratipāditām |
uddiṣṭamānasaṃ bheje niyukto yuktamātmanaḥ || 11 ||

tatastatsaṃgamādeva munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām |
sotkaṃṭhamabhavaccitaṃ śrotuṃ paurāṇikīṃ kathām || 12 ||

tadā tamanukūlābhirvāgbhiḥ pūjya maharṣayaḥ |
atīvābhimukhaṃ kṛtvā vacanaṃ cedamabruvan || 13 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ /

romaharṣaṇa sarvajña bhavānno bhāgyagauravāt |
saṃprāptodya mahābhāga śaivarāja mahāmate || 14 ||

purāṇavidyāmakhilāṃ vyāsātpratyakṣamīyivān |
tasmādāścaryabhūtānāṃ kathānāṃ tvaṃ hi bhājanam || 15 ||

ratnānāmurusārāṇāṃ ratnākara ivārṇavaḥ |
yacca bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyaṃ yaccānyadvastu vartate || 16 ||

na tavāviditaṃ kiñcittriṣu lokeṣu vidyate |
tvamadṛṣṭavaśādasmaddarśanārthamihāgataḥ |
akurvankimapi śreyo na vṛthā gantumarhasi || 17 ||

tasmācchrāvyataraṃ puṇyaṃ satkathājñānasaṃhitam |
vedāntasārasarvasvaṃ purāṇaṃ śrāvayāśu naḥ || 18 ||

evamabhyarthitassūto munibhirvedavādibhiḥ |
ślakṣṇāṃ ca nyāyasaṃyuktāṃ pratyuvāca śubhāṃ giram || 19 ||

sūta uvāca |

pūjito .anugṛhītaśca bhavadbhiriti coditaḥ |
kasmātsamyaGna vibrūyāṃ purāṇamṛṣipūjitam || 20 ||

abhivandya mahādevaṃ devīṃ skandaṃ vināyakam |
nandinaṃ ca tathā vyāsaṃ sākṣātsatyavatīsutam || 21 ||

vakṣyāmi paramaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam |
śivajñānārṇavaṃ sākṣādbhaktimuktiphalapradam || 22 ||

śabdārthanyāyasaṃyuktai rāgamārthairvibhūṣitam |
śvetakalpaprasaṃgena vāyunā kathitaṃ purā || 23 ||

vidyāsthānāni sarvāṇi purāṇānukramaṃ tathā |
tatpurāṇasya cotpattiṃ bruvato me nibodhata || 24 ||

aṃgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsānyāyavistaraḥ |
purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyāścetāścaturdaśa || 25 ||

āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaścetyanukramāt |
arthaśāstraṃ paraṃ tasmādvidyā hyaṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ || 26 ||

aṣṭādaśānāṃ vidyānāmetāsāṃ bhinnavartmanām |
ādikarttā kavissākṣācchūlapāṇiriti śrutiḥ || 27 ||

sa hi sarvajagannāthaḥ sisṛkṣurakhilaṃ jagat |
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe sākṣātputramagre sanātanam || 28 ||

tasmai prathamaputrāya brahmaṇe viśvayonaye |
vidyāścemā dadau pūrvaṃ viśvasṛṣṭyarthamīśvaraḥ || 29 ||

pālanāya hariṃ devaṃ rakṣāśaktiṃ dadau tataḥ |
madhyamaṃ tanayaṃ viṣṇuṃ pātāraṃ brahmaṇo .api hi || 30 ||

labdhavidyena vidhinā prajāsṛṣṭiṃ vitanvatā |
prathamaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā smṛtam || 31 ||

anantaraṃ tu vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ |
pravṛttissarvaśāstrāṇāṃ tanmukhādabhavattataḥ || 32 ||

yadāsya vistaraṃ śaktā nādhigantuṃ prajā bhuvi |
tadā vidyāsamāsārthaṃ viśveśvaraniyogataḥ || 33 ||

dvāparānteṣu viśvātmā viṣṇurviśvaṃbharaḥ prabhuḥ |
vyāsanāmnā caratyasminnavatīrya mahītale || 34 ||

evaṃ vyastāśca vedāśca dvāparedvāpare dvijāḥ |
nirmitāni purāṇāni anyāni ca tataḥ param || 35 ||

sa punardvāpare cāsminkṛṣṇadvaipāyanākhyayā |
araṇyāmiva havyāśī satyavatyāmajāyata || 36 ||

saṃkṣipya sa punarvedāṃścaturddhā kṛtavānmuniḥ |
vyastavedatayā loke vedavyāsa iti śrutaḥ || 37 ||

purāṇānāñca saṃkṣiptaṃ caturlakṣapramāṇataḥ |
adyāpi devaloke tacchatakoṭipravistaram || 38 ||

yo vidyāccaturo vedān sāṃgopaṇiṣadāndvijaḥ |
na cetpurāṇaṃ saṃvidyānnaiva sa syādvicakṣaṇaḥ || 39 ||

itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet |
bibhetyalpaśrutādvedo māmayaṃ pratariṣyati || 40 ||

sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca |
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ paṃcalakṣaṇam || 41 ||

daśadhā cāṣṭadhā caitatpurāṇamupadiśyate |
bṛhatsūkṣmaprabhedena munibhistattvavittamaiḥ || 42 ||

brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā |
bhaviṣyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṃḍeyamataḥ param || 43 ||

āgneyaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṃgaṃ vārāhameva ca |
skāndaṃ ca vāmanaṃ caiva kaurmyaṃ mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍam || 44 ||

brahmāṃḍaṃ ceti puṇyo .ayaṃ purāṇānāmanukramaḥ |
tatra śaivaṃ turīyaṃ yacchārvaṃ sarvārthasādhakam || 45 ||

grantho lakṣapramāṇaṃ tadvyastaṃ dvādaśasaṃhitam |
nirmitaṃ tacchivenaiva tatra dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ || 46 ||

taduktenaiva dharmeṇa śaivāstraivarṇikā narāḥ |
tasmādvimukutimanvicchañcchivameva samāśrayet || 47 ||

tamāśrityaiva devānāmapi muktirna cānyathā || 48 ||

yadidaṃ śaivamākhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam |
tasya bhedānsamāsena bruvato me nibodhata || 49 ||

vidyeśvaraṃ tathā raudraṃ vaināyakamanuttamam |
aumaṃ mātṛpurāṇaṃ ca rudraikādaśakaṃ tathā || 50 ||

kailāsaṃ śatarudraṃ ca śatarudrākhyameva ca |
sahasrakoṭirudrākhyaṃ vāyavīyaṃ tataḥparam || 51 ||

dharmasaṃjñaṃ purāṇaṃ cetyevaṃ dvādaśa saṃhitāḥ |
vidyeśaṃ daśasāhasramuditaṃ granthasaṃkhyayā || 52 ||

raudraṃ vaināyakaṃ caumaṃ mātṛkākhyaṃ tataḥ param |
pratyekamaṣṭasāhasraṃ trayodaśasahasrakam || 53 ||

raudrakādaśakākhyaṃ yatkailāsaṃ ṣaṭsahasrakam |
śatarudraṃ trisāhasraṃ koṭirudraṃ tataḥ param || 54 ||

sahasrairnavabhiryuktaṃ sarvārthajñānasaṃyutam |
sahasrakoṭirudrākhyamekādaśasahasrakam || 55 ||

catussahasrasaṃkhyeyaṃ vāyavīyamanuttamam |
dharmasaṃjñaṃ purāṇaṃ yattaddvādaśasahasrakam || 56 ||

tadevaṃ lakṣamuddiṣṭaṃ śaivaṃ śākhāvibhedataḥ |
purāṇaṃ vedasāraṃ tadbhuktimuktiphalapradam || 57 ||

vyāsena tattu saṃkṣiptaṃ caturviṃśatsahasrakam |
śaivantatra purāṇaṃ vai caturthaṃ saptasaṃhitam || 58 ||

vidyeśvarākhyā tatrādyā dvitīyā rudrasaṃhitā |
tṛtīyā śatarudrākhyā koṭirudrā caturthikā || 59 ||

paṃcamī kathitā comā ṣaṣṭhī kailāsasaṃhitā |
saptamī vāyavīyākhyā saptaivaṃ saṃhitā iha || 60 ||

vidyeśvaraṃ dvisāhasraṃ raudraṃ paṃcaśatāyutam |
triṃśattathā dvisāhasraṃ sārddhaikaśatamīritam || 61 ||

śatarudrantathā koṭirudraṃ vyomayugādhikam |
dvisāhasraṃ ca dviśataṃ tathomaṃ bhūsahasrakam || 62 ||

catvāriṃśatsāṣṭaśataṃ kailāsaṃ bhūsahasrakam |
catvāriṃśacca dviśataṃ vāyavīyamataḥ param || 63 ||

catussāhasrasaṃkhyākamevaṃ saṃkhyāvibhedataḥ |
śrutamparamapuṇyantu purāṇaṃ śivasaṃjñakam || 64 ||

catuḥsāhasrakaṃ yattu vāyavīyamudīritam |
tadidaṃ varttayiṣyāmi bhāgadvayasamanvitam || 65 ||

nāvedaviduṣe vācyamidaṃ śāstramanuttamam |
na caivāśraddhadhānāya nāpurāṇavide tathā || 66 ||

parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya dhārmikāyānasūyave |
pradeyaṃ śivabhaktāya śivadharmānusāriṇe || 67 ||

purāṇasaṃhitā yasya prasādānmayi varttate |
namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase || 68 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vidyāvatārakathanaṃ nāmaprathamo .adhyāyaḥ || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

purā kālena mahatā kalpetīte punaḥpunaḥ |
asminnupasthite kalpe pravṛtte sṛṣṭhikarmaṇi || 1 ||

pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārtāyāṃ prabuddhāsu prajāsu ca |
munīnāṃ ṣaṭkulīyānāṃ bruvatāmitaretaram || 2 ||

idaṃ paramidaṃ neti vivādassumahānabhūt |
parasya durnirūpatvānna jātastatra niścayaḥ || 3 ||

te .abhijagmurvidhātāraṃ draṣṭuṃ brahmāṇamavyayam |
yatrāste bhagavān brahmā stūyamānassurāsuraiḥ || 4 ||

meruśṛṃge śubhe ramye devadānavasaṃkule |
siddhacāraṇasaṃvāde yakṣagandharvasevite || 5 ||

vihaṃgasaṃghasaṃghuṣṭe maṇividrumabhūṣite |
nikuṃjakandaradarīgṛhānirjharaśobhite || 6 ||

tatra brahmavanaṃ nāma nānāmṛgasamākulam |
daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ śatayojanamāyatam || 7 ||

surasāmalapānīyapūrṇaramyasarovaram |
mattabhramarasaṃchannaramyapuṣpitapādapam || 8 ||

taruṇādityasaṃkāśaṃ tatra cāru mahatpuram |
durddharṣabaladṛptānāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām || 9 ||

taptajāṃbūnadamayaṃ prāṃśuprākāratoraṇam |
nirvyūhavalabhīkūṭapratolīśatamaṃḍitam || 10 ||

mahārhamaṇicitrābhirlelihānamivāṃbaram |
mahābhavanakoṭībhiranekābhiralaṃkṛtam || 11 ||

tasminnivasati brahmā sabhyaiḥ sārddhaṃ prajāpatiḥ |
tatra gatvā mahātmānaṃ sākṣāllokapitāmaham || 12 ||

daddaśurmunayo devā devarṣigaṇasevitam |
śuddhacāmīkaraprakhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 13 ||

prasannavadanaṃ saumyaṃ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇam |
divyakāntisamāyuktaṃ divyagandhānulepanam || 14 ||

divyaśuklāṃbaradharaṃ divyamālāvibhūṣitam |
surāsurendrayogīndravandyamānapadāṃbujam || 15 ||

sarvalakṣaṇayuktāṃgyā labdhacāmarahastayā |
bhrājamānaṃ sarasvatyā prabhayeva divākaram || 16 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayassarve prasannavadanekṣaṇāḥ |
śirasyaṃjalimādhāya tuṣṭuvussurapuṃgavam || 17 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ sargasthityantahetave |
puruṣāya purāṇāya brahmaṇe paramātmane || 18 ||

namaḥ pradhānadehāya pradhānakṣobhakāriṇe |
trayoviṃśatibhedena vikṛtāyāvikāriṇe || 19 ||

namo brahmāṇḍadehāya brahmāṃḍodaravartine |
tatra saṃsiddhakāryāya saṃsiddhakaraṇāya ca || 20 ||

namostu sarvalokāya sarvalokavidhāyine |
sarvātmadehasaṃyoga viyogavidhihetave || 21 ||

tvayaiva nikhilaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ pālitaṃ jagat |
tathāpi māyayā nātha na vidmastvāṃ pitāmaha || 22 ||

sūta uvāca |

evaṃ brahmā mahābhāgairmaharṣibhirabhiṣṭutaḥ |
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā munīn prahlādayanniva || 23 ||

brahmovāca |

ṛṣayo he mahābhāgā mahāsattvā mahaujasaḥ |
kimarthaṃ sahitāssarve yūyamatra samāgatāḥ || 24 ||

tamevaṃvādinaṃ devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ brahmavittamāḥ |
vāgbhirvinayagarbhābhissarve prāṃjalayo .abruvan || 25 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

bhagavannandhakāreṇa mahatā vayamāvṛtāḥ |
khinnā vivadamānāśca na paśyāmo .atra yatparam || 26 ||

tvaṃ hi sarvajagaddhātā sarvakāraṇakāraṇam |
tvayā hyaviditaṃ nātha neha kiṃcana vidyate || 27 ||

kaḥ pumān sarvasattvebhyaḥ purāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ paraḥ |
viśuddhaḥ paripūrṇaśca śāśvataḥ parameśvaraḥ || 28 ||

kenaiva citrakṛtyena prathamaṃ sṛjyate jagat |
tattvaṃ vada mahāprājña svasaṃdehāpanuttaye || 29 ||

evaṃ pṛṣṭastadā brahmā vismayasmeravīkṣaṇaḥ |
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca munīnāmapi sannidhau || 30 ||

utthāya suciraṃ dhyātvā rudra ityuddharan girim |
ānandaklinnasarvāṃgaḥ kṛtāṃjalirabhāṣata || 31 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe muniprastāvavarṇanaṃ nāma dvitīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 2 ||

brahamovāca |

yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha |
ānandaṃ yasya vai vidvānna bibheti kutaścana || 1 ||

yasmātsarvamidaṃ brahmaviṣṇurudrendrapūrvakam |
saha bhūtendriyaiḥ sarvaiḥ prathamaṃ saṃprasūyate || 2 ||

kāraṇānāṃ ca yo dhātā dhyātā paramakāraṇam |
na saṃprasūyate .anyasmātkutaścana kadācana || 3 ||

sarvaiśvaryeṇa saṃpanno nāmnā sarveśvaraḥ svayam |
sarvairmumukṣubhirdhyeyaśśaṃbhurākāśamadhyagaḥ || 4 ||

yo .agre māṃ vidadhe putraṃ jñānaṃ ca prahiṇoti me |
tatprasādānmayālabdhaṃ prājāpatyamidaṃ padam || 5 ||

īśo vṛkṣa iva stabdho ya eko divi tiṣṭhati |
yenedamakhilaṃ pūrṇaṃ puruṣeṇa mahātmanā || 6 ||

eko bahūnāṃ jantūnāṃ niṣkriyāṇāṃ ca sakriyaḥ |
ya eko bahudhā bījaṃ karoti sa maheśvaraḥ || 7 ||

jīvairebhirimĀllokānsarvānīśo ya īśate |
ya eko bhāgavānrudro na dvitīyo .asti kaścana || 8 ||

sadā janānāṃ hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭo .api yaḥ paraiḥ |
alakṣyo lakṣayanviśvamadhitiṣṭhati sarvadā || 9 ||

yastu kālātpramuktāni kāraṇānyakhilānyapi |
anantaśaktirevaiko bhagavānadhitiṣṭhati || 10 ||

na yasya divaso rātrirna samāno na cādhikaḥ |
svabhāvikī parāśaktirnityā jñānakriye api || 11 ||

yadidaṃ kṣaramavyaktaṃ yadapyamṛtamakṣaram |
tāvubhāvakṣarātmānāveko devaḥ svayaṃ haraḥ || 12 ||

īśate tadabhidhyānādyojanāsattvabhāvanaḥ |
bhūyo hyasya paśorante viśvamāyā nivarttate || 13 ||

yasminna bhāsate vidyunna sūryo na ca candramāḥ |
yasya bhāsā vibhātīdamityeṣā śāśvatī śrutiḥ || 14 ||

eko devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ |
na tasya paramaṃ kiṃcitpadaṃ samadhigamyate || 15 ||

ayamādiranādyantassvabhāvādeva nirmalaḥ |
svatantraḥ paripūrṇaśca svecchādhīnaścarācaraḥ || 16 ||

aprākṛtavapuḥ śrīmĀllakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitaḥ |
ayaṃ mukto mocakaśca hyakālaḥ kālacodakaḥ || 17 ||

sarvoparikṛtāvāsassarvāvāsaśca sarvavit |
ṣaḍvidhādhvamayasyāsya sarvasya jagataḥ patiḥ || 18 ||

uttarottarabhūtānāmuttaraśca niruttaraḥ |
anantānantasandohamakarandamadhuvrataḥ || 19 ||

akhaṃḍajagadaṃḍānāṃ piṃḍīkaraṇapaṃḍitaḥ |
audāryavīryagāṃbhīryyamādhuryyamakarālayaḥ || 20 ||

naivāsya sadṛśaṃ vastu nādhikaṃ cāpi kiṃcana |
atulaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ rājarājaśca tiṣṭhati || 21 ||

anena citrakṛtyena prathamaṃ sṛjyate jagat |
antakāle punaścedaṃ tasminpralayameṣyate || 22 ||

asya bhūtāni vaśyāni ayaṃ sarvaniyojakaḥ |
ayaṃ tu parayā bhaktyā dṛśyate nānyathā kvacit || 23 ||

vratāni sarvadānāni tapāṃsi niyamāstathā |
kathitāni purā sadbhirbhāvārthaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ || 24 ||

hariścāhaṃ ca rudraśca tathānye ca surāsurāḥ |
tapobhirugrairadyāpi tasya darśanakāṃkṣiṇaḥ || 25 ||

adṛśyaḥ patitairmūḍhairdurjanairapi kutsitaiḥ |
bhaktairantarbahiścāpi pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣya eva ca || 26 ||

tadidaṃ trividhaṃ rūpaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tataḥ param |
asmadādyamarairdṛśyaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tu yogibhiḥ || 27 ||

tataḥ paraṃ tu yannityaṃ jñānamānandamavyayam |
tanniṣṭhaistatparairbhaktairdṛśyaṃ tadvratamāśritaiḥ || 28 ||

bahunātra kimuktena guhyādguhyataraṃ param |
śive bhaktirna sandehastayā yukto vimucyate || 29 ||

prasādādeva sā bhaktiḥ prasādo bhaktisaṃbhavaḥ |
yathā cāṃkurato bījaṃ bījato vā yathāṃkuraḥ || 30 ||

prasādapūrvikā eva paśossarvatra siddhayaḥ |
sa eva sādhanairante sarvairapi ca sādhyate || 31 ||

prasādasādhanaṃ dharmassa ca vedena darśitaḥ |
tadabhyāsavaśātsāmyaṃ pūrvayoḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ || 32 ||

sāmyātprasādasaṃparko dharmasyātiśayastataḥ |
dharmātiśayamāsādya paśoḥ pāpaparikṣayaḥ || 33 ||

evaṃ prakṣīṇapāpasya bahubhirjanmabhiḥ kramāt |
sāṃbe sarveśvare bhaktirjñānapūrvā prajāyate || 34 ||

bhāvānuguṇamīśasya prasādo vyatiricyate |
prasādātkarmasaṃtyāgaḥ phalato na svarūpataḥ || 35 ||

tasmātkarmaphalatyāgācchivadharmānvayaḥ śubhaḥ |
sa ca gurvanapekṣaśca tadapekṣa iti dvidhā || 36 ||

tatrānapekṣātsāpekṣo mukhyaḥ śataguṇādhikaḥ |
śivadharmānvayasyāsya śivajñānasamanvayaḥ || 37 ||

jñanānvayavaśātpuṃsaḥ saṃsāre doṣadarśanam |
tato viṣayavairāgyaṃ vairāgyādbhāvasādhanam || 38 ||

bhāvasiddhyupapannasya dhyāne niṣṭhā na karmaṇi |
jñānadhyānābhiyuktasya puṃso yogaḥ pravartate || 39 ||

yogena tu parā bhaktiḥ prasādastadanantaram |
prasādānmucyate janturmuktaḥ śivasamo bhavet || 40 ||

anugrahaprakārasya kramo .ayamavivakṣitaḥ |
yādṛśī yogyatā puṃsastasya tādṛganugrahaḥ || 41 ||

garbhastho mucyate kaścijjāyamānastathāparaḥ |
bālo vā taruṇo vātha vṛddho vā mucyate paraḥ || 42 ||

tiryagyonigataḥ kaścinmucyate nārako .aparaḥ |
aparastu padaṃ prāpto mucyate svapadakṣaye || 43 ||

kaścitkṣīṇapado bhūtvā punarāvartya mucyate |
kaścidadhvagatastasmin sthitvāsthitvā vimucyate || 44 ||

tasmānnaikaprakāreṇa narāṇāṃ muktiriṣyate |
jñānabhāvānurūpeṇa prasādenaiva nirvṛtiḥ || 45 ||

tasmādasya prasādārthaṃ vāGmanodoṣavarjitāḥ |
dhyāyantaśśivamevaikaṃ sadāratanayāgnayaḥ || 46 ||

tanniṣṭhāstatparāssarve tadyuktāstadupāśrayāḥ |
sarvakriyāḥ prakurvāṇāstameva manasāgatāḥ || 47 ||

dīrghasūtrasamārabdhaṃ divyavarṣasahasrakam |
satrānte mantrayogena vāyustatra gamiṣyati || 48 ||

sa eva bhavataḥ śreyaḥ sopāyaṃ kathayiṣyati |
tato vārāṇasī puṇyā purī paramaśobhanā || 49 ||

gantavyā yatra viśveśo devyā saha pinākadhṛk |
sadā viharati śrīmān bhaktānugrahakāraṇāt || 50 ||

tatrāścaryaṃ mahaddṛṣṭvā matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyatha |
tato vaḥ kathayiṣyāmi mokṣopāya dvijottamāḥ || 51 ||

yenaikajanmanā muktiryuṣmatkaratale sthitā |
anekajanmasaṃsārabandhanirmokṣakāriṇī || 52 ||

etanmanomayaṃ cakraṃ mayā sṛṣṭaṃ visṛjyate |
yatrāsya śīryate nemiḥ sa deśastapasaśśubhaḥ || 53 ||

ityuktvā sūryasaṃkāśaṃ cakraṃ dṛṣṭvā manomayam |
praṇipatya mahādevaṃ visasarja pitāmahaḥ || 54 ||

te .api hṛṣṭatarā viprāḥ praṇamya jagatāṃ prabhum |
prayayustasya cakrasya yatra nemiraśīryata || 55 ||

cakraṃ tadapi saṃkṣiptaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ cāruśilātale |
vimalasvādupānīye nijapāta vane kvacit || 56 ||

tadvanaṃ tena vikhyātaṃ naimiṣaṃ munipūjitam |
anekayakṣagandharvavidyādharasamākulam || 57 ||

aṣṭādaśa samudrasya dvīpānaśnanpurūravāḥ |
vilāsavaśamurvaśyā yāto daivena coditaḥ || 58 ||

akrameṇa haranmohādyajñavāṭaṃ hiraṇmayam |
munibhiryatra saṃkruddhaiḥ kuśavajrairnipātitaḥ || 59 ||

viśvaṃ sisṛkṣamāṇā vai yatra viśvasṛjaḥ purā |
satramārebhire divyaṃ brahmajñā gārhapatyagāḥ || 60 ||

ṛṣibhiryatra vidvadbhiḥ śabdārthanyāyakovidaiḥ |
śaktiprajñākriyāyogairvidhirāsīdanuṣṭhitaḥ || 61 ||

yatra vedavido nityaṃ vedavādabahiṣkṛtān |
vādajalpabalairghnanti vacobhirativādinaḥ || 62 ||

sphaṭikamayamahībhṛtpādajābhyaśśilābhyaḥ prasaradamṛtakalpassvacchapānīyaramyam |
atirasaphalavṛkṣaprāyamavyālasattvaṃ tapasa ucitamāsīnnaimiṣaṃ tanmunīnām || 63 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe naimiṣopākhyānaṃ nāma tṛtīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 3 ||

sūta uvāca |

tasmindeśe mahābhāgā munayaśśaṃsitavratāḥ |
arcayanto mahādevaṃ satramārebhire tadā || 1 ||

tacca satraṃ pravavṛte sarvāścaryaṃ maharṣiṇām |
viśvaṃ sisṛkṣamāṇānāṃ purā viśvasṛjāmiva || 2 ||

atha kāle gate satre samāpte bhūridakṣiṇe |
pitāmahaniyogena vāyustatrāgamatsvayam || 3 ||

śiṣyassvayaṃbhuvo devassarvapratyakṣadṛgvaśī |
ājñāyāṃ maruto yasya saṃsthitāssaptasaptakāḥ || 4 ||

prerayañchaśvadaṃgāni prāṇādyābhiḥ svavṛttibhiḥ |
sarvabhūtaśarīrāṇāṃ kurute yaśca dhāraṇam || 5 ||

aṇimādibhiraṣṭābhiraiśvaryaiśca samanvitaḥ |
tiryakkālādibhirmedhyairbhuvanāni bibharti yaḥ || 6 ||

ākāśayonirdviguṇaḥ sparśaśabdasamanvayāt |
tejasāṃ prakṛtiśceti yamāhustattvacintakāḥ || 7 ||

tamāśramagataṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo dīrghasatriṇaḥ |
pitāmahavacaḥ smṛtvā praharṣamatulaṃ yayuḥ || 8 ||

abhyutthāya tatassarve praṇamyāṃbarasaṃbhavam |
cāmīkaramayaṃ tasmai viṣṭaraṃ samakalpayan || 9 ||

sopi tatra samāsīno munibhissamyagarcitaḥ |
pratinandya ca tān sarvān papraccha kuśalaṃ tataḥ || 10 ||

vāyuruvāca |

atra vaḥ kuśalaṃ viprāḥ kaccidvṛtte mahākratau |
kaccidyajñahano daityā na bādheransuradviṣaḥ || 11 ||

prāyaścittaṃ duriṣṭaṃ vā na kaccitsamajāyata |
stotraśastragṛhairdevān pitR̥n pitryaiśca karmabhiḥ || 12 ||

kaccidabhyarcya yuṣmābhirvidhirāsītsvanuṣṭhitaḥ |
nivṛtte ca mahāsatre paścātkiṃ vaścikīrṣitam || 13 ||

ityuktā munayaḥ sarve vāyunā śivabhāvinā |
prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ pūtāḥ pratyūcurvinayānvitāḥ || 14 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

adya naḥ kuśalaṃ sarvamadya sādhu bhavettapaḥ |
asmacchreyobhivṛddhyarthaṃ bhavānatrāgato yataḥ || 15 ||

śṛṇu cedaṃ purāvṛttaṃ tamasākrāntamānasaiḥ |
upāsitaḥ purāsmābhirvijñānārthaṃ prajāpatiḥ || 16 ||

sopyasmānanugṛhyāha śaraṇyaśśaraṇāgatān |
sarvasmādadhiko rudro viprāḥ paramakāraṇam || 17 ||

tamapratarkyaṃ yāthātmyaṃ bhaktimāneva paśyati |
bhaktiścāsya prasādena prasādādeva nirvṛtiḥ || 18 ||

tasmādasya prasādārthaṃ naimiṣe satrayogataḥ |
yajadhvaṃ dīrghasatreṇa rudraṃ paramakāraṇam || 19 ||

tatprasādena satrānte vāyustatrāgamiṣyati |
tanmukhājjñānalābho vastatra śreyo bhaviṣyati || 20 ||

ityādiśya vayaṃ sarve preṣitā parameṣṭhinā |
asmindeśe mahābhāga tavāgamanakāṃkṣiṇaḥ || 21 ||

dīrghasatraṃ samāsīnā divyavarṣasahasrakam |
atastavāgamādanyatprārthyaṃ no nāsti kiṃcana || 22 ||

ityākarṇya purāvṛttamṛṣīṇāṃ dīrghasatriṇām |
vāyuḥ prītamanā bhūtvā tatrāsīnmunisaṃvṛtaḥ || 23 ||

tatastairmunibhiḥ pṛṣṭasteṣāṃ bhāvavivṛddhaye |
sargādi śārvamaiśvaryaṃ samāsāda vadadvibhuḥ || 24 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vāyusamāgamo nāma caturtho .adhyāyaḥ || 4 ||

sūta uvāca |

tatra pūrvaṃ mahābhāgā naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ |
praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ papracchuḥ pavanaṃ prabhum || 1 ||

naimiṣīyā ūcuḥ |

bhavān kathamanuprāpto jñānamīśvaragocaram |
kathaṃ ca śivabhāvaste brahmaṇo .avyaktajanmanaḥ || 2 ||

vāyuruvāca |

ekonaviṃśatiḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ |
tasminkalpe caturvaktrassraṣṭukāmo .atapattapaḥ || 3 ||

tapasā tena tīvreṇa tuṣṭastasya pitā svayam |
divyaṃ kaumāramāsthāya rūpaṃ rūpavatāṃ varaḥ || 4 ||

śveto nāma munirbhūtvā divyāṃ vācamudīrayan |
darśanaṃ pradadau tasmai devadevo maheśvaraḥ || 5 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā pitaraṃ brahmā brahmaṇo .adhipatiṃ patim |
praṇamya paramajñānaṃ gāyatryā saha labdhavān || 6 ||

tatassa labdhavijñāno viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ |
asṛjatsarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca || 7 ||

yataśśrutvāmṛtaṃ labdhaṃ brahmaṇā parameśvarāt |
tatastadvadanādeva mayā labdhaṃ tapobalāt || 8 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kiṃ tajjñānaṃ tvayā labdhaṃ tathyāttathyantaraṃ śubham |
yatra kṛtvā parāṃ niṣṭhāṃ puruṣassukhamṛcchati || 9 ||

vayuruvāca |

paśupāśapatijñānaṃ yallabdhaṃ tu mayā purā |
tatra niṣṭhā parā kāryā puruṣeṇa sukhārthinā || 10 ||

ajñānaprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ jñānenaiva nivarttate |
jñānaṃ vastuparicchedo vastu ca dvividhaṃ smṛtam || 11 ||

ajaḍaṃ ca jaḍaṃ caiva niyantṛ ca tayorapi |
paśuḥ pāśaḥ patiśceti kathyate tattrayaṃ kramāt || 12 ||

akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva kṣarākṣaraparaṃ tathā |
tadetattritayaṃ bhūmnā kathyate tattvavedibhiḥ || 13 ||

akṣaraṃ paśurityuktaḥ kṣaraṃ pāśa udāhṛtaḥ |
kṣarākṣaraparaṃ yattatpatirityabhidhīyate || 14 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kiṃ tadakṣaramityuktaṃ kiṃ ca kṣaramudāhṛtam |
tayośca paramaṃ kiṃ vā tadetad brūhi māruta || 15 ||

vāyuruvāca |

prakṛtiḥ kṣaramityuktaṃ puruṣo .akṣara ucyate |
tāvimau prerayatyanyassa parā parameśvaraḥ || 16 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kaiṣā prakṛtirityuktā ka eṣa puruṣo mataḥ |
anayoḥ kena sambandhaḥ koyaṃ preraka īśvaraḥ || 17 ||

vāyuruvāca |

māyā prakṛtiruddiṣṭā puruṣo māyayā vṛtaḥ |
saṃbandho mūlakarmabhyāṃ śivaḥ preraka īśvaraḥ || 18 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

keyaṃ māyā samā khyātā kiṃrūpo māyayā vṛtaḥ |
mūlaṃ kīdṛk kuto vāsya kiṃ śivatvaṃ kutaśśivaḥ || 19 ||

vāyuruvāca |

māyā māheśvarī śaktiścidrūpo māyayā vṛtaḥ |
malaścicchādako naijo viśuddhiśśivatā svataḥ || 20 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

āvṛṇoti kathaṃ māyā vyāpinaṃ kena hetunā |
kimarthaṃ cāvṛtiḥ puṃsaḥ kena vā vinivartate || 21 ||

vāyuruvāca |

āvṛtirvyapino .api syādvyāpi yasmātkalādyapi |
hetuḥ karmaiva bhogārthaṃ nivarteta malakṣayāt || 22 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kalādi kathyate kiṃ tatkarma vā kimudāhṛtam |
tatkimādi kimantaṃ vā kiṃ phalaṃ vā kimāśrayam || 23 ||

kasya bhogena kiṃ bhogyaṃ kiṃ vā tadbhogasādhanam |
malakṣayasya ko hetuḥ kīdṛk kṣīṇamalaḥ pumān || 24 ||

vāyuruvāca |

kalā vidyā ca rāgaśca kālo niyatireva ca |
kalādayassamākhyātā yo bhoktā puruṣo bhavet || 25 ||

puṇyapāpātmakaṃ karma sukhaduḥkhaphalaṃ tu yat |
anādimalabhogāntamajñānātmasamāśrayam || 26 ||

bhogaḥ karmavināśāya bhogamavyaktamucyate |
bāhyāntaḥkaraṇadvāraṃ śarīraṃ bhogasādhanam || 27 ||

bhāvātiśayalabdhena prasādena malakṣayaḥ |
kṣīṇe cātmamale tasmin pumāñcchivasamo bhavet || 28 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kalādipaṃcatattvānāṃ kiṃ karma pṛthagucyate |
bhokteti puruṣaśceti yenātmā vyapadiśyate || 29 ||

kimātmakaṃ tadavyaktaṃ kenākāreṇa bhujyate |
kiṃ tasya śaraṇaṃ bhuktau śarīraṃ ca kimucyate || 30 ||

vāyuruvāca |

dikkriyāvyaṃjakā vidyā kālo rāgaḥ pravartakaḥ |
kālo .avacchedakastatra niyatistu niyāmikā || 31 ||

avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattattriguṇaṃ prabhavāpyayam |
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhustattvacintakāḥ || 32 ||

kalātastadabhivyaktamanabhivyaktalakṣaṇam |
sukhaduḥkhavimohātmā bhujyate guṇavāṃstridhā || 33 ||

sattvaṃ rajastama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavāḥ |
prakṛtau sūkṣmarūpeṇa tile tailamiva sthitāḥ || 34 ||

sukhaṃ ca sukhahetuśca samāsātsāttvikaṃ smṛtam |
rājasaṃ tadviparyāsātstaṃbhamohau tu tāmasau || 35 ||

sāttvikyūrdhvagatiḥ proktā tāmasī syādadhogatiḥ |
madhyamā tu gatiryā sā rājasī paripaṭhyate || 36 ||

tanmātrāpañcakaṃ caiva bhūtapaṃcakameva ca |
jñānendriyāṇi paṃcaikyaṃ paṃca karmendriyāṇi ca || 37 ||

pradhānabuddhyahaṃkāramanāṃsi ca catuṣṭayam |
samāsādevamavyaktaṃ savikāramudāhṛtam || 38 ||

tatkāraṇadaśāpannamavyaktamiti kathyate |
vyaktaṃ kāryadaśāpannaṃ śarīrādighaṭādivat || 39 ||

yathā ghaṭādikaṃ kāryaṃ mṛdādernātibhidyate |
śarīrādi tathā vyaktamavyaktānnātibhidyate || 40 ||

tasmādavyaktamevaikyakāraṇaṃ karaṇāni ca |
śarīraṃ ca tadādhāraṃ tadbhogyaṃ cāpi netarat || 41 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

buddhīndriyaśarīrebhyo vyatirekasya kasyacit |
ātmaśabdābhidheyasya vastuto .api kutaḥ sthitiḥ || 42 ||

vāyuruvāca |

buddhīndriyaśarīrebhyo vyatireko vibhorddhruvam |
astyeva kaścidātmeti hetustatra sudurgamaḥ || 43 ||

buddhīndriyaśarīrāṇāṃ nātmatā sadbhiriṣyate |
smṛteraniyatajñānādayāvaddehavedanāt || 44 ||

ataḥ smartānubhūtānāmaśeṣajñeyagocaraḥ |
antaryyāmīti vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate || 45 ||

sarvaṃ tatra sa sarvatra vyāpya tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ |
tathāpi kvāpi kenāpi vyaktameṣa na dṛśyate || 46 ||

naivāyaṃ cakṣuṣā grāhyo nāparairindriyairapi |
manasaiva pradīptena mahānātmāvasīyate || 47 ||

na ca strī na pumāneṣa naiva cāpi napuṃsakaḥ |
naivorddhvaṃ nāpi tiryak nādhastānna kutaścana || 48 ||

aśarīraṃ śarīreṣu caleṣu sthāṇumavyayam |
sadā paśyati taṃ dhīro naraḥ pratyavamarśanāt || 49 ||

kimatra bahunoktena puruṣo dehataḥ pṛthak |
apṛthagye tu paśyanti hyasamyakteṣu darśanam || 50 ||

yaccharīramidaṃ proktaṃ puruṣasya tataḥ param |
aśuddhamavaśaṃ duḥkhamadhruvaṃ na ca vidyate || 51 ||

vipadāṃ vījabhūtena puruṣastena saṃyutaḥ |
sukhī duḥkhī ca mūḍhaśca bhavati svena karmaṇā || 52 ||

adbhirāplavitaṃ kṣetraṃ janayatyaṃkuraṃ yathā |
ājñānātplāvitaṃ karma dehaṃ janayate tathā || 53 ||

atyantamasukhāvāsāssmṛtāścaikāntamṛtyavaḥ |
anāgatā atītāśca tanavo .asya sahasraśaḥ || 54 ||

āgatyāgatya śīrṇeṣu śarīreṣu śarīriṇaḥ |
atyantavasatiḥ kvāpi na kenāpi ca labhyate || 55 ||

chāditaśca viyuktaśca śarīraireṣu lakṣyate |
candrabiṃbavadākāśe taralairabhrasaṃcayaiḥ || 56 ||

anekadehabhedena bhinnā vṛttirihātmanaḥ |
aṣṭāpadaparikṣepe hyakṣamudreva lakṣyate || 57 ||

naivāsya bhavitā kaścinnāsau bhavati kasyacit |
pathi saṃgama evāyaṃ dāraiḥ putraiśca bandhubhiḥ || 58 ||

yathā kāṣṭhaṃ ca kāṣṭhaṃ ca sameyātāṃ mahodadhau |
sametya ca vyapeyātāṃ tadvadbhūtasamāgamaḥ || 59 ||

sa paśyati śarīraṃ taccharīraṃ tanna paśyati |
tau paśyati paraḥ kaścittāvubhau taṃ na paśyataḥ || 60 ||

brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntaśca paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ |
paśūnāmeva sarveṣāṃ proktametannidarśanam || 61 ||

sa eṣa badhyate pāśaiḥ sukhaduḥkhāśanaḥ paśuḥ |
līlāsādhanabhūto ya īśvarasyeti sūrayaḥ || 62 ||

ajño janturanīśo .ayamātmanassukhaduḥkhayoḥ |
īśvaraprerito gacchetsvargaṃ vā śvabhrameva vā || 63 ||

sūta uvāca |

ityākarṇyānilavaco munayaḥ prītamānasāḥ |
procuḥ praṇamya taṃ vāyuṃ śaivāgamavicakṣaṇam || 64 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śivatattvajñānavarṇanaṃ nāma paṃcamo .adhyāyaḥ || 5 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

yo .ayaṃ paśuriti prokto yaśca pāśa udāhṛtaḥ |
abhyāṃ vilakṣaṇaḥ kaścitkoyamasti tayoḥ patiḥ || 1 ||

// vāyuruvāca |

asti kaścidaparyantaramaṇīyaguṇāśrayaḥ |
patirviśvasya nirmātā paśupāśavimocanaḥ || 2 ||

abhāve tasya viśvasya sṛṣṭireṣā kathaṃ bhavet |
acetanatvādajñānādanayoḥ paśupāśayoḥ || 3 ||

pradhānaparamāṇvādi yāvatkiṃcidacetanam |
tatkartṛkaṃ svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ buddhimatkāraṇaṃ vinā || 4 ||

jagacca kartṛsāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ sāvayavaṃ yataḥ |
tasmātkāryasya kartṛtvaṃ patyurna paśupāśayoḥ || 5 ||

paśorapi ca kartṛtvaṃ patyuḥ preraṇapūrvakam |
ayathākaraṇajñānamandhasya gamanaṃ yathā || 6 ||

ātmānaṃ ca pṛthaGmatvā preritāraṃ tataḥ pṛthak |
asau juṣṭastatastena hyamṛtatvāya kalpate || 7 ||

paśoḥ pāśasya patyuśca tattvato .asti padaṃ param |
brahmavittadviditvaiva yonimukto bhaviṣyati || 8 ||

saṃyuktametaddvitayaṃ kṣaramakṣarameva ca |
vyaktāvyaktaṃ bibhartīśo viśvaṃ viśvavimocakaḥ || 9 ||

bhoktā bhogyaṃ prerayitā mantavyaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam |
nātaḥ paraṃ vijānadbhirveditavyaṃ hi kiṃcanaḥ || 10 ||

tileṣu vā yathā tailaṃ dadhni vā sarpirarpitam |
yathāpaḥ srotasi vyāptā yathāraṇyāṃ hutāśanaḥ || 11 ||

evameva mahātmānamātmanyātmavilakṣaṇam |
satyena tapasā caiva nityayukto .anupaśyati || 12 ||

ya eko jālavānīśa īśānībhissvaśaktibhiḥ |
sarvāṃllokānimān kṛtvā eka eva sa īśate || 13 ||

eka eva tadā rudro na dvitīyo .asti kaścana |
saṃsṛjya viśvabhuvanaṃ goptā te saṃcukoca yaḥ || 14 ||

viśvataścakṣurevāyamutāyaṃ viśvatomukhaḥ |
tathaiva viśvatobāhuviśvataḥ pādasaṃyutaḥ || 15 ||

dyāvābhūmī ca janayan deva eko maheśvaraḥ |
sa eva sarvadevānāṃ prabhavaścodbhavastathā || 16 ||

hiraṇyagarbhaṃ devānāṃ prathamaṃ janayedayam |
viśvasmādadhiko rudro maharṣiriti hi śrutiḥ || 17 ||

vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntamamṛtaṃ dhruvam |
ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastātsaṃsthitaṃ prabhum || 18 ||

asmānnāsti paraṃ kiṃcidaparaṃ paramātmanaḥ |
nāṇīyo .asti na ca jyāyastena pūrṇamidaṃ jagat || 19 ||

sarvānanaśirogrīvaḥ sarvabhūtaguhāśayaḥ |
sarvavyāpī ca bhagavāṃstasmātsarvagataśśivaḥ || 20 ||

sarvataḥ pāṇipādo .ayaṃ sarvato .akṣiśiromukhaḥ |
sarvataḥ śrutimĀlloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati || 21 ||

sarvendriyaguṇābhāsassarvendriyavivarjitaḥ |
sarvasya prabhurīśānaḥ sarvasya śaraṇaṃ suhṛt || 22 ||

acakṣurapi yaḥ paśyatyakarṇo .api śṛṇoti yaḥ |
sarvaṃ vetti na vettāsya tamāhuḥ puruṣaṃ param || 23 ||

aṇoraṇīyānmahato mahīyānayamavyayaḥ |
guhāyāṃ nihitaścāpi jantorasya maheśvaraḥ || 24 ||

tamakratuṃ kratuprāyaṃ mahimātiśayānvitam |
dhātuḥ prasādādīśānaṃ vītaśokaḥ prapaśyati || 25 ||

vedāhamenamajaraṃ purāṇaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum |
nirodhaṃ janmano yasya vadanti brahmavādinaḥ || 26 ||

eko .api trīnimĀllokān bahudhā śaktiyogataḥ |
vidadhāti vicetyante viśvamādau maheśvaraḥ || 27 ||

viśvadhātrītyajākhyā ca śaivī citrā kṛtiḥ parā |
tāmajāṃ lohitāṃ śuklāṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ tvajaḥ prajām || 28 ||

janitrīmanuśete .anyojuṣamāṇassvarūpiṇīm |
tāmevājāmajo .anyastu bhaktabhogā jahāti ca || 29 ||

dvau suparṇau ca sayujau samānaṃ vṛkṣamāsthitau |
eko .atti pippalaṃ svādu paro .anaśnan prapaśyati || 30 ||

vṛkṣesmin puruṣo magno guhyamānaśca śocati |
juṣṭamanyaṃ yadā paśyedīśaṃ paramakāraṇam || 31 ||

tadāsya mahimānaṃ ca vītaśokassukhī bhavet |
chandāṃsi yajñāḥ ṛtavo yadbhūtaṃ bhavyameva ca || 32 ||

māyī viśvaṃ sṛjatyasminniviṣṭo māyayā paraḥ |
māyāṃ tu prakṛtiṃ vidyānmāyinaṃ tu maheśvaram || 33 ||

tasyāstvavayavaireva vyāptaṃ sarvamidaṃ jagat |
sūkṣmātisūkṣmamīśānaṃ kalalasyāpi madhyataḥ || 34 ||

sraṣṭāramapi viśvasya veṣṭitāraṃ ca tasya tu |
śivameveśvaraṃ jñātvā śāntimatyantamṛcchati || 35 ||

sa eva kālo goptā ca viśvasyādhipatiḥ prabhuḥ |
taṃ viśvādhipatiṃ jñātvā mṛtyupāśātpramucyate || 36 ||

ghṛtātparaṃ maṃḍamiva sūkṣmaṃ jñātvā sthitaṃ prabhum |
sarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaṃ ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate || 37 ||

eṣa eva paro devo viśvakarmā maheśvaraḥ |
hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaṃ taṃ jñātvaivāmṛtamaśnute || 38 ||

yadā samastaṃ na divā na rātrirna sadapyasat |
kevalaśśiva evaiko yataḥ prajñā purātanī || 39 ||

nainamūrddhvaṃ na tiryakca na madhyaṃ paryajigrahat |
na tasya pratimā cāsti yasya nāma mahadyaśaḥ || 40 ||

ajātamimamevaike buddhā janmani bhīravaḥ |
rudrasyāsya prapadyante rakṣārthaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sukham || 41 ||

dve akṣare brahmapare tvanante samudāhṛte |
vidyāvidye samākhyāte nihite yatra gūḍhavat || 42 ||

kṣaraṃ tvavidyā hyamṛtaṃ vidyeti parigīyate |
te ubhe īśate yastu so .anyaḥ khalu maheśvaraḥ || 43 ||

ekaikaṃ bahudhā jālaṃ vikurvannekavacca yaḥ |
sarvādhipatyaṃ kurute sṛṣṭvā sarvān pratāpavān || 44 ||

diśa ūrdhvamadhastiryak bhāsayan bhrājate svayam |
yo niḥsvabhāvādapyeko vareṇyastvadhitiṣṭhati || 45 ||

svabhāvavācakān sarvān vācyāṃśca pariṇāmayan |
guṇāṃśca bhogyabhoktṛtve tadviśvamadhitiṣṭhati || 46 ||

te vai guhyopaṇiṣadi gūḍhaṃ brahma parātparam |
brahmayoniṃ jagatpūrvaṃ vidurdevā maharṣayaḥ || 47 ||

bhāvagrāhyamanīhākhyaṃ bhāvābhāvakaraṃ śivam |
kalāsargakaraṃ devaṃ ye viduste jahustanum || 48 ||

svabhāvameke manyante kālameke vimohitāḥ |
devasya mahimā hyeṣa yenedaṃ bhrāmyate jagat || 49 ||

yenedamāvṛtaṃ nityaṃ kālakālātmanā yataḥ |
teneritamidaṃ karma bhūtaiḥ saha vivartate || 50 ||

tatkarma bhūyaśaḥ kṛtvā vinivṛtya ca bhūyaśaḥ |
tattvasya saha tattvena yogaṃ cāpi sametya vai || 51 ||

aṣṭābhiśca tribhiścaivaṃ dvābhyāṃ caikena vā punaḥ |
kālenātmaguṇaiścāpi kṛtsnameva jagat svayam || 52 ||

guṇairārabhya karmāṇi svabhāvādīni yojayet |
teṣāmabhāve nāśaḥ syātkṛtasyāpi ca karmaṇaḥ || 53 ||

karmakṣaye punaścānyattato yāti sa tattvataḥ |
sa evādissvayaṃ yoganimittaṃ bhoktṛbhogayoḥ || 54 ||

parastrikālādakalassa eva parameśvaraḥ |
sarvavit triguṇādhīśo brahmasākṣātparātparaḥ || 55 ||

taṃ viśvarūpamabhavaṃ bhavamīḍyaṃ prajāpatim |
devadevaṃ jagatpūjyaṃ svacittasthamupāsmahe || 56 ||

kālādibhiḥ paro yasmātprapaṃcaḥ parivartate |
dharmāvahaṃ pāpanudaṃ bhogeśaṃ viśvadhāma ca || 57 ||

tamīśvarāṇāṃ paramaṃ maheśvaraṃ taṃ devatānāṃ paramaṃ ca daivatam |
patiṃ patīnāṃ paramaṃ parastādvidāma devaṃ bhuvaneśvareśvaram || 58 ||

na tasya vidyeta kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca na vidyate |
na tatsamo .adhikaścāpi kvacijjagati dṛśyate || 59 ||

parāsya vividhā śaktiḥ śrutau svābhāvikī śrutā |
jñānaṃ balaṃ kriyā caiva yābhyo viśvamidaṃ kṛtam || 60 ||

tasyāsti patiḥ kaścinnaiva liṃgaṃ na ceśitā |
kāraṇaṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca sa teṣāmadhipādhipaḥ || 61 ||

na cāsya janitā kaścinna ca janma kutaścana |
na janmahetavastadvanmalamāyādisaṃjñakāḥ || 62 ||

sa ekassarvabhūteṣu gūḍho vyāptaśca viśvataḥ |
sarvabhūtāntarātmā ca dharmādhyakṣassa kathyate || 63 ||

sarvabhūtādhivāsaśca sākṣī cetā ca nirguṇaḥ |
eko vaśī niṣkriyāṇāṃ bahūnāṃ vivaśātmanām || 64 ||

nityānāmapyasau nityaścetanānāṃ ca cetanaḥ |
eko bahūnāṃ cākāmaḥ kāmānīśaḥ prayacchati || 65 ||

sāṃkhyayogādhigamyaṃ yatkāraṇaṃ jagatāṃ patim |
jñātvā devaṃ paśuḥ pāśaissarvaireva vimucyate || 66 ||

viśvakṛdviśvavitsvātmayonijñaḥ kālakṛdguṇī |
pradhānaḥ kṣetrajñapatirguṇeśaḥ pāśamocakaḥ || 67 ||

brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe pūrvaṃ vedāṃścopādiśatsvayam |
yo devastamahaṃ buddhvā svātmabuddhiprasādataḥ || 68 ||

mumukṣurasmātsaṃsārātprapadye śaraṇaṃ śivam |
niṣphalaṃ niṣkriyaṃ śāntaṃ niravadyaṃ niraṃjanam || 69 ||

amṛtasya paraṃ setuṃ dagdhendhanamivānilam |
yadā carmavadākāśaṃ veṣṭayiṣyanti mānavāḥ || 70 ||

tadā śivamavijñāya duḥkhasyānto bhaviṣyati || 71 ||

tapaḥprabhāvāddevasya prasādācca maharṣayaḥ |
atyāśramocitajñānaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam || 72 ||

vedānte paramaṃ guhyaṃ purākalpapracoditam |
brahmaṇo vadanāllabdhaṃ mayedaṃ bhāgyagauravāt || 73 ||

nāpraśāntāya dātavyametajjñānamanuttamam |
na putrāyāśuvṛttāya nāśiṣyāya ca sarvathā || 74 ||

yasya deve parābhaktiryathā deve tathā gurau |
tasyaite kathitāhyarthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ || 75 ||

ataśca saṃkṣepamidaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ śivaḥ parastātprakṛteśca puṃsaḥ |
sa sargakāle ca karoti sarvaṃ saṃhārakāle punarādadāti || 76 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho .adhyāyaḥ || 6 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kālādutpadyate sarvaṃ kāladeva vipadyate |
na kālanirapekṣaṃ hi kvacitkiṃcana vidyate || 1 ||

yadāsyāntargataṃ viśvaṃ śaśvatsaṃsāramaṇḍalam |
sargasaṃhṛtimudrābhyāṃ cakravatparivartate || 2 ||

brahmā hariśca rudraśca tathānye ca surāsurāḥ |
yatkṛtāṃ niyatiṃ prāpya prabhavo nātivartitum || 3 ||

bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyādyairvibhajya jarayan prajāḥ |
atiprabhuriti svairaṃ vartate .atibhayaṃkaraḥ || 4 ||

ka eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ kasya vā vaśavartyayam |
ka evāsya vaśe na syātkathayaitadvicakṣaṇa || 5 ||

vāyuruvāca |

kālakāṣṭhānimeṣādikalākalitavigraham |
kālātmeti samākhyātaṃ tejo māheśvaraṃ param || 6 ||

yadalaṃghyamaśeṣasya sthāvarasya carasya ca |
niyogarūpamīśasya balaṃ viśvaniyāmakam || 7 ||

tasyāṃśāṃśamayī muktiḥ kālātmani mahātmani |
tato niṣkramya saṃkrāntā visṛṣṭāgrerivāyasī || 8 ||

tasmātkālavaśe viśvaṃ na sa viśvavaśe sthitaḥ |
śivasya tu vaśe kālo na kālasya vaśe śivaḥ || 9 ||

yato .apratihataṃ śārvaṃ tejaḥ kāle pratiṣṭhitam |
mahatī tena kālasya maryādā hi duratyayā || 10 ||

kālaṃ prajñāviśeṣeṇa ko .ativartitumarhati |
kālena tu kṛtaṃ karma na kaścidativartate || 11 ||

ekacchatrāṃ mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ ye parākramya śāsati |
te .api naivātivartante kālavelāmivābdhayaḥ || 12 ||

ye nigṛhyendriyagrāmaṃ jayanti sakalaṃ jagat |
na jayantyapi te kālaṃ kālo jayati tānapi || 13 ||

āyurvedavido vaidyāstvanuṣṭhitarasāyanāḥ |
na mṛtyumativartante kālo hi duratikramaḥ || 14 ||

śriyā rūpeṇa śīlena balena ca kulena ca |
anyaccintayate jantuḥ kālo .anyatkurute balāt || 15 ||

apriyaiśca priyaiścaiva hyacintitagamāgamaiḥ |
saṃyojayati bhūtāni viyojayati ceśvaraḥ || 16 ||

yadaiva duḥkhitaḥ kaścittadaiva sukhitaḥ paraḥ |
durvijñeyasvabhāvasya kālāsyāho vicitratā || 17 ||

yo yuvā sa bhavedvṛddho yo balīyānsa durbalaḥ |
yaḥ śrīmānso .api niḥśrīkaḥ kālaścitragatirdvijā || 18 ||

nābhijātyaṃ na vai śīlaṃ na balaṃ na ca naipuṇam |
bhavetkāryāya paryāptaṃ kālaśca hyanirodhakaḥ || 19 ||

ye sanāthāśca dātāro gītavādyairupasthitāḥ |
ye cānāthāḥ parānnādāḥ kālasteṣu samakriyaḥ || 20 ||

phalantyakāle na rasāyanāni samyakprayuktānyapi cauṣadhāni |
tānyeva kālena samāhṛtāni siddhiṃ prayāntyāśu sukhaṃ diśanti || 21 ||

nākālato .ayaṃ mriyate jāyate vā nākālataḥ puṣṭimagryāmupaiti |
nākālataḥ sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vā nākālikaṃ vastu samasti kiṃcit || 22 ||

kālena śītaḥ prativāti vātaḥkālena vṛṣṭirjaladānupaiti |
kālena coṣmā praśamaṃ prayāti kālena sarvaṃ saphalatvameti || 23 ||

kālaśca sarvasya bhavasya hetuḥ kālena sasyāni bhavanti nityam |
kālena sasyāni layaṃ prayānti kālena saṃjīvati jīvalokaḥ || 24 ||

itthaṃ kālātmanastattvaṃ yo vijānāti tattvataḥ |
kālātmānamatikramya kālātītaṃ sa paśyati || 25 ||

na yasya kālo na ca bandhamuktī na yaḥ pumānna prakṛtirna viśvam |
vicitrarūpāya śivāya tasmai namaḥparasmai parameśvarāya || 26 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe kālamahimavarṇanaṃ nāma saptamo .adhyāyaḥ || 7 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kena mānena kālesminnāyussaṃkhyā prakalpyate |
saṃkhyārūpasya kālasya kaḥ punaḥ paramo .avadhiḥ || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

āyuṣo .atra nimeṣākhyamādyamānaṃ pracakṣate |
saṃkhyārūpasya kālasya śānttvatītakalāvadhi || 2 ||

akṣipakṣmaparikṣepo nimeṣaḥ parikalpitaḥ |
tādṛśānāṃ nimeṣāṇāṃ kāṣṭhā daśa ca paṃca ca || 3 ||

kāṣṭhāṃstriṃśatkalā nāma kalāṃstriṃśanmuhūrtakaḥ |
muhūrttānāmapi triṃśadahorātraṃ pracakṣate || 4 ||

triṃśatsaṃkhyairahorātrairmāsaḥ pakṣadvayātmakaḥ || 5 ||

jñeyaṃ pitryamahorātraṃ māsaḥ kṛṣṇasitātmakaḥ || 6 ||

māsaistairayanaṃ ṣaḍbhirvarṣaṃ dve cāyanaṃ matam |
laukikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ || 7 ||

etaddivyamahorātramiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ |
dakṣiṇaṃ cāyanaṃ rātristathodagayanaṃ dinam || 8 ||

māsastriṃśadahorātrairdivyo mānuṣavatsmṛtaḥ |
saṃvatsaro .api devānāṃ māsairdvādaśabhistathā || 9 ||

trīṇi varṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣayutānyapi |
divyassaṃvatsaro jñeyo mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ || 10 ||

divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṃkhyā pravartate |
catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni kavayo viduḥ || 11 ||

pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate |
dvāparaṃ ca kaliścaiva yugānyetāni kṛtsnaśaḥ || 12 ||

catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam |
tasya tāvacchatīsandhyā sandhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ || 13 ||

itareṣu sasandhyeṣu sasandhyāṃśeṣu ca triṣu |
ekāpāyena vartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca || 14 ||

etaddvādaśasāhasraṃ sādhikaṃ ca caturyugam |
caturyugasahasraṃ yatsaṃkalpa iti kathyate || 15 ||

caturyugaikasaptatyā manorantaramucyate |
kalpe caturdaśaikasminmanūnāṃ parivṛttayaḥ || 16 ||

etena kramayogena kalpamanvantarāṇi ca |
saprajāni vyatītāni śataśo .atha sahasraśaḥ || 17 ||

ajñeyatvācca sarveṣāmasaṃkhyeyatayā punaḥ |
śakyo naivānupūrvyādvai teṣāṃ vaktuṃ suvistaraḥ || 18 ||

kalpo nāma divā prokto brahmaṇo .avyaktajanmanaḥ |
kalpānāṃ vai sahasraṃ ca brāhmaṃ varṣamihocyate || 19 ||

varṣāṇāmaṣṭasāhasraṃ yacca tadbrahmaṇo yugam |
savanaṃ yugasāhasraṃ brahmaṇaḥ padmajanmanaḥ || 20 ||

savanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca triguṇaṃ trivṛtaṃ tathā |
kalpyate sakalaḥ kālo brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ || 21 ||

tasya vai divase yānti caturdaśa purandarāḥ |
śatāni māse catvāri viṃśatyā sahitāni ca || 22 ||

abde paṃca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśadyutāni ca |
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi paṃca lakṣāṇi cāyuṣi || 23 ||

brahmā viṣṇordine caiko viṣṇū rudradine tathā |
īśvarasya dine rudrassadākhyasya tatheśvaraḥ || 24 ||

sākṣācchivasya tatsaṃkhyastathā so .api sadāśivaḥ |
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi paṃcalakṣāṇi cāyuṣi || 25 ||

tasminsākṣācchivenaiṣa kālātmā sampravartate |
yattatsṛṣṭessamākhyātaṃ kālāntaramiha dvijāḥ |
etatkālāntaraṃ jñeyamaharvai pārameśvaram // 26 |
rātriśca tāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśaḥ // 26 || 26 ||

ahastasya tu yā sṛṣṭī rātriśca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ |
aharna vidyate tasya na rātririti dhārayet || 27 ||

eṣopacāraḥ kriyate lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā |
prajāḥ prajānāṃ patayo mūrttayaśca surāsurāḥ || 28 ||

indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca mahābhūtāni paṃca ca |
tanmātrāṇyatha bhūtādirbuddhiśca saha daivataḥ || 29 ||

ahastiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi pārameśasya dhīmataḥ |
aharante pralīyante rātryante viśvasaṃbhavaḥ || 30 ||

yo viśvātmā karmakālasvabhāvādyarthe śaktiryasya nollaṃghanīyā |
yasyaivājñādhīnametatsamastaṃ namastasmai mahate śaṃkarāya || 31 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvabhāge kālaprabhāve tridevāyurvarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭamo .adhyāyaḥ || 8 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

kathaṃ jagadidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vidhāya ca nidhāya ca |
ājñayā paramāṃ krīḍāṃ karoti parameśvaraḥ || 1 ||

kiṃ tatprathamasaṃbhūtaṃ kenedamakhilaṃ tatam |
kenā vā punarevedaṃ grasyate pṛthukukṣiṇā || 2 ||

// vāyuruvāca |

śaktiḥ prathamasambhūtā śāntyatītapadottarā |
tato māyā tato .avyaktaṃ śivācchaktimataḥ prabhoḥ || 3 ||

śāntyatītapadaṃ śaktestataḥ śāntipadakramāt |
tato vidyāpadaṃ tasmātpratiṣṭhāpadasaṃbhavaḥ || 4 ||

nivṛttipadamutpannaṃ pratiṣṭhāpadataḥ kramāt |
evamuktā samāsena sṛṣṭirīśvaracoditā || 5 ||

ānulomyāttathaiteṣāṃ pratilomyena saṃhṛtiḥ |
asmātpañcapadoddiṣṭātparassraṣṭā samiṣyate || 6 ||

kalābhiḥ paṃcabhirvyāptaṃ tasmādviśvamidaṃ jagat |
avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattadātmanā samanuṣṭhitam || 7 ||

mahadādiviśeṣāntaṃ sṛjatītyapi saṃmatam |
kiṃ tu tatrāpi kartṛtvaṃ nāvyaktasya na cātmanaḥ || 8 ||

acetanatvātprakṛterajñatvātpuruṣasya ca |
pradhānaparamāṇvādi yāvatkiñcidacetanam || 9 ||

tatkartṛkaṃ svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ buddhimatkāraṇaṃ vinā |
jagacca kartṛsāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ sāvayavaṃ yataḥ || 10 ||

tasmācchaktassvatantro yaḥ sarvaśaktiśca sarvavit |
anādinidhanaścāyaṃ mahadaiśvaryasaṃyutaḥ || 11 ||

sa eva jagataḥ kartā mahādevo maheśvarāḥ |
pātā hartā ca sarvasya tataḥ pṛthagananvayaḥ || 12 ||

pariṇāmaḥ pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ puruṣasya ca |
sarvaṃ satyavratasyaiva śāsanena pravartate || 13 ||

itīyaṃ śāśvatī niṣṭhā satāṃ manasi vartate |
na cainaṃ pakṣamāśritya vartate svalpacetanaḥ || 14 ||

yāvadādisamāraṃbho yāvadyaḥ pralayo mahān |
tāvadapyeti sakalaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śāradāṃ śatam || 15 ||

paramityāyuṣo nāma brahmaṇo .avyaktajanmanaḥ |
tatparākhyaṃ tadarddhaṃ ca parārddhamabhidhīyate || 16 ||

parārddhadvayakālānte pralaye samupasthite |
avyaktamātmanaḥ kāryamādāyātmani tiṣṭhati || 17 ||

ātmanyavasthite .avyakte vikāre pratisaṃhṛte |
sādharmyeṇādhitiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau || 18 ||

tamaḥ sattvaguṇāvetau samatvena vyavasthitau |
anudriktāvanantau tāvotaprotau parasparam || 19 ||

guṇasāmye tadā tasminnavibhāge tamodaye |
śāntavātaikanīre ca na prājñāyata kiṃcana || 20 ||

aprajñāte jagatyasminneka eva maheśvaraḥ |
upāsya rajanīṃ kṛtsnāṃ parāṃ māheśvarīṃ tataḥ || 21 ||

prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ pradhānapuruṣāvubhau |
praviśya kṣobhayāmāsa māyāyogānmaheśvaraḥ || 22 ||

tataḥ punaraśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayāt |
avyaktādabhavatsṛṣṭirājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ || 23 ||

viśvottarottaravicitramanorathasya yasyaikaśaktiśakale sakalassamāptaḥ |
ātmānamadhvapatimadhvavido vadanti tasmai namaḥ sakalalokavilakṣaṇāya || 24 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvabhāge sṛṣṭipālanapralayakartṛtvavarṇanaṃ nāma navamo .adhyāyaḥ || 9 ||

vāyuruvāca |

puruṣādhiṣṭhitātpūrvamavyaktādīśvarājñayā |
buddhyādayo viśeṣāntā vikārāścābhavan kramāt || 1 ||

tatastebhyo vikārebhyo rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ |
kāraṇatvena sarveṣāṃ trayo devāḥ prajajñire || 2 ||

sarvato bhuvanavyāptiśaktimavyāhatāṃ kvacit |
jñānamapratimaṃ śaśvadaiśvaryaṃ cāṇimādikam || 3 ||

sṛṣṭisthitilayākhyeṣu karmasu triṣu hetutām |
prabhutvena sahaiteṣāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ || 4 ||

kalpāntare punasteṣāmasparddhā buddhimohinām |
sargarakṣālayācāraṃ pratyekaṃ pradadau ca saḥ || 5 ||

ete parasparotpannā dhārayanti parasparam |
paraspareṇa vardhante parasparamanuvratāḥ || 6 ||

kvacidbrahmā kvacidviṣṇuḥ kvacidrudraḥ praśasyate |
nānena teṣāmādhikyamaiśvaryaṃ cātiricyate || 7 ||

mūrkhā nindanti tānvāgbhiḥ saṃraṃbhābhiniveśinaḥ |
yātudhānā bhavantyeva piśācāśca na saṃśayaḥ || 8 ||

devo guṇatrayātītaścaturvyūho maheśvaraḥ |
sakalassakalādhāraśakterutpattikāraṇam || 9 ||

soyamātmā trayasyāsya prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca |
līlākṛtajagatsṛṣṭirīśvaratve vyavasthitaḥ || 10 ||

yassarvasmātparo nityo niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ |
sa eva ca tadādhārastadātmā tadadhiṣṭhitaḥ || 11 ||

tasmānmaheśvaraścaiva prakṛtiḥ puruṣastathā |
sadāśivabhavo viṣṇurbrahmā sarvaśivātmakam || 12 ||

pradhānātprathamaṃ jajñe vṛddhiḥ khyātirmatirmahān |
mahattattvasya saṃkṣobhādahaṃkārastridhā .abhavat || 13 ||

ahaṃkāraśca bhūtāni tanmātrānīndriyāṇi ca |
vaikārikādahaṃkārātsattvodriktāttu sāttvikaḥ || 14 ||

vaikārikaḥ sa sargastu yugapatsaṃpravartate |
buddhīndriyāṇi paṃcaiva paṃcakarmendriyāṇi ca || 15 ||

ekādaśaṃ manastatra svaguṇenobhayātmakam |
tamoyuktādahaṃkārādbhūtatanmātrasaṃbhavaḥ || 16 ||

bhūtānāmādibhūtatvādbhūtādiḥ kathyate tu saḥ |
bhūtādeśśabdamātraṃ syāttatra cākāśasaṃbhavaḥ || 17 ||

ākāśātsparśa utpannaḥ sparśādvāyusamudbhavaḥ |
vāyo rūpaṃ tatastejastejaso rasasaṃbhavaḥ || 18 ||

rasādāpassamutpannāstebhyo gandhasamudbhavaḥ |
gandhācca pṛthivī jātā bhūtebhyonyaccarācaram || 19 ||

puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca |
mahadādiviśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te || 20 ||

tatra kāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ brahmaṇo yadā |
tadaṃḍe supravṛddho .abhūt kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ || 21 ||

sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣa ucyate |
ādikartā sa bhūtānāṃ brahmāgre samavartata || 22 ||

tasyeśvarasya pratimā jñānavairāgyalakṣaṇā |
dharmaiśvaryakarī buddhirbrāhmī yajñe .abhimāninaḥ || 23 ||

avyaktājjāyate tasya manasā yadyadīpsitam |
vaśī vikṛtvāttraiguṇyātsāpekṣatvātsvabhāvataḥ || 24 ||

tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ trailokye saṃpravarttate |
sṛjate grasate caiva vīkṣate ca tribhissvayam || 25 ||

caturmukhastu brahmatve kālatve cāntakassmṛtaḥ |
sahasramūrddhā puruṣastisrovasthāssvayaṃbhuvaḥ || 26 ||

sattvaṃ rajaśca brahmā ca kālatve ca tamo rajaḥ |
viṣṇutve kevalaṃ sattvaṃ guṇavṛddhistridhā vibhau || 27 ||

brahmatve sṛjate lokān kālatve saṃkṣipatyapi |
puruṣatve .atyudāsīnaḥ karma ca trividhaṃ vibhoḥ || 28 ||

evaṃ tridhā vibhinnatvādbrahmā triguṇa ucyate |
caturddhā pravibhaktatvāccāturvyūhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 29 ||

āditvādādidevo .asāvajātatvādajaḥ smṛtaḥ |
pāti yasmātprajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiriti smṛtaḥ || 30 ||

hiraṇmayastu yo merustasyolbaṃ sumahātmanaḥ |
garbhodakaṃ samudrāśca jarāyuścā.api parvatāḥ || 31 ||

tasminnaṃḍe tvime lokā antarviśvamidaṃ jagat |
candrādityau sanakṣatrau sagrahau saha vāyunā || 32 ||

adbhirdaśaguṇābhistu bāhyatoṇḍaṃ samāvṛtam |
āpo daśaguṇenaiva tejasā bahirāvṛtāḥ || 33 ||

tejo daśaguṇenaiva vāyunā bahirāvṛtam |
ākāśenāvṛto vāyuḥ khaṃ ca bhūtādināvṛtam || 34 ||

bhūtādirmahatā tadvadavyaktenāvṛto mahān |
etairāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhirbahirāvṛtam || 35 ||

etadāvṛttya cānyonyamaṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ |
sṛṣṭipālanavidhvaṃsakarmakartryo dvijottamāḥ || 36 ||

evaṃ parasparotpannā dhārayanti parasparam |
ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāstu vikāriṣu || 37 ||

kūrmoṃgāni yathā pūrvaṃ prasāryya viniyacchati |
vikārāṃśca tathā .avyaktaṃ sṛṣṭvā bhūyo niyacchati || 38 ||

avyaktaprabhavaṃ sarvamānulomyena jāyate |
prāpte pralayakāle tu pratilomyenulīyate || 39 ||

guṇāḥ kālavaśādeva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ |
guṇasāmye layo jñeyo vaiṣamye sṛṣṭirucyate || 40 ||

tadidaṃ brahmaṇo yoniretadaṃḍaṃ ghanaṃ mahat |
brahmaṇaḥ kṣetramuddiṣṭaṃ brahmā kṣetrajña ucyate || 41 ||

itīdṛśānāmaṇḍānāṃ koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahasraśaḥ |
sarvagatvātpradhānasya tiryyagūrdhvamadhaḥ sthitāḥ || 42 ||

tatra tatra caturvaktrā brahmāṇo harayo bhavāḥ |
sṛṣṭā pradhānena tathā labdhvā śaṃbhostu sannidhim || 43 ||

maheśvaraḥ parovyaktādaṃḍamavyaktasaṃbhavam |
aṇḍājjajñe vibhurbrahmā lokāstena kṛtāstvime || 44 ||

abuddhipūrvaḥ kathito mayaiṣa pradhānasargaḥ prathamaḥ pravṛtaḥ |
ātyantikaśca pralayontakāle līlākṛtaḥ kevalamīśvarasya || 45 ||

yattatsmṛtaṃ kāraṇamaprameyaṃ brahmā pradhānaṃ prakṛteḥ prasūtiḥ |
anādimadhyāntamanantavīryaṃ śuklaṃ suraktaṃ puruṣeṇa yuktam || 46 ||

utpādakatvādrajasotirekāllokasya saṃtānavivṛddhihetūn |
aṣṭau vikārānapi cādikāle sṛṣṭvā samaśnāti tathāntakāle || 47 ||

prakṛtyavasthāpitakāraṇānāṃ yā ca sthitiryā ca punaḥ pravṛttiḥ |
tatsarvamaprākṛtavaibhavasya saṃkalpamātreṇa maheśvarasya || 48 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ brahmāṃḍasthitivarṇanaṃ nāma daśamo .adhyāyaḥ || 10 ||

munaya ūcuḥ |

manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi kalpabhedāṃśca sarvaśaḥ |
teṣvevāntarasargaṃ ca pratisargaṃ ca no vada || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

kālasaṃkhyāvivṛttasya parārddho brahmaṇassmṛtaḥ |
tāvāṃścaivāsya kālonyastasyānte pratisṛjyate || 2 ||

divase divase tasya brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajanmanaḥ |
caturdaśamahābhāgā manūnāṃ parivṛttayaḥ || 3 ||

anāditvādanantatvādajñeyatvācca kṛtsnaśaḥ |
manvantarāṇi kalpāśca na śakyā vacanātpṛthak || 4 ||

ukteṣvapi ca sarveṣu śṛṇvatāṃ vo vaco mama |
kimihāsti phalaṃ tasmānna pṛthak vaktumutsahe || 5 ||

ya eva khalu kalpeṣu kalpaḥ saṃprati vartate |
tatra saṃkṣipya vartante sṛṣṭayaḥ pratisṛṣṭayaḥ || 6 ||

yastvayaṃ vartate kalpo vārāho nāma nāmataḥ |
asminnapi dvijaśreṣṭhā manavastu caturdaśa || 7 ||

svāyaṃbhuvādayassapta sapta sāvarṇikādayaḥ |
teṣu vaivasvato nāma saptamo vartate manuḥ || 8 ||

manvantareṣu sarveṣu sargasaṃhāravṛttayaḥ |
prāyaḥ samābhavantīti tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā || 9 ||

pūrvakalpe parāvṛtte pravṛtte kālamārute |
samunmūlitamūleṣu vṛkṣeṣu ca vaneṣu ca || 10 ||

jaganti tṛṇavaktrīṇi deve dahati pāvake |
vṛṣṭyā bhuvi niṣiktāyāṃ viveleṣvarṇaveṣu ca || 11 ||

dikṣu sarvāsu magnāsu vāripūre mahīyasi |
tadadbhiścaṭulākṣepaistaraṃgabhujamaṇḍalaiḥ || 12 ||

prārabdhacaṇḍanṛtyeṣu tataḥ pralayavāriṣu |
brahmā nārāyaṇo bhūtvā suṣvāpa salile sukham || 13 ||

imaṃ codāharanmantraṃ ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati |
taṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ muniśreṣṭhāstadarthaṃ cākṣarāśrayam || 14 ||

āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ |
ayanaṃ tasya tā yasmāttena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || 15 ||

śivayogamayīṃ nidrāṃ kurvantaṃ tridaśeśvaram |
baddhāṃjali puṭāssiddhā janalokanivāsinaḥ || 16 ||

stotraiḥ prabodhayāmāsuḥ prabhātasamaye surāḥ |
yathā sṛṣṭyādisamaye īśvaraṃ śrutayaḥ purā || 17 ||

tataḥ prabuddha utthāya śayanāttoyamadhyagāt |
udaikṣata diśaḥ sarvā yoganidrālasekṣaṇaḥ || 18 ||

nāpaśyatsa tadā kiṃcitsvātmano vyatireki yat |
savismaya ivāsīnaḥ parāṃ cintāmupāgamat || 19 ||

kva sā bhagavatī yā tu manojñā mahatī mahī |
nānāvidhamahāśailanadīnagarakānanā || 20 ||

evaṃ saṃcintayanbrahmā bubudhe naiva bhūsthitim |
tadā sasmāra pitaraṃ bhagavantaṃ trilocanam || 21 ||

smaraṇāddevadevasya bhavasyāmitatejasaḥ |
jñātavānsalile magnāṃ dharaṇīṃ dharaṇīpatiḥ || 22 ||

tato bhūmessamuddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
jalakrīḍocitaṃ divyaṃ vārāhaṃ rūpamasmarat || 23 ||

mahāparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ mahājaladaniḥsvanam |
nīlameghapratīkāśaṃ dīptaśabdaṃ bhayānakam || 24 ||

pīnavṛttaghanaskandhapīnonnatakaṭītaṭam |
hrasvavṛttorujaṃghāgraṃ sutīkṣṇapuramaṇḍalam || 25 ||

padmarāgamaṇiprakhyaṃ vṛttabhīṣaṇalocanam |
vṛttadīrghamahāgātraṃ stabdhakarṇasthalojjvalam || 26 ||

udīrṇocchvāsaniśvāsaghūrṇitapralayārṇavam |
visphuratsusaṭācchannakapolaskandhabandhuram || 27 ||

maṇibhirbhūṣaṇaiścitrairmahāratnaiḥpariṣkṛtam |
virājamānaṃ vidyudbhirmeghasaṃghamivonnatam || 28 ||

āsthāya vipulaṃ rūpaṃ vārāhamamitaṃ vidhiḥ |
pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam || 29 ||

sa tadā śuśubhe .atīva sūkaro girisaṃnibhaḥ |
liṃgākṛtermaheśasya pādamūlaṃ gato yathā || 30 ||

tatassa salile magnāṃ pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīṃdharaḥ |
uddhṛtyāliṃgya daṃṣṭrābhyāmunmamajja rasātalāt || 31 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayassiddhā janalokanivāsinaḥ |
mumudurnanṛturmūrdhni tasya puṣpairavākiran || 32 ||

vapurmahāvarāhasya śuśubhe puṣpasaṃvṛtam |
patadbhiriva khadyotaiḥ prāśuraṃjanaparvataḥ || 33 ||

tataḥ saṃsthānamānīya varāho mahatīṃ mahīm |
svameva rūpamāsthāya sthāpayāmāsa vai vibhuḥ || 34 ||

pṛthivīṃ ca samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ sthāpayangirīn |
bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat || 35 ||

iti saha mahatīṃ mahīṃ mahīdhraiḥ pralayamahājaladheradhaḥsthamadhyāt |
upari ca viniveśya viśvakarmā caramacaraṃ ca jagatsasarja bhūyaḥ || 36 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vā.. pū.. sṛṣṭyādivarṇanaṃ nāmaikādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 11 ||

vāyuruvāca |

sargaṃ cintayatastasya tadā vai buddhipūrvakam |
pradhyānakāle mohastu prādurbhūtastamomayaḥ || 1 ||

tamomoho mahāmohastāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ |
avidyā pañcamī caiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ || 2 ||

paṃcadhā .avasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyatastvabhimāninaḥ |
sarvvatastamasātīva bījakumbhavadāvṛtaḥ || 3 ||

bahirantaścāprakāśaḥ stabdho niḥsaṃjña eva ca |
tasmātteṣāṃ vṛtā buddhirmukhāni karaṇāni ca || 4 ||

tasmātte saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā.asādhakaṃ brahmā prathamaṃ sargamīdṛśam || 5 ||

aprasannamanā bhūtvā dvitīyaṃ so .abhyamanyata |
tasyābhidhāyataḥ sargaṃ tiryyaksroto .abhyavarttata || 6 ||

antaḥprakāśāstiryyaṃca āvṛtāśca bahiḥ punaḥ |
paśvātmānastato jātā utpathagrāhiṇaśca te || 7 ||

tamapyasādhakaṃ jñātvā sargamanyamamanyata |
tadorddhvasrotaso vṛtto devasargastu sāttvikaḥ || 8 ||

te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantaśca nāvṛtāḥ |
prakāśā bahirantaścasvabhāvādeva saṃjñitāḥ || 9 ||

tato .abhidhyāyatovyaktādarvvāksrotastu sādhakaḥ |
manuṣyanāmā sañjātaḥ sargo duḥkhasamutkaṭaḥ || 10 ||

prakāśābahirantaste tamodriktā rajo .adhikāḥ |
paṃcamonugrahaḥ sargaścaturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ || 11 ||

viparyyayeṇa śaktyā ca tuṣṭyāsiddhyā tathaiva ca |
te .aparigrāhiṇaḥ sarvve saṃvibhāgaratāḥ punaḥ || 12 ||

khādanāścāpyaśīlāśca bhūtādyāḥ parikīrttitāḥ |
prathamo mahataḥ sargo brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ || 13 ||

tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate |
vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 14 ||

ityeṣa prakṛteḥ sargaḥ sambhṛto .abuddhipūrvakaḥ |
mukhyasargaścaturthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ || 15 ||

tiryyaksrotastu yaḥ proktastiryagyoniḥ sa pañcamaḥ |
tadūrddhvasrotasaḥ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ || 16 ||

tato .arvāk srotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ |
aṣṭamo .anugrahaḥ sargaḥ kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ || 17 ||

prākṛtāśca trayaḥ pūrvve sargāste .abuddhipūrvakāḥ |
buddhipūrvvaṃ pravarttante mukhyādyāḥ pañca vaikṛtāḥ || 18 ||

agre sasarjja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān |
sanandaṃ sanakañcaiva vidvāṃsañca sanātanam || 19 ||

ṛbhuṃ sanatkumārañca pūrvvameva prajāpatiḥ |
sarvve te yogino jñeyā vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ || 20 ||

iśvarāsaktamanaso na cakruḥ sṛṣṭaye matim |
teṣu sṛṣṭyanapekṣeṣu gateṣu sanakādiṣu || 21 ||

sraṣṭukāmaḥ punarbrahmā tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ |
tasyaivaṃ tapyamānasya na kiṃcitsamavarttata || 22 ||

tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhātkrodho vyajāyata |
krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ || 23 ||

tatastebhyo .aśrubindubhyo bhūtāḥ pretāstadābhavan |
sarvāṃstānaśrujāndṛṣṭvā brahmātmānamanindata || 24 ||

tasya tīvrā .abhavanmūrcchā krodhāmarṣasamudbhavā |
mūrcchitastu jahau prāṇānkrodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ || 25 ||

tataḥ prāṇeśvaro rudro bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ |
prasādamatulaṃ karttuṃ prādurāsītprabhormukhāt || 26 ||

daśadhā caikadhā cakre svātmānaṃ prabhurīśvaraḥ |
te tenoktā mahātmāno daśadhā caikadhā kṛtāḥ || 27 ||

yūyaṃ sṛṣṭā mayā vatsā lokānugrahakāraṇāt |
tasmātsarvvasya lokasya sthāpanāya hitāya ca || 28 ||

prajāsantānahetośca prayatadhvamatandritāḥ |
evamuktāśca rurudurdudruvuśca samantataḥ || 29 ||

rodanāddrāvaṇāccaiva te rudrā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ |
ye rudrāste khalu prāṇā ye prāṇāste mahātmakāḥ || 30 ||

tato mṛtasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |
ghṛṇī dadau punaḥ prāṇānbrahmaputro maheśvaraḥ || 31 ||

prahṛṣṭavadano rudraḥ prāṇapratyāgamādvibhoḥ |
abhyabhāṣata viśveśo brahmāṇaṃ paramaṃ vacaḥ || 32 ||

mābhairmābhairmahābhāga viriṃca jagatāṃ guro |
mayā te prāṇitāḥ prāṇāḥ sukhamuttiṣṭha suvrata || 33 ||

svapnānubhūtamiva tacchrutvā vākyaṃ manoharam |
haraṃ nirīkṣya śanakairnetraiḥ phullāmbujaprabhaiḥ || 34 ||

tathā pratyāgataprāṇaḥ snigdhagambhīrayā girā |
uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā tamuddiśya kṛtāñjaliḥ || 35 ||

tvaṃ hi darśanamātreṇa cānandayasi me manaḥ |
ko bhavān viśvamūrtyā vā sthita ekādaśātmakaḥ || 36 ||

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ |
spṛśan kārābhyāṃ brahmāṇaṃ susukhābhyāṃ sureśvaraḥ || 37 ||

māṃ viddhi paramātmānaṃ tava putratvamāgatam |
ete caikādaśa rudrāstvāṃ surakṣitumāgatāḥ || 38 ||

tasmāttīvrāmimāmmūrcchāṃ vidhūya madanugrahāt |
prabuddhasva yathāpūrvaṃ prajā vai sraṣṭumarhasi || 39 ||

evaṃ bhagavatā prokto brahmā prītamanā hyabhūt |
nānāṣṭakena viśvātmā tuṣṭāva parameśvaram || 40 ||

brahmovāca |

namaste bhagavan rudra bhāskarāmitatejase |
namo bhavāya devāya rasāyāmbumayātmane |
śarvāya kṣitirūpāya nandīsurabhaye namaḥ // 41 || 41 ||

īśāya vasave tubhyaṃ namassparśamayātmane |
paśūnāṃ pataye caiva pāvakāyātitejase |
bhīmāya vyomarūpāya śabdamātrāya te namaḥ // 42 || 42 ||

ugrāyograsvarūpāya yajamānātmane namaḥ |
mahādevāya somāya namostvamṛtamūrtaye || 43 ||

evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ |
prārthayāmāsa viśveśaṃ girā praṇatipūrvayā || 44 ||

bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa mama putra maheśvara |
sṛṣṭihetostvamutpanno mamāṃge .anaṃganāśanaḥ || 45 ||

tasmānmahati kāryesmin vyāpṛtasya jagatprabho |
sahāyaṃ kuru sarvatra sraṣṭumarhasi sa prajāḥ || 46 ||

tenaiṣāṃ pāvito devo rudrastripuramardanaḥ |
bāḍhamityeva tāṃ vāṇīṃ pratijagrāha śaṃkaraḥ || 47 ||

tatassa bhagavān brahmā hṛṣṭaṃ tamabhinandya ca |
sraṣṭuṃ tenābhyanujñātastathānyāścāsṛjatprajāḥ || 48 ||

marīcibhṛgvaṃgirasaḥ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum |
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so .asṛjanmanasaiva ca |
purastādasṛjadbrahmā dharmaṃ saṃkalpameva ca // 49 || 49 ||

ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā dvādaśādau prakīrtitāḥ |
saha rudreṇa saṃbhūtāḥ purāṇā gṛhamedhinaḥ || 50 ||

teṣāṃ dvādaśa vaṃśāḥ syurdivyā devagaṇānvitāḥ |
prajāvantaḥ kriyāvanto maharṣibhiralaṃkṛtāḥ || 51 ||

atha devāsurapitR̥n manuṣyāṃśca catuṣṭayam |
saha rudreṇa sisṛkṣuraṃbhasyetāni vai vidhiḥ || 52 ||

sa sṛṣṭyarthaṃ samādhāya brahmātmānamayūyujat |
mukhādajanayaddevān pitR̥ṃścaivopapakṣataḥ || 53 ||

jaghanādasurān sarvān prajanādapi mānuṣān |
avaskare kṣudhāviṣṭā rākṣasāstasya jajñire || 54 ||

putrāstamorajaḥprāyā balinaste niśācarāḥ |
sarpā yakṣāstathā bhūtā gandharvāḥ saṃprajajñire || 55 ||

vayāṃsi pakṣataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pakṣiṇo vakṣaso .asṛjat |
mukhatojāṃstathā pārśvāduragāṃśca vinirmame || 56 ||

padbhyāṃ cāśvānsamātaṃgān śarabhān gavayān mṛgān |
uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva nyaṃkūnanyāśca jātayaḥ || 57 ||

auṣadhyaḥ phalamūlāni romabhyastasya jajñire |
gāyatrīṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsāma rathantaram || 58 ||

agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt |
yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandaḥstomaṃ paṃcadaśaṃ tathā || 59 ||

bṛhatsāma tathokthaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt |
sāmāni jagatīchandaḥ stomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā || 60 ||

vairūpyamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjan mukhāt |
ekaviṃśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmāṇameva ca || 61 ||

anuṣṭubhaṃ sa vairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt |
uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire || 62 ||

yakṣāḥ piśācā gandharvāstathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ |
narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥpaśumṛgoragāḥ || 63 ||

avyayaṃ caiva yadidaṃ sthāṇusthāvarajaṃgamam |
teṣāṃ vai yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭāni prapedire || 64 ||

tānyeva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte || 65 ||

tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate |
mahābhūteṣu nānātvamindriyārtheṣu muktiṣu || 66 ||

viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vyadadhatsvayam |
nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ prākṛtānāṃ prapaṃcanam || 67 ||

vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame .asau pitāmahaḥ |
ārṣāṇi caiva nāmāni yāśca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ || 68 ||

śarvaryyante prasūtānāṃ tānyevaibhyo dadāvajaḥ |
yathartāvṛtuliṃgāni nānārūpāṇi paryyaye || 69 ||

dṛśyante tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu |
ityeṣa karaṇodbhūto lokasargassvayaṃbhuvaḥ || 70 ||

mahadādyoviśeṣānto vikāraḥ prakṛteḥ svayam |
candrasūryaprabhājuṣṭo grahanakṣatramaṃḍitaḥ || 71 ||

nadībhiśca samudraiśca parvataiśca sa maṃḍitaḥ |
paraiśca vividhairamyaissphītairjanapadaistathā || 72 ||

tasmin brahmavane .avyakto brahmā carati sarvavit |
avyaktabījaprabhava īśvarānugrahe sthitaḥ || 73 ||

buddhiskandhamahāśākha indriyāntarakoṭaraḥ |
mahābhūtapramāṇaśca viśeṣāmalapallavaḥ || 74 ||

dharmādharmasupuṣpāḍhyaḥ sukhaduḥkhaphalodayaḥ |
ājīvyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ || 75 ||

dyāṃ mūrddhānaṃ tasya viprā vadanti khaṃ vai nābhiṃ candrasūryau ca netre |
diśaḥ śrotre caraṇau ca kṣitiṃ ca so .acintyātmā sarvabhūtapraṇetā || 76 ||

vaktrāttasya brahmaṇāssaṃprasūtāstadvakṣasaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pūrvabhāgāt |
vaiśyā urubhyāṃ tasya padbhyāṃ ca śūdrāḥ sarve varṇā gātrataḥ saṃprasūtāḥ || 77 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe sṛṣṭivarṇanaṃ nāma dvādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 12 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

bhavatā kathitā sṛṣṭirbhavasya paramātmanaḥ |
caturmukhamukhāttasya saṃśayo naḥ prajāyate || 1 ||

devaśreṣṭho virūpākṣo dīptaśśūladharo haraḥ |
kālātmā bhagavān rudraḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ || 2 ||

sabrahmakamimaṃ lokaṃ saviṣṇumapi pāvakam |
yaḥ saṃharati saṃkruddho yugānte samupasthite || 3 ||

yasya brahmā ca viṣṇuśca praṇāmaṃ kuruto bhayāt |
lokasaṃkocakasyāsya yasya tau vaśavartinau || 4 ||

yo .ayaṃ devaḥ svakādaṃgādbrahmaviṣṇū purāsṛjat |
sa eva hi tayornityaṃ yogakṣemakaraḥ prabhuḥ || 5 ||

sa kathaṃ bhagavān rudra ādidevaḥ purātanaḥ |
putratvamagamacchaṃbhurbrahmaṇo .avyaktajanmanaḥ || 6 ||

prajāpatiśca viṣṇuśca rudrasyaitau parasparam |
sṛṣṭau parasparasyāṃgāditi prāgapi śuśruma || 7 ||

kathaṃ punaraśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ hetubhūtayoḥ |
guṇapradhānabhāvena prādurbhāvaḥ parasparāt || 8 ||

nāpṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā kiṃcinnāśrutaṃ ca kathaṃcana |
bhagavacchiṣyabhūtena bhavatā sakalaṃ smṛtam || 9 ||

tattvaṃ vada yathā brahmā munīnāmavadadvibhuḥ |
vayaṃ śraddhālavastāta śrotumīśvarasadyaśaḥ || 10 ||

vāyuruvāca |

sthāne pṛṣṭamidaṃ viprā bhavadbhiḥ praśnakovidaiḥ |
idameva purā pṛṣṭo mama prāha pitāmahaḥ || 11 ||

tadahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi yathā rudrasamudbhavaḥ |
yathā ca punarutpattirbrahmaviṣṇvoḥ parasparam || 12 ||

trayaste kāraṇātmāno jatāssākṣānmaheśvarāt |
carācarasya viśvasya sargasthityantahetavaḥ || 13 ||

paramaiśvaryasaṃyuktāḥ parameśvarabhāvitāḥ |
tacchaktyādhiṣṭhitā nityaṃ tatkāryakaraṇakṣamāḥ || 14 ||

pitrā niyamitāḥ pūrvaṃ trayopi triṣu karmasu |
brahmā sarge haristrāṇe rudraḥ saṃharaṇe tathā || 15 ||

tathāpyanyonyamātsaryādanyonyātiśayāśinaḥ |
tapasā toṣayitvā svaṃ pitaraṃ parameśvaram || 16 ||

labdhvā sarvātmanā tasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ |
brahmanārāyaṇau pūrvaṃ rudraḥ kalpāntare .asṛjat || 17 ||

kalpāntare punarbrahmā rudraviṣṇū jaganmayaḥ |
viṣṇuśca bhagavānrudraṃ brahmāṇamasṛjatpunaḥ || 18 ||

nārāyaṇaṃ punarbrahmā brahmāṇamasṛjatpunaḥ |
evaṃ kalpeṣu kalpeṣu brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ || 19 ||

paraspareṇa jāyante parasparahitaiṣiṇaḥ |
tattatkalpāntavṛttāntamadhikṛtya maharṣibhiḥ || 20 ||

prabhāvaḥ kathyate teṣāṃ parasparasamudbhavāt |
śṛṇu teṣāṃ kathāṃ citrāṃ puṇyāṃ pāpapramocinīm || 21 ||

kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttāṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |
purā nārāyaṇo nāma kalpe vai meghavāhane || 22 ||

divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu megho bhūtvāvahaddharām |
tasya bhāvaṃ samālakṣya viṣṇorviśvajagadguruḥ || 23 ||

sarvassarvātmabhāvena pradadau śaktimavyayām |
śaktiṃ labdhvā tu sarvātmā śivātsarveśvarāttadā || 24 ||

sasarja bhagāvan viṣṇurviśvaṃ viśvasṛjā saha |
viṣṇostadvaibhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭastena pitāmahaḥ || 25 ||

īrṣyayā parayā grastaḥ prahasannidamabravīt |
gaccha viṣṇo mayā jñātaṃ tava sargasya kāraṇam |
āvayoradhikaścāsti sa rudro nātra saṃśayaḥ // 26 || 26 ||

tasya devādhidevasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ |
sraṣṭā tvaṃ bhagavānādyaḥ pālakaḥ paramārthataḥ || 27 ||

ahaṃ ca tapasārādhya rudraṃ tridaśanāyakam |
tvayā saha jagatsarvaṃ srakṣyāmyatra na saṃśayaḥ || 28 ||

evaṃ viṣṇumupālabhya bhagavānabjasambhavaḥ |
evaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa tapasā prāpya śaṃkaram || 29 ||

bhagavan devadeveśa viśveśvara maheśvara |
tava vāmāṃgajo viṣṇurdakṣiṇāṃgabhavo hyaham || 30 ||

mayā saha jagatsarvaṃ tathāpyasṛjadacyutaḥ |
sa matsarādupālabdhastvadāśrayabalānmayā || 31 ||

madbhāvānnādhikasteti bhāvastvayi maheśvare |
tvatta eva samutpattirāvayossadṛśī yataḥ || 32 ||

tasya bhaktyā yathāpūrvaṃ prasādaṃ kṛtavānasi |
tathā mamāpi tatsarvaṃ dātumarhasi śaṃkara || 33 ||

iti vijñāpitastena bhagavān bhaganetrahā |
nyāyena vai dadau sarvaṃ tasyāpi sa ghṛṇānidhiḥ || 34 ||

labdhvaivamīśvarādeva brahmā sarvātmatāṃ kṣaṇāt |
tvaramāṇotha saṃgamya dadarśa puruṣottamam || 35 ||

kṣīrārṇavālaye śubhre vimāne sūryasaṃnibhe |
hemaratnānvite divye manasā tena nirmite || 36 ||

anantabhogaśayyāyāṃ śayānaṃ paṃkajekṣaṇam |
caturbhujamudārāṃgaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 37 ||

śaṃkhacakradharaṃ saumyaṃ candrabiṃbasamānanam |
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ prasannamadhurasmitam || 38 ||

dharāmṛdukarāṃbhojasparśaraktapadāṃbujam |
kṣīrārṇavāmṛtamiva śayānaṃ yoganidrayā || 39 ||

tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṃḍajam |
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram || 40 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ brahmā pragalbhamidamabravīt |
grasāmi tvāmahaṃ viṣṇo tvamātmānaṃ yathā purā || 41 ||

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratibuddhya pitāmaham |
udaikṣata mahābāhussmitamīṣaccakāra ca || 42 ||

tasminnavasare viṣṇurgrastastena mahātmanā |
sṛṣṭaśca brahmaṇā sadyo bhruvormadhyādayatnataḥ || 43 ||

tasminnavasare sākṣādbhagavānindubhūṣaṇaḥ |
śaktiṃ tayorapi draṣṭumarūpo rūpamāsthitaḥ || 44 ||

prasādamatulaṃ kartuṃ purā dattavarastayoḥ |
āgacchattatra yatremau brahmanārāyaṇau sthitau || 45 ||

atha tuṣṭuvaturdevaṃ prītau bhītau ca kautukāt |
praṇematuśca bahuśo bahumānena dūrataḥ || 46 ||

bhavopi bhagavānetāvanugṛhya pinākadhṛk |
sādaraṃ paśyatoreva tayorantaradhīyata || 47 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe brahmaviṣṇusṛṣṭikathanaṃ nāma trayodaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 13 ||

vāyuruvāca |

pratikalpaṃ pravakṣyāmi rudrāvirbhāvakāraṇam |
yato vicchinnasaṃtānā brahmasṛṣṭiḥ pravartate || 1 ||

kalpekalpe prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā brahmā brahmāṃḍasaṃbhavaḥ |
avṛddhihetorbhūtānāṃ mumoha bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ || 2 ||

tasya duḥkhapraśāntyarthaṃ prajānāṃ ca vivṛddhaye |
tattatkalpeṣu kālātmā rudro rudragaṇādhipaḥ || 3 ||

nirdiṣṭaḥ pamameśena maheśo nīlalohitaḥ |
putro bhūtvānugṛhṇāti brahmāṇaṃ brahmaṇonujaḥ || 4 ||

sa eva bhagavānīśastejorāśiranāmayaḥ |
anādinidhanodhātā bhūtasaṃkocako vibhuḥ || 5 ||

paramaiśvaryasaṃyuktaḥ parameśvarabhāvitaḥ |
tacchaktyādhiṣṭhitaśśaśvattaccihnairapi cihnitaḥ || 6 ||

tannāmanāmā tadrūpastatkāryakaraṇakṣamaḥ |
tattulyavyavahāraśca tadājñāparipālakaḥ || 7 ||

sahasrādityasaṃkāśaścandrāvayavabhūṣaṇaḥ |
bhujaṃgahārakeyūravalayo muṃjamekhalaḥ || 8 ||

jalaṃdharaviriṃcendrakapālaśakalojjvalaḥ |
gaGgātuṃgataraṃgārddhapiṃgalānanamūrddhajaḥ || 9 ||

bhagnadaṃṣṭrāṃkurākrāntaprāntakāntadharādharaḥ |
savyaśravaṇapārśvāntamaṃḍalīkṛtakuṇḍalaḥ || 10 ||

mahāvṛṣabhaniryāṇo mahājaladaniḥsvanaḥ |
mahānalasamaprakhyo mahābalaparākramaḥ || 11 ||

evaṃ ghoramahārūpo brahmaputrīṃ maheśvaraḥ |
vijñānaṃ brahmaṇe dattvā sarge sahakaroti ca || 12 ||

tasmādrudraprasādena pratikalpaṃ prajāpateḥ |
pravāharūpato nityā prajāsṛṣṭiḥ pravartate || 13 ||

kadācitprārthitaḥ sraṣṭuṃ brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ |
svātmanā sadṛśān sarvān sasarja manasā vibhuḥ || 14 ||

kaparddino nirātaṃkānnīlagrīvĀstrilocanān |
jarāmaraṇanirmuktān dīptaśūlavarāyudhān || 15 ||

taistu saṃcchāditaṃ sarvaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ jagat |
tāndṛṣṭā vividhānrudrān rudramāha pitāmahaḥ || 16 ||

namaste devadeveśa māsrākṣīrīdṛśīḥ prajāḥ |
anyāḥ sṛja tvaṃ bhadraṃ te prajā mṛtyusamanvitāḥ || 17 ||

ityuktaḥ prahasanprāha brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ |
nāsti me tādṛśassargassṛja tvamaśubhāḥ prajāḥ || 18 ||

ye tvime manasā sṛṣṭā mahātmāno mahābalāḥ |
cariṣyanti mayā sārddhaṃ sarva eva hi yājñikāḥ || 19 ||

ityuktvā viśvakarmāṇaṃ viśvabhūteśvaro haraḥ |
saha rudraiḥ prajāsargānnivṛttātmā vyatiṣṭhata || 20 ||

tataḥ prabhṛti devo .asau na prasūte prajāḥ śubhāḥ |
ūrddhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuryāvadābhūtasaṃplavam || 21 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe rudrāvirbhāvavarṇanaṃ nāma caturdaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 14 ||

vāyuruvāca |

yadā punaḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭā na vyavarddhanta vedhasaḥ |
tadā maithunajāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ brahmā kartumamanyata || 1 ||

na nirgataṃ purā yasmānnārīṇāṃ kulamīśvarāt |
tena maithunajāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ na śaśāka pitāmahaḥ || 2 ||

tatassa vidadhe buddhimarthaniścayagāminīm |
prajānameva vṛddhyarthaṃ praṣṭavyaḥ parameśvara || 3 ||

prasādena vinā tasya na varddherannimāḥ prajāḥ |
evaṃ saṃcintya viśvātmā tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame || 4 ||

tadādyā paramā śaktiranantā lokabhāvinī |
ādyā sūkṣmatarā śuddhā bhāvagamyā manoharā || 5 ||

nirguṇā niṣprapaṃcā ca niṣkalā nirupaplavā |
nirantaratarā nityā nityamīśvarapārśvagā || 6 ||

tayā paramayā śaktyā bhagavantaṃ triyambakam |
saṃcintya hṛdaye brahmā tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ || 7 ||

tīvreṇa tapasā tasya yuktasya parameṣṭhinaḥ |
acireṇaiva kālena pitā saṃpratutoṣa ha || 8 ||

tataḥ kenacidaṃśena mūrtimāviśya kāmapi |
arddhanārīśvaro bhūtvā yayau devassvayaṃ haraḥ || 9 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaṃ devaṃ tamasaḥ paramavyayam |
advitīyamanirdeśyamadṛśyamakṛtātmabhiḥ || 10 ||

sarvalokavidhātāraṃ sarvalokeśvareśvaram |
sarvalokavidhāyinyā śaktyā paramayā yutam || 11 ||

apratarkyamanābhāsamameyamajaraṃ dhruvam |
acalaṃ nirguṇaṃ śāntamanantamahimāspadam || 12 ||

sarvagaṃ sarvadaṃ sarvasadasadvyaktivarjitam |
sarvopamānanirmuktaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śāśvataṃ śivam || 13 ||

praṇamya daṃḍavadbrahmā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ |
śraddhāvinayasaṃpannaiḥ śrāvyaiḥ saṃskarasaṃyutaiḥ || 14 ||

yathārthayuktasarvārthairvedārthaparibṛṃhitaiḥ |
tuṣṭāva devaṃ devīṃ ca sūktaiḥ sūkṣmārthagocaraiḥ || 15 ||

brahmovāca |

jaya deva mahādeva jayeśvara maheśvara |
jaya sarvaguṇa śreṣṭha jaya sarvasurādhipa || 16 ||

jaya prakṛti kalyāṇi jaya prakṛtināyike |
jaya prakṛtidūre tvaṃ jaya prakṛtisundari || 17 ||

jayāmoghamahāmāya jayāmogha manoratha |
jayāmoghamahālīla jayāmoghamahābala || 18 ||

jaya viśvajaganmātarjaya viśvajaganmaye |
jaya viśvajagaddhātri jaya viśvajagatsakhi || 19 ||

jaya śāśvatikaiśvarye jaya śāśvatikālaya |
jaya śāśvatikākāra jaya śāśvatikānuga || 20 ||

jayātmatrayanirmātri jayātmatrayapālini |
jayātmatrayasaṃhartri jayātmatrayanāyike || 21 ||

jayāvalokanāyattajagatkāraṇabṛṃhaṇa |
jayopekṣākaṭākṣotthahutabhugbhuktabhautika || 22 ||

jaya devādyavijñeye svātmasūkṣmadṛśojjvale |
jaya sthūlātmaśaktyeśejaya vyāptacarācare || 23 ||

jaya nāmaikavinyastaviśvatattvasamuccaya |
jayāsuraśironiṣṭhaśreṣṭhānugakadaṃbaka || 24 ||

jayopāśritasaṃrakṣāsaṃvidhānapaṭīyasi |
jayonmūlitasaṃsāraviṣavṛkṣāṃkurodgame || 25 ||

jaya prādeśikaiśvaryavīryaśauryavijṛṃbhaṇa |
jaya viśvabahirbhūta nirastaparavaibhava || 26 ||

jaya praṇītapaṃcārthaprayogaparamāmṛta |
jaya paṃcārthavijñānasudhāstotrasvarūpiṇi || 27 ||

jayati ghorasaṃsāramahārogabhiṣagvara |
jayānādimalājñānatamaḥpaṭalacandrike || 28 ||

jaya tripurakālāgne jaya tripurabhairavi |
jaya triguṇanirmukte jaya triguṇamardini || 29 ||

jaya prathamasarvajña jaya sarvaprabodhika |
jaya pracuradivyāṃga jaya prārthitadāyini || 30 ||

kva deva te paraṃ dhāma kva ca tucchaṃ ca no vacaḥ |
tathāpi bhagavan bhaktyā pralapantaṃ kṣamasva mām || 31 ||

vijñāpyaivaṃvidhaiḥ sūktairviśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ |
namaścakāra rudrāya radrāṇyai ca muhurmuhuḥ || 32 ||

idaṃ stotravaraṃ puṇyaṃ brahmaṇā samudīritam |
arddhanārīśvaraṃ nāma śivayorharṣavarddhanam || 33 ||

ya idaṃ kīrttayedbhaktyā yasya kasyāpi śikṣayā |
sa tatphalamavāpnoti śivayoḥ prītikāraṇāt || 34 ||

sakalabhuvanabhūtabhāvanābhyāṃ jananavināśavihīnavigrahābhyām |
naravarayuvatīvapurddharābhyāṃ satatamahaṃ praṇatosmi śaṃkarābhyām || 35 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pū.. śivaśivāstutivarṇanaṃ nāma paṃcadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 15 ||

vāyuruvāca |

atha devo mahādevo mahājaladanādayā |
vācā madhuragaṃbhīraśivadaślakṣṇavarṇayā || 1 ||

arthasaṃpannapadayā rājalakṣaṇayuktayā |
aśeṣaviṣayāraṃbharakṣāvimaladakṣayā || 2 ||

manoharatarodāramadhurasmitapūrvayā |
saṃbabhāṣe susaṃpīto viśvakarmāṇamīśvaraḥ || 3 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsa vatsa mahābhāga mama putra pitāmaha |
jñātameva mayā sarvaṃ tava vākyasya gauravam || 4 ||

prajānāmeva bṛddhyarthaṃ tapastaptaṃ tvayādhunā |
tapasā .anena tuṣṭosmi dadāmi ca tavepsitam || 5 ||

ityuktvā paramodāraṃ svabhāvamadhuraṃ vacaḥ |
sasarja vapuṣo bhāgāddevīṃ devavaro haraḥ || 6 ||

yāmāhurbrahmavidvāṃso devīṃ divyaguṇānvitām |
parasya paramāṃ śaktiṃ bhavasya paramātmanaḥ || 7 ||

yasyāṃ na khalu vidyante janma mṛtyujarādayaḥ |
yā bhavānī bhavasyāṃgātsamāvirabhavatkila || 8 ||

yasyā vāco nivartante manasā cendriyaiḥ saha |
sā bharturvapuṣo bhāgājjāteva samadṛśyata || 9 ||

yā sā jagadidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ mahimnā vyāpya tiṣṭhati |
śarīriṇīva sa devī vicitraṃ samalakṣyata || 10 ||

sarvaṃ jagadidaṃ caiṣā saṃmohayati māyayā |
īśvarātsaiva jātābhūdajātā paramārthataḥ || 11 ||

na yasyā paramo bhāvaḥ surāṇāmapi gocaraḥ |
viśvāmareśvarī caiva vibhaktā bharturaṃgataḥ || 12 ||

tāṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānīṃ sarvalokamaheśvarīm |
sarvajñāṃ sarvagāṃ sūkṣmāṃ sadasadvyaktivarjitām || 13 ||

paramāṃ nikhilaṃ bhāsā bhāsayantīmidaṃ jagat |
praṇipatya mahādevīṃ prārthayāmāsa vai virāṭ || 14 ||

brahmovāca |

devi devena sṛṣṭo .ahamādau sarvajaganmayi |
prajāsarge niyuktaśca sṛjāmi sakalaṃ jagat || 15 ||

manasā nirmitāḥ sarve devi devādayo mayā |
na vṛddhimupagacchanti sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ || 16 ||

mithunaprabhavāmeva kṛtvā sṛṣṭimataḥ param |
saṃvardhayitumicchāmi sarvā eva mama prajāḥ || 17 ||

na nirgataṃ purā tvatto nārīṇāṃ kulamavyayam |
tena nārīkulaṃ sraṣṭuṃ śaktirmama na vidyate || 18 ||

sarvāsāmeva śaktīnāṃ tvattaḥ khalu samudbhavaḥ |
tasmātsarvatra sarveṣāṃ sarvaśaktipradāyinīm || 19 ||

tvāmeva varadāṃ māyāṃ prārthayāmi sureśvarīm |
carācaravivṛddhyarthamaṃśenaikena sarvage || 20 ||

dakṣasya mama putrasya putrī bhava bhavārdini |
evaṃ sā yācitā devī brahmaṇā brahmayoninā || 21 ||

śaktimekāṃ bhruvormadhyātsasarjātmasamaprabhām |
tāmāha prahasanprekṣya devadevavaro haraḥ || 22 ||

brahmāṇaṃ tapasārādhya kuru tasya yathepsitam |
tāmājñāṃ parameśasya śirasā pratigṛhya sā || 23 ||

brahmaṇo vacanāddevī dakṣasya duhitābhavat |
dattvaivamatulāṃ śaktiṃ brahmaṇe brahmarūpiṇīm || 24 ||

viveśa dehaṃ devasya devaścāntaradhīyata |
tadā prabhṛti loke .asmin striyāṃ bhogaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ || 25 ||

prajāsṛṣṭiśca viprendrā maithunena pravartate |
brahmāpi prāpa sānandaṃ santoṣaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 26 ||

etadvassarvamākhyātaṃ devyāḥ śaktisamudbhavam |
puṇyavṛddhikaraṃ śrāvyaṃ bhūtasargānupaṃgataḥ || 27 ||

ya idaṃ kīrtayennityaṃ devyāḥ śaktisamudbhavam |
puṇyaṃ sarvamavāpnoti putrāṃśca labhate śubhān || 28 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe devīśaktyudbhavo nāma ṣoḍaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 16 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evaṃ labdhvā parāṃ śaktimīśvarādeva śāśvatīm |
maithunaprabhavāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ kartṛkāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ || 1 ||

svayamapyadbhuto nārī cārddhena puruṣo .abhavat |
yārddhena nārī sā tasmācchatarūpā vyajāyata || 2 ||

virājamasṛjadbrahmā so .arddhana puruṣo .abhavat |
sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvaṃ puruṣo manurucyate || 3 ||

sā devī śatarūpā tu tapaḥ kṛtvā suduścaram |
bharttāraṃ dīptayaśasaṃ manumevānvapadyata || 4 ||

tasmāttu śatarūpā sā putradvayamasūyata |
priyavratottānapādau putrau putravatāṃ varau || 5 ||

kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyāṃ jātāstvimāḥ prajāḥ |
ākūtirekā vijñeyā prasūtiraparā smṛtā || 6 ||

svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtiṃ ca dadau dakṣāya tāṃ prabhuḥ |
ruceḥ prajāpatiścaiva cākūtiṃ samapādayat / || 7 ||

ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham |
yajñaśca dakṣiṇā caiva yābhyāṃ saṃvartitaṃ jagat || 8 ||

svāyaṃbhuvasutāyāṃ tu prasūtyāṃ lokamātaraḥ |
catasro viṃśatiḥ kanyā dakṣastvajanayatprabhuḥ || 9 ||

śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtiḥ puṣṭistuṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā |
buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāntissiddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśī || 10 ||

patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ |
tābhyaḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ || 11 ||

khyātiḥ satyarthasaṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā |
sannatiścānasūyā ca ūrjjā svāhā svadhā tathā || 12 ||

bhṛguśśarvo marīciśca aṃgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ |
pulastyo .atrirviśiṣṭhaśca pāvakaḥ pitarastathā || 13 ||

khyātyādyā jagṛhuḥ kanyāmunayo munisattamāḥ |
kāmādyāstu yaśontā ye te trayodaśa sūnavaḥ || 14 ||

dharmasya jajñire tāstu śraddhādyāssusukhottarāḥ |
duḥkhottarāśca hiṃsāyāmadharmasya ca saṃtatau || 15 ||

nikṛtyādaya utpannāḥputrāśca dharmalakṣaṇāḥ |
naiṣāṃ bhāryāśca putrā vā sarve tvaniyamāḥ smṛtāḥ || 16 ||

sa eṣa tāmasassargo jajñe dharmaniyāmakaḥ |
yā sā dakṣasya duhitā rudrasya dayitā satī || 17 ||

bhartṛnindāprasaṃgena tyaktvā dākṣāyiṇīṃ tanum |
dakṣaṃ ca dakṣabhāryyāṃ ca vinindya saha bandhubhiḥ || 18 ||

sā menāyāmāvirabhūtputrī himavato gireḥ |
rudrastu tāṃ satīṃ dṛṣṭvā rudrāṃstvātmasamaprabhān || 19 ||

yathāsṛjadasaṃkhyātāṃstathā kathitameva ca |
bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṃ samutpannā lakṣmīrnārāyaṇapriyā || 20 ||

devau dhātṛvidhātārau manvantaravidhāriṇau |
tayorvai putrapautrādyāśśataśo .atha sahasraśaḥ || 21 ||

svāyaṃbhuve .antare nītāḥ sarve te bhārgavā matāḥ |
marīcerapi saṃbhūtiḥ paurṇamāsamasūyata || 22 ||

kanyācatuṣṭayaṃ caiva mahīyāṃsastadanvayāḥ |
yeṣāṃ vaṃśe samutpanno bahuputrasya kaśyapaḥ || 23 ||

smṛtiścāṃgirasaḥ patnī janayāmāsa vai sutau |
āgnīdhraṃ śarabhañcaiva tathā kanyācatuṣṭayam || 24 ||

tadīyāḥ putrapautrāśca yetītāste sahasraśaḥ |
prītyāṃ pulastyabhāryāyāṃ dantognirabhavatsutaḥ |
pūrvajanmani yogastyassmṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuve .antare // 25 || 25 ||

tatsaṃtatīyā bahavaḥ paulastyā iti viśrutāḥ |
kṣamā tu suṣuve putrānpulahasya prajāpateḥ || 26 ||

kardamaśca suriścaiva sahiṣṇuśceti te trayaḥ |
tretāgnivarcasassarve yeṣāṃ vaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ || 27 ||

kratoḥ kratusamānbhāryā sannatissuṣuve sutān |
naiṣāṃ bhāryāśca putrāśca sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ || 28 ||

ṣaṣṭistāni sahasrāṇi vālakhilyā iti smṛtāḥ |
anūroragrato yānti parivāryya divākaram || 29 ||

atrerbhāryānusūyā ca pañcātreyānasūyata |
kanyakāṃ ca śrutiṃ nāma mātā śaṃkhapadasya ca || 30 ||

satyanetraśca havyaśca āpomūrtiśśanaiścaraḥ |
somaśca paṃcamastvete paṃcātreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 31 ||

teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca hyātreyāṇāṃ mahātmanām |
svāyaṃbhuve .antare .atītāḥ śataśo .atha sahasraśaḥ || 32 ||

ūrjāyāṃ tu vasiṣṭhasya putrā vai sapta jajñire |
jyāyasī ca svasā teṣāṃ puṃḍarīkā sumadhyamā || 33 ||

rajo gātrorddhvabāhū ca savanaścānayaśca yaḥ |
sutapāśśukra ityete sapta saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ || 34 ||

gotrāṇi nāmabhisteṣāṃ vāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām |
svāyaṃbhuve .antare .atītānyarbudāni śatāni ca || 35 ||

ityeṣa ṛṣisargastu sānubandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
samāsādvistarādvaktumaśakyo .ayamiti dvijāḥ || 36 ||

yo .asau rudrātmako bahnibrahmaṇo mānasassutaḥ |
svāhā tasya priyā lebhe putrāṃstrīnamitaujasaḥ || 37 ||

pāvakaḥ pavamānaśca śucirityeṣa te trayaḥ |
nirmanthyaḥ pavamānassyādvaidyutaḥ pāvakassmṛtaḥ || 38 ||

sūrye tapati yaścāsau śuciḥ saura udāhṛtaḥ |
havyavāhaḥ kavyavāhaḥ saharakṣā iti trayaḥ || 39 ||

trayāṇāṃ kramaśaḥ putrā devapitṛsurāśca te |
eteṣāṃ putrapautrāśca catvāriṃśannavaiva te || 40 ||

kāmyanaimittikājasrakarmasu triṣu saṃsthitāḥ |
sarve tapasvino jñeyāḥ sarve vratabhṛtastathā || 41 ||

sarve rudrātmakaścaiva sarve rudraparāyaṇāḥ |
tasmādagnimukhe yattaddhutaṃ syādeva kenacit || 42 ||

tatsarvaṃ rudramuddiśya dattaṃ syānnātra saṃśayaḥ |
ityevaṃ niścayognīnāmanukrānto yathātatham || 43 ||

nātivistarato viprāḥ pitR̥nvakṣyāmyataḥ param |
yasmātṣaḍṛtavasteṣāṃ sthānaṃ sthānābhimāninām || 44 ||

ṛtavaḥ pitarastasmādityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ |
yuṣmādṛtuṣu sarve hi jāyante sthāsnujaṃgamā || 45 ||

tasmādete pitara ārtavā iti ca śrutam |
evaṃ pitR̥ṇāmeteṣāmṛtukālābhimāninām || 46 ||

ātmaiśvaryā mahātmānastiṣṭhantīhābbhrasaṃgamāt |
āgniṣvāttā barhiṣadaḥ pitaro dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ || 47 ||

ayajvānaśca yajvānaḥ kramātte mṛhamedhinaḥ |
svadhāsūta pitṛbhyaśca dve kanye lokaviśrute || 48 ||

menāṃ ca dharaṇīṃ caiva yābhyāṃ viśvamidaṃ dhṛtam |
agniṣvāttasutā menā dharaṇī barhiṣatsutā || 49 ||

menā himavataḥ patnī mainākaṃ krauṃcameva ca |
gaurīṃ gaṃgāṃ ca suṣuve bhavāṃgāśleṣapāvanīm || 50 ||

merostu dharaṇī patnī divyauṣadhisamanvitam |
mandaraṃ suṣuve putraṃ citrisundarakandharam || 51 ||

sa eva mandaraḥ śrīmānmeruputrastapobalāt |
sākṣācchrīkaṃṭhanāthasya śivasyāvasathaṃ gataḥ || 52 ||

sāsūtā dharaṇī bhūyastriṃśatkanyāśca viśrutāḥ |
velāṃ ca niyatiṃ caiva tṛtīyāmapi cāyatim || 53 ||

āyatirniyatiścaiva patnyau dve bhṛguputrayoḥ |
svāyaṃbhuve .antare pūrvaṃ kathitaste tadanvayaḥ || 54 ||

suṣuve sāgarādvelā kanyāmekāmaninditām |
savarṇāṃ nāma sāmudrīṃ patnīṃ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ || 55 ||

sāmudrī suṣuve putrāndaśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ |
sarve prācetasā nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ || 56 ||

yeṣāṃ svāyaṃbhuve dakṣaḥ putratvamagamatpurā |
triyambakasya śāpena cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ || 57 ||

ityete brahmaputrāṇāṃ dharmādīnāmmahātmanām |
nātisaṃkṣepato viprā nāti vistarataḥ kramāt || 58 ||

varṇitā vai mayā vaṃśā divyā devagaṇānvitāḥ |
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharddhibhiralaṃkṛtāḥ || 59 ||

prajānāṃ saṃniveśo .ayaṃ prajāpatisamudbhavaḥ |
na hi śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātuṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi || 60 ||

rājñāmapi ca yo vaṃśo dvidhā so .api pravartate |
sūryavaṃśassomavaṃśa iti puṇyatamaḥ kṣitau || 61 ||

ikṣvākurambarīṣaśca yayātirnāhuṣādayaḥ |
