puṇyaślokāḥ śrutā ye .atra te pi tadvaṃśasaṃbhavāḥ || 62 ||

anye ca rājaṛṣayo nānāvīryasamanvitā |
kiṃ taiḥ phalamanutkrāntairuktapūrvaiḥ purātanaiḥ || 63 ||

kiṃ ceśvarakathā vṛttā yatra tatrānyakīrtanam |
na sadbhiḥ saṃmataṃ matvā notsahe bahubhāṣitum || 64 ||

prasaṃgādīśvarasyaiva prabhāvadyotanādapi |
sargādayo .api kathitā ityatra tatpravistaraiḥ || 65 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe sṛṣṭikathanaṃ nāma saptadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 17 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

devī dakṣasya tanayā tyaktvā dākṣāyaṇī tanum |
kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī menāyāmabhavatpurā || 1 ||

kathaṃ ca nindito rudro dakṣeṇa ca mahātmanā |
nimittamapi kiṃ tatra yena syānnindito bhavaḥ || 2 ||

utpannaśca kathaṃ dakṣo abhiśāpādbhavasya tu |
cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvaṃ manoḥ prabrūhi māruta || 3 ||

vāyuruvāva

śṛṇvantu kathayiṣyāmi dakṣasya laghucetasaḥ |
vṛttaṃ pāpātpramādācca viśvāmaravidūṣaṇam || 4 ||

purā surāsurāḥ sarve siddhāśca paramarṣayaḥ |
kadāciddraṣṭumīśānaṃ himavacchikharaṃ yayuḥ || 5 ||

tadā devaśca devī ca divyāsanagatāvubhau |
darśanaṃ dadatusteṣāṃ devādīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ || 6 ||

tadānīmeva dakṣo .api gatastatra sahāmaraiḥ |
jāmātaraṃ haraṃ draṣṭuṃ draṣṭuṃ cātmasutāṃ satīm || 7 ||

tadātmagauravāddevo devyā dakṣe samāgate |
devādibhyo viśeṣeṇa na kadācidabhūtsmṛtiḥ || 8 ||

tasya tasyāḥ paraṃ bhāvamajñātuścāpi kevalam |
putrītyevaṃ vimūḍhasya tasyāṃ vairamajāyata || 9 ||

tatastenaiva vaireṇa vidhinā ca pracoditaḥ |
nājuvāha bhavaṃ dakṣo dīkṣitastāmapi dviṣan || 10 ||

anyāñjāmātarassarvānāhūya sa yathākramam |
śataśaḥ puṣkalāmarcāñcakāra ca pṛthakpṛthak || 11 ||

tathā tānsaṃgatāñchrutvā nāradasya mukhāttadā |
yayau rudrāya rudrāṇī vijñāpya bhavanaṃ pituḥ || 12 ||

atha saṃnihitaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ viśvatomukham |
lakṣaṇāḍhyaṃ sukhārohamatimātramanoharam || 13 ||

taptajāṃbūnadaprakhyaṃ citraratnapariṣkṛtam |
muktāmayavitānāgnyaṃ sragdāmasamalaṃkṛtam || 14 ||

taptakaṃcananirvyūhaṃ ratnastaṃbhaśatāvṛtam |
vajrakalpitasopānaṃ vidrumastaṃbhatoraṇam || 15 ||

puṣpapaṭṭaparistīrṇaṃ citraratnamahāsanam |
vajrajālakiracchidramacchidramaṇikuṭṭimam || 16 ||

maṇidaṃḍamanojñena mahāvṛṣabhalakṣmaṇā |
alaṃkṛtapurobhāgamabbhraśubbhreṇa ketunā || 17 ||

ratnakaṃcukaguptāṃgaiścitravetrakapāṇibhiḥ |
adhiṣṭhitamahādvāramapradhṛṣyairguṇeśvaraiḥ || 18 ||

mṛdaṃgatālagītādiveṇuvīṇāviśāradaiḥ |
vidagdhaveṣabhāṣaiśca bahubhiḥ strījanairvṛtam || 19 ||

āruroha mahādevī saha priyasakhījanaiḥ |
cāmāravyañjanaṃ tasyā vajradaṃḍamanohare || 20 ||

gṛhītvā rudrakanye dve vivījaturubhe śubhe |
tadācāmarayormadhye devyā vadanamābabhau || 21 ||

anyonyaṃ yudhyatormadhye haṃsayoriva paṃkajam |
chatraṃ śaśinibhaṃ tasyāścūḍopari sumālinī || 22 ||

dhṛtamuktāparikṣiptaṃ babhāra premanirbharā |
tacchatramujjvalaṃ devyā ruruce vadanopari || 23 ||

uparyamṛtabhāṃḍasya maṃḍalaṃ śaśino yathā |
atha cāgre samāsīnā susmitāsyā śubhāvatī || 24 ||

akṣadyūtavinodena ramayāmāsa vai satīm |
suyaśāḥ pāduke devyāśśubhe ratnapariṣkṛte || 25 ||

stanayorantare kṛtvā tadā devīmasevataḥ |
anyā kāṃcanacārvaṃgī dīptaṃ jagrāha darpaṇam || 26 ||

aparā tālavṛntaṃ ca parā tāṃbūlapeṭikām |
kācitkrīḍāśukaṃ cāru kare .akuruta bhāminī || 27 ||

kācittu sumanojñāni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca |
kācidābharaṇādhāraṃ babhāra kamalekṣaṇā || 28 ||

kācicca punarālepaṃ suprasūtaṃ śubhāṃjanam |
anyāśca sadṛśāstāstā yathāsvamucitakriyāḥ || 29 ||

āvṛttyā tāṃ mahādevīmasevanta samantataḥ |
atīva śuśubhe tāsāmantare parameśvarī || 30 ||

tārāpariṣado madhye candralekheva śāradī |
tataḥ śaṃkhasamutthasya nādasya samanantaram || 31 ||

prāsthāniko mahānādaḥ paṭahaḥ samatāḍyata |
tato madhuravādyāni saha tālodyataissvanaiḥ || 32 ||

anāhatāni sanneduḥ kāhalānāṃ śatāni ca |
sāyudhānāṃ gaṇeśānāṃ maheśasamatejasām || 33 ||

sahasrāṇi śatānyaṣṭau tadānīṃ purato yayuḥ |
teṣāṃ madhye vṛṣārūḍho gajārūḍho yathā guruḥ || 34 ||

jagāma gaṇapaḥ śrīmān somanandīśvarārcitaḥ |
devadundubhayo nedurdivi divyasukhā ghanāḥ || 35 ||

nanṛturmunayassarve mumuduḥ siddhayoginaḥ |
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca vitānopari vāridāḥ || 36 ||

tadā devagaṇaiścānyaiḥ pathi sarvatra saṃgatā |
kṣaṇādiva piturgehaṃ praviveśa maheśvarī || 37 ||

tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kupito dakṣaścātmanaḥ kṣayakāraṇāt |
tasyā yavīyasībhyo .api cakre pūjāma satkṛtām || 38 ||

tadā śaśimukhī devī pitaraṃ sadasi sthitam |
aṃbikā yuktamavyagramuvācākṛpaṇaṃ vacaḥ || 39 ||

devyuvāca |

brahmādayaḥ piśācāntā yasyājñāvaśavartinaḥ |
sa devassāṃprataṃ tāta vidhinā nārcitaḥ kila || 40 ||

tadāstāṃ mama jyāyasyāḥ putryāḥ pūjāṃ kimīdṛśīm |
asatkṛtāmavajñāya kṛtavānasi garhitam || 41 ||

evamukto .abravīdenāṃ dakṣaḥ krodhādamarṣitaḥ |
tvattaḥ śreṣṭhā viśiṣṭāśca pūjyā bālāḥ sutā mama || 42 ||

tāsāṃ tu ye ca bharttāraste me bahumatā mudā |
gunaiścāpyadhikāssarvairbhartuste tryaṃbakādapi || 43 ||

stabdhātmā tāmasaśśarvastvamimaṃ samupāśritā |
tena tvāmavamanye .ahaṃ pratikūlo hi me bhavaḥ || 44 ||

tathoktā pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ kruddhā devī tamabravīt |
śṛṇvatāmeva sarveṣāṃ ye yajñasadasi sthitāḥ || 45 ||

akasmānmama bhartāramajātāśeṣadūṣaṇam |
vācā dūṣayase dakṣa sākṣāllokamaheśvaram || 46 ||

vidyācauro gurudrohī vedeśvaravidūṣakaḥ |
ta ete bahupāpmānassarve daṃḍyā iti śrutiḥ || 47 ||

tasmādatyutkaṭasyāsya pāpasya sadṛśo bhṛśam |
sahasā dāruṇo daṃḍastava daivādbhaviṣyati || 48 ||

tvayā na pūjito yasmāddevadevastriyaṃbakaḥ |
tasmāttava kulaṃ duṣṭaṃ naṣṭamityavadhāraya || 49 ||

ityuktvā pitaraṃ ruṣṭā satī saṃtyaktasādhvasā |
tadīyāṃ ca tanuṃ tyaktvā himavantaṃ yayau girim || 50 ||

sa parvataparaḥ śrīmĀllabdhapuṇyaphalodayaḥ |
tadarthameva kṛtavān suciraṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ || 51 ||

tasmāttamanugṛhṇāti bhūdhareśvaramīśvarī |
svecchayā pitaraṃ cakre svātmano yogamāyayā || 52 ||

yadā gatā satī dakṣaṃ vinindya bhayavihvalā |
tadā tirohitā mantrā vihataśca tato .adhvaraḥ || 53 ||

tadupaśrutya gamanaṃ devyāstripurumardanaḥ |
dakṣāya ca ṛṣibhyaśca cukopa ca śaśāpa tān || 54 ||

yasmādavamatā dakṣamatkṛte .anāgasā satī |
pūjitāścetarāḥ sarvāḥ svasutā bhartṛbhiḥ saha || 55 ||

vaivasvate .antare tasmāttava jāmātarastvamī |
utpatsyante samaṃ sarve brahmayajñeṣvayonijāḥ || 56 ||

bhavitā mānuṣo rājā cākṣuṣasya tvamanvaye |
prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraścāpi pracetasaḥ || 57 ||

ahaṃ tatrāpi te vighnamācariṣyāmi durmate |
dharmārthakāmayukteṣu karmasvapi punaḥ punaḥ || 58 ||

tenaivaṃ vyāhṛto dakṣo rudreṇāmitatejasā |
svāyaṃbhuvīṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā papāta bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ || 59 ||

tataḥ prācetaso dakṣo jajñe vai cākṣuṣe .antare |
prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraścaiva pracetasām || 60 ||

bhṛgvādayo .api jātā vai manorvaivasvatasya tu |
antare brahmaṇo yajñe vāruṇīṃ bibhratastanum || 61 ||

tadā dakṣasya dharmārthaṃ yajñe tasya durātmanaḥ |
maheśaḥ kṛtavānvighnaṃ manā vavasvate sati || 62 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe satīdehatyāgo nāmāṣṭādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 18 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kathaṃ dakṣasya dharmārthaṃ pravṛttasya durātmanaḥ |
maheśaḥ kṛtavān vighnametadicchāma veditum || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

viśvasya jagato māturapi devyāstapobalāt |
pitṛbhāvamupāgamya mudite himavadgirau || 2 ||

deve .api tatkṛtodvāhe himavacchikharālaye |
saṃkīḍati tayā sārddhaṃ kāle bahutare gate || 3 ||

vaivasvate .antare prāpte dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ svayam |
aśvamedhena yajñena yakṣyamāṇo .anvapadyata || 4 ||

tato himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe dakṣo vai yajñamāharat |
gaṃgādvāre śubhe deśe ṛṣisiddhaniṣevite || 5 ||

tasya tasminmakhedevāḥ sarve śakra purogamāḥ |
gamanāya samāgamya buddhimāpedire tadā || 6 ||

ādityā vasavo rudrāssādhyāssaha marudgaṇaiḥ |
ūṣmapāḥ somapāścaiva ājyapā dhūmapāstathā || 7 ||

aśvinau pitaraścaiva tathā cānye maharṣayaḥ |
viṣṇunā sahitāḥ sarve svāgatā yajñabhāginaḥ || 8 ||

dṛṣṭvā devakulaṃ sarvamīśvareṇa vināgatam |
dadhīco manyunāviṣṭo dakṣamevamabhāṣata || 9 ||

dadhīca uvāca |

aprapūjye caiva pūjā pūjyānāṃ cāpya pūjane |
naraḥ pāpamavāpnoti mahadvai nātra saṃśayaḥ || 10 ||

asatāṃ saṃmatiryatra satāmavamatistathā |
daṃḍo devakṛtastatra sadyaḥ patati dāruṇaḥ || 11 ||

evamuktvā tu viprarṣiḥ punardakṣamabhāṣata |
pūjyaṃ tu paśubhartāraṃ kasmānnārcayase prabhum || 12 ||

dakṣa uvāca |

santi me bahavo rudrāḥ śūlahastāḥ kapardinaḥ |
ekādaśāvasthitā ye nānyaṃ vedmi maheśvaram || 13 ||

dadhīca uvāca |

kimebhiramarairanyaiḥ pūjitairadhvare phalam |
rājā cedadhvarasyāsya na rudraḥ pūjyate tvayā || 14 ||

brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ sraṣṭā yaḥ prabhuravyayaḥ |
brahmādayaḥ piśācāntā yasya kaiṃkaryavādinaḥ || 15 ||

prakṛtīnāṃ paraścaiva puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ |
cintyate yogavidvadbhi ṛṣibhistattvadarśibhiḥ || 16 ||

akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma hyasacca sadasacca yat |
anādimadhyanidhanamapratarkyaṃ sanātanam || 17 ||

yaḥ sraṣṭā caiva saṃhartā bhartā caiva maheśvaraḥ |
tasmādanyaṃ na paśyāmi śaṃkarātmānamadhvare || 18 ||

dakṣa uvāca |

etanmakheśasya suvarṇapātre haviḥ samastaṃ vidhimantrapūtam |
viṣṇornayāmyapratimasya bhāgaṃ prabhorvibhajyāvahanīyamadya || 19 ||

dadhīca uvāca |

yasmānnārādhito rudrassarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ |
tasmāddakṣa tavāśeṣo yajño .ayaṃ na bhaviṣyati || 20 ||

ityuktvā vacanaṃ kruddho dadhīco munisattamaḥ |
nirgamya ca tato deśājjagāma svakamāśramam || 21 ||

nirgate .api munau tasmindevā dakṣaṃ na tatyajuḥ |
avaśyamanubhāvitvādanarthasya tu bhāvinaḥ || 22 ||

etasminneva kāle tu jñātvaitatsarvamīśvarāt |
dagdhuṃ dakṣādhvaraṃ viprā devī devamacodayat || 23 ||

devyā saṃcodito devo dakṣādhvarajighāṃsayā |
sasarja sahasā vīraṃ vīrabhadraṃ gaṇeśvaram || 24 ||

sahasravadanaṃ devaṃ sahasrakamalekṣaṇam |
sahasramudgaradharaṃ sahasraśarapāṇikam || 25 ||

śūlaṭaṃkagadāhastaṃ dīptakārmukadhāriṇam |
cakravajradharaṃ ghoraṃ candrārddhakṛtaśekharam || 26 ||

kuliśodyotitakaraṃ taḍijjvalitamūrddhajam |
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ bibhrāṇaṃ mahāvaktraṃ mahodaram || 27 ||

vidyujjihvaṃ pralaṃboṣṭhaṃ meghasāgaraniḥsvanam |
vasānaṃ carma vaiyāghraṃ mahadrudhiranisravam || 28 ||

gaṇḍadvitayasaṃsṛṣṭamaṇḍalīkṛtakuṇḍalam |
varāmaraśiromālāvalīkalitaśekharam || 29 ||

raṇannūpurakeyūramahākanakabhūṣitam |
ratnasaṃcayasaṃdīptaṃ tārahārāvṛtorasam || 30 ||

mahāśarabhaśārdūlasiṃhaiḥ sadṛśavikramam |
praśastamattamātaṃgasamānagamanālasam || 31 ||

śaṃkhacāmarakundendumṛṇālasadṛśaprabham |
satuṣāramivādrīndraṃ sākṣājjaṃgamatāṃ gatam || 32 ||

jvālāmālāparikṣiptaṃ dīptamauktikabhūṣaṇam |
tejasā caiva dīvyantaṃ yugānta iva pāvakam || 33 ||

sa jānubhyāṃ mahīṃ gatvā praṇataḥ prāṃjalistataḥ |
pārśvato devadevasya paryyatiṣṭhadgaṇeśvaraḥ || 34 ||

manyunā cāsṛjadbhadrāṃ bhadrakālīṃ maheśvarīm |
ātmanaḥ karmasākṣitve tena gantuṃ sahaiva tu || 35 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvāvasthitaṃ vīrabhadraṃ kālāgnisannibham |
bhadrayā sahitaṃ prāha bhadramastviti śaṃkaraḥ || 36 ||

sa ca vijñāpayāmāsa saha devyā maheśvaram |
ājñāpaya mahādeva kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāṇyaham || 37 ||

tatastripurahā prāha haimavatyāḥ priyecchayā |
vīrabhadraṃ mahābāhuṃ vācā vipulanādayā || 38 ||

devadeva uvāca |

prācetasasya dakṣasya yajñaṃ sadyo vināśaya |
bhadrakālyā sahāsi tvametatkṛtyaṃ gaṇeśvara || 39 ||

ahamapyanayā sārddhaṃ raibhyāśramasapīpataḥ |
sthitvā vīkṣe gaṇeśāna vikramaṃ tava duḥsaham || 40 ||

vṛkṣā kanakhale ye tu gaṃgādvārasamīpagāḥ |
suvarṇaśṛṃgasya girermerumandarasaṃnibhāḥ || 41 ||

tasminpradeśe dakṣasya yujñaḥ saṃprati vartate |
sahasā tasya yajñasya vighātaṃ kuru mā ciram || 42 ||

ityukte sati devena devī himagirīndrajā |
bhadraṃ bhadraṃ ca saṃprekṣya vatsaṃ dhenurivaurasam || 43 ||

āliṃgya ca samāghrāya mūrdhni ṣaḍvadanaṃ yathā |
sasmitā vacanaṃ prāha madhuraṃ madhuraṃ svayam || 44 ||

devyuvāca |

vatsa bhadra mahābhāga mahābalaparākrama |
matpriyārthaṃ tvamutpanno mama manyuṃ pramārjaka || 45 ||

yajñeśvaramanāhūya yajñakarmarato .abhavat |
dakṣaṃ vaireṇa taṃ tasmādbhindhi yajñaṃ gaṇeśvara || 46 ||

yajñalakṣmīmalakṣmīṃ tvaṃ bhadra kṛtvā mamājñayā |
yajamānaṃ ca taṃ hatvā vatsa hiṃsaya bhadrayā || 47 ||

aśeṣāmiva tāmājñāṃ śivayościtrakṛtyayoḥ |
mūrdhni kṛtvā namaskṛtya bhadro gantuṃ pracakrame || 48 ||

athaiṣa bhagavānkruddhaḥ pretāvāsakṛtālayaḥ |
vīrabhadro mahādevo devyā manyupramārjakaḥ || 49 ||

sasarja romakūpebhyo romajākhyāngaṇeśvarān |
dakṣiṇādbhujadeśāttu śatakoṭigaviśvarān || 50 ||

pādāttathorudeśācca pṛṣṭhātpārśvānmukhādgalāt |
guhyādgulphācchiromadhyātkaṃṭhādāsyāttathodarāt || 51 ||

tadā gaṇeśvarairbhadrairbhadratulyaparākramaiḥ |
saṃchāditamabhūtsarvaṃ sākāśavivaraṃ jagat || 52 ||

sarve sahasrahastāste sahasrāyudhapāṇayaḥ |
rudrasyānucarāssarve sarve rudrasamaprabhāḥ || 53 ||

śūlaśaktigadāhastāṣṭaṃkopalaśilādharāḥ |
kālāgnirudrasadṛśāstrinetrāśca jaṭādharāḥ || 54 ||

nipeturbhṛśamākāśe śataśassiṃhavāhanāḥ |
vineduśca mahānādāñjaladā iva bhadrajāḥ || 55 ||

tairbhadrairbhagavānmadrastathā parivṛto babhau |
kālānalaśatairyukto yathānte kālabhairavaḥ || 56 ||

teṣāṃ madhye samāruhya vṛṣendraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ |
jagāma bhagavānbhadraśśubhamabhraṃ yathā bhavaḥ || 57 ||

tasminvṛṣabhamārūḍhe bhadre tu bhasitaprabhaḥ |
babhāra mauktikaṃ chatraṃ gṛhītasitacāmaraḥ || 58 ||

sa tadā śuśubhe pārśve bhadrasya bhasitaprabhaḥ |
bhagavāniva śailendraḥ pārśve viśvajagadguroḥ || 59 ||

so .api tena babhau bhadraḥ śvetacāmarapāṇinā |
bālasomena saumyena yathā śūlavarāyudhaḥ || 60 ||

dadhmau śaṃkhaṃ sitaṃ bhadraṃ bhadrasya purataḥ śubham |
bhānukaṃpo mahātejā hemaratnairalaṃkṛtaḥ || 61 ||

devadundubhayo nedurdivyasaṃkulaniḥsvanāḥ |
vavṛṣuśśataśo mūrdhni puṣpavarṣaṃ balāhakāḥ || 62 ||

phullānāṃ madhugarbhāṇāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ gandhabandhavaḥ |
mārgānukūlasaṃvāhā vabuśca pathi mārutāḥ || 63 ||

tato gaṇeśvarāḥ sarve mattā yuddhabaloddhatāḥ |
nanṛturmumudurnedurjahasurjagadurjaguḥ || 64 ||

tadā bhadragaṇāntaḥstho babhau bhadraḥ sa bhadrayā |
yathā rudragaṇāntaḥsthastryambakoṃbikayā saha || 65 ||

tatkṣaṇādeva dakṣasya yajñavāṭaṃ raṇmayam |
praviveśa mahābāhurvīrabhadro mahānugaḥ || 66 ||

tatastu dakṣapratipāditasya kratupradhānasya gaṇapradhānaḥ |
prayogabhūmiṃ praviveśa bhadro rudro yathānte bhuvanaṃ didhakṣuḥ || 67 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vīrabhadrotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 19 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tato viṣṇupradhānānāṃ surāṇāmamitaujasām |
dadarśa ca mahatsatraṃ citradhvajaparicchadam || 1 ||

sudarbhaṛtusaṃstīrṇaṃ susamiddhahutāśanam |
kāṃcanairyajñabhāṃḍaiśca bhrājiṣṇubhiralaṃkṛtam || 2 ||

ṛṣibhiryajñapaṭubhiryathāvatkarmakartṛbhiḥ |
vidhinā vedadṛṣṭena svanuṣṭhitabahukramam || 3 ||

devāṃganāsahasrāḍhyamapsarogaṇasevitam |
veṇuvīṇāravairjuṣṭaṃ vedaghoṣaiśca bṛṃhitam || 4 ||

dṛṣṭvā dakṣādhvare vīro vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān |
siṃhanādaṃ tadā cakre gaṃbhīro jalado yathā || 5 ||

tataḥ kilakilāśabda ākāśaṃ pūrayanniva |
gaṇeśvaraiḥ kṛto jajñe mahānnyakkṛtasāgaraḥ || 6 ||

tena śabdena mahatāḥ grastā sarvedivaukasaḥ |
dudruvuḥ parito bhītāḥ srastavastravibhūṣaṇāḥ || 7 ||

kiṃsvidbhagno mahāmeruḥ kiṃsvitsaṃdīryate mahī |
kimidaṃ kimidaṃ veti jajalpustridaśā bhṛśam || 8 ||

mṛgendrāṇāṃ yathā nādaṃ gajendrā gahane vane |
śrutvā tathāvidhaṃ kecittatyajurjīvitaṃ bhayāt || 9 ||

parvatāśca vyaśīryanta cakampe ca vasundharā |
marutaśca vyaghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ || 10 ||

agnayo naiva dīpyante na ca dīpyati bhāskaraḥ |
grahāśca na prakāśante nakṣatrāṇi ca tārakāḥ || 11 ||

etasminneva kāle tu yajñavāṭaṃ tadujjvalam |
saṃprāpa bhagavānbhadro bhadraiśca saha bhadrayā || 12 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhītabhīto .api dakṣo dṛḍha iva sthitaḥ |
kruddhavadvacanaṃ prāha ko bhavān kimihecchasi || 13 ||

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ |
vīrabhadro mahātejā meghasaṃbhīranissvanaḥ || 14 ||

smayanniva tamālokya dakṣaṃ devāśca ṛtvijaḥ |
arthagarbhamasaṃbhrāntamavocaducitaṃ vacaḥ || 15 ||

vīrabhadra uvāca |

vayaṃ hyanucarāḥ sarve śarvasyāmitatejasaḥ |
bhāgābhilipsayā prāptā bhāgo nassaṃpradīyatām || 16 ||

atha cedadhvare .asmākaṃ na bhāgaḥ parikalpitaḥ |
kathyatāṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra yudhyatāṃ vā mayāmaraiḥ || 17 ||

ityuktāste gaṇendreṇa devā dakṣapurogamāḥ |
ūcurmantrāḥ pramāṇaṃ no na vayaṃ prabhavastviti || 18 ||

mantrā ūcussurā yūyaṃ mohopahatacetasaḥ |
yena prathamabhāgārhaṃ na yajadhvaṃ maheśvaram || 19 ||

mantroktā api te devāḥ sarve saṃmūḍhacetasaḥ |
bhadrāya na dadurbhāgaṃ tatprahāṇamabhīpsavaḥ || 20 ||

yadā tathyaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca svavākyaṃ tadvṛthā .abhavat |
tadā tato yayurmandā brahmalokaṃ sanātanam || 21 ||

athovāca gaṇādhyakṣo devānviṣṇupurogamān |
mantrāḥ pramāṇaṃ na kṛtā yuṣmābhirbalagarvitaiḥ || 22 ||

yasmādasmin makhe devairitthaṃ vayamasatkṛtāḥ |
tasmādvo jīvitaissārddhamapaneṣyāmi garvitam || 23 ||

ityuktvā bhagavān kruddho vyadahannetravahninā |
yakṣavāṭaṃ mahākūṭaṃ yathātisraḥ puro haraḥ || 24 ||

tato gaṇeśvarāssarve parvatodagravigrahāḥ |
yūpānutpāṭya hotR̥ṇāṃ kaṃṭheṣvābadhya rajjubhiḥ || 25 ||

yajñapātrāṇi citrāṇi bhittvā saṃcūrṇya vāriṇi |
gṛhītvā caiva yajñāṃgaṃ gaṃgāsrotasi cikṣipuḥ || 26 ||

tatra divyānnapānānāṃ rāśayaḥ parvatopamāḥ |
kṣīranadyo .amṛtasrāvāḥ susnigdhadadhikardamāḥ || 27 ||

uccāvacāni māṃsāni bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca |
rasavanti ca pānāni lehyacoṣyāṇi tāni vai || 28 ||

vīrāstadbhujate vaktrairviluṃpanti kṣipanti ca |
vajraiścakrairmahāśūlaiśśaktibhiḥ pāśapaṭṭiśaiḥ || 29 ||

musalairasibhiṣṭaṃkairbhidhipālaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ |
uddhatāṃstridaśānsarvĀllokapālapurassarān || 30 ||

bibhidurbalino vīrā vīrabhadrāṃgasaṃbhavāḥ |
chindhi bhindhi kṣipa kṣipraṃ māryatāṃ dāryatāmiti || 31 ||

harasva praharasveti pāṭayotpāṭayeti ca |
saṃraṃbhaprabhavāḥ krūrāśśabdāḥ śravaṇaśaṃkavaḥ || 32 ||

yatratatra gaṇeśānāṃ jajñire samarocitāḥ |
vivṛttanayanāḥ keciddaṣṭadaṃṣṭroṣṭhatālavaḥ || 33 ||

āśramasthānsamākṛṣya mārayanti tapodhanāt |
sruvānapaharantaśca kṣipantogniṃ jaleṣu ca || 34 ||

kalaśānapi bhindantaśchindanto maṇivedikāḥ |
gāyantaśca nadantaśca hasantaśca muhurmuhuḥ || 35 ||

raktāsavaṃ pibantaśca nanṛturgaṇapuṃgavāḥ |
nirmathya sendrānamarān gaṇendrānvṛṣendranāgendramṛgendrasārāḥ || 36 ||

cakrurbahūnyapratimabhāvāḥ saharṣaromāṇi viceṣṭitāni |
nandanti kecitpraharanti keciddhāvanti kecitpralapanti kecit || 37 ||

nṛtyanti kecidvihasanti kecidvalganti kecitpramathā balena || 38 ||

kecijjighṛkṣanti ghanānsa toyānkecidgrahītuṃ ravimutpatanti |
kecitprasartuṃ pavanena sārddhamicchanti bhīmāḥ pramathā viyatsthāḥ || 39 ||

ākṣipya kecicca varāyudhāni mahā bhujaṃgāniva vainateyāḥ |
bhramanti devānapi vidravantaḥ khamaṃḍale parvatakūṭakalpāḥ || 40 ||

utpāṭya cotpāṭyagṛhāṇi kecitsajālavātāyanavedikāni |
vikṣipya vikṣipya jalasya madhye kālāṃbudābhāḥ pramathā nineduḥ || 41 ||

udvartitadvārakapāṭakuḍyaṃ vidhvastaśālāvalabhīgavākṣam |
aho batābhajyata yajñavāṭamanāthavadvākyamivāyathārtham || 42 ||

hā nātha tāteti pituḥ suteti bhratarmamāmbeti ca mātuleti |
utpāṭyamāneṣu gṛheṣu nāryo hyānāthaśabdānbahuśaḥ pracakruḥ || 43 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe yajñavidhvaṃsano nāma viṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 20 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tatastridaśamukhyāste viṣṇuśakrapurogamāḥ |
sarve bhayaparitrastādudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ || 1 ||

nijairadūṣitairaṃgairdṛṣṭvā devānupadrutān |
daṃḍyānadaṃḍitānmatvā cukopa gaṇapuṃgavaḥ || 2 ||

tatastriśūlamādāya śarvaśaktinibarhaṇam |
ūrdhvadṛṣṭirmahābāhurmukhājjvālāḥ samutsṛjan || 3 ||

amarānapi dudrāva dviradāniva kesarī |
tānabhidravatastasya gamanaṃ sumanoharam || 4 ||

vārāṇasyeva mattasya jagāma prekṣaṇīyatām |
tatastatkṣobhayāmāsa mahatsurabalaṃ balī || 5 ||

mahāsarovaraṃ yadvanmatto vāraṇayūthapaḥ |
vikurvanbahudhāvarṇānnīlapāṃḍuralohitān || 6 ||

vibhradvyāghrājinaṃ vāso hemapravaratārakam |
chindanbhindannudaklindandārayanpramathannapi || 7 ||

vyacaraddevasaṃgheṣu bhadro .agniriva kakṣagaḥ |
tatra tatra mahāvegāccarantaṃ śūladhāriṇam || 8 ||

tamekaṃ tridaśāḥ sarve sahasramiva menire |
bhadrakālī ca saṃkruddhā yuddhavṛddhamadoddhatā || 9 ||

muktajvālena śūlena nirbibheda raṇe surān |
sa tayā ruruce bhadro rudrakopasamudbhavaḥ || 10 ||

prabhayeva yugāntāgniścalayā dhūmadhūmrayā |
bhadrakālī tadāyuddhe vidrutatridaśābabhau || 11 ||

kalpe śeṣānalajvālādagdhāviśvajagadyathā |
tadā savājinaṃ sūryaṃ rudrānrudragaṇāgraṇīḥ || 12 ||

bhadro mūrdhni jaghānāśu vāmapādena līlayā |
asibhiḥ pāvakaṃ bhadraḥ paṭṭiśaistu yamaṃ yamī || 13 ||

rudrāndṛḍhena śūlena mudgarairvaruṇaṃ dṛḍhaiḥ |
parighairnirṛtiṃ vāyuṃ ṭaṃkaiṣṭaṃkadharaḥ svayam || 14 ||

nirbibheda raṇe vīro līlayaiva gaṇeśvaraḥ |
sarvāndevagaṇānsadyo munīñchaṃbhorvirodhinaḥ || 15 ||

tato devaḥ sarasvatyā nāsikāgraṃ suśobhanam |
ciccheda karajāgreṇa devamātustathaiva ca || 16 ||

ciccheda ca kuṭhāreṇa bāhudaṃḍaṃ vibhāvasoḥ |
agrato dvyaṃgulāṃ jihvāṃ māturdevyā lulāva ca || 17 ||

svāhādevyāstathā devo dakṣiṇaṃ nāsikāpuṭam |
cakarta karajāgreṇa vāmaṃ ca stanacūcukam || 18 ||

bhagasya vipule netre śatapatrasamaprabhe |
prasahyotpāṭayāmāsa bhadraḥ paramavegavān || 19 ||

pūṣṇo daśanarekhāṃ ca dīptāṃ muktāvalīmiva |
jaghāna dhanuṣaḥ koṭyā sa tenāspaṣṭavāgabhūt || 20 ||

tataścandramasaṃ devaḥ pādāṃguṣṭhena līlayā |
kṣaṇaṃ kṛmivadākramya gharṣayāmāsa bhūtale || 21 ||

śiraściccheda dakṣasya bhadraḥ paramakopataḥ |
krośantyāmeva vairiṇyāṃ bhadrakālyai dadau ca tat || 22 ||

tatprahṛṣṭā samādāya śirastālaphalopamam |
sā devī kaṃḍukakrīḍāṃ cakāra samarāṃgaṇe || 23 ||

tato dakṣasya yajñastrī kuśīlā bhartṛbhiryathā |
pādābhyāṃ caiva hastābhyāṃ hanyate sma gaṇeśvaraiḥ || 24 ||

ariṣṭanemine somaṃ dharmaṃ caiva prajāpatim |
bahuputraṃ cāṃgirasaṃ kṛśāśvaṃ kaśyapaṃ tathā || 25 ||

gale pragṛhya balino gaṇapāḥ siṃhavikramāḥ |
bhartsayanto bhṛśaṃ vāgbhirnirjaghnurmūrdhni muṣṭibhiḥ || 26 ||

dharṣitā bhūtavetālairdārāssutaparigrahāḥ |
yathā kaliyuge jārairbalena kulayoṣitaḥ || 27 ||

tacca vidhvastakalaśaṃ bhagnayūpaṃ gatotsavam |
pradīpitamahāśālaṃ prabhinnadvāratoraṇam || 28 ||

utpāṭitasurānīkaṃ hanyamānaṃ tapodhanam |
praśāntabrahmanirghoṣaṃ prakṣīṇajanasaṃcayam || 29 ||

krandamānāturastrīkaṃ hatāśeṣaparicchadam |
śūnyāraṇyanibhaṃ jajñe yajñavāṭaṃ tadārditam || 30 ||

śūlavegaprarugṇāśca bhinnabāhūruvakṣasaḥ |
vinikṛttottamāṃgāśca petururvyāṃ surottamāḥ || 31 ||

hateṣu teṣu deveṣu patiteṣuḥ sahasraśaḥ |
praviveśa gaṇeśānaḥ kṣaṇādāhavanīyakam || 32 ||

praviṣṭamatha taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadraṃ kālāgnisaṃnibham |
dudrāva maraṇādbhīto yajño mṛgavapurdharaḥ || 33 ||

sa visphāryya mahaccāpaṃ dṛḍhajyāghoṣaṇabhīṣaṇam |
bhadrastamabhidudrāva vikṣipanneva sāyakān || 34 ||

ākarṇapūrṇamākṛṣṭaṃ dhanurambudasaṃnibham |
nādayāmāsa ca jyāṃ dyāṃ khaṃ ca bhūmiṃ ca sarvaśaḥ || 35 ||

tamupaśritya sannādaṃ hato .asmītyeva vihvalam |
śaraṇārdhena vakreṇa sa vīro .adhvarapūruṣam || 36 ||

mahābhayaskhalatpādaṃ vepantaṃ vigatatviṣam |
mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ viśiraskaṃ tadākarot || 37 ||

tamīdṛśamavajñātaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai sūryasaṃbhavam |
viṣṇuḥ paramasaṃkruddho yuddhāyābhavadudyataḥ || 38 ||

tamuvāha mahāvegātskandhena natasandhinā |
sarveṣāṃ vayasāṃ rājā garuḍaḥ pannagāśanaḥ / || 39 ||

devāśca hataśiṣṭā ye devarājapurogamāḥ |
pracakrustasya sāhāyyaṃ prāṇāṃstyaktumivodyatāḥ || 40 ||

viṣṇunā sahitāndevānmṛgendraḥ kroṣṭukāniva |
dṛṣṭvā jahāsa bhūtendro mṛgendra iva vivyathaḥ || 41 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe devadaṃḍavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 21 ||

tasminnavasare vyomni samāvirabhavadrathaḥ |
sahasrasūryasaṃkāśaścārucīravṛṣadhvajaḥ || 1 ||

aśvaratnadvayodāro rathacakracatuṣṭayaḥ |
sañcitānekadivyāstraśastraratnapariṣkṛtaḥ || 2 ||

tasyāpi rathavaryasya syātsa eva hi sārathiḥ |
yathā ca traipure yuddhe pūrvaṃ śārvarathe sthitaḥ || 3 ||

sa taṃ rathavaraṃ brahmā śāsanādeva śūlinaḥ |
haressamīpamānīya kṛtāñjalirabhāṣata || 4 ||

bhagavanbhadra bhadrāṃga bhagavānindubhūṣaṇaḥ |
ājñāpayati vīrastvāṃ rathamāroḍhumavyayaḥ || 5 ||

rebhyāśramasamīpasthastryaṃbako .aṃbikayā saha |
sampaśyate mahābāho dussahaṃ te parākramam || 6 ||

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sa vīro gaṇakuñjaraḥ |
āruroha rathaṃ divyamanugṛhya pitāmaham || 7 ||

tathā rathavare tasminsthite brahmaṇi sārathau |
bhadrasya vavṛdhe lakṣmī rudrasyeva puradviṣaḥ || 8 ||

tataḥ śaṃkhavaraṃ dīptaṃ pūrṇacandrasamaprabham |
pradadhmau vadane kṛtvā bhānukaṃpo mahābalaḥ || 9 ||

tasya śaṃkhasya taṃ nādaṃ bhinnasārasasannibham |
śrutvā bhayena devānāṃ jajvāla jaṭharānalaḥ || 10 ||

yakṣavidyādharāhīndraiḥ siddhairyuddhadidṛkṣubhiḥ |
kṣaṇena nibaḍībhūtāḥ sākāśavivarā diśāḥ || 11 ||

tataḥ śārGgeṇa cāpāGkātsa nārāyaṇanīradaḥ |
mahatā bāṇavarṣeṇa tutoda gaṇagovṛṣam || 12 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṇumāyāntaṃ śatadhā bāṇavarṣiṇam |
sa cādade dhanurjaitraṃ bhadro bāṇasahasramuk || 13 ||

samādāya ca taddivyaṃ dhanussamarabhairavam |
śanairvisphārayāmāsa meruṃ dhanuriveśvaraḥ || 14 ||

tasya visphāryyamāṇasya dhanuṣo .abhūnmahāsvanaḥ |
tena svanena mahatā pṛthivīṃ samakaṃpayat || 15 ||

tataḥ śaravaraṃ ghoraṃ dīptamāśīviṣopamam |
jagrāha gaṇapaḥ śrīmānsvayamugraparākramaḥ || 16 ||

bāṇoddhāre bhujo hyasya tūṇīvadanasaṃgataḥ |
pratyadṛśyata valmīkaṃ vivekṣuriva pannagaḥ || 17 ||

samuddhṛtaḥ kare tasya tatkṣaṇaṃ ruruce śareḥ |
mahābhujaṃgasaṃdaṣṭo yathā bālabhujaGgamaḥ || 18 ||

śareṇa ghanatīvreṇa bhadro rudraparākramaḥ |
vivyādha kupito gāḍhaṃ lalāṭe viṣṇumavyayam || 19 ||

lalāṭe .abhihito viṣṇuḥ pūrvamevāvamānitaḥ |
cukopa gaṇapendrāya mṛgendrāyeva govṛṣaḥ || 20 ||

tatastvaśanikalpena krūrāsyena maheṣuṇā |
vivyādha gaṇarājasya bhuje bhujagasannibhe || 21 ||

so .api tasya bhuje bhūyaḥ sūryāyutasamaprabham |
visasarja śaraṃ vegādvīrabhadro mahābalaḥ || 22 ||

sa ca viṣṇuḥ punarbhadraṃ bhadro viṣṇuṃ tathā punaḥ |
sa ca taṃ sa ca taṃ viprāśśaraistāvanujaghnatuḥ || 23 ||

tayoḥ parasparaṃ vegāccharānāśu vimuṃcatoḥ |
dvayossamabhavadyuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam || 24 ||

taddṛṣṭvā tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ tayoreva parasparam |
hāhākāro mahānāsīdākāśe khecareritaḥ || 25 ||

tatastvanalatuṃḍena śareṇādityavarcasā |
vivyādha sudṛḍhaṃ bhadro viṣṇormahati vakṣasi || 26 ||

sa tu tīvraprapātena śareṇa dṛḍhamāhataḥ |
mahatīṃ rujamāsādya nipapāta vimohitaḥ || 27 ||

punaḥ kṣaṇādivotthāya labdhasaṃjñastadā hariḥ |
sarvāṇyapi ca divyāstrāṇyathainaṃ pratyavāsṛjat || 28 ||

sa ca viṣṇurdhanurmuktānsarvāñcharvacamūpatiḥ |
sahasā vārayāmāsa ghoraiḥ pratiśaraiḥ śarān || 29 ||

tato viṣṇussvanāmāṃkaṃ bāṇamavyāhataṃ kvacit |
sasarja krodharaktā kṣastamuddiśya gaṇeśvaram |
taṃ bāṇaṃ bāṇavaryeṇa bhadro bhadrāhvayeṇa tu // 30 || 30 ||

aprāptameva bhagavāñciccheda śatadhā pathi |
athaikeneṣuṇā śārGgaṃ dvābhyāṃ pakṣau garutmataḥ || 31 ||

nimeṣādeva ciccheda tadadbhutamivābhavat |
tato yogabalādviṣṇurdehāddevānsudāruṇān || 32 ||

śaṃkhacakragadāhastān visasarja sahasraśaḥ |
sarvāṃstānkṣaṇamātreṇa traipurāniva śaṃkaraḥ || 33 ||

nirdadāha mahābāhurnetrasṛṣṭena vahninā |
tataḥ kruddhataro viṣṇuścakramudyamya satvaraḥ || 34 ||

tasminvīro samutsraṣṭuṃ tadānīmudyato .abhavat |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cakramudyamya purataḥ samupasthitam || 35 ||

smayanniva gaṇeśāno vyaṣṭaṃbhayadayatnataḥ |
staṃbhitāṃgastu taccakraṃ ghoramapratimaṃ kvacit || 36 ||

icchannapi samutsraṣṭuṃ na viṣṇurabhavatkṣamaḥ |
śvasannivaikamuddhṛtya bāhuṃ cakrasamanvitam || 37 ||

atiṣṭhadalaso bhūtvā pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ |
viśarīro yathājīvo viśṛGgo vā yathā vṛṣaḥ || 38 ||

vidaṃṣṭraśca yathā siṃhastathā viṣṇuravasthitaḥ |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā durdaśāpannaṃ viṣṇumindrādayaḥ surāḥ |
samunnaddhā gaṇendreṇa mṛgendreṇeva govṛṣāḥ // 39 || 39 ||

pragṛhītāyudhā yauddhuṃkruddhāḥ samupatasthire |
tāndṛṣṭvā samare bhadraḥkṣudrāniva harirmṛgān || 40 ||

sākṣādrudratanurvīro varavīragaṇāvṛtaḥ |
aṭṭahāsena ghoreṇa vyaṣṭaṃ bhayadaninditaḥ || 41 ||

tathā śatamakhasyāpi savajro dakṣiṇaḥ karaḥ |
sisṛkṣoreva udvajraścitrīkṛta ivābhavat || 42 ||

anyeṣāmapi sarveṣāṃ saraktā api bāhavaḥ |
alasānāmivāraṃbhāstādṛśāḥ pratiyāntyuta || 43 ||

evaṃ bhagavatā tena vyāhatāśeṣavaibhavāt |
amarāḥ samare tasya purataḥ sthātumakṣamāḥ || 44 ||

stabdhairavayavaireva dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ |
sthitiṃ ca cakrire yuddhe vīratejobhayākulāḥ || 45 ||

vidrutāṃstridaśānvīrānvīrabhadro mahābhujaḥ / |
vivyādha niśitairbāṇairmagho varṣairivācalān || 46 ||

bahavastasya vīrasya bāhavaḥ parighopamāḥ |
śastraiścakāśire dīptaiḥ sāgnijvālā ivoragāḥ || 47 ||

astraśastrāṇyanekānisavīro visṛjanbabhau |
visṛjansarvabhūtāni yathādau viśvasaṃbhavaḥ || 48 ||

yathā raśmibhirādityaḥ pracchādayati medinīm |
tathā vīraḥ kṣaṇādeva śaraiḥ prācchādayaddiśaḥ || 49 ||

khamaṃḍale gaṇendrasya śarāḥ kanakabhūṣitāḥ |
utpatantastaḍidrūpairupamānapadaṃ yayuḥ || 50 ||

mahāntaste suragaṇān maṃḍūkānivaḍuṃḍubhāḥ |
prāṇairviyojayāmāsuḥ papuśca rudhirāsavam || 51 ||

nikṛttabāhavaḥ kecitkecillūnavarānanāḥ |
pārśve vidāritāḥ kecinnipeturamarā bhuvi || 52 ||

viśikhonmathitairgātrairbahubhiśchinnasandhibhiḥ |
vivṛttanayanāḥ kecinnipeturbhūtale mṛtāḥ |
gāṃ praveṣṭumivecchantaḥ khaṃ gantumiva lipsavaḥ // 54 || 53 ||

alabdhātmanirodhānāṃ vyalīyantaḥ parasparam |
bhūmau kecitpraviviśuḥ parvatānāṃ guhāḥ pare || 54 ||

apare jagmurākāśaṃ pare ca viviśurjalam |
tathā saṃchinnasarvāṃgaissa vīrastridaśairbabhau || 55 ||

parigrastaprajāvargo bhagavāniva bhairavaḥ |
dagdhatripurasaṃvyūhastripurāriryathābhavat || 56 ||

evaṃ devabalaṃ sarvaṃ dīnaṃ bībhatsadarśanam |
gaṇeśvarasamutpannaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ vapurādade || 57 ||

tadā tridaśavīrāṇāmasṛksalilavāhinī |
prāvartata nadī ghorā prāṇināṃ bhayaśaṃsinī || 58 ||

rudhireṇa pariklinnā yajñabhūmistadā babhau |
raktārdravasanā śyāmā hataśuṃbheva kaiśikī || 59 ||

tasminmahati saṃvṛtte samare bhṛśadāruṇe |
bhayeneva paritrastā pracacāla vasundharā || 60 ||

mahormikalilāvartaścukṣubhe ca mahodadhiḥ |
petuścolkā mahotpātāḥ śākhāśca mumucurdrumāḥ || 61 ||

aprasannā diśaḥ sarvāḥ pavanaścāśivo vavau |
aho vidhiviparyāsastvaśvamedhoyamadhvaraḥ |
yajamānassvayaṃ dakṣau brahmaputraprajāpatiḥ // 62 || 62 ||

dharmādayassadasyāśca rakṣitā garuḍadhvajaḥ |
bhāgāṃśca pratigṛhṇanti sākṣādindrādayaḥ surāḥ || 63 ||

tathāpi yajamānasya yajñasya ca sahartvijaḥ |
sadya eva śiraśchedassādhu saṃpadyate phalam || 64 ||

tasmānnāvedanirdiṣṭaṃ na ceśvarabahiṣkṛtam |
nāsatparigṛhītaṃ ca karma kuryātkadācana || 65 ||

kṛtvāpi sumahatpuṇyamiṣṭvā yajñaśatairapi |
na tatphalamavāpnoti bhaktihīno maheśvare || 66 ||

kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpaṃ bhaktyā yajati yaśśivam |
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvairnātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 67 ||

bahunātra kimuktena vṛthā dānaṃ vṛthā tapaḥ |
vṛthā yajño vṛthā homaḥ śivanindāratasya tu || 68 ||

tataḥ sanārāyaṇakāssarudrāḥ salokapālāssamare suraughāḥ |
gaṇendracāpacyutabāṇaviddhāḥ pradudruvurgāḍharujābhibhūtāḥ || 69 ||

celuḥ kvacitkecana śīrṇakeśāḥ seduḥ kvacitkecana dīrghagātrāḥ |
petuḥ kvacitkecana bhinnavaktrā neśuḥ kvacitkecana devavīrāḥ || 70 ||

kecicca tatra tridaśā vipannā visrastavastrābharaṇāstraśastrāḥ |
nipeturudbhāsitadīnamudrā madaṃ ca darpaṃ ca balaṃ ca hitvā || 71 ||

sasmutpathaprasthitamapradhṛṣyo vikṣipya dakṣādhvaramakṣatāstraiḥ |
babhau gaṇeśassa gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ madhye sthitaḥ siṃha ivarṣabhāṇām || 72 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrkhaṇḍe dakṣayajñavidhvaṃsavarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 22 ||

vāyuruvāca |

iti sañchinnabhinnāṃgā devā viṣṇupurogamāḥ |
kṣaṇātkaṣṭāṃ daśāmetya tresuḥ stokāvaśeṣitā || 1 ||

trastāṃstānsamare vīrān devānanyāṃśca vai gaṇāḥ |
pramathāḥ paramakruddhā vīrabhadrapraṇoditāḥ || 2 ||

pragṛhya ca tathā doṣaṃ nigaḍairāyasairdṛḍhaiḥ |
babandhuḥ pāṇipādeṣu kandhareṣūdareṣu ca || 3 ||

tasminnavasare brahmā bhadramadrīndrajānutam |
sārathyāllabdhavātsalyaḥ prārthayan praṇato .abravīt || 4 ||

alaṃ krodhena bhagavannaṣṭāścaite divaukasaḥ |
prasīda kṣamyatāṃ sarvaṃ romajaissaha suvrata || 5 ||

evaṃ vijñāpitastena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā |
śamaṃ jagāma saṃprīto gaṇapastasya gauravāt || 6 ||

devāśca labdhāvasarā devadevasya mantriṇaḥ |
dhārayanto .añjalīnmūrdhni tuṣṭuvurvividhaiḥ stavaiḥ || 7 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

namaḥ śivāya śāntāya yajñahantre triśūline |
rudrabhadrāya rudrāṇāṃ pataye rudrabhūtaye || 8 ||

kālāgnirudrarūpāya kālakāmāṃgahāriṇe |
devatānāṃ śirohantre dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ || 9 ||

saṃsargādasya pāpasya dakṣasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ |
śāsitāḥ samare vīra tvayā vayamaninditā || 10 ||

dagdhāścāmī vayaṃ sarve tvatto bhītāśca bho prabho |
tvameva gatirasmākaṃ trāhi naśśaraṇāgatān || 11 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tuṣṭastvevaṃ stuto devān visṛjya nigaḍātprabhuḥ |
ānayaddevadevasya samīpamamarāniha || 12 ||

devopi tatra bhagavānantarikṣe sthitaḥ prabhuḥ |
sagaṇaḥ sarvagaḥ śarvassarvalokamaheśvaraḥ || 13 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ devā viṣṇupurogamāḥ |
prītā api ca bhītāśca namaścakrurmaheśvaram || 14 ||

dṛṣṭvā tānamarānbhītānpraṇatārtiharo haraḥ |
idamāha mahādevaḥ prahasan prekṣya pārvatīm || 15 ||

mahādeva uvāca |

mābhaiṣṭa tridaśāssarve yūyaṃ vai māmikāḥ prajāḥ |
anugrahārthameveha dhṛto daṃḍaḥ kṛpālunā || 16 ||

bhavatāṃ nirjjarāṇāṃ hi kṣānto .asmābhirvyatikramaḥ |
kruddheṣvasmāsu yuṣmākaṃ na sthitirna ca jīvitam || 17 ||

vāyuruvāca |

ityuktāstridaśāssarve śarveṇāmitatejasā |
sadyo vigatasandehā nanṛturvibudhā mudā || 18 ||

prasannamanaso bhūtvānandavihvalamānasāḥ |
stutimārebhire kartuṃ śaṃkarasya divaukasaḥ || 19 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

tvameva devākhilalokakartā pātā ca hartā parameśvaro .asi |
kaviṣṇurudrākhyasvarūpabhedai rajastamassattvadhṛtātmamūrtte || 20 ||

sarvamūrtte namaste .astu viśvabhāvana pāvana |
amūrtte bhaktahetorhi gṛhītākṛtisaukhyada || 21 ||

candro .agado hi deveśa kṛpātastava śaṃkara |
nimajjanānmṛtaḥ prāpa sukhaṃ mihirajājaliḥ || 22 ||

sīmantinī hatadhavā tava pūjanataḥ prabho |
saubhāgyamatulaṃ prāpa somavāravratātsutān || 23 ||

śrīkarāya dadau devaḥ svīyaṃ padamanuttamam |
sudarśanamarakṣastvaṃ nṛpamaṃḍalabhītitaḥ || 24 ||

meduraṃ tārayāmāsa sadāraṃ ca ghṛṇānidhiḥ |
śāradāṃ vidhavāṃ cakre sadhavāṃ kriyayā bhavān || 25 ||

bhadrāyuṣo vipattiṃ ca vicchidya tvamadāḥ sukham |
sauminī bhavabandhādvai muktā .abhūttava sevanāt || 26 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

tvaṃ śaṃbho kaharīśāśca rajassattvatamoguṇaiḥ |
kartā pātā tathā hartā janānugrahakāṃkṣayā || 27 ||

sarvagarvāpahārī ca sarvatejovilāsakaḥ |
sarvavidyādigūḍhaśca sarvānugrahakārakaḥ || 28 ||

tvattaḥ sarvaṃ ca tvaṃ sarvaṃ tvayi sarvaṃ girīśvara |
trāhi trāhi punastrāhi kṛpāṃ kuru mamopari || 29 ||

athāsminnantare brahmā praṇipatya kṛtāṃjaliḥ |
evaṃ tvavasaraṃ prāpya vyajñāpayata śūline || 30 ||

brahmovāca |

jaya deva mahādeva praṇatārtivibhaṃjana |
īdṛśeṣvaparādheṣu ko .anyastvattaḥ prasīdati || 31 ||

labdhamāno bhaviṣyanti ye purā nihitā mṛdhe |
pratyāpattirna kasya syātprasanne parameśvare || 32 ||

yadidaṃ devadevānāṃ kṛtamantuṣu dūṣaṇam |
tadidaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ manyeta aṃgīkāragauravāt || 33 ||

iti vijñāpyamānastu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā |
vilokya vadanaṃ devyā devadevassmayanniva || 34 ||

putrabhūtasya vātsalyādbrahmaṇaḥ padmajanmanaḥ |
devādīnāṃ yathāpūrvamaṃgāni pradadau prabhuḥ || 35 ||

prathamādyaiśca yā devyo daṃḍitā devamātaraḥ |
tāsāmapi yathāpūrvāṇyaṃgāni giriśo dadau || 36 ||

dakṣasya bhagavāneva svayaṃ brahmā pitāmahaḥ |
tatpāpānuguṇaṃ cakre jaracchāgamukhaṃ mukham || 37 ||

so .api saṃjñāṃ tato labdhvā sa dṛṣṭvā jīvitaḥ sudhī |
bhītaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ śaṃbhuṃ tuṣṭāva pralapanbahu || 38 ||

dakṣa uvāca |

jaya deva jagannātha lokānugrahakāraka |
kṛpāṃ kuru maheśānāparādhaṃ me kṣamasva ha || 39 ||

karttā bharttā ca hartā ca tvameva jagatāṃ prabho |
mayā jñātaṃ viśeṣeṇa viṣṇvādisakaleśvaraḥ || 40 ||

tvayaiva vitataṃ sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ na nāśitam |
na hi tvadadhikāḥ kecidīśāste .acyutakādayaḥ || 41 ||

vāyuruvāca |

taṃ tathā vyākulaṃ bhītaṃ pralapantaṃ kṛtāgasam |
smayannivāvadatprekṣya mā bhairiti ghṛṇānidhiḥ || 42 ||

tathoktvā brahmaṇastasya pituḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
gāṇapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākṣayamīśvaraḥ || 43 ||

tato brahmādayo devā abhivandya kṛtaaṃjaliḥ |
tuṣṭuvuḥ praśrayā vācā śaṃkaraṃ girijādhipam || 44 ||

brahmādaya ūcuḥ |

jaya śaṃkara deveśa dīnānātha mahāprabho |
kṛpāṃ kuru maheśānāparādhaṃ no kṣamasva vai || 45 ||

makhapāla makhādhīśa makhavidhvaṃsakāraka |
kṛpāṃ kuru maśānāparādhaṃ naḥ kṣamasva vai || 46 ||

devadeva pareśāna bhaktaprāṇaprapoṣaka |
duṣṭadaṇḍaprada svāminkṛpāṃ kuru namo .astu te || 47 ||

tvaṃ prabho garvahartā vai duṣṭānāṃ tvāmajānatām |
rakṣako hi viśeṣeṇa satāṃ tvatsaktacetasām || 48 ||

adbhutaṃ caritaṃ te hi niścitaṃ kṛpayā tava |
sarvāparādhaḥ kṣantavyo vibhavo dīnavatsalāḥ || 49 ||

vāyuruvāca |

iti stuto mahādevo brahmādyairamaraiḥ prabhuḥ |
sa bhaktavatsalassvāmī tutoṣa karuṇodadhiḥ || 50 ||

cakārānugrahaṃ teṣāṃ brahmādīnāṃ divaukasām |
dadau narāṃśca suprītyā śaṃkaro dīnavatsalaḥ || 51 ||

sa ca tatastridaśāñcharaṇāgatān paramakāruṇikaḥ parameśvaraḥ |
anugatasmitalakṣaṇayā girā śamitasarvabhayaḥ samabhāṣata || 52 ||

śiva uvāca |

yadidamāga ihācaritaṃ surairvidhiniyogavaśādiva yantritaiḥ |
śaraṇameva gatānavalokya vastadakhilaṃ kila vismṛtameva naḥ || 53 ||

tadiha yūyamapi prakṛtaṃ manasyavigaṇayya vimardamapatrapāḥ |
hariviriṃcisurendramukhāssukhaṃ vrajata devapuraṃ prati saṃprati || 54 ||

iti surānabhidhāya sureśvaro nikṛtadakṣakṛtakraturakratuḥ |
sagirijānucarassaparicchadaḥ sthita ivāmbaratontaradhāddharaḥ || 55 ||

atha surā api te vigatavyathāḥ kathitabhadrasubhadraparākramāḥ |
sapadi khena sukhena yathāsukhaṃ yayuranekamukhāḥ maghavanmukhāḥ || 56 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe giriśānunayo nāma trayoviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 23 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

antardhānagato devyā saha sānucaro haraḥ |
kva yātaḥ kutra vāsaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā virarāma ha || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

mahīdharavaraḥ śrīmān mandaraścitrakandaraḥ |
dayito devadevasya nivāsastapaso .abhavat || 2 ||

tapo mahatkṛtaṃ tena voḍhuṃ svaśirasā śivau |
cireṇa labdhaṃ tatpādapaṃkajasparśajaṃ sukham || 3 ||

tasya śailasya saundaryyaṃ sahasravadanairapi |
na śakyaṃ vistarādvaktuṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi || 4 ||

śakyamapyasya saundaryyaṃ na varṇayitumutsahe |
parvatāntarasaundaryyaṃ sādhāraṇavidhāraṇāt || 5 ||

idantu śakyate vaktumasminparvatasundare |
ṛddhyā kayāpi saundaryamīśvarāvāsayogyatā || 6 ||

ata eva hi devena devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā |
atīva ramaṇīyoyaṃ girirantaḥpurīkṛtaḥ || 7 ||

mekhalābhūmayastasya vimalopalapādapāḥ |
śivayornityasānnidhyānnyakkurvantyakhilaṃjagat || 8 ||

pitṛbhyāṃ jagato nityaṃ snānapānopayogataḥ |
avāptapuṇyasaṃskāraḥ prasaradbhiritastataḥ || 9 ||

laghuśītalasaṃsparśairacchācchairnirjharāmbubhiḥ |
adhirājyena cādrīṇāmadrīreṣo .abhiṣicyate || 10 ||

niśāsu śikharaprāntarvartinā sa śiloccayaḥ |
candreṇācala sāmrājyacchatreṇeva virājate || 11 ||

sa śailaścaṃcalībhūtairbālaiścāmarayoṣitām |
sarvaparvatasāmrājyacāmarairiva vījyate || 12 ||

prātarabhyudite bhānau bhūdharo ratnabhūṣitaḥ |
darpaṇe dehasaubhāgyaṃ draṣṭukāma iva sthitaḥ || 13 ||

kūjadvihaṃgavācālairvātoddhṛtalatābhujaiḥ |
vimuktapuṣpaiḥ satataṃ vyālambimṛdupallavaiḥ || 14 ||

latāpratānajaṭilaistarubhistapasairiva |
jayāśiṣā sahābhyarcya niṣevyata ivādrirāṭ || 15 ||

adhomukhairūrddhvamukhaiśśṛṃgaistiryaGmukhaistathā |
prapatanniva pātāle bhūpṛṣṭhādutpatanniva || 16 ||

parītaḥ sarvato dikṣu bhramanniva vihāyasi |
paśyanniva jagatsarvaṃ nṛtyanniva nirantaram || 17 ||

guhāmukhaiḥ pratidinaṃ vyāttāsyo vipulodaraiḥ |
ajīrṇalāvaṇyatayā jṛṃbhamāṇa ivācalaḥ || 18 ||

grasanniva jagatsarvaṃ pibanniva payonidhim |
vamanniva tamontasthaṃ mādyanniva khamambudaiḥ || 19 ||

nivāsa bhūmayastāstā darpaṇapratimodarāḥ |
tiraskṛtātapāssnigdhāśramacchāyāmahīruhāḥ || 20 ||

saritsarastaḍāgādisaṃparkaśiśirānilāḥ |
tatra tatra niṣaṇṇābhyāṃ śivābhyāṃ saphalīkṛtāḥ || 21 ||

tamimaṃ sarvataḥ śreṣṭhaṃ smṛtvā sāmbastriyambakaḥ |
raibhyāśramasamīpasthaścāntardhānaṃ gato yayau || 22 ||

tatrodyānamanuprāpya devyā saha maheśvaraḥ |
rarāma ramaṇīyāsu devyāntaḥpurabhūmiṣu || 23 ||

tathā gateṣu kāleṣu pravṛddhāsu prajāsu ca |
daityau śuṃbhaniśuṃbhākhyau bhrātarau saṃbabhūvatuḥ || 24 ||

tābhyāṃ tapo balāddattaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā |
avadhyatvaṃ jagatyasminpuruṣairakhilairapi || 25 ||

ayonijā tu yā kanyā hyaṃbikāṃśasamudbhavā |
ajātapuṃsparśaratiravilaṃghyaparākramā || 26 ||

tayā tu nau vadhaḥ saṃkhye tasyāṃ kāmābhibhūtayoḥ |
iti cābhyarthito brahmā tābhyāmprāha tathāstviti || 27 ||

tataḥ prabhṛti śakrādīnvijitya samare surān |
niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāraṃ jagaccakraturakramāt || 28 ||

tayorvadhāya deveśaṃ brahmābhyarthitavānpunaḥ |
vinindyāpi rahasyaṃ vāṃ krodhayitvā yathā tathā || 29 ||

tadvarṇakośajāṃ śaktimakāmāṃ kanyakātmikām |
niśumbhaśuṃbhayorhantrīṃ surebhyo dātumarhasi || 30 ||

evamabhyarthito dhātrā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ |
kālītyāha rahasyaṃ vāṃ nindayanniva sasmitaḥ || 31 ||

tataḥ kruddhā tadā devī suvarṇā varṇakāraṇāt |
smayantī cāha bhartāramasamādheyayā girā || 32 ||

devyuvāca |

īdṛśo mama varṇesminna ratirbhavato .asti cet |
evāvantaṃ ciraṃ kālaṃ kathameṣā niyamyate || 33 ||

aratyā vartamāno .api kathaṃ ca ramase mayā |
na hyaśakyaṃ jagatyasminnīśvarasya jagatprabhoḥ || 34 ||

svātmārāmasya bhavato ratirna sukhasādhanam |
iti hetoḥ smaro yasmātprasabhaṃ bhasmasātkṛtaḥ || 35 ||

yā ca nābhimatā bharturapi sarvāṃgasundarī |
sā vṛthaiva hi jāyeta sarvairapi guṇāntaraiḥ || 36 ||

bharturbhogaikaśeṣo hi sarga evaiṣa yoṣitām |
tathāsatyanyathābhūtā nārī kutropayujyate || 37 ||

tasmādvarṇamimaṃ tyaktvā tvayā rahasi ninditam |
varṇāntaraṃ bhajiṣye vā na bhajiṣyāmi vā svayam || 38 ||

ityuktvotthāya śayanāddevī sācaṣṭa gadgadam |
yayāce .anumatiṃ bhartustapase kṛtaniścayā || 39 ||

tathā praṇayabhaṃgena bhīto bhūtapatiḥ svayam |
pādayoḥ praṇamanneva bhavānīṃ pratyabhāṣata || 40 ||

īśvara uvāca |

ajānatī ca krīḍoktiṃ priye kiṃ kupitāsi me |
ratiḥ kuto vā jāyeta tvattaścedaratirmama || 41 ||

mātā tvamasya jagataḥ pitāhamadhipastathā |
kathaṃ tadutpapadyeta tvatto nābhiratirmama || 42 ||

āvayorabhikāmo .api kimasau kāmakāritaḥ |
yataḥ kāmasamutpattiḥ prāgeva jagadudbhavaḥ || 43 ||

pṛthagjanānāṃ rataye kāmātmā kalpito mayā |
tataḥ kathamupālabdhaḥ kāmadāhādahaṃ tvayā || 44 ||

māṃ vai tridaśasāmānyaṃ manyamāno manobhavaḥ |
manākparibhavaṃ kurvanmayā vai bhasmasātkṛtaḥ || 45 ||

vihāropyāvayorasya jagatastrāṇakāraṇāt |
tatastadarthaṃ tvayyadya krīḍoktiṃ kṛtavāhanam || 46 ||

sa cāyamacirādarthastavaivāviṣkariṣyate |
krodhasya janakaṃ vākyaṃ hṛdi kṛtvedamabravīt || 47 ||

devyuvāca |

śrutapūrvaṃ hi bhagavaṃstava cāṭu vaco mayā |
yenaivamatidhīrāhamapi prāgabhivaṃcitā || 48 ||

prāṇānapyapriyā bharturnārī yā na parityajet |
kulāṃganā śubhā sadbhiḥ kutsitaiva hi gamyate || 49 ||

bhūyasī ca tavāprītiragauramiti me vapuḥ |
krīḍoktirapi kālīti ghaṭate kathamanyathā || 50 ||

sadbhirvigarhitaṃ tasmāttava kārṣṇyamasaṃmatam |
anutsṛjya tapoyogātsthātumeveha notsahe || 51 ||

śiva uvāca |

sa yadyevaṃvidhatāpaste tapasā kiṃ prayojanam |
mamecchayā svecchayā vā varṇāntaravatī bhava || 52 ||

devyuvāca |

necchāmi bhavato varṇaṃ svayaṃ vā kartumanyathā |
brahmāṇaṃ tapasārādhya kṣipraṃ gaurī bhavāmyaham || 53 ||

īśvara uvāca |

matprasādātpurā brahmā brahmatvaṃ prāptavānpurā |
tamāhūya mahādevi tapasā kiṃ kariṣyasi || 54 ||

devyuvāca |

tvatto labdhapadā eva sarve brahmādayaḥ surāḥ |
tathāpyārādhya tapasā brahmāṇaṃ tvanniyogataḥ || 55 ||

purā kila satī nāmnā dakṣasya duhitā .abhavam |
jagatāṃ patimevaṃ tvāṃ patiṃ prāptavatī tathā || 56 ||

evamadyāpi tapasā toṣayitvā dvijaṃ vidhim |
gaurī bhavitumicchāmi ko doṣaḥ kathyatāmiha || 57 ||

evamukto mahādevyā vāmadevaḥ smayanniva |
na tāṃ nirbandhayāmāsa devakāryacikīrṣayā || 58 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śivamandaragirinivāsakrīḍoktavarṇanaṃ nāma caturviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 24 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya patimambā pativratā |
niyamya ca viyogārtiṃ jagāma himavadgirim || 1 ||

tapaḥkṛtavatī pūrvaṃ deśe yasminsakhījanaiḥ |
tameva deśamavṛnottapase praṇayātpunaḥ || 2 ||

tataḥ svapitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā mātaraṃ ca tayorgṛhe |
praṇamya vṛttaṃ vijñāpya tābhyāṃ cānumatā satī || 3 ||

punastapovanaṃ gatvā bhūṣaṇāni visṛjya ca |
snātvā tapasvino veṣaṃ kṛtvā paramapāvanam || 4 ||

saṃkalpya ca mahātīvraṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram |
sadā manasi sandhāya bhartuścaraṇapaṃkajam || 5 ||

tameva kṣaṇike liṃge dhyātvā bāhyavidhānataḥ |
trisandhyamabhyarcayantī vanyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalādibhiḥ || 6 ||

sa eva brahmaṇo mūrtimāsthāya tapasaḥ phalam |
pradāsyati mametyevaṃ nityaṃ kṛtvā .akarottapaḥ || 7 ||

tathā tapaścarantīṃ tāṃ kāle bahutithe gate |
dṛṣṭaḥ kaścinmahāvyāghro duṣṭabhāvādupāgamat || 8 ||

tathaivopagatasyāpi tasyātīvadurātmanaḥ |
gātraṃ citrārpitamiva stabdhaṃ tasyāssakāśataḥ || 9 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvāpi tathā vyāghraṃ duṣṭabhāvādupāgatam |
na pṛthagjanavaddevī svabhāvena vivicyate || 10 ||

sa tu viṣṭabdhasarvāṃgo bubhukṣāparipīḍitaḥ |
mamāmiṣaṃ tato nānyaditi matvā nirantaram || 11 ||

nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ satataṃ devīmeva tadā .aniśam |
atiṣṭhadagratastasyā upāsanamivācarat || 12 ||

devyāśca hṛdaye nityaṃ mamaivāyamupāsakaḥ |
trātā ca duṣṭasattvebhya iti pravavṛte kṛpā || 13 ||

tasyā eva kṛpā yogātsadyonaṣṭamalatrayaḥ |
babhūva sahasā vyāghro devīṃ ca bubudhe tadā || 14 ||

nyavartata bubhukṣā ca tasyāṃgastambhanaṃ tathā |
daurātmyaṃ janmasiddhaṃ ca tṛptiśca samajāyata || 15 ||

tadā paramabhāvena jñātvā kārtārthyamātmanaḥ |
sadyopāsaka evaiṣa siṣeve parameśvarīm || 16 ||

duṣṭānāmapi sattvānāṃ tathānyeṣāndurātmanām |
sa eva drāvako bhūtvā vicacāra tapovane || 17 ||

tapaśca vavṛdhe devyāstīvraṃ tīvratarātmakam |
devāśca daityanirbandhādbrahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ || 18 ||

cakrurnivedanaṃ devāḥ svaduḥkhasyāripīḍanāt |
yathā ca dadatuḥ śumbhaniśumbhau varasammadāt || 19 ||

so .api śrutvā vidhirduḥkhaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛpayānvitaḥ |
āsīddaityavadhāyaiva smṛtvā hetvāśrayāṃ kathām || 20 ||

sāmaraḥ prārthito brahmā yayau devyāstapovanam |
saṃsmaranmanasā devaduḥkhamokṣaṃ svayatnataḥ || 21 ||

dadarśa ca suraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhe tapasi niṣṭhitām |
pratiṣṭhāmiva viśvasya bhavānīṃ parameśvarīm || 22 ||

nanāma cāsya jagato mātaraṃ svasya vai hareḥ |
rudrasya ca piturbhāryāmāryāmadrīśvarātmajām || 23 ||

brahmāṇamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā devī devagaṇaiḥ saha |
arghyaṃ tadarhaṃ dattvā .asmai svāgatādyairupācarat || 24 ||

tāṃ ca pratyupacāroktiṃ puraskṛtyābhinandya ca |
papraccha tapaso hetumajānanniva padmajaḥ || 25 ||

brahmovāca |

tīvreṇa tapasānena devyā kimiha sādhyate |
tapaḥphalānāṃ sarveṣāṃ tvadadhīnā hi siddhayaḥ || 26 ||

yaścaiva jagatāṃ bhartā tameva parameśvaram |
bhartāramātmanā prāpya prāptañca tapasaḥ phalam || 27 ||

athavā sarvamevaitatkrīḍāvilasitaṃ tava |
idantu citraṃ devasya virahaṃ sahase katham || 28 ||

devyuvāca |

sargādau bhavato devādutpattiḥ śrūyate yadā |
tadā prajānāṃ prathamastvaṃ me prathamajaḥ sutaḥ || 29 ||

yadā punaḥ prajāvṛddhyai lalāṭādbhavato bhavaḥ |
utpanno .abhūttadā tvaṃ me guruḥ śvaśurabhāvataḥ || 30 ||

yadā bhavadgirīndraste putro mama pitā svayam |
tadā pitāmahastvaṃ me jāto lokapitāmaha || 31 ||

tadīdṛśasya bhavato lokayātrāvidhāyinaḥ |
vṛttavantaḥpure bhartā kathayiṣye kathaṃ punaḥ || 32 ||

kimatra bahunā dehe yaścāyaṃ mama kālimā |
tyaktvā sattvavidhānena gaurī bhavitumutsahe || 33 ||

brahmovāca |

etāvatā kimarthena tīvraṃ devi tapaḥ kṛtam |
svecchaiva kimaparyāptā krīḍeyaṃ hi tavedṛśī || 34 ||

krīḍā .api ca jaganmātastava lokahitāya vai |
ato mameṣṭamanayā phalaṃ kimapi sādhyatām || 35 ||

niśuṃbhaśuṃbhanāmānau daityau dattavarau mayā |
dṛptau devānprabādhete tvatto labdhastayorvadhaḥ || 36 ||

alaṃ vilaṃbanenātra tvaṃ kṣaṇena sthirā bhava |
śaktirvisṛjyamānā .adya tayormṛtyurbhaviṣyati || 37 ||

brāhmaṇābhyarthitā caiva devī girivarātmajā |
tvakkośaṃ sahasotsṛjya gaurī sā samajāyata || 38 ||

sā tvakkośātmanotsṛṣṭā kauśikī nāma nāmataḥ |
kālī kālāmbudaprakhyā kanyakā samapadyata || 39 ||

sā tu māyātmikā śaktiryoganidrā ca vaiṣṇavī |
śaṃkhacakratriśūlādisāyudhāṣṭamahābhujā || 40 ||

saumyā ghorā ca miśrā ca trinetrā candraśekharā |
ajātapuṃsparśaratiradhṛṣyā cātisundarī || 41 ||

dattā ca brahmaṇe devyā śaktireṣā sanātanī |
niśuṃbhasya ca śuṃbhasya nihantrī daityasiṃhayoḥ || 42 ||

brahmaṇāpi prahṛṣṭena tasyai paramaśaktaye |
prabalaḥ kesarī datto vāhanatve samāgataḥ || 43 ||

vindhye ca vasatiṃ tasyāḥ pūjāmāsavapūrvakaiḥ |
māṃsairmatsyairapūpaiśca nirvartyāsau samādiśat || 44 ||

sā caiva saṃmatā śaktirbrahmaṇo viśvakarmaṇaḥ |
praṇamya mātaraṃ gaurīṃ brahmāṇaṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ || 45 ||

śaktibhiścāpi tulyābhiḥ svātmajābhiranekaśaḥ |
parītā prayayau vindhyaṃ daityendrau hantumudyatā || 46 ||

nihatau ca tayā tatra samare daityapuṃgavau |
tadbāṇaiḥ kāmabāṇaiśca cchinnabhinnāṃgamānasau || 47 ||

tadyuddhavistaraścātra na kṛto .anyatra varṇanāt |
ūhanīyaṃ parasmācca prastutaṃ varṇayāmi vaḥ || 48 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe devīgauratvabhavanaṃ nāma paṃcaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 25 ||

vāyuruvāca |

utpādya kauśikīṃ gaurī brahmaṇe pratipādya tām |
tasya pratyupakārāya pitāmahamathābravīt || 1 ||

devyuvāca |

dṛṣṭaḥ kimeṣa bhavatā śārdūlo madupāśrayaḥ |
anena duṣṭasattvebhyo rakṣitaṃ mattapovanam || 2 ||

mayyarpitamanā eṣa bhajate māmananyadhīḥ |
asya saṃrakṣaṇādanyatpriyaṃ mama na vidyate || 3 ||

bhavitavyamanenāto mamāntaḥpuracāriṇā |
gaṇeśvarapadaṃ cāsmai prītyā dāsyati śaṃkaraḥ || 4 ||

enamagresaraṃ kṛtvā sakhībhirgantumutsahe |
pradīyatāmanujñā me prajānāṃ patinā tvayā || 5 ||

ityuktaḥ prahasanbrahmā devīmmugdhāmiva smayan |
tasya tīvraiḥ purāvṛttairdaurātmyaṃ samavarṇayat || 6 ||

brahmovāca |

paśau devi mṛgāḥ krūrāḥ kva ca te .anugrahaḥ śubhaḥ |
āśīviṣamukhe sākṣādamṛtaṃ kiṃ niṣicyate || 7 ||

vyāghramātreṇa sanneṣa duṣṭaḥ ko .api niśācaraḥ |
anena bhakṣitā gāvo brāhmaṇāśca tapodhanāḥ || 8 ||

tarpayaṃstānyathākāmaṃ kāmarūpī caratyasau |
avaśyaṃ khalu bhoktavyaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ || 9 ||

ataḥ kiṃ kṛpayā kṛtyamīdṛśeṣu durātmasu |
anena devyāḥ kiṃ kṛtyaṃ prakṛtyā kaluṣātmanā || 10 ||

devyuvāca |

yaduktaṃ bhavatā sarvaṃ tathyamastvayamīdṛśaḥ |
tathāpi māṃ prapanno .abhūnna tyājyo māmupāśritaḥ || 11 ||

brahmovāca |

asya bhaktimavijñāya prāgvṛttaṃ te niveditam |
bhaktiścedasya kiṃ pāpairna te bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati || 12 ||

puṇyakarmāpi kiṃ kuryyāttvadīyājñānapekṣayā |
ajā prajñā purāṇī ca tvameva parameśvarī || 13 ||

tvadadhīnā hi sarveṣāṃ bandhamokṣavyavasthitiḥ |
tvadṛte paramā śaktiḥ saṃsiddhiḥ kasya karmaṇā || 14 ||

tvameva vividhā śaktiḥ bhavānāmatha vā svayam |
aśaktaḥ karmakaraṇe kartā vā kiṃ kariṣyati || 15 ||

viṣṇośca mama cānyeṣāṃ devadānavarakṣasām |
tattadaiśvaryasamprāptyai tavaivājñā hi kāraṇam || 16 ||

atītāḥ khalvasaṃkhyātā brahmāṇo harayo bhavāḥ |
anāgatāstvasaṃkhyātāstvadājñānuvidhāyinaḥ || 17 ||

tvāmanārādhya deveśi puruṣārthacatuṣṭayam |
labdhuṃ na śakyamasmābhirapi sarvaiḥ surottamaiḥ || 18 ||

vyatyāso .api bhavetsadyo brahmatvasthāvaratvayoḥ |
sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ cāpi tvayeva sthāpitaṃ yataḥ || 19 ||

tvaṃ hi sarvajagadbhartuśśivasya paramātmanaḥ |
anādimadhyanidhanā śaktirādyā sanātanī || 20 ||

samastalokayātrārthaṃ mūrtimāviśya kāmapi |
krīḍase vividhairbhāvaiḥ kastvāṃ jānāti tattvataḥ || 21 ||

ato duṣkṛtakarmāpi vyāghro .ayaṃ tvadanugrahāt |
prāpnotu paramāṃ siddhimatra kaḥ pratibandhakaḥ || 22 ||

ityātmanaḥ paraṃ bhāvaṃ smārayitvānurūpataḥ |
brahmaṇābhyarthitā gaurī tapaso .api nyavartata || 23 ||

tato devīmanujñāpya brahmaṇyantarhite sati |
devīṃ ca mātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā menāṃ himavatā saha || 24 ||

praṇamyāśvāsya bahudhā pitarau virahāsahau |
tapaḥ praṇayino devī tapovanamahīruhān || 25 ||

viprayogaśucevāgre puṣpabāṣpaṃ vimuṃcataḥ |
tattucchākhāsamārūḍhavihago dīritai rutaiḥ || 26 ||

vyākulaṃ bahudhā dīnaṃ vilāpamiva kurvataḥ |
sakhībhyaḥ kathayantyevaṃ sattvarā bhartṛdarśane || 27 ||

puraskṛtya ca taṃ vyāghraṃ snehātputramivaurasam |
dehasya prabhayā caiva dīpayantī diśo daśa || 28 ||

prayayau mandaraṃ gaurī yatra bhartā maheśvaraḥ |
sarveṣāṃ jagatāṃ dhātā kartā pātā vināśakṛt || 29 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vyāghragativarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 26 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kṛtvā gauraṃ vapurdivyaṃ devī girivarātmajā |
kathaṃ dadarśa bhartāraṃ praviṣṭā manditaṃ satī || 1 ||

praveśasamaye tasyā bhavanadvāragocaraiḥ |
gaṇeśaiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ devastāndṛṣṭvā kintadā .akarot || 2 ||

vāyuruvāca |

pravaktumaṃjasā .aśakyaḥ tādṛśaḥ paramo rasaḥ |
yena praṇayagarbheṇa bhāvo bhāvavatāṃ hṛtaḥ || 3 ||

dvāsthaissasaṃbhramaireva devo devyāgamotsukaḥ |
śaṃkamānā praviṣṭāntastañca sā samapaśyata || 4 ||

taistaiḥ praṇayabhāvaiśca bhavanāntaravarttibhiḥ |
gaṇendrairvanditā vācā praṇanāma triyambakam || 5 ||

praṇamya notthitā yāvattāvattāṃ parameśvaraḥ |
pragṛhya dorbhyāmāśliṣya paritaḥ parayā mudā || 6 ||

svāṃke dhartuṃ pravṛtto .api sā paryyaṃke nyaṣīdata |
paryyaṃkato balāddevīṃ soGkamāropya susmitām || 7 ||

sasmito vivṛtairnetraistadvaktraṃ prapibanniva |
tayā saṃbhāṣaṇāyeśaḥ pūrvabhāṣitamabravīt || 8 ||

devadeva uvāca |

sā daśā ca vyatītā kiṃ tava sarvāṃgasundari |
yasyāmanunayopāyaḥ ko .api kopānna labhyate || 9 ||

svecchayāpi na kālīti nānyavarṇavatīti ca |
tvatsvabhāvāhṛtaṃ cittaṃ subhru ciṃtāvahaṃ mama || 10 ||

vismṛtaḥ paramo bhāvaḥ kathaṃ svecchāṃgayogataḥ |
na sambhavanti ye tatra cittakāluṣyahetavaḥ || 11 ||

pṛthagjanavadanyonyaṃ vipriyasyāpi kāraṇam |
āvayorapi yadyasti nāstyevaitaccarācaram || 12 ||

ahamagniśironiṣṭhastvaṃ somaśirasi sthitā |
agnīṣomātmakaṃ viśvamāvābhyāṃ samadhiṣṭhitam || 13 ||

jagaddhitāya caratoḥ svecchādhṛtaśarīrayoḥ |
āvayorviprayoge hi syānnirālambanaṃ jagat || 14 ||

asti hetvantaraṃ cātra śāstrayuktiviniścitam |
vāgarthamiva me vaitajjagatsthāvarajaṃgamam || 15 ||

tvaṃ hi vāgamṛtaṃ sākṣādahamarthāmṛtaṃ param |
dvayamapyamṛtaṃ kasmādviyuktamupapadyate || 16 ||

vidyāpratyāyikā tvaṃ me vedyo .ahaṃ pratyayāttava |
vidyāvedyātmanoreva viśleṣaḥ kathamāvayoḥ || 17 ||

na karmaṇā sṛjāmīdaṃ jagatpratisṛjāmi ca |
sarvasyājñaikalabhyatvādājñātvaṃ hi garīyasī || 18 ||

ājñaikasāramaiśvaryyaṃ yasmātsvātantryalakṣaṇam |
ājñayā viprayuktasya caiśvaryyaṃ mama kīdṛśam || 19 ||

na kadācidavasthānamāvayorviprayuktayoḥ |
devānāṃ kāryyamuddiśya līloktiṃ kṛtavānaham || 20 ||

tvayāpyaviditaṃ nāsti kathaṃ kupitavatyasi |
tatastrilokarakṣārthe kopo mayyapi te kṛtaḥ || 21 ||

yadanarthāya bhūtānāṃ na tadasti khalu tvayi |
iti priyaṃvade sākṣādīśvare parameśvare || 22 ||

śṛṃgārabhāvasārāṇāṃ janmabhūmirakṛtrimā |
svabhartrā lalitantathyamuktaṃ matvā smitottaram || 23 ||

lajjayā na kimapyūce kauśikī varṇanātparam |
tadeva varṇayāmyadya śṛṇu devyāśca varṇanam || 24 ||

devyuvāca |

kiṃ devena na sā dṛṣṭā yā sṛṣṭā kauśikī mayā |
tādṛśī kanyakā loke na bhūtā na bhaviṣyati || 25 ||

tasyā vīryyaṃ balaṃ vindhyanilayaṃ vijayaṃ tathā |
śuṃbhasya ca niśuṃbhasya māraṇe ca raṇe tayoḥ || 26 ||

pratyakṣaphaladānaṃ ca lokāya bhajate sadā |
lokānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ śaśvadbrahmā vijñāpayiṣyati || 27 ||

iti saṃbhāṣamāṇāyā devyā evājñayā tadā |
vyāghraḥ sakhyā samānīya puro .avasthāpitastadā || 28 ||

taṃ prekṣyāha punardevī devānītamupāyatam |
vyāghraṃ paśya na cānena sadṛśo madupāsakaḥ || 29 ||

anena duṣṭasaṃghebhyo rakṣitaṃ mattapovanam |
atīva mama bhaktaśca viśrabdhaśca svarakṣaṇāt || 30 ||

svadeśaṃ ca parityajya prasādārthaṃ samāgataḥ |
yadi prītirabhūnmattaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ karoṣi me || 31 ||

nityamantaḥpuradvāri niyogānnandinaḥ svayam |
rakṣibhissaha taccihnairvartatāmayamīśvara || 32 ||

vāyuruvāca |

madhuraṃ praṇayodarkaṃ śrutvā devyāḥ śubhaṃ vacaḥ |
prīto .asmītyāha taṃ devassa cādṛśyata tatkṣaṇāt || 33 ||

bibhradvetralatāṃ haimīṃ ratnacitraṃ ca kaṃcukam |
churikāmuragaprakhyāṃ gaṇeśo rakṣaveṣadhṛk || 34 ||

yasmātsomo mahādevo nandī cānena nanditaḥ |
somanandīti vikhyātastasmādeṣa samākhyayā || 35 ||

itthaṃ devyāḥ priyaṃ kṛtvā devaścarddhendubhūṣaṇaḥ |
bhūṣayāmāsa tandivyairbhūṣaṇai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ || 36 ||

tatassa gaurīṃ giriśo girīndrajāṃ sagauravāṃ sarvamanoharāṃ haraḥ |
paryyaṃkamāropya varāṃgabhūṣaṇairvibhūṣayāmāsa śaśāṃkabhūṣaṇaḥ || 37 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe saptaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 27 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

devīṃ samādadhānena devenedaṃ kimīritam |
agniṣomātmakaṃ viśvaṃ vāgarthātmakamityapi || 1 ||

ājñaikasāramaiśvaryyamājñā tvamiti coditam |
tadidaṃ śrotumicchāmo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ || 2 ||

vāyuruvāca |

agnirityucyate raudrī ghorā yā taijasī tanuḥ |
somaḥ śākto .amṛtamayaḥ śakteḥ śāntikarī tanuḥ || 3 ||

amṛtaṃ yatpratiṣṭhā sā tejo vidyā kalā svayam |
bhūtasūkṣmeṣu sarveṣu ta eva rasatejasī || 4 ||

dvividhā tejaso vṛttisūryyātmā cānalātmikā |
tathaiva rasavṛttiśca somātmā ca jalātmikā || 5 ||

vidyudādimayantejo madhurādimayo rasaḥ |
tejorasavibhedaistu dhṛtametaccarācaram || 6 ||

agneramṛtaniṣpattiramṛtenāgniredhate |
ata eva hi vikrāntamagnīṣomaṃ jagaddhitam || 7 ||

haviṣe sasyasampattirvṛṣṭiḥ sasyābhivṛddhaye |
vṛṣṭereva havistasmādagnīṣomadhṛtaṃ jagat || 8 ||

agnirūrddhvaṃ jvalatyeṣa yāvatsaumyaṃ parāmṛtam |
yāvadagnyāspadaṃ saumyamamṛtaṃ ca sravatyadhaḥ || 9 ||

ata eva hi kālāgniradhastācchaktirūrddhvataḥ |
yāvadādahanaṃ corddhvamadhaścāplāvanaṃ bhavet || 10 ||

ādhāraśaktyaiva dhṛtaḥ kālāgnirayamūrddhvagaḥ |
tathaiva nimnagaḥ somaśśivaśaktipadāspadaḥ || 11 ||

śivaścorddhvamadhaśśaktirūrddhvaṃ śaktiradhaḥ śivaḥ |
taditthaṃ śivaśaktibhyānnāvyāptamiha kiñcana || 12 ||

asakṛccāgninā dagdhaṃ jagadyadbhasmasātkṛtam |
agnervīryamidaṃ cāhustadvīryaṃ bhasma yattataḥ || 13 ||

yaścetthaṃ bhasmasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā snāti ca bhasmanā |
agnirityādibhirmantrairbaddhaḥ pāśātpramucyate || 14 ||

agnervīryaṃ tu yadbhasma somenāplāvitampunaḥ |
ayogayuktyā prakṛteradhikārāya kalpate || 15 ||

yogayuktyā tu tadbhasma plāvyamānaṃ samantataḥ |
śāktenāmṛtavarṣeṇa cādhikārānnivartayet || 16 ||

ato mṛtyuṃjayāyetthamamṛtaplāvanaṃ sadā |
śivaśaktyamṛtasparśe labdhaṃ yena kuto mṛtiḥ || 17 ||

yo veda dahanaṃ guhyaṃ plāvanaṃ ca yathoditam |
agnīṣomapadaṃ hitvā na sa bhūyo .abhijāyate || 18 ||

śivāgninā tanuṃ dagdhvā śaktisaumyā mṛtena yaḥ |
plāvayedyogamārgeṇa so .amṛtatvāya kalpate || 19 ||

hṛdi kṛtvemamarthaṃ vai devena samudāhṛtam |
agnīṣomātmakaṃ viśvaṃ jagadityanurūpataḥ || 20 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe bhasmatattvavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 28 ||

vāyuruvāca |

nivedayāmi jagato vāgarthātmyaṃ kṛtaṃ yathā |
ṣaḍadhvavedanaṃ samyak samāsānna tu vistarāt || 1 ||

nāsti kaścidaśabdārtho nāpi śabdo nirarthakaḥ |
tato hi samaye śabdassarvassarvārthabodhakaḥ || 2 ||

prakṛteḥ pariṇāmo .ayaṃ dvidhā śabdārthabhāvanā |
tāmāhuḥ prākṛtīṃ mūrtiṃ śivayoḥ paramātmanoḥ || 3 ||

śabdātmikā vibhūtiryā sā tridhā kathyate budhaiḥ |
sthūlā sūkṣmā parā ceti sthūlā yā śrutigocarā || 4 ||

sūkṣmā cintāmayī proktā ciṃtayā rahitā parā |
yā śaktiḥ sā parā śaktiśśivatattvasamāśrayā || 5 ||

jñānaśaktisamāyogādicchopodbalikā tathā |
sarvaśaktisamaṣṭyātmā śaktitattvasamākhyayā || 6 ||

samastakāryajātasya mūlaprakṛtitāṃ gatā |
saiva kuṇḍalinī māyā śuddhādhvaparamā satī || 7 ||

sā vibhāgasvarūpaiva ṣaḍadhvātmā vijṛṃbhate |
tatra śabdāstrayo .adhvānastrayaścārthāḥ samīritāḥ || 8 ||

sarveṣāmapi vai puṃsāṃ naijaśuddhyanurūpataḥ |
layabhogādhikārāssyussarvatattvavibhāgataḥ || 9 ||

kalābhistāni tattvāni vyāptānyeva yathātatham |
parasyāḥ prakṛterādau paṃcadhā pariṇāmataḥ || 10 ||

kalāśca tā nivṛttyādyāḥ paryyāptā iti niścayaḥ |
mantrādhvā ca padādhvā ca varṇādhvā ceti śabdataḥ || 11 ||

bhuvanādhvā ca tattvādhvā kalādhvā cārthataḥ kramāt |
atrānyonyaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vyāpyavyāpakatocyate || 12 ||

mantrāḥ sarvaiḥ padairvyāptā vākyabhāvātpadāni ca |
varṇairvarṇasamūhaṃ hi padamāhurvipaścitaḥ || 13 ||

varṇāstu bhuvanairvyāptāsteṣāṃ teṣūpalaṃbhanāt |
bhuvanānyapi tattvaughairutpattyāntarbahiṣkramāt || 14 ||

vyāptāni kāraṇaistattvairārabdhatvādanekaśaḥ |
antarādutthitānīha bhuvanāni tu kānicit || 15 ||

paurāṇikāni cānyāni vijñeyāni śivāgame |
sāṃkhyayogaprasiddhāni tattvānyapi ca kānicit || 16 ||

śivaśāstraprasiddhāni tatonyānyapi kṛtsnaśaḥ |
kalābhistāni tattvāni vyāptānyeva yathātatham || 17 ||

parasyāḥ prakṛterādau paṃcadhā pariṇāmataḥ |
kalāśca tā nivṛttyādyā vyāptāḥ paṃca yathottaram || 18 ||

vyāpikātaḥ parā śaktiravibhaktā ṣaḍadhvanām |
paraprakṛtibhāvasya tatsattvācchivatattvataḥ || 19 ||

śaktyādi ca pṛthivyantaṃ śivatattvasamudbhavam |
vyāptamekena tenaiva mṛdā kuṃbhādikaṃ yathā || 20 ||

śaivaṃ tatparamaṃ dhāma yatprāpyaṃ ṣaḍbhiradhvabhiḥ |
vyāpikā .avyāpikā śaktiḥ paṃcatattvaviśodhanāt || 21 ||

nivṛttyā rudraparyyantaṃ sthitiraṇḍasya śodhyate |
pratiṣṭhayā tadūrdhvaṃ tu yāvadavyaktagocaram || 22 ||

tadūrdhvaṃ vidyayā madhye yāvadviśveśvarāvadhi |
śāntyā tadūrdhvaṃ madhvānte viśuddhiḥ śāntyatītayā || 23 ||

yāmāhuḥ paramaṃ vyoma paraprakṛtiyogataḥ |
etāni paṃcatattvāni yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat || 24 ||

tatraiva sarvamevedaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ khalu sādhakaiḥ |
adhvavyāptimavijñāya śuddhiṃ yaḥ kartumicchati || 25 ||

sa vipralambhakaḥ śuddhernālamprāpayituṃ phalam |
vṛthā pariśramastasya nirayāyaiva kevalam || 26 ||

śaktipātasamāyogādṛte tattvāni tattvataḥ |
tadvyāptistadvivṛddhiśca jñātumevaṃ na śakyate || 27 ||

śaktirājñā parā śaivī cidrūpā marameśvarī |
śivo .adhitiṣṭhatyakhilaṃ yayā kāraṇabhūtayā || 28 ||

nātmano naiva māyaiṣā na vikāro vicārataḥ |
na bandho nāpi muktiśca bandhamuktividhāyinī || 29 ||

sarvaiśvaryaparākāṣṭā śivasya vyabhicāriṇī |
samānadharmiṇī tasya taistairbhāvairviśeṣataḥ || 30 ||

sa tayaiva gṛhī sāpi tenaiva gṛhiṇī sadā |
tayorapatyaṃ yatkāryaṃ paraprakṛtijaṃ jagat || 31 ||

sa kartā kāraṇaṃ seti tayorbhedo vyavasthitaḥ |
eka eva śivaḥ sākṣāddvidhā .asau samavasthitaḥ || 32 ||

strīpuṃsabhāvena tayorbheda ityapi kecana |
apare tu parā śaktiḥ śivasya samavāyinī || 33 ||

prabheva bhānościdrūpā bhinnaiveti vyavasthitaḥ |
tasmācchivaḥ paro hetustasyājñā parameśvarī || 34 ||

tayaiva preritā śaivī mūlaprakṛtiravyayā |
mahāmāyā ca māyā ca prakṛtistriguṇeti ca || 35 ||

trividhā kāryavedhena sā prasūte ṣaḍadhvanaḥ |
sa vāgarthamayaścādhvā ṣaḍvidho nikhilaṃ jagat || 36 ||

asyaiva vistaraṃ prāhuḥ śāstrajātamaśeṣataḥ || 37 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vāgarthakatattvavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 29 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

caritāni vicitrāṇi gṛhyāṇi gahanāni ca |
durvijñeyāni devaiśca mohayanti manāṃsi naḥ || 1 ||

śivayostattvasambandhe na doṣa upalabhyate |
caritaiḥ prākṛto bhāvastayorapi vibhāvyate || 2 ||

brahmādayo .api lokānāṃ sṛṣṭisthityantahetavaḥ |
nigrahānugrahau prāpya śivasya vaśavartinaḥ || 3 ||

śivaḥ punarna kasyāpi nigrahānugrahāspadam |
ato .anāyattamaiśvaryaṃ tasyaiveti viniścitam || 4 ||

yadyevamīdṛśaiśvaryyaṃ tattu svātantryalakṣaṇam |
svabhāvasiddhaṃ caitasya mūrtimattāspadaṃ bhavet || 5 ||

na mūrtiśca svatantrasya ghaṭate mūlahetunā |
mūrterapi ca kāryatvāttatsiddhiḥ syādahaitukī || 6 ||

sarvatra paramo bhāvo .aparamaścānya ucyate |
paramāparamau bhāvau kathamekatra saṃgatau || 7 ||

niṣphalo hi svabhāvo .asya paramaḥ paramātmanaḥ |
sa eva sakalaḥ kasmātsvabhāvo hyaviparyayaḥ || 8 ||

svabhāvo viparītaścetsvatantraḥ svecchayā yadi |
na karoti kimīśāno nityānityaviparyayam || 9 ||

mūrtātmā sakalaḥ kaścitsa cānyo niṣphalaḥ śivaḥ |
śivenādhiṣṭhitaśceti sarvatra laghu kathyate || 10 ||

mūrtyātmaiva tadā mūrtiḥ śivasyāsya bhavediti |
tasya mūrtau mūrtimatoḥ pāratantryaṃ hi niścitam || 11 ||

anyathā nirapekṣeṇa mūrtiḥ svīkriyate katham |
mūrtisvīkaraṇaṃ tasmānmūrtau sādhyaphalepsayā || 12 ||

na hi svecchāśarīratvaṃ svātantryāyopapadyate |
svecchaiva tādṛśī puṃsāṃ yasmātkarmānusāriṇī || 13 ||

svīkartuṃ svecchayā dehaṃ hātuṃ ca prabhavantyuta |
brahmādayaḥ piśācāntāḥ kiṃ te karmātivartinaḥ || 14 ||

icchayā dehanirmāṇamindrajālopamaṃ viduḥ |
aṇimādiguṇaiśvaryyavaśīkārānatikramāt || 15 ||

viśvarūpaṃ dadhadviṣṇurdadhīcena maharṣiṇā |
yudhyatā samupālabdhastadrūpaṃ dadhatā svayam || 16 ||

sarvasmādadhikasyāpi śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
śarīravattayānyātmasādharmyaṃ pratibhāti naḥ || 17 ||

sarvānugrāhakaṃ prāhuśśivaṃ paramakāraṇam |
sa nirgṛhṇāti devānāṃ sarvānugrāhakaḥ katham || 18 ||

ciccheda bahuśo devo brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ |
śivanindāṃ prakurvvantaṃ putreti kumaterhaṭhāt || 19 ||

viṣṇorapi nṛsiṃhasya rabhasā śarabhākṛtiḥ |
bibheda padbhyāmākramya hṛdayaṃ nakharaiḥ kharaiḥ || 20 ||

devastrīṣu ca deveṣu dakṣasyādhvarakāraṇāt |
vīreṇa vīrabhadreṇa na hi kaścidadaṇḍitaḥ || 21 ||

puratrayaṃ ca sastrīkaṃ sadaityaṃ saha bālakaiḥ |
kṣaṇenaikena devena netrāgnerindhanīkṛtam || 22 ||

prajānāṃ ratihetuśca kāmo ratipatissvayam |
krośatāmeva devānāṃ huto netrahutāśane || 23 ||

gāvaśca kaściddugdhaughaṃ sravantyo mūrdhni khecarāḥ |
saruṣā prekṣya devena tatkṣaṇe bhasmasātkṛtaḥ || 24 ||

jalaṃdharāsuro dīrṇaścakrīkṛtya jalaṃ padā |
baddhvānantena yo viṣṇuṃ cikṣepa śatayojanam || 25 ||

tameva jalasaṃdhāyī śūlenaiva jaghāna saḥ |
taccakraṃ tapasā labdhvā labdhavīryyo harissadā || 26 ||

jighāṃsatāṃ surārīṇāṃ kulaṃ nirghṛṇacetasām |
triśūlenāndhakasyoraḥ śikhinaivopatāpitam || 27 ||

kaṇṭhātkālāṃganāṃ sṛṣṭvā dārako .api nipātitaḥ |
kauśikīṃ janayitvā tu gauryyāstvakkośagocarām || 28 ||

śuṃbhassaha niśuṃbhena prāpito maraṇaṃ raṇe |
śrutaṃ ca mahadākhyānaṃ skānde skandasamāśrayam || 29 ||

vadhārthe tārakākhyasya daityendrasyendravidviṣaḥ |
brahmaṇābhyarthito devo mandarāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ || 30 ||

vihṛtya suciraṃ devyā vihārā .atiprasaGgataḥ |
rasāṃ rasātalaṃ nītāmiva kṛtvābhidhāṃ tataḥ || 31 ||

devīṃ ca vaṃcayaṃstasyāṃ svavīryamatidurvaham |
avisṛjya visṛjyāgnau haviḥ pūtamivāmṛtam || 32 ||

gaṃgādiṣvapi nikṣipya vahnidvārā tadaṃśataḥ |
tatsamāhṛtya śanakaistokaṃstokamitastataḥ || 33 ||

svāhayā kṛttikārūpātsvabhartrā ramamāṇayā |
suvarṇībhūtayā nyastaṃ merau śaravaṇe kvacit || 34 ||

saṃdīpayitvā kālena tasya bhāsā diśo daśa |
rañjayitvā girīnsarvānkāṃcanīkṛtya meruṇā || 35 ||

tataścireṇa kālena saṃjāte tatra tejasi |
kumāre sukumārāṃge kumārāṇāṃ nidarśane || 36 ||

tacchaiśavaṃ svarūpaṃ ca tasya dṛṣṭvā manoharam |
saha devasurairlokairvismite ca vimohite || 37 ||

devo .api svayamāyātaḥ putradarśanalālasaḥ |
saha devyāṃkamāropya tato .asya smeramānanam || 38 ||

pītāmṛtamiva snehavivaśenāntarātmanā |
deveṣvapi ca paśyatsu vītarāgaistapasvibhiḥ || 39 ||

svasya vakṣaḥsthale svairaṃ nartayitvā kumārakam |
anubhūya ca tatkrīḍāṃ saṃbhāvya ca parasparam || 40 ||

stanyamājñāpayandevyāḥ pāyayitvāmṛtopamam |
tavāvatāro jagatāṃ hitāyetyanuśāsya ca || 41 ||

svayandevaśca devī ca na tṛptimupajagmatuḥ |
tataḥ śakreṇa saṃdhāya bibhyatā tārakāsurāt || 42 ||

kārayitvābhiṣekaṃ ca senāpatye divaukasām |
putramantarataḥ kṛtvā devena tripuradviṣā || 43 ||

svayamantarhitenaiva skandamindrādirakṣitam |
tacchaktyā krauñcabhedinyā yudhi kālāgnikalpayā || 44 ||

cheditaṃ tārakasyāpi śiraśśakrabhiyā saha |
stutiṃ cakrurviśeṣeṇa haridhātṛmukhāḥ surāḥ || 45 ||

tathā rakṣodhipaḥ sākṣādrāvaṇo balagarvitaḥ |
uddharansvabhujairdīrghaiḥ kailāsaṃ girimātmanaḥ || 46 ||

tadāgo .asahamānasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ |
padāṃguṣṭhaparispandānmamajja mṛdito bhuvi || 47 ||

baṭoḥ kenacidarthena svāśritasya gatāyuṣaḥ |
tvarayāgatya devena pādāntaṃ gamitontakaḥ || 48 ||

svavāhanamavijñāya vṛṣendraṃ vaḍavānalaḥ |
sagalagrahamānītastato .astyekodakaṃ jagat || 49 ||

alokaviditaistaistairvṛttairānandasundaraiḥ |
aṃgahārasvasenedamasakṛccālitaṃ jagat || 50 ||

śānta eva sadā sarvamanugṛhṇāti cecchivaḥ |
sarvāṇi pūrayedeva kathaṃ śaktena mocayet || 51 ||

anādikarma vaicitryamapi nātra niyāmakam |
kāraṇaṃ khalu karmāpi bhavedīśvarakāritam || 52 ||

kimatra bahunoktena nāstikyaṃ hetukārakam |
yathā hyāśu nivarteta tathā kathaya māruta || 53 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śivatattvapraśno nāma triṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 30 ||

vāyuruvāca |

sthane saṃśayitaṃ viprā bhavadbhirhetucoditaiḥ |
jijñāsā hi na nāstikyaṃ sādhayetsādhubuddhiṣu || 1 ||

pramaṇamatra vakṣyāmi satāmmohanivartakam |
asatāṃ tvanyathābhāvaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ || 2 ||

śivasya paripūrṇasya parānugrahamantarā |
na kiṃcidapi kartavyamiti sādhu viniścitam || 3 ||

svabhāva eva paryyāptaḥ parānugrahakarmaṇi |
anyathā nissvabhavena na kimapyanugṛhyate || 4 ||

paraṃ sarvamanugrāhyaṃ paśupāśātmakaṃ jagat |
parasyānugrahārthaṃ tu patyurājñāsamanvayaḥ || 5 ||

patirājñāpakaḥ sarvamanugṛhṇāti sarvvadā |
tadarthamarthasvīkāre paratantraḥ kathaṃ śivaḥ || 6 ||

anugrāhyanapekṣo .asti na hi kaścidanugrahaḥ |
ataḥ svātantryaśabdārthānanapekṣatvalakṣaṇaḥ || 7 ||

etatpunaranugrāhyaṃ paratantraṃ tadiṣyate |
anugrahādṛte tasya bhuktimuktyorananvayāt || 8 ||

mūrtātmano .apyanugrāhyā śivājñānanivartanāt |
ajñānādhiṣṭhitaṃ śambhorna kiṃcidiha vidyate || 9 ||

yenopalabhyate .asmābhissakalenāpi niṣkalaḥ |
sa mūrtyātmā śivaḥ śaivamūrtirityupacaryate || 10 ||

na hyasau niṣkalaḥ sākṣācchivaḥ paramakāraṇam |
sākāreṇānubhāvena kenāpyanupalakṣitaḥ || 11 ||

pramāṇagamyatāmātraṃ tatsvabhāvopapādakam |
na tāvatātropekṣādhīrupalakṣaṇamantarā || 12 ||

ātmopamolvaṇaṃ sākṣānmūrtireva hi kācana |
śivasya mūrtirmūrtyātmā parastasyopalakṣaṇam || 13 ||

yathā kāṣṭheṣvanārūḍho na vahnirupalabhyate |
evaṃ śivo .api mūrtyātmanyanārūḍha iti sthitiḥ || 14 ||

yathāgnimānayetyukte jvalatkāṣṭhādṛte svayam |
nāgnirānīyate tadvatpūjyo mūrtyātmanā śivaḥ || 15 ||

ata eva hi pūjādau mūrtyātmaparikalpanam |
mūrtyātmani kṛtaṃ sākṣācchiva eva kṛtaṃ yataḥ || 16 ||

liṃgādāvapi tatkṛtyamarcāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
tattanmūrtyātmabhāvena śivo .asmābhirupāsyate || 17 ||

yathānugṛhyate so .api mūrtyātmā pārameṣṭhinā |
tathā mūrtyātmaniṣṭhena śivena paśavo vayam || 18 ||

lokānugrahaṇāyaiva śivena parameṣṭhinā |
sadāśivādayassarve mūrtyātmano .apyadhiṣṭhitāḥ || 19 ||

ātmanāmeva bhogāya mokṣāya ca viśeṣataḥ |
tattvātattvasvarūpeṣu mūrtyātmasu śivānvayaḥ || 20 ||

bhogaḥ karmavipākātmā sukhaduḥkhātmako mataḥ |
na ca karma śivo .astīti tasya bhogaḥ kimātmakaḥ || 21 ||

sarvaṃ śivo .anugṛhṇāti na nigṛhṇāti kiṃcana |
nigṛhṇatāṃ tu ye doṣāśśive teṣāmasaṃbhavāt || 22 ||

ye punarnigrahāḥ kecidbrahmādiṣu nidarśitāḥ |
te .api lokahitāyaiva kṛtāḥ śrīkaṇṭhamūrtinā || 23 ||

brahmāṇḍasyādhipatyaṃ hi śrīkaṇṭhasya na saṃśayaḥ |
śrīkaṇṭhākhyāṃ śivo mūrtiṃ krīḍatīmadhitiṣṭhati || 24 ||

sadoṣā eva devādyā nigṛhītā yathoditam |
tatastepi vipāpmānaḥ prajāścāpi gatajvarāḥ || 25 ||

nigraho .api svarūpeṇa viduṣāṃ na jugupsitaḥ |
ata eva hi daṇḍyeṣu daṇḍo rājñāṃ praśasyate || 26 ||

yatsiddhirīśvaratvena kāryavargasya kṛtsnaśaḥ |
na sa cedīśatāṃ kuryājjagataḥ kathamīśvaraḥ || 27 ||

īśecchā ca vidhātṛtvaṃ vidherājñāpanaṃ param |
ājñāvaśyamidaṃ kuryānna kuryāditi śāsanam || 28 ||

tacchāsanānuvartitvaṃ sādhubhāvasya lakṣaṇam |
viparītasamādhoḥ syānna sarvaṃ tattu dṛśyate || 29 ||

sādhu saṃrakṣaṇīyaṃ cedvinivartyamasādhu yat |
nivartate ca sāmāderante daṇḍo hi sādhanam || 30 ||

hitārthalakṣaṇaṃ cedaṃ daṇḍāntamanuśāsanam |
ato yadviparītaṃ tadahitaṃ saṃpracakṣate || 31 ||

hite sadā niṣaṇṇānāmīśvarasya nidarśanam |
sa kathaṃ duṣyate sadbhirasatāmeva nigrahāt || 32 ||

ayuktakāriṇo loke garhaṇīyāvivekitā |
yadudvejayate lokantadayuktaṃ pracakṣate || 33 ||

sarvo .api nigraho loke na ca vidveṣapūrvakaḥ |
na hi dveṣṭi pitā putraṃ yo nigṛhyāti śikṣayet || 34 ||

mādhyasthenāpi nigrāhyānyo nigṛhṇāti mārgataḥ |
tasyāpyavaśyaṃ yatkiṃcinnairghṛṇyamanuvartate || 35 ||

anyathā na hinastyeva sadoṣānapyasau parān |
hinasti cāyamapyajñānparaṃ mādhyasthyamācaran || 36 ||

tasmādduḥkhātmikāṃ hiṃsāṃ kurvāṇo yaḥ sanirghṛṇaḥ |
iti nirbandhayantyeke niyamo neti cāpare || 37 ||

nidānajñasya bhiṣajo rugṇo hiṃsāṃ prayuṃjataḥ |
na kiṃcidapi nairghṛṇyaṃ ghṛṇaivātra prayojikā || 38 ||

ghṛṇāpi na guṇāyaiva hiṃsreṣu pratiyogiṣu |
tādṛśeṣu ghṛṇī bhrāntyā ghṛṇāntaritanirghṛṇaḥ || 39 ||

upekṣāpīha doṣāha rakṣyeṣu pratiyogiṣu |
śaktau satyāmupekṣāto rakṣyassadyo vipadyate || 40 ||

sarpasyā .a.asyagatampaśyanyastu rakṣyamupekṣate |
doṣābhāsānsamutprekṣya phalataḥ so .api nirghṛṇaḥ || 41 ||

tasmād ghṛṇā guṇāyaiva sarvatheti na saṃmatam |
saṃmataṃ prāptakāmitvaṃ sarvaṃ tvanyadasammatam || 42 ||

mūrtyātmasvapi rāgādyā doṣāḥ santyeva vastutaḥ |
tathāpi teṣāmevaite na śivasya tu sarvathā |
agnāvapi samāviṣṭaṃ tāmraṃ khalu sakālikam // 43 || 43 ||

iti nāgnirasau duṣyettāmrasaṃsargakāraṇāt |
nāgneraśucisaṃsargādaśucitvamapekṣate || 44 ||

aśucestvagnisaṃyogācchucitvamapi jāyate |
evaṃ śodhyātmasaṃsargānna hyaśuddhaḥ śivo bhavet || 45 ||

śivasaṃsargatastveṣa śodhyātmaiva hi śudhyati |
ayasyagnau samāviṣṭe dāho .agnereva nāyasaḥ || 46 ||

mūrttātmanyevamaiśvaryyamīśvarasyaiva nātmanām |
na hi kāṣṭhaṃ jvalatyūrddhvamagnireva jvalatyasau || 47 ||

kāṣṭhasyāṃgāratā nāgnerevamatrāpi yojyatām |
ata eva jagatyasminkāṣṭhapāṣāṇamṛtsvapi || 48 ||

śivāveśavaśādeva śivatvamupacaryate |
maitryādayo guṇā gauṇāstasmātte bhinnavṛttayaḥ || 49 ||

tairguṇairuparaktānāṃ doṣāya ca guṇāya ca |
yattu gauṇamagauṇaṃ ca tatsarvamanugṛhṇataḥ |
na guṇāya na doṣāya śivasya guṇavṛttayaḥ // 50 || 50 ||

na cānugrahaśabdārthaṃ gauṇamāhurvipaścitaḥ |
saṃsāramocanaṃ kiṃ tu śaivamājñāmayaṃ hitam || 51 ||

hitaṃ tadājñākaraṇaṃ yaddhitaṃ tadanugrahaḥ |
sarvaṃ hite niyuñjāvaḥ sarvānugrahakārakaḥ || 52 ||

yastūpakāraśabdārthastamapyāhuranugraham |
tasyāpi hitarūpatvācchivaḥ sarvopakārakaḥ || 53 ||

hite sadā niyuktaṃ tu sarvaṃ cidacidātmakam |
svabhāvapratibandhaṃ tatsamaṃ na labhate hitam || 54 ||

yathā vikāsayatyeva raviḥ padmāni bhānubhiḥ |
samaṃ na vikasantyeva svasvabhāvānurodhataḥ || 55 ||

svabhāvo .api hi bhāvānāṃ bhāvino .arthasya kāraṇam |
na hi svabhāvo naśyantamarthaṃ kartṛṣu sādhayet || 56 ||

suvarṇameva nāṃgāraṃ drāvayatyagnisaṃgamaḥ |
evaṃ pakvamalāneva mocayenna śivaparān || 57 ||

yadyathā bhavituṃ yogyaṃ tattathā na bhavetsvayam |
vinā bhāvanayā kartā svatantrassantato bhavet || 58 ||

svabhāvavimalo yadvatsarvānugrāhakaśśivaḥ |
svabhāvamalināstadvadātmano jīvasaṃjñitāḥ || 59 ||

anyathā saṃsarantyete niyamānna śivaḥ katham |
karmamāyānubandhosya saṃsāraḥ kathyate budhaiḥ || 60 ||

anubandho .ayamasyaiva na śivasyeti hetumān |
sa heturātmanāmeva nijo nāgantuko malaḥ || 61 ||

āgantukatve kasyāpi bhāvyaṃ kenāpi hetunā |
yo .ayaṃ heturasāvekastvavicitrasvabhāvataḥ || 62 ||

ātmatāyāḥ samatve .api baddhā muktāḥ pare yataḥ |
baddheṣveva punaḥ kecillayabhogādhikārataḥ || 63 ||

jñānaiśvaryādivaiṣamyaṃ bhajante sottarādharāḥ |
kecinmūrtyātmatāṃ yānti kecidāsannagocarāḥ || 64 ||

mūrtyātmasu śivāḥ kecidadhvanāṃ mūrddhasu sthitāḥ |
madhye maheśvarā rudrāstvarvācīnapade sthitāḥ || 65 ||

āsanne .api ca māyāyāḥ parasmātkāraṇāttrayam |
tatrāpyātmā sthito .adhastādantarātmā ca madhyataḥ || 66 ||

parastātparamātmeti brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ |
vartante vasavaḥ kecitparamātmapadāśrayāḥ || 67 ||

antarātmapade kecitkecidātmapade tathā |
śāntyatītapade śaivāḥ śānte māheśvare tataḥ || 68 ||

vidyāyāntu yathā raudrāḥ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ tu vaiṣṇavāḥ |
nivṛttau ca tathātmāno brahmā brahmāṃgayonayaḥ || 69 ||

devayonyaṣṭakaṃ mukhyaṃ mānuṣyamatha madhyamam |
pakṣyādayo .adhamāḥ paṃcayonayastāścaturdaśa || 70 ||

uttarādharabhāvo .api jñeyassaṃsāriṇo malaḥ |
yathāmabhāvo muktasya pūrvaṃ paścāttu pakvatā || 71 ||

malo .apyāmaśca pakvaśca bhavetsaṃsārakāraṇam |
āme tvadharatā puṃsāṃ pakve tūttaratā kramāt || 72 ||

paśvātmānastridhābhinnā ekadvitrimalāḥ kramāt |
atrottarā ekamalā dvimalā madhyamā matāḥ |
trimalāstvadhamā jñeyā yathottaramadhiṣṭhitāḥ // 73 || 73 ||

trimalānadhitiṣṭhanti dvimalaikamalāḥ kramāt |
itthamaupādhiko bhedo viśvasya parikalpitaḥ || 74 ||

ekadvitrimalānsarvāñchiva eko .adhitiṣṭhati |
aśivātmakamapyetacchivenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yathā || 75 ||

arudrātmakamityevaṃ rudrairjagadadhiṣṭhitam |
aṇḍāntā hi mahābhūmiśśatarudrādyadhiṣṭhitā || 76 ||

māyāntamantarikṣaṃ tu hyamareśādibhiḥ kramāt |
aṃguṣṭhamātraparyantaissamantātsantataṃ tatam || 77 ||

mahāmāyāvasānā dyaurvāyvādyairbhuvanādhipaiḥ |
anāśritāntairadhvāntarvarttibhissamadhiṣṭhitāḥ || 78 ||

te hi sākṣāddiviṣadastvantarikṣasadastathā |
pṛthivīpada ityevaṃ devā devavrataiḥ stutā || 79 ||

evantribhirmalairāmaiḥ pakvaireva pṛthakpṛthak |
nidānabhūtaissaṃsārarogaḥ puṃsāṃ pravartate || 80 ||

asya rogasya bhaiṣajyaṃ jñānameva na cāparam |
bhiṣagājñāpakaḥ śambhuśśivaḥ paramakāraṇam || 81 ||

aduḥkhenā .api śakto .asau paśūnmocayituṃ śivaḥ |
kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ karotīti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 82 ||

duḥkhameva hi sarvo .api saṃsāra iti niścitam |
kathaṃ duḥkhamaduḥkhaṃ syātsvabhāvo hyaviparyayaḥ || 83 ||

na hi rogī hyarogī syādbhiṣagbhaiṣajyakāraṇāt |
rogārtaṃ tu bhiṣagrogādbhaiṣajaissukhamuddharet || 84 ||

evaṃ svabhāvamalinānsvabhāvādduḥkhinaḥ paśūn |
svājñauṣadhavidhānena duḥkhānmocayate śivaḥ || 85 ||

na bhiṣakkāraṇaṃ roge śivaḥ saṃsārakāraṇam |
ityetadapi vaiṣamyaṃ na doṣāyāsya kalpate || 86 ||

duḥkhe svabhāvasaṃsiddhe kathantatkāraṇaṃ śivaḥ |
svābhāviko malaḥ puṃsāṃ sa hi saṃsārayatyamūn || 87 ||

saṃsārakāraṇaṃ yattu malaṃ māyādyacetanam |
tatsvayaṃ na pravarteta śivasānnidhyamantarā || 88 ||

yathā maṇirayaskāntassānnidhyādupakārakaḥ |
ayasaścalatastadvacchivo .apyasyeti sūrayaḥ || 89 ||

na nivartayituṃ śakyaṃ sānnidhyaṃ sadakāraṇam |
adhiṣṭhātā tato nityamajñāto jagataśśivaḥ || 90 ||

na śivena vinā kiṃcitpravṛttamiha vidyate |
tatpreritamidaṃ sarvaṃ tathāpi na sa muhyati || 91 ||

śaktirājñātmikā tasya niyantrī viśvatomukhī |
tayā tatamidaṃ śaśvattathāpi sa na duṣyati || 92 ||

anidaṃ prathamaṃ sarvamīśitavyaṃ sa īśvaraḥ |
īśanācca tadīyājñā tathāpi sa na duṣyati || 93 ||

yo .anyathā manyate mohātsa vinaṣyati durmatiḥ |
tacchaktivaibhavādeva tathāpi sa na duṣyati || 94 ||

etasminnantare vyomnaḥ śrutāḥ vāgarīriṇī |
satyamomamṛtaṃ saumyamityāvirabhavatsphuṭam || 95 ||

tato hṛṣṭatarāḥ sarvve vinaṣṭāśeṣasaṃśayāḥ |
munayo vismayāviṣṭāḥ preṇemuḥ pavanaṃ prabhum || 96 ||

tathā vigatasandehānkṛtvāpi pavano munīn |
naite pratiṣṭhitajñānā iti matvaivamabravīt || 97 ||

vāyuruvācva

parokṣamaparokṣaṃ ca dvividhaṃ jñānamiṣyate |
parokṣamasthiraṃ prāhuraparokṣaṃ tu susthiram || 98 ||

hetūpadeśagamyaṃ yattatparokṣaṃ pracakṣate |
aparokṣaṃ punaḥ śreṣṭhādanuṣṭhānādbhaviṣyati || 99 ||

nāparokṣādṛte mokṣa iti kṛtvā viniścayam |
śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānasiddhyarthaṃ prayatadhvamatandritāḥ || 100 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe jñānopadeśo nāmaikatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 31 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kiṃ tacchreṣṭamanuṣṭhānaṃ mokṣo yenaparokṣitaḥ |
tattasya sādhanaṃ cādya vaktumarhasi māruta || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

śaivo hi paramo dharmaḥ śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānaśabditaḥ |
yatrāparokṣo lakṣyeta sākṣānmokṣapradaḥ śivaḥ || 2 ||

sa tu paṃcavidho jñeyaḥ paṃcabhiḥ parvabhiḥ kramāt |
kriyātapojapadhyānajñānātmabhiranuttaraiḥ || 3 ||

taireva sottaraissiddho dharmastu paramo mataḥ |
parokṣamaparokṣaṃ ca jñānaṃ yatra ca mokṣadam || 4 ||

paramo .aparamaścobhau dharmau hi śruticoditau |
dharmaśabdābhidheyerthe pramāṇaṃ śrutireva naḥ || 5 ||

paramo yogaparyanto dharmaḥ śrutiśirogataḥ |
dharmastvaparamastadvadadhaḥ śrutimukhotthitaḥ || 6 ||

apaśvātmādhikāratvādyo dharamaḥ paramo mataḥ |
sādhāraṇastato .anyastu sarveṣāmadhikārataḥ || 7 ||

sa cāyaṃ paramo dharmaḥ paradharmasya sādhanam |
dharmaśāstrādibhissamyak sāṃga evopabṛṃhitaḥ || 8 ||

śaivo yaḥ paramo dharmaḥ śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānaśabditaḥ |
itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ kathaṃcidupabṛṃhitaḥ || 9 ||

śaivāgamaistu saṃpannaḥ sahāṃgopāṃvistaraḥ |
tatsaṃskārādhikāraiśca samyagevopabṛṃhitaḥ || 10 ||

śaivāgamo hi dvividhaḥ śrauto .aśrautaśca saṃskṛtaḥ |
śrutisāramayaḥ śrautassvatantra itaro mataḥ || 11 ||

svatantro daśadhā pūrvaṃ tathāṣṭādaśadhā punaḥ |
kāmikādisamākhyābhissiddhaḥ siddhāntasaṃjñitaḥ || 12 ||

śrutisāramayo yastu śatakoṭipravistaraḥ |
paraṃ pāśupataṃ yatra vrataṃ jñānaṃ ca kathyate || 13 ||

yugāvarteṣu śiṣyeta yogācāryyasvarūpiṇā |
tatratatrāvatīrṇena śivenaiva pravartyate || 14 ||

saṃkṣipyāsya pravaktāraścatvāraḥ paramarṣaya |
rururdadhīco .agastyaśca upamanyurmahāyaśāḥ || 15 ||

te ca pāśupatā jñeyāssaṃhitānāṃ pravartakāḥ |
tatsantatīyā guravaḥ śataśo .atha sahasraśaḥ || 16 ||

tatroktaḥ paramo dharmaścaryādyātmā caturvidhaḥ |
teṣu pāśupato yogaḥ śivaṃ pratyakṣayeddṛḍham || 17 ||

tasmācchreṣṭhamanuṣṭhānaṃ yogaḥ pāśupato mataḥ |
tatrāpyupāyako yukto brahmaṇā sa tu kathyate || 18 ||

nāmāṣṭakamayo yogaśśivena parikalpitaḥ |
tena yogena sahasā śaivī prajñā prajāyate || 19 ||

prajñayā paramaṃ jñānamacirāllabhate sthiram |
prasīdati śivastasya yasya jñānaṃ pratiṣṭhitam || 20 ||

prasādātparamo yogo yaḥ śivaṃ cāparokṣayet |
śivāparokṣātsaṃsārakāraṇena viyujyate || 21 ||

tataḥ syānmuktasaṃsāro muktaḥ śivasamo bhavet |
brahmaprokta ityupāyaḥ sa eva pṛthagucyate || 22 ||

śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ |
saṃsāravaidyaḥ sarvajñaḥ paramātmeti mukhyataḥ || 23 ||

nāmāṣṭakamidaṃ mukhyaṃ śivasya pratipādakam |
ādyantu pañcakaṃ jñeyaṃ śāntyatītādyanukramāt || 24 ||

saṃjñā sadāśivādīnāṃ paṃcopādhiparigrahāt |
upādhivinivṛttau tu yathāsvaṃ vinivartate || 25 ||

padameva hi tannityamanityāḥ padinaḥ smṛtāḥ |
padānāṃ pratikṛttau tu mucyante padino yataḥ || 26 ||

parivṛttyantare bhūyastatpadaprāptirucyate |
ātmāntarābhidhānaṃ syādyadādyaṃ nāma pañcakam || 27 ||

anyattu tritayaṃ nāmnāmupādānādiyogataḥ |
trividhopādhivacanācchiva evānuvartate || 28 ||

anādimalasaṃśleṣaḥ prāgabhāvātsvabhāvataḥ |
atyantaṃ pariśuddhātmetyato .ayaṃ śiva ucyate || 29 ||

athavāśeṣakalyāṇaguṇaikadhana īśvaraḥ |
śiva ityucyate sadbhiśśivatattvārthavādibhiḥ || 30 ||

trayoviṃśatitattvebhyaḥ prakṛtirhi parā matā |
prakṛtestu paraṃ prāhuḥ puruṣaṃ pañcaviṃśakam || 31 ||

yaṃ vedādau svaraṃ prāhurvācyavācakabhāvataḥ |
vedaikavedyayāthātmyādvedānte ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ || 32 ||

tasya prakṛtilīnasya yaḥ parassa maheśvaraḥ |
tadadhīnapravṛttitvātprakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca || 33 ||

athavā triguṇaṃ tattvamupeyamidamavyayam |
māyāntu prakṛtiṃ vidyānmāyinaṃ tu maheśvaram || 34 ||

māyāvikṣobhako .ananto maheśvarasamanvayāt |
kālātmā paramātmādiḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 35 ||

rudduḥkhaṃ duḥkhaheturvā tadrāvayati naḥ prabhuḥ |
