rudra ityucyate sadbhiḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam || 36 ||

tattvādibhūtaparyantaṃ śarīrādiṣvatandritaḥ |
vyāpyādhitiṣṭhati śivastato rudra itastataḥ || 37 ||

jagataḥ pitṛbhūtānāṃ śivo mūrtyātmanāmapi |
pitṛbhāvena sarveṣāṃ pitāmaha udīritaḥ || 38 ||

nidānajño yathā vaidyo rogasya vinivartakaḥ |
upāyairbheṣajaistadvallayabhogādhikārataḥ || 39 ||

saṃsārasyeśvaro nityaṃ samūlasya nivartakaḥ |
saṃsāravaidya ityuktaḥ sarvatattvārthavedibhiḥ || 40 ||

daśārthajñānasiddhyarthamindriyeṣveṣu satsvapi |
trikālabhāvino bhāvānsthūlānsūkṣmānaśeṣataḥ || 41 ||

aṇavo naiva jānanti māyayaiva malāvṛtāḥ |
asatsvapi ca sarveṣu sarvārthajñānahetuṣu || 42 ||

yadyathāvasthitaṃ vastu tattathaiva sadāśivaḥ |
ayatnenaiva jānāti tasmātsarvajña ucyate || 43 ||

sarvātmā paramairebhirguṇairnityasamanvayāt |
svasmātparātmavirahātparamātmā śivaḥ svayam || 44 ||

nāmāṣṭakamidaṃ caiva labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ |
nivṛttyādikalāgranthiṃ śivādyaiḥ paṃcanāmabhiḥ || 45 ||

yathāsvaṃ kramaśaśchitvā śodhayitvā yathāguṇam |
guṇitaireva soddhātairaniruddhairathāpi vā || 46 ||

hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhyabrahmarandhrasamanvitām |
chittvā paryaṣṭakākāraṃ svātmānaṃ ca suṣumṇayā || 47 ||

dvādaśāntaḥsthitasyendornītvopari śivaujasi |
saṃhṛtyaṃ vadanaṃ paścādyathāsaṃskaraṇaṃ layāt || 48 ||

śāktenāmṛtavarṣeṇa saṃsiktāyāṃ tanau punaḥ |
avatārya svamātmānamamṛtātmākṛtiṃ hṛdi || 49 ||

dvādaśāntaḥsthitasyendoḥ parastācchvetapaṃkaje |
samāsīnaṃ mahādevaṃ śaṃkarambhaktavatsalam || 50 ||

arddhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ nirmalaṃ madhurākṛtim |
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ prasannaṃ śītaladyutim || 51 ||

dhyātvā hi mānase devaṃ svasthacitto .atha mānavaḥ |
śivanāmāṣṭakenaiva bhāvapuṣpaissamarcayet || 52 ||

abhyarccanānte tu punaḥ prāṇānāyamya mānavaḥ |
samyakcittaṃ samādhāya śārvaṃ nāmāṣṭakaṃ japet || 53 ||

nābhau cāṣṭāhutīrhutvā pūrṇāhutyā namastataḥ |
aṣṭapuṣpapradānena kṛtvābhyarccanamantimam || 54 ||

nivedayetsvamātmānaṃ culukodakavartmanā |
evaṃ kṛtvā cirādeva jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ śubham || 55 ||

labhate tatpratiṣṭhāṃ ca vṛttaṃ cānuttamaṃ tathā |
yogaṃ ca paramaṃ labdhvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 56 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 32 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

bhagavañchrotumicchāmo vrataṃ pāśupataṃ param |
brahmādayo .api yatkṛtvā sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ || 1 ||

vāyuruvāca |

rahasyaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpanikṛntanam |
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ śrautamatharvaśirasi śrutam || 2 ||

kālaścaitrī paurṇamāsī deśaḥ śivaparigrahaḥ |
kṣetrārāmādyaraṇyaṃ vā praśastaśśubhalakṣaṇaḥ || 3 ||

tatra pūrvaṃ trayodaśyāṃ susnātaḥ sukṛtāhnikaḥ |
anujñāpya svamācāryaṃ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca || 4 ||

pūjāṃ vaiśeṣikīṃ kṛtvā śuklāṃbaradharaḥ svayam |
śuklayajñopavītī ca śuklamālyānulepanaḥ || 5 ||

darbhāsane samāsīno darbhamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca |
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā prāGmukho vāpyudaGmukhaḥ |
dhyātvā devaṃ ca devīṃ ca tadvijñāpanavartmanā // 6 || 6 ||

vratametatkaromīti bhavetsaṃkalpya dīkṣitaḥ |
yāvaccharīrapātaṃ vā dvādaśābdamathāpi vā || 7 ||

tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā māsadvādaśakaṃ tu vā |
tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā māsamekamathāpi vā || 8 ||

dinadvādaśakaṃ vā .atha dinaṣaṭkamathāpi vā |
tadardhaṃ dinamekaṃ vā vratasaṃkalpanāvadhi || 9 ||

agnimādhāya vidhivadvirajāhomakāraṇāt |
hutvājyena samidbhiśca caruṇā ca yathākramam || 10 ||

pūrṇāmāpūrya tāṃ bhūyastattvānāṃ śuddhimuddiśan |
juhuyānmūlamantreṇa taireva samidādibhiḥ || 11 ||

tattvānyetāni maddehe śuddhyantāmityanusmaran |
pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāḥ pañcakarmendriyāṇi ca || 12 ||

jñānakarmavibhedena pañcakarmavibhāgaśaḥ |
tvagādidhātavassapta pañca prāṇādivāyavaḥ || 13 ||

manobuddhirahaṃ khyātirguṇāḥ prakṛtipūruṣau |
rāgo vidyākale caiva niyatiḥ kāla eva ca || 14 ||

māyā ca śuddhividyā ca maheśvarasadāśivau |
śaktiśca śivatattvaṃ ca tattvāni kramaśo viduḥ || 15 ||

mantraistu virajairhutvā hotāsau virajā bhavet |
śivānugrahamāsādya jñānavānsa hi jāyate || 16 ||

atha gomayamādāya piṇḍīkṛtyābhimantrya ca |
vinyasyāgnau ca samprokṣya dine tasminhaviṣyabhuk || 17 ||

prabhāte tu caturdaśyāṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ puroditam |
dine tasminnirāhāraḥ kālaṃ śeṣaṃ samāpayet || 18 ||

prātaḥ parvaṇi cāpyevaṃ kṛtvā homā vasānataḥ |
upasaṃhṛtya rudrāgniṃ gṛhṇīyādbhasma yatnataḥ || 19 ||

tataśca jaṭilo muṇḍī śikhaikajaṭa eva vā |
bhūtvā snātvā tato vītalajjaścetsyāddigambaraḥ || 20 ||

api kāṣāyavasanaścarmacīrāmbaro .atha vā |
ekāmbaro valkalī vā bhaveddaṇḍī ca mekhalī || 21 ||

prakṣālya caraṇau paścāddvirācamyātmanastanum |
saṃkulīkṛtya tadbhasma virajānalasaṃbhavam || 22 ||

agnirityādibhirmantraiḥ ṣaḍbhirātharvaṇaiḥ kramāt |
vibhṛjyāṃgāni mūrddhādicaraṇāntāni taisspṛśet || 23 ||

tatastena krameṇaiva samuddhṛtya ca bhasmanā |
sarvāṃgoddhūlanaṃ kuryātpraṇavena śivena vā || 24 ||

tatastripuṇḍraṃ racayettriyāyuṣasamāhvayam |
śivabhāvaṃ samāgamya śivayogamathācaret || 25 ||

kuryātstrisandhyamapyevametatpāśupataṃ vratam |
bhuktimuktipradaṃ caitatpaśutvaṃ vinivartayet || 26 ||

tatpaśutvaṃ parityajya kṛtvā pāśupataṃ vratam |
pūjanīyo mahādevo liṃgamūrtissanātanaḥ || 27 ||

padmamaṣṭadalaṃ haimaṃ navaratnairalaṃkṛtam |
karṇikākeśaropetamāsanaṃ parikalpayet || 28 ||

vibhave tadabhāve tu raktaṃ sitamathāpi vā |
padmaṃ tasyāpyabhāve tu kevalaṃ bhāvanāmayam || 29 ||

tatpadmakarṇikāmadhye kṛtvā liṃgaṃ kanīyasam |
sphīṭikaṃ pīṭhikopetaṃ pūjayedvidhivatkramāt || 30 ||

pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānena talliṃgaṃ kṛtaśodhanam |
parikalpyāsanaṃ mūrtiṃ paṃcavaktraprakārataḥ || 31 ||

paṃcagavyādibhiḥ pūrṇairyathāvibhavasaṃbhṛtaiḥ |
snāpayetkalaśaiḥ pūrṇairaṣṭāpadasamudbhavaiḥ || 32 ||

gandhadravyaissakarpūraiścandanādyaissakuṃkumaiḥ |
savedikaṃ samālipya liṃgaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣitam || 33 ||

bilvapatraiśca padmaiśca raktaiḥ śvetaistathotpalaiḥ |
nīlotpalaistathānyaiśca puṣpaistaistaissugandhibhiḥ || 34 ||

puṇyaiḥ praśastaiḥ patraiśca citrairdūrvākṣatādibhiḥ |
samabhyarcya yathālābhaṃ mahāpūjāvidhānataḥ || 35 ||

dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ tathā cāpi naivedyaṃ ca samādiśet |
nivedayitvā vibhave kalyāṇaṃ ca samācaret || 36 ||

iṣṭāni ca viśiṣṭāni nyāyenopārjitāni ca |
sarvadravyāṇi deyāni vrate tasminviśeṣataḥ || 37 ||

śrīpatrotpalapadmānāṃ saṃkhyā sāhasrikī matā |
pratyekamaparā saṃkhyā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ dvijāḥ || 38 ||

tatrāpi ca viśeṣeṇa na tyajedbilvapatrakam |
haimamekaṃ paraṃ prāhuḥ padmaṃ padmasahasrakāt || 39 ||

nīlotpalādiṣvapyetatsamānaṃ bilbapatrakaiḥ |
puṣpāntare na niyamo yathālābhaṃ nivedayet || 40 ||

aṣṭāGgamarghyamutkṛṣṭaṃ dhūpālepau viśeṣataḥ |
candanaṃ vāmadevākhye haritālaṃ ca pauruṣe || 41 ||

īśāne bhasitaṃ kecidālepanamitīdṛśām |
na dhūpamiti manyante dhūpāntaravidhānataḥ |
sitāgurumaghorākhye mukhe kṛṣṇāguruṃ punaḥ // 42 || 42 ||

pauruṣe guggulaṃ savye saumye saugandhikaṃ mukhe |
īśāne .api hyuśīrādi deyāddhūpaṃ viśeṣataḥ || 43 ||

śarkarāmadhukarpūrakapilāghṛtasaṃyutam |
candanāgurukāṣṭhādyaṃ sāmānyaṃ saṃpracakṣate || 44 ||

karpūravartirājyāḍhyā deyā dīpāvalistataḥ |
arghyamācamanaṃ deyaṃ prativaktramataḥ param || 45 ||

prathamāvaraṇe pūjyo kramāddherambaṣaṇmukhau |
brahmāṃgāni tataścaiva prathamāvaraṇercite || 46 ||

dvitīyāvaraṇe pūjyā vighneśāścakravartinaḥ |
tṛtīyāvaraṇe pūjyā bhavādyā aṣṭamūrtayaḥ || 47 ||

mahādevādayastatra tathaikādaśamūrtayaḥ |
caturthāvaraṇe pūjyāḥ sarva eva gaṇeśvarāḥ || 48 ||

bahireva tu padmasya paṃcamāvaraṇe kramāt |
daśadikpatayaḥ pūjyāḥ sāstrāḥ sānucarāstathā || 49 ||

brahmaṇo mānasāḥ putrāḥ sarve .api jyotiṣāṃ gaṇāḥ |
sarvā devyaśca devāśca sarve sarve ca khecarāḥ || 50 ||

pātālavāsinaścānye sarve munigaṇā api |
yogino hi sakhāssarve pataṃgā mātarastathā || 51 ||

kṣetrapālāśca sagaṇāḥ sarvaṃ caitaccarācaram |
pūjanīyaṃ śivaprītyā mattvā śaṃbhuvibhūtimat || 52 ||

athāvaraṇapūjānte saṃpūjya parameśvaram |
sājyaṃ savyaṃ janaṃ hṛdyaṃ havirbhaktyā nivedayet || 53 ||

mukhavāsādikaṃ dattvā tāmbūlaṃ sopadaṃśakam |
alaṃkṛtya ca bhūyo .api nānāpuṣpavibhūṣaṇaiḥ || 54 ||

nīrājanānte vistīrya pūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet |
caṣakaṃ sopakāraṃ ca śayanaṃ ca samarpayet || 55 ||

candrasaṃkāśahāraṃ ca śayanīyaṃ samarpayet |
ādyaṃ nṛpocitaṃ hṛdyaṃ tatsarvamanurūpataḥ || 56 ||

kṛtvā ca kārayitvā ca hitvā ca pratipūjanam |
stotraṃ vyapohanaṃ japtvā vidyāṃ paṃcākṣarīṃ japet || 57 ||

pradakṣiṇāṃ praṇāmaṃ ca kṛtvātmānaṃ samarpayet |
tataḥ purastāddevasya guruviprau ca pūjayet || 58 ||

dattvārghyamaṣṭau puṣpāṇi devamudvāsya liṃgataḥ |
agneścāgniṃ susaṃyamya hyudvāsya ca tamapyuta || 59 ||

pratyahaṃ ca janastvevaṃ kuryātsevāṃ puroditām |
tatastatsāmbujaṃ liṃgaṃ sarvopakaraṇānvitam || 60 ||

samarpayetsvagurave sthāpayedvā śivālaye |
saṃpūjya ca gurūnviprānvratinaśca viśeṣataḥ || 61 ||

bhaktāndvijāṃśca śaktaśceddīnānāthāṃśca toṣayet |
svayaṃ cānaśane śaktaḥ phalamūlāśane .atha vā || 62 ||

payovrato vā bhikṣāśī bhavedekāśanastathā |
naktaṃ yuktāśano nityaṃ bhūśayyānirataḥ śuciḥ || 63 ||

bhasmaśāyī tṛṇeśāyī cīrājinadhṛto .athavā |
brahmacaryavrato nityaṃ vratametatsamācaret || 64 ||

arkavāre tathārdrāyāṃ paṃcadaśyāṃ ca pakṣayoḥ |
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ śaktastūpavasedapi || 65 ||

pākhaṇḍipatitodakyāssūtakāntyajapūrvakān |
varjayetsarvayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā || 66 ||

kṣamadānadayāsatyāhiṃsāśīlaḥ sadā bhavet |
santuṣṭaśca praśāntaśca japadhyānaratastathā || 67 ||

kuryāttriṣavaṇasnānaṃ bhasmasnānamathāpi vā |
pūjāṃ vaiśeṣikīṃ caiva manasā vacasā girā || 68 ||

bahunātra kimuktena nācaredaśivaṃ vratī |
pramādāttu tathācāre nirūpya gurulāghave || 69 ||

ucitāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kuryātpūjāhomajapādibhiḥ |
āsamāptervratasyaivamācarenna pramādataḥ || 70 ||

godānaṃ ca vṛṣotsargaṃ kuryātpūjāṃ ca saṃpadā |
bhaktaśca śivaprītyarthaṃ sarvakāmavivarjitaḥ || 71 ||

sāmānyametatkathitaṃ vratasyāsya samāsataḥ |
pratimāsaṃ viśeṣaṃ ca pravadāmi yathāśrutam || 72 ||

vaiśākhe vajraliṃgaṃ tu jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ śubham |
āṣāḍhe mauktikaṃ vidyācchrāvaṇe nīlanirmitam || 73 ||

māse bhādrapade caiva padmarāgamayaṃ param |
āśvine māsi vidyādvai liṃgaṃ gomedakaṃ varam || 74 ||

kārtikyāṃ vaidrumaṃ liṃgaṃ vaidūryaṃ mārgaśīrṣake |
puṣparāgamayaṃ pauṣe māghe dyumaṇijantathā || 75 ||

phālguṇe candrakāntotthaṃ caitre tadvyatyayo .athavā |
sarvamāseṣu ratnānāmalābhe haimameva vā || 76 ||

haimābhāve rājataṃ vā tāmrajaṃ śailajantathā |
mṛnmayaṃ vā yathālābhaṃ jātuṣaṃ cānyadeva vā || 77 ||

sarvagandhamayaṃ vātha liṃgaṃ kuryādyathāruci |
vratāvasānasamaye samācaritanityakaḥ || 78 ||

kṛtvā vaiśeṣikīṃ pūjāṃ hutvā caiva yathā purā |
saṃpūjya ca tathācāryaṃ vratinaśca viśeṣataḥ || 79 ||

deśikenāpyanujñātaḥ prāGmukho vāpyudaGmukhaḥ |
darbhāsano darbhapāṇiḥ prāṇāpānau niyamya ca || 80 ||

japitvā śaktito mūlaṃ dhyātvā sāmbaṃ triyambakam |
anujñāpya yathāpūrvaṃ namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ || 81 ||

samutsṛjāmi bhagavanvratametattvadājñayā |
ityuktvā liṃgamūlasthāndarbhānuttaratastyajet || 82 ||

tato daṇḍajaṭācīramekhalā api cotsṛjet |
punarācamya vidhivatpaṃcākṣaramudīrayet || 83 ||

yaḥ kṛtvātyantikīṃ dīkṣāmādehāntamanākulaḥ |
vratametatprakurvīta sa tu vai naiṣṭhikaḥ smṛtaḥ || 84 ||

so .atyāśramī ca vijñeyo mahāpāśupatastathā |
sa eva tapatāṃ śreṣṭha sa eva ca mahāvratī || 85 ||

na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścitkṛtakṛtyo mumukṣuṣu |
yo yatirnaiṣṭhiko jātastamāhurnaiṣṭhikottamam || 86 ||

yo .anvahaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā vratametatsamācaret |
so .api naiṣṭhikatulyaḥ syāttīvravratasamanvayāt || 87 ||

ghṛtākto yaścaredetadvrataṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ |
dvitraikadivasaṃ vāpi sa ca kaścana naiṣṭhikaḥ || 88 ||

kṛtyamityeva niṣkāmo yaścaredvratamuttamam |
śivārpitātmā satataṃ na tena sadṛśaḥ kvacit || 89 ||

bhasmacchanno dvijo vidvānmahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ |
pāpaissudāruṇaissadyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 90 ||

rudrāgniryatparaṃ vīryyantadbhasma parikīrtitam |
tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu vīryavānbhasmasaṃyutaḥ || 91 ||

bhasmaniṣṭhasya naśyanti deṣā bhasmāgnisaṃgamāt |
bhasmasnānaviśuddhātmā bhasmaniṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ || 92 ||

bhasmanā digdhasarvāṃgo bhasmadīptatripuṃḍrakaḥ |
bhasmasnāyī ca puruṣo bhasmaniṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ || 93 ||

bhūtapretapiśāsāśca rogāścātīva dussahāḥ |
bhasmaniṣṭhasya sānnidhyādvidravanti na saṃśayaḥ || 94 ||

bhāsanādbhāsitaṃ proktaṃ bhasma kalmaṣabhakṣaṇāt |
bhūtibhūtikarī caiva rakṣā rakṣākarī param || 95 ||

kimanyadiha vaktavyaṃ bhasmamāhātmyakāraṇam |
vratī ca bhasmanā snātassvayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ || 96 ||

paramāstraṃ ca śaivānāṃ bhasmaitatpārameśvaram |
dhaumyāgrajasya tapasi vyāpado yannivāritāḥ || 97 ||

tasmātsarvaprayatnena kṛtvā pāśupatavratam |
dhanavadbhasma saṃgṛhya bhasmasnānarato bhavet || 98 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe paśupativratavidhānavarṇanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 33 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

dhaumyāgrajena śuśunā kṣīrārthaṃ hi tapaḥ kṛtam |
tasmāt kṣīrārṇavo dattastasmai devena śūlinā || 1 ||

sa kathaṃ śiśuko lebhe śivaśāstrapravaktṛtām |
kathaṃ vā śivasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā tapasi niṣṭhitaḥ || 2 ||

kathaṃ ca labdhavijñānastapaścaraṇaparvaṇi |
rudrāgneryatparaṃ vīryaṃ labhe bhasma svarakṣakam || 3 ||

vāyuruvāca |

na hyeṣa śiśukaḥ kaścitprākṛtaḥ kṛtavāṃstapaḥ |
munivaryasya tanayo vyāghrapādasya dhīmataḥ || 4 ||

janmāntareṇa saṃsiddhaḥ kenāpi khalu hetunā |
svapadapracyuto diṣṭyā prāpto munikumāratām || 5 ||

mahādevaprasādasya bhāgyāpannasya bhāvinaḥ |
dugdhābhilāṣaprabhavadvāratāmagamattapaḥ || 6 ||

ataḥ sarvagaṇeśatvaṃ kumāratvaṃ ca śāśvatam |
saha dugdhābdhinā tasmai pradadau śaṃkaraḥ svayam || 7 ||

tasya jñānāgamopyasya prasādādeva śāṃkarāt |
kaumāraṃ hi paraṃ sākṣājjñānaṃ śaktimayaṃ viduḥ || 8 ||

śivaśāstrapravaktṛtvamapi tasya hi tatkṛtam |
kumāro munito labdhajñānābdhiriva nandanaḥ || 9 ||

dṛṣṭaṃ tu kāraṇaṃ tasya śivajñānasamanvaye |
svamātṛvacanaṃ sākṣācchokajaṃ kṣīrakāraṇāt || 10 ||

kadācitkṣīramatyalpaṃ pītavānmātulāśrame |
īrṣayayā mātulasutaṃ santṛptakṣīramuttamam / || 11 ||

pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai mātulātmajam |
upamanyurvyāghrapādiḥ prītyā provāca mātaram || 12 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini |
gavyaṃ kṣīramatisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ pibāmyaham || 13 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tacchrutvā putravacanaṃ tanmātā ca tapasvinī |
vyāghrapādasya mahiṣī duḥkhamāpattadā ca sā || 14 ||

upalālyātha suprītyā putramāliṃgya sādaram |
duḥkhitā vilalāpātha smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ || 15 ||

smṛtvāsmṛtvā punaḥ kṣīramupamanyussa bālakaḥ |
dehi dehīti tāmāha rudranbhūyo mahādyutiḥ || 16 ||

taddhaṭhaṃ sā parijñāya dvijapatnī tapasvinī |
śāntaye taddhaṭhasyātha śubhopāyamarīracat || 17 ||

uñchavṛttyārjitānbījānsvayaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca sā tadā |
bījapiṣṭamathāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī || 18 ||

ehyehi mama putreti sāmapūrvaṃ tatassutam |
āliṃgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ || 19 ||

pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrāṃ dattaṃ sa bālakaḥ |
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ || 20 ||

duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣyāghrāya mūrddhani |
samārjya netra putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate || 21 ||

jananyuvāca |

taṭinī ratnapūrṇāstāssvargapātālagocarāḥ |
bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāśca ye śive || 22 ||

rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam |
na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ na tuṣyati yadā śivaḥ || 23 ||

bhavaprasādajaṃ sarvaṃ nānyaddevaprasādajam |
anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca || 24 ||

kṣīraṃ tatra kuto .asmākaṃ vane nivasatāṃ sadā |
kva dugdhasādhanaṃ vatsa kva vayaṃ vanavāsinaḥ || 25 ||

kṛtsnābhāvena dāridryānmayā te bhāgyahīnayā |
mithyādugdhamidaṃ dattampiṣṭamāloḍya vāriṇā || 26 ||

tvaṃ mātulagṛhe svalpaṃ pītvā svādu payaḥ śṛtam |
jñātvā svādu tvayā pītaṃ tajjātīyamanusmaran || 27 ||

dattaṃ na paya ityuktvā rudan duḥkhīkaroṣi mām |
prasādena vinā śaṃbho payastava na vidyate || 28 ||

pādapaṃkajayostasya sāmbasya sagaṇasya ca |
bhaktyā samarpitaṃ yattatkāraṇaṃ sarvasampadām || 29 ||

adhunā vasudosmābhirmahādevo na pūjitaḥ |
sakāmānāṃ yathākāmaṃ yathoktaphaladāyakaḥ || 30 ||

dhanānyuddiśya nāsmābhiritaḥ prāgarcitaḥ śivaḥ |
ato daridrāssaṃjātā vayaṃ tasmānna te payaḥ || 31 ||

pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamuddiśya vai sutaḥ |
tadeva labhyate nānyadviṣṇumuddiśya vā prabhum || 32 ||

vāyuruvāca |

iti mātṛvacaḥ śrutvā tathyaṃ śokādisūcakam |
bālo .apyanutapannantaḥ pragalbhamidamabravīt || 33 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śokenālamito mataḥ sāṃbo yadyasti śaṃkaraḥ |
tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge sarvaṃ bhadraṃ bhaviṣyati || 34 ||

śṛṇu mātarvaco medya mahādevo .asti cetkvacit |
cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham || 35 ||

vāyuruvāca |

iti śrutvā vacastasya bālakasya mahāmateḥ |
praytuvāca tadā mātā suprasannā manasvinī || 36 ||

mātovāca |

śubhaṃ vicāritaṃ tāta tvayā matprītivarddhanam |
vilaṃbaṃ mā kathāstvaṃ hi bhaja sāṃbaṃ sadāśivam || 37 ||

sarvasmādadhiko .astyeva śivaḥ paramakāraṇam |
tatkṛtaṃ hi jagatsarvaṃ brahmādyāstasya kiṃkarāḥ || 38 ||

tatprasādakṛtaiśvaryā dāsāstasya vayaṃ prabhoḥ |
taṃ vinānyaṃ na jānīmaśśaṃkaraṃ lokaśaṃkaram || 39 ||

anyāndevānparityajya karmaṇā manasā girā |
tameva sāṃbaṃ sagaṇaṃ bhaja bhāvapurassaram || 40 ||

tasya devādhidevasya śivasya varadāyinaḥ |
sākṣānnamaśśivāyeti mantro .ayaṃ vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 41 ||

saptakoṭimahāmantrāḥ sarve sapraṇavāḥ pare |
tasminneva vilīyante punastasmādvinirgatāḥ || 42 ||

saprasādāśca te mantrāḥ svādhikārādyapekṣayā |
sarvādhikārastveko .ayaṃ mantra eveśvarājñayā || 43 ||

yathā nikṛṣṭānutkṛṣṭānsarvānapyātmanaḥ śivaḥ |
kṣamate rakṣituṃ tadvanmantro .ayamapi sarvadā || 44 ||

prabalaśca tathā hyeṣa mantro mantrāntarādapi |
sarvarakṣākṣamo .apyeṣa nāparaḥ kaścidiṣyate || 45 ||

tasmānmantrāntarāṃstyaktvā paṃcākṣaraparo bhava |
tasmiñjihvāntaragate na kiṃcidiha durlabham || 46 ||

adhorāstraṃ ca śaivānāṃ rakṣāheturanuttamam |
tacca tatprabhavaṃ matvā tatparo bhava nānyathā || 47 ||

bhasmedantu mayā labdhaṃ pitureva tavottamam |
virajānalasaṃsiddhaṃ mahāvyāpannivāraṇam || 48 ||

mantraṃ ca te mayā dattaṃ gṛhāṇa madanujñayā |
anenaivāśu japtena rakṣā tava bhaviṣyati || 49 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evaṃ mātrā samādiśya śivamastvityudīrya ca |
visṛṣṭastadvaco mūrdhni kurvanneva tadā muniḥ || 50 ||

tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā ca tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame |
tamāha ca tadā mātā śubhaṃ kurvantu te surāḥ || 51 ||

anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sa duścaram |
himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ || 52 ||

aṣṭeṣṭakābhiḥ prasādaṃ kṛtvā liṃgaṃ ca mṛnmayam |
tatrāvāhya mahādevaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam || 53 ||

bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇaiva putraiḥ puṣpairvanodbhavaiḥ |
samabhyarcya ciraṃ kālaṃ cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ || 54 ||

tatastapaścarattaṃ taṃ bālamekākinaṃ kṛśam |
upamanyuṃ dvijavaraṃ śivasaṃsaktamānasam || 55 ||

purā marīcinā śaptāḥ kecinmunipiśācakāḥ |
saṃpīḍya rākṣasairbhāvaistapasovighnamācaran || 56 ||

sa ca taiḥ pīḍyamāno .api tapaḥ kurvankathañcana |
sadā namaḥ śivāyeti krośati smārtanādavat || 57 ||

tannādaśravaṇādeva tapaso vighnakāriṇaḥ |
te taṃ bālaṃ samutsṛjya munayassamupācaran || 58 ||

tapasā tasya viprasya copamanyormahātmanaḥ |
carācaraṃ ca munayaḥ pradīpitamabhūjjagat || 59 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe upamanyutapovarṇanaṃ nāma catustriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 34 ||

vāyuruvāca |

atha sarve pradīptāṃgā vaikuṇṭhaṃ prayayurdrutam |
praṇamyāhuśca tatsarvaṃ haraye devasattamāḥ || 1 ||

śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ |
kimidantviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ || 2 ||

jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā |
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provāca sukṛtāṃjaliḥ || 3 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

bhagavanbrāhmaṇaḥ kaścidupamanyuriti śrutaḥ |
kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā tannivāraya || 4 ||

vāyuruvāca |

iti śrutvā vaco viṣṇoḥ prāha devo maheśvaraḥ |
śiśuṃ nivārayiṣyāmi tattvaṃ gaccha svamāśramam || 5 ||

tacchrutvā śaṃbhuvacanaṃ sa viṣṇurdevavallabhaḥ |
jagāmāśvāsya tānsarvānsvalokamamarādikān || 6 ||

etasminnantare devaḥ pinākī parameśvaraḥ |
śakrasya rūpamāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tataḥ || 7 ||

atha jagāma munestu tapovanaṃ gajavareṇa sitena sadāśivaḥ |
saha surāsurasiddhamahoragairamararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ || 8 ||

sa vāraṇaścāru tadā vibhuṃ taṃ nivījya vālavyajanena divyam |
dadhāra śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa vāmena śitātapatram || 9 ||

rarāja bhagavānsomaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ |
tenātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ || 10 ||

āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ |
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartumupamanyostadāśramam || 11 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam |
praṇamya śirasā prāha mahāmunivaraḥ svayam || 12 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

pāvitaścāśramasso .ayaṃ mama deveśvara svayam |
prāpto yattvaṃ jagannātha bhagavandevasattama || 13 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evamuktvā sthitaṃ prekṣya kṛtāṃjalipuṭaṃ dvijam |
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ || 14 ||

śakra uvāca |

tuṣṭo .asmi te varaṃ brūhi tapasānena suvrata |
dadāmi cepsitānsarvāndhaumyāgraja mahāmune || 15 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evamuktastadā tena śakreṇa munipuṃgavaḥ |
vārayāmi śive bhaktimityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ || 16 ||

tanniśamya hariḥ prāha māṃ na jānāsi lekhapam |
trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam || 17 ||

madbhakto bhava viprarṣe māmevārcaya sarvadā |
dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam || 18 ||

rudreṇa nirguṇenāpi kiṃ te kāryaṃ bhaviṣyati |
devapaGktibahirbhūto yaḥ piśācatvamāgataḥ || 19 ||

vāyuruvāca |

tacchrutvā prāha sa munirjapanpaṃcākṣaraṃ manum |
manyamāno dharmavighnaṃ prāha taṃ kartumāgatam || 20 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

tvayaivaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavanindāratena vai |
prasaṃgādeva devasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ || 21 ||

tvaṃ na jānāmi vai rudraṃ sarvadeveśvareśvaram |
brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ janaka prakṛteḥ param || 22 ||

sadasadvyaktamavyaktaṃ yamāhurbrahmavādinaḥ |
nityamekamanekaṃ ca varaṃ tasmādvṛṇomyaham || 23 ||

hetuvādavinirmuktaṃ sāṃkhyayogārthadamparam |
upāsate yaṃ tattvajñā varaṃ tasmādvṛṇomyaham || 24 ||

nāsti śaṃbhoḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇāt |
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāṃ sraṣṭurguṇaparādvibhoḥ || 25 ||

bahunātra kimuktena mayādyānumitaṃ mahat |
bhavāntare kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya cet || 26 ||

śrutvā nindāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva santyajet |
svadehaṃ tannihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati || 27 ||

āstāṃ tāvanmameccheyaṃ kṣīraṃ prati surādhama |
nihatya tvāṃ śivāstreṇa tyajāmyetaṃ kalevaram || 28 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evamuktvopamanyustaṃ martuṃ vyavasitassvayam |
kṣīre vāñchāmapi tyaktvā nihantuṃ śakramudyataḥ || 29 ||

bhasmādāya tadā ghoramaghorāstrābhimantritam |
visṛjya śakramuddiśya nanāda sa munistadā || 30 ||

smṛtvā śaṃbhupadadvandvaṃ svadehaṃ dugdhumudyataḥ |
āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ bibhradupamanyuravasthitaḥ || 31 ||

evaṃ vyavasite vipre bhagavānbhaganetrahā |
vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ || 32 ||

tadvisṛṣṭamaghorāstraṃ nandīśvaraniyogataḥ |
jagṛhe madhyataḥ kṣiptaṃ nandī śaṃkaravallabhaḥ || 33 ||

svaṃ rūpameva bhagavānāsthāya parameśvaraḥ |
darśayāmāsa śiprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam || 34 ||

kṣīrārṇavasahasraṃ ca pīyūṣārṇavameva vā |
dadhyāderarṇavāṃścaiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca || 35 ||

phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣya bhojyārṇavaṃ tathā |
apūpānāṃ giriṃ caiva darśayāmāsa sa prabhuḥ || 36 ||

evaṃ sa dadṛśe devo devyā sārddhaṃ vṛṣopari |
gaṇeśvaraistriśūlādyairdivyāstrairapi saṃvṛtaḥ || 37 ||

divi dundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca |
viṣṇubrahmendrapramukhairdevaiśchannā diśo daśa || 38 ||

athopamanyurānandasamudrormibhirāvṛtaḥ |
papāta daṇḍavadbhūmau bhaktinamreṇa cetasā || 39 ||

etasminsamaye tatra sasmito bhagavānbhavaḥ |
ehyehīti tamāhūya mūrdhnyāghrāya dadau varān || 40 ||

śiva uvāca |

bhakṣyabhojyānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavairbhukṣva sarvadā |
sukhī bhava sadā duḥkhānnirmuktā bhaktimānmama || 41 ||

upamanyo mahābhāga tavāmbaiṣā hi pārvatī |
mayā putrīkṛto hyadya dattaḥ kṣīrodakārṇavaḥ || 42 ||

madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhyannārṇava eva ca |
ājyaudanārṇavaścaiva phalādyarṇava eva ca || 43 ||

apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavastathā |
ete dattā mayā te hi tvaṃ gṛhṇīṣva mahāmune || 44 ||

pitā tava mahādevo mātā vai jagadambikā |
amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam || 45 ||

varānvaraya suprītyā mano .abhilaṣitānparān |
prasanno .ahaṃ pradāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 46 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhyatam |
mūrdhnyāghrāya sutaste .ayamiti devyai nyavedayat || 47 ||

devī ca guhavatprītyā mūrdhni tasya karāmbujam |
vinyasya pradadau tasmai kumārapadamavyayam || 48 ||

kṣīrābdhirapi sākāraḥ kṣīraṃ svādu kare dadhat |
upasthāya dadau piṇḍībhūtaṃ kṣīramanaśvaram || 49 ||

yogaiśvaryaṃ sadā tuṣṭiṃ brahmavidyāmanaśvarām |
samṛddhiṃ paramāntasmai dadau santuṣṭamānasaḥ || 50 ||

atha śaṃbhuḥ prasannātmā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapomahaḥ |
punardadau varaṃ divyaṃ munaye hyupamanyave || 51 ||

vrataṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ vratayogaṃ ca tattvataḥ |
dadau tasmai pravaktṛtvapāṭavaṃ suciraṃ param || 52 ||

so .api labdhvā varāndivyānkumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā |
tasmācchivācca tasyāśca śivāyā mudito .abhavat || 53 ||

tataḥ prasannacetaskaḥ supraṇamya kṛtāṃjaliḥ |
yayāce sa varaṃ vipro devadevānmaheśvarāt || 54 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

prasīda devadeveśa prasīda parameśvara |
svabhaktindehi paramāndivyāmavyabhicāriṇīm || 55 ||

śraddhāndehi mahādeva dvasambandhiṣu me sadā |
svadāsyaṃ paramaṃ snehaṃ sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā || 56 ||

evamuktvā prasannātmāharṣagadgadayā girā |
satuṣṭāva mahādevamupamanyurdvijottamaḥ || 57 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

devadeva mahādeva śaraṇāgatavatsala |
prasīda karuṇāsindho sāmba śaṃkara sarvadā || 58 ||

vāyuruvāca |

evamukto mahādevaḥ sarveṣāṃ ca varapradaḥ |
pratyuvāca prasannātmopamanyuṃ munisattamam || 59 ||

śiva uvāca |

vatsopamanyo tuṣṭo .asmi sarvaṃ dattaṃ mayā hi te |
dṛḍhabhakto .asi viprarṣe mayā vijñāsito hyasi || 60 ||

ajaraścāmaraścaiva bhava tvanduḥkhavarjitaḥ |
yaśasvī tejasā yukto divyajñānasamanvitaḥ || 61 ||

akṣayā bāndhavāścaiva kulaṃ gotraṃ ca te sadā |
bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha mayi bhaktiśca śāśvatī || 62 ||

sānnidhyaṃ cāśrame nityaṃ kariṣyāmi dvijottama |
upakaṃṭhaṃ mama tvaṃ vai sānandaṃ vihariṣyasi || 63 ||

evamuktvā sa bhagavānsūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ |
īśānassa varāndattvā tatraivāntardadhe haraḥ || 64 ||

upamanyuḥ prasannātmā prāpya tasmādvarādvarān |
jagāma jananīsthānaṃ sukhaṃ prāpādhikaṃ ca saḥ || 65 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vaiyāsikyāṃ caturviṃśatisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ tadantargatāyāṃ saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe upamanyucaritavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 35 ||

samāpto .ayaṃ saptamyā vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāḥ pūrvakhaṇḍaḥ // śrīḥ

śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ // śrīgaurīśaṃkarābhyāṃ namaḥ // atha saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍaḥ prārabhyate

.o

namassamastasaṃsāracakrabhramaṇahetave |
gaurīkucataṭadvandvakuṃkumāṃkitavakṣase || 1 ||

sūta uvāca |

uktvā bhagavato labdhaprasādādupamanyunā |
niyamādutthito vāyurmadhye prāpte divākare || 2 ||

ṛṣayaścāpi te sarve naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ |
athāyamarthaḥ praṣṭavya iti kṛtvā viniścayam || 3 ||

kṛtvā yathā svakaṃ kṛtyaṃ pratyahaṃ te yathā purā |
bhagavantamupāyāntaṃ samīkṣya samupāviśan || 4 ||

athāsau niyamasyānte bhagavānambarodbhavaḥ |
madhye munisabhāyāstu bheje kLptaṃ varāsanam || 5 ||

sukhāsanopaviṣṭaśca vāyurlokanamaskṛtaḥ |
śrīmadvibhūtimīśasya hṛdi kṛtvedamabravīt || 6 ||

taṃ prapadye mahādevaṃ sarvajñamaparājitam |
vibhūtissakalaṃ yasya carācaramidaṃ jagat || 7 ||

ityākarṇya śubhāṃ vāṇīmṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ |
vibhūtivistaraṃ śrotumūcuste paramaṃ vacaḥ || 8 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

uktaṃ bhagavatā vṛttamupamanyormahātmanaḥ |
kṣīrārthenāpi tapasā yatprāptaṃ parameśvarāt || 9 ||

dṛṣṭo .asau vāsudevena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā |
dhaumyāgrajastatastena kṛtvā pāśupataṃ vratam || 10 ||

prāptaṃ ca paramaṃ jñānamiti prāgeva śuśruma |
kathaṃ sa labdhavān kṛṣṇo jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ param || 11 ||

vāyuruvāca |

svecchayā hyavatīrṇopi vāsudevassanātanaḥ |
nindayanniva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ || 12 ||

putrārthaṃ hi tapastaptuṃ gatastasya mahāmuneḥ |
āśramaṃ munibhirdṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭavāṃstatra vai munim || 13 ||

bhasmāvadātasarvāṃgaṃ tripuṃḍrāṃkitamastakam |
rudrākṣamālābharaṇaṃ jaṭāmaṃḍalamaṃḍitam || 14 ||

tacchiṣyabhūtairmunibhiśśāstrairvedamivāvṛtam |
śivadhyānarataṃ śāntamupamanyuṃ mahādyutim || 15 ||

namaścakāra taṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhaḥ |
bahumānena kṛṣṇo .asau triḥ kṛtvā tu pradakṣiṇām |
stutiṃ cakāra suprītyā nataskandhaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ // 16 || 16 ||

tasyāvalokanādeva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ |
naṣṭamāsīnmalaṃ sarvaṃ māyājaṃ kārmameva ca || 17 ||

tapaḥkṣīṇamalaṃ kṛṣṇamupamanyuryathāvidhiḥ |
bhasmanoddhūlya taṃ mantrairagnirityādibhiḥ kramāt || 18 ||

atha pāśupataṃ sākṣādvrataṃ dvādaśamāsikam |
kārayitvā munistasmai pradadau jñānamuttamam || 19 ||

tadāprabhṛti taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ munayaśśaṃsitavratāḥ |
divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve parivṛtyopatasthire || 20 ||

tato guruniyogādvai kṛṣṇaḥ paramaśaktimān |
tapaścakāra putrārthaṃ sāṃbamuddiśya śaṃkaram || 21 ||

tapaso tena varṣānte dṛṣṭo .asau parameśvaraḥ |
śriyā paramayā yuktassāṃbaśca sagaṇaśśivaḥ || 22 ||

varārthamāvirbhūtasya harasya subhagākṛteḥ |
stutiṃ cakāra natvāsau kṛṣṇaḥ samyakkṛtāṃjaliḥ || 23 ||

sāṃbaṃ samagaṇavyagro labdhavānputramātmanaḥ |
tapasā tuṣṭacittena dattaṃ viṣṇośśivena vai || 24 ||

yasmātsāṃbo mahādevaḥ pradadau putramātmanaḥ |
tasmājjāṃbavatīsūnuṃ sāṃbaṃ cakre sa nāmataḥ || 25 ||

tadetatkathitaṃ sarvaṃ kṛṣṇasyāmitakarmaṇaḥ |
maharṣerjñānalābhaśca putralābhaśca śaṃkarāt || 26 ||

ya idaṃ kīrtayennityaṃ śṛṇuyācchrāvayettathā |
sa viṣṇorjñānamāsādya tenaiva saha modate || 27 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe kṛṣṇaputraprāptivarṇanaṃ nama prathamo .adhyāyaḥ || 1 ||

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

kiṃ tatpāśupataṃ jñānaṃ kathaṃ paśupatiśśivaḥ |
kathaṃ dhaumyāgrajaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā || 1 ||

etatsarvaṃ samācakṣva vāyo śaṃkaravigraha |
tatsamo na hi vaktāsti trailokyeṣvaparaḥ prabhuḥ || 2 ||

sūta uvāca |

ityākarṇya vacasteṣāṃ maharṣīṇāṃ prabhaṃjanaḥ |
saṃsmṛtya śivamīśānaṃ pravaktumupacakrame || 3 ||

vāyuruvāca |

purā sākṣānmaheśena śrīkaṃṭhākhyena mandare |
devyai devena kathitaṃ jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ param || 4 ||

tadeva pṛṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā |
paśutvaṃ ca surādīnāṃ patitvaṃ ca śivasya ca || 5 ||

yathopadiṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇāya muninā hyupamanyunā |
tathā samāsato vakṣye tacchṛṇudhvamatandritāḥ || 6 ||

puropamanyumāsīnaṃ viṣṇuḥkṛṣṇavapurdharaḥ |
praṇipatya yathānyāyamidaṃ vacanamabravīt || 7 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavañchrotumicchāmi devyai devena bhāṣitam |
divyaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ vibhūtiṃ vāsya kṛtsnaśaḥ || 8 ||

kathaṃ paśupatirdevaḥ paśavaḥ ke prakīrtitāḥ |
kaiḥ pāśaiste nibadhyante vimucyante ca te katham || 9 ||

iti saṃcoditaḥ śrīmānupamanyurmahātmanā |
praṇamya devaṃ devīṃ ca prāha puṣṭo yathā tathā || 10 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca devadevasya śūlinaḥ |
paśavaḥ parikīrtyante saṃsāravaśavartinaḥ || 11 ||

teṣāṃ patitvāddeveśaḥ śivaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ |
malamāyādibhiḥ pāśaiḥ sa badhnāti paśūnpatiḥ || 12 ||

sa eva mocakasteṣāṃ bhaktyā samyagupāsitaḥ |
caturviṃśatitattvāni māyākarmaguṇā amī || 13 ||

viṣayā iti kathyante pāśā jīvanibandhanāḥ |
brahmādistambaparyantān paśūnbaddhvā maheśvaraḥ || 14 ||

pāśairetaiḥ patirdevaḥ kāryaṃ kārayati svakam |
tasyājñayā maheśasya prakṛtiḥ puruṣocitām || 15 ||

buddhiṃ prasūte sā buddhirahaṃkāramahaṃkṛtiḥ |
indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca tanmātrāpañcakaṃ tathā || 16 ||

śāsanāddevadevasya śivasya śivadāyinaḥ |
tanmātrāṇyapi tasyaiva śāsanena mahīyasā || 17 ||

mahābhūtānyaśeṣāṇi bhāvayantyanupūrvaśaḥ |
brahmādīnāṃ tṛṇāntānāṃ dehināṃ dehasaṃgatim || 18 ||

mahābhūtānyaśeṣāṇi janayanti śivājñayā |
adhyavasyati vai buddhirahaṃkārobhimanyate || 19 ||

cittaṃ cetayate cāpi manaḥ saṃkalpayatyapi |
śrotrādīni ca gṛhṇanti śabdādīnviṣayān pṛthak || 20 ||

svāneva nānyāndevasya divyenājñābalena vai |
vāgādīnyapi yānyāsaṃstāni karmendriyāṇi ca || 21 ||

yathā svaṃ karma kurvanti nānyatkiṃcicchivājñayā |
śabdādayopi gṛhyante kriyante vacanādayaḥ || 22 ||

avilaṃghyā hi sarveṣāmājñā śaṃbhorgarīyasī |
avakāśamaśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ saṃprayacchati || 23 ||

ākāśaḥ parameśasya śāsanādeva sarvagaḥ |
prāṇādyaiśca tathā nāmabhedairantarbahirjagat || 24 ||

bibharti sarvaṃ śarvasya śāsanena prabhañjanaḥ |
havyaṃ vahati devānāṃ kavyaṃ kavyāśināmapi || 25 ||

pākādyaṃ ca karotyagniḥ parameśvaraśāsanāt |
saṃjīvanādyaṃ sarvasya kurvatyāpastadājñayā || 26 ||

viśvambharā jagannityaṃ dhatte viśveśvarājñayā |
devānpātyasurān hanti trilokamabhirakṣati / || 27 ||

ājñayā tasya devendraḥ sarvairdevairalaṃghyayā |
ādhipatyamapāṃ nityaṃ kurute varuṇassadā || 28 ||

pāśairbadhnāti ca yathā daṃḍyāṃstasyaiva śāsanāt |
dadāti nityaṃ yakṣendro draviṇaṃ draviṇeśvaraḥ || 29 ||

puṇyānurūpaṃ bhūtebhyaḥ puruṣasyānuśāsanāt |
karoti saṃpadaḥ śaśvajjñānaṃ cāpi sumedhasām || 30 ||

nigrahaṃ cāpyasādhūnāmīśānaśśivaśāsanāt |
dhatte tu dharaṇīṃ mūrdhnā śeṣaḥ śivaniyogataḥ || 31 ||

yāmāhustāmasīṃ raudrīṃ mūrtimantakarīṃ hareḥ |
sṛjatyaśeṣamīśasya śāsanāccaturānanaḥ || 32 ||

anyābhirmūrtibhiḥ svābhiḥ pāti cānte nihanti ca |
viṣṇuḥ pālayate viśvaṃ kālakālasya śāsanāt || 33 ||

sṛjate trasate cāpi svakābhistanubhistribhiḥ |
haratyante jagatsarvaṃ harastasyaiva śāsanāt || 34 ||

sṛjatyapi ca viśvātmā tridhā bhinnastu rakṣati |
kālaḥ karoti sakalaṃ kālassaṃharati prajāḥ || 35 ||

kālaḥ pālayate viśvaṃ kālakālasya śāsanāt |
tribhiraṃśairjagadbibhrattejobhirvṛṣṭimādiśan || 36 ||

divi varṣatyasau bhānurdevadevasya śāsanāt |
puṣṇātyoṣadhijātāni bhūtānyāhlādayatyapi || 37 ||

devaiśca pīyate candraścandrabhūṣaṇaśāsanāt |
ādityā vasavo rudrā aśvinau marutastathā || 38 ||

khecarā ṛṣayassiddhā bhogino manujā mṛgāḥ |
paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaścaiva kīṭādyāḥ sthāvarāṇi ca || 39 ||

nadyassamudrā girayaḥ kānanāni sarāṃsi ca |
vedāḥ sāṃgāśca śāstrāṇi mantrastomamakhādayaḥ || 40 ||

kālāgnyādiśivāntāni bhuvanāni sahādhipaiḥ |
brahmāṃḍānyapyasaṃkhyāni teṣāmāvaraṇāni ca || 41 ||

vartamānānyatītāni bhaviṣyantyapi kṛtsnaśaḥ |
diśaśca vidiśaścaiva kālabhedāḥ kalādayaḥ || 42 ||

yacca kiṃcijjagatyasmin dṛśyate śrūyate .api vā |
tatsarvaṃ śaṃkarasyājñā balena samadhiṣṭhitam || 43 ||

ājñābalāttasya dharā sthiteha dharādharā vāridharāḥ samudrāḥ |
jyotirgaṇāḥ śakramukhāśca devāḥ sthiraṃ ciraṃ vā cidacidyadasti || 44 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

atyāścaryamidaṃ kṛṣṇa śaṃbhoramitakarmaṇaḥ |
ājñākṛtaṃ śṛṇuṣvaitacchrutaṃ śrutimukhe mayā || 45 ||

purā kila surāḥ sendrā vivadantaḥ parasparam |
asurānsamare jitvā jetāhamahamityuta || 46 ||

tadā maheśvarasteṣāṃ madhyato varaveṣadhṛk |
svalakṣaṇairvihīnāṃgaḥ svayaṃ yakṣa ivābhavat || 47 ||

sa tānāha surānekaṃ tṛṇamādāya bhūtale |
ya etadvikṛtaṃ kartuṃ kṣamate sa tu daityajit || 48 ||

yakṣasya vacanaṃ śrutvā vajrapāṇiḥ śacīpatiḥ |
kiṃcitkruddho vihasyainaṃ tṛṇamādātumudyataḥ || 49 ||

na tattṛṇamupadātuṃ manasāpi ca śakyate |
yathā tathāpi tacchettuṃ vajraṃ vajradharo .asṛjat || 50 ||

tadvajraṃ nijavajreṇa saṃsṛṣṭamiva sarvataḥ |
tṛṇenābhihataṃ tena tiryagagraṃ papāta ha || 51 ||

tataścānye susaṃrabdhā lokapālā mahābalāḥ |
sasṛjustṛṇamuddiśya svāyudhāni sahasraśaḥ || 52 ||

prajajjvāla mahāvahniḥ pracaṃḍaḥ pavano vavau |
pravṛddho .apāṃpatiryadvatpralaye samupasthite || 53 ||

evaṃ devaissamārabdhaṃ tṛṇamuddiśya yatnataḥ |
vyarthamāsīdaho kṛṣṇa yakṣasyātmabalena vai || 54 ||

tadāha yakṣaṃ devendraḥ ko bhavānityamarṣitaḥ |
tatassa paśyatāmeva teṣāmantaradhādatha || 55 ||

tadantare haimavatī devī divyavibhūṣaṇā |
āvirāsīnnabhoraṃge śobhamānā śucismitā || 56 ||

tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayāviṣṭā devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ |
praṇamya yakṣaṃ papracchuḥ ko .asau yakṣo vilakṣaṇaḥ || 57 ||

sā .abravītsasmitaṃ devī sa yuṣmākamagocaraḥ |
tenedaṃ bhramyate cakraṃ saṃsārākhyaṃ carācaram || 58 ||

tenādau kriyate viśvaṃ tena saṃhriyate punaḥ |
na tanniyantā kaścitsyāttena sarvaṃ niyamyate || 59 ||

ityuktvā sā mahādevī tatraivāntaradhatta vai |
devāśca vismitāḥ sarve tāṃ praṇamya divaṃ yayuḥ || 60 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṃḍe dvitīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 2 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śṛṇu kṛṣṇa maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
mūrtyātmabhistataṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagadetaccarācaram || 1 ||

sa śivassarvamevedaṃ svakīyābhiśca mūrtibhiḥ |
adhitiṣṭhatyameyātmā hyetatsarvamanusmṛtam || 2 ||

brahmā viṣṇustathā rudro maheśānassadāśivaḥ |
mūrttayastasya vijñeyā yābhirviśvamidaṃ tatam || 3 ||

athānyāścāpi tanavaḥ paṃca brahmasamāhvayāḥ |
tanūbhistābhirāvyāptamiha kiṃcinna vidyate || 4 ||

īśānaḥ puruṣo .aghoro vāmaḥ sadyastathaiva ca |
brahmāṇyetāni devasya mūrttayaḥ paṃca viśrutāḥ || 5 ||

īśānākhyā tu yā tasya mūrttirādyā garīyasī |
bhoktāraṃ prakṛteḥ sākṣātkṣetrajñamadhitiṣṭhati || 6 ||

sthāṇostatpuruṣākhyā yā mūrttirmūrttimataḥ prabhoḥ |
guṇāśrayātmakaṃ bhogyamavyaktamadhitiṣṭhati || 7 ||

dharmādyaṣṭāṃgasaṃyuktaṃ buddhitattvaṃ pinākinaḥ |
adhitiṣṭhatyaghorākhyā mūrttiratyantapūjitā || 8 ||

vāmadevāhvayāṃ mūrttiṃ mahādevasya vedhasaḥ |
ahaṃkṛteradhiṣṭhātrīmāhurāgamavedinaḥ || 9 ||

sadyo jātāhvayāṃ mūrttiṃ śambhoramitavarcasaḥ |
mānasaḥ samadhiṣṭhātrīṃ matimantaḥ pracakṣate || 10 ||

śrotrasya vācaḥ śabdasya vibhorvyomnastathaiva ca |
īśvarīmīśvarasyemāmīśākhyāṃ hi vidurbudhāḥ || 11 ||

tvakpāṇisparśavāyūnāmīśvarīṃ mūrtimaiśvarīm |
puruṣākhyaṃ vidussarve purāṇārthaviśāradāḥ || 12 ||

cakṣuṣaścaraṇasyāpi rūpasyāgnestathaiva ca |
aghorākhyāmadhiṣṭhātrīṃ mūrtimāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ || 13 ||

ramanāyāśca pāyośca rasasyāpāṃ tathaiva ca |
īśvarīṃ vāmadevākhyāṃ mūrttiṃ tanniratāṃ viduḥ || 14 ||

ghrāṇasya caivopasthasya gandhasya ca bhuvastathā |
sadyo jātāhvayāṃ mūrtimīśvarīṃ saṃpracakṣate || 15 ||

mūrtayaḥ paṃca devasya vandanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ |
śreyorthibhirnarairnityaṃ śreyasāmekahetavaḥ || 16 ||

tasya devādidevasya mūrttyaṣṭakamayaṃ jagat |
tasminvyāpya sthitaṃ viśvaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva || 17 ||

śarvo bhavastathā rudra ugro bhīmaḥ paśoḥ patiḥ |
īśānaśca mahādevo mūrttayaścāṣṭa viśrutāḥ || 18 ||

bhūmyaṃbhognimarudvyomakṣetrajñārkaniśākarāḥ |
adhiṣṭhitā maheśasya śarvādyairaṣṭamūrttibhiḥ || 19 ||

carācarātmakaṃ viśvaṃ dhatte viśvaṃbharātmikā |
śārvīrśivāhvayā mūrtiriti śāstrasya niścayaḥ || 20 ||

saṃjīvanaṃ samastasya jagatassalilātmikā |
bhāvīti gīyate mūrttibhavasya paramātmanaḥ || 21 ||

bahirantargatā viśvaṃ vyāpya tejomayī śubhā |
raudrī rudrāvyayā mūrtirāsthitā ghorarūpiṇī || 22 ||

spandayatyanilātmadaṃ bibharti spandate svayam |
augrīti kathyate sadbhirmūrtirugrasya vedhasaḥ || 23 ||

sarvāvakāśadā sarvavyāpikā gaganātmikā |
mūrtirbhīmasya bhīmākhyā bhūtavṛndasya bhedikā || 24 ||

sarvātmanāmadhiṣṭhātrī sarvakṣetranivāsinī |
mūrtiḥ paśupaterjñeyā paśupāśanikṛṃtanī || 25 ||

dīpayantī jagatsarvaṃ divākarasamāhvayā |
īśānākhyamaheśasya mūrtirdivi visarpati || 26 ||

āpyāyayati yo viśvamamṛtāṃśurniśākaraḥ |
mahādevasya sā mūrtirmahādevasamāhvayā || 27 ||

ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
vyāpiketaramūrtīnāṃ viśvaṃ tasmācchivātmakam || 28 ||

vṛkṣasya mūlasekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā |
śivasya pūjayā tadvatpuṣyatyasya vapurjagat || 29 ||

sarvābhayapradānaṃ ca sarvānugrahaṇaṃ tathā |
sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ śivasyārādhanaṃ viduḥ || 30 ||

yatheha putrapautrādeḥ prītyā prīto bhavetpitā |
tathā sarvasya saṃprītyā prīto bhavati śaṃkaraḥ || 31 ||

dehino yasya kasyāpi kriyate yadi nigrahaḥ |
aniṣṭamaṣṭamūrtestatkṛtameva na saṃśayaḥ || 32 ||

aṣṭamūrtyātmanā viśvamadhiṣṭhāya sthitaṃ śivam |
bhajasva sarvabhāvena rudraḥ paramakāraṇam || 33 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe tṛtīyo .adhyāyaḥ || 3 ||

kṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavanparameśasya śarvasyāmitatejasaḥ |
mūrtibhirviśvamevedaṃ yathā vyāptaṃ tathā śrutam || 1 ||

athaitajjñātumicchāmi yāthātmyaṃ pameśayoḥ |
strīpuṃbhāvātmakaṃ cedaṃ tābhyāṃ kathamadhiṣṭhitam || 2 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śrīmadvibhūtiṃ śivayoryāthātmyaṃ ca samāsataḥ |
vakṣye tadvistarādvaktuṃ bhavenāpi na śakyate || 3 ||

śaktiḥ sākṣānmahādevī mahādevaśca śaktimān |
tayorvibhūtileśo vai sarvametaccarācaram || 4 ||

vastu kiṃcidacidrūpaṃ kiṃcidvastu cidātmakam |
dvayaṃ śuddhamaśuddhaṃ ca paraṃ cāparameva ca || 5 ||

yatsaṃsarati ciccakramaciccakrasamanvitam |
tadevāśuddhamaparamitaraṃ tu paraṃ śubham || 6 ||

aparaṃ ca paraṃ caiva dvayaṃ cidacidātmakam |
śivasya ca śivāyāśca svāmyaṃ caitatsvabhāvataḥ || 7 ||

śivayorvai vaśe viśvaṃ na viśvasya vaśe śivau |
īśitavyamidaṃ yasmāttasmādviśveśvarau śivau || 8 ||

yathā śivastathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ |
nānayorantaraṃ vidyāccandracandrikayoriva || 9 ||

candro na khalu bhātyeṣa yathā candrikayā vinā |
na bhāti vidyamāno .api tathā śaktyā vinā śivaḥ || 10 ||

prabhayā hi vināyadvadbhānureṣa na vidyate |
prabhā ca bhānunā tena sutarāṃ tadupāśrayā || 11 ||

evaṃ parasparāpekṣā śaktiśaktimatoḥ sthitā |
na śivena vinā śaktirna śaktyā ca vinā śivaḥ || 12 ||

śaktauyayā śivo nityaṃ bhaktau muktau ca dehinām |
ādyā saikā parā śaktiścinmayī śivasaṃśrayā || 13 ||

yāmāhurakhileśasya taistairanuguṇairguṇaiḥ |
samānadharmiṇīmeva śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 14 ||

saikā parā ca cidrūpā śaktiḥ prasavadharmiṇī |
vibhajya bahudhā viśvaṃ vidadhāti śivecchayā || 15 ||

sā mūlaprakṛtirmāyā triguṇā ca tridhā smṛtā |
śivayā ca viparyastaṃ yayā tatamidaṃ jagat || 16 ||

ekadhā ca dvidhā caiva tathā śatasahasradhā |
śaktayaḥ khalu bhidyante bahudhā vyavahārataḥ || 17 ||

śivecchayā parāśaktiḥ śivatattvaikatāṃ gatā |
tataḥ parisphuratyādau sarge tailaṃ tilādiva || 18 ||

tataḥ kriyākhyayā śaktyā śaktau śaktimadutthayā |
tasyāṃ vikṣobhyamāṇāyāmādau nādaḥ samudbabhau || 19 ||

nādādviniḥsṛto bindurbindodevassadāśivaḥ |
tasmānmaheśvaro jātaḥ śuddhavidyā maheśvarāt || 20 ||

sā vācāmīśvarī śaktirvāgīśākhyā hi śūlinaḥ |
yā sā varṇasvarūpeṇa mātṛkepi vijṛmbhate || 21 ||

athānantasamāveśānmāyā kālamavāsṛjat |
niyatiñca kalāṃ vidyāṃ kalātorāgapūruṣau || 22 ||

māyātaḥ punarevābhūdavyaktaṃ triguṇātmakam |
triguṇācca tato vyaktādvibhaktāḥ syustrayo guṇāḥ || 23 ||

sattvaṃ rajastamaśceti yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat |
guṇebhyaḥ kṣobhyamāṇebhyo guṇeśākhyāstrimūrttayaḥ || 24 ||

abhavanmahadādīni tattvāni ca yathākramam |
tebhyassyuraṇḍapiṇḍāni tvasaṃkhyāni śivājñayā |
adhiṣṭhitānyanantādyairvidyeśaiścakravartibhiḥ || 25 ||

śarīrāntarabhedena śakterbhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
nānārūpāstu vijñeyāḥ sthūlasūkṣmavibhedataḥ || 26 ||

rudrasya raudrī sā śaktirviṣṇaurvai vaiṣṇavī matā |
brahmāṇī brahmaṇaḥ proktā cendrasyaindrīti kathyate || 27 ||

kimatra bahunoktena yadviśvamiti kīrtitam |
śakyātmanaiva tadvyāptaṃ yathā dehe .antarātmanā || 28 ||

tasmācchaktimayaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam |
kalā yā paramā śaktiḥ kathitā paramātmanaḥ || 29 ||

evameṣā parā śaktirīśvarecchānuyāyinī |
sthiraṃ caraṃ ca yadviśvaṃ sṛjatīti viniścayaḥ || 30 ||

jñānakriyā cikīrṣābhistisṛbhissvātmaśaktibhiḥ |
śaktimānīśvaraḥ śaśvadviśvaṃ vyāpyādhitiṣṭhati || 31 ||

idamitthamidaṃ netthaṃ bhavedityevamātmikā |
icchāśaktirmaheśasya nityā kāryyaniyāmikā || 32 ||

jñānaśaktistu tatkāryaṃ karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā |
prayojanaṃ ca tattvena buddhirūpādhyavasyati || 33 ||

yathepsitaṃ kriyāśaktiryathādhyavasitaṃ jagat |
kalpayatyakhilaṃ kāryaṃ kṣaṇātsaṃkalparūpiṇī || 34 ||

yathā śaktitrayotthānaṃ śaktiprasavadharmiṇī |
śaktyā paramayā nunnā prasūte sakalaṃ jagat || 35 ||

evaṃ śaktisamāyogācchaktimānucyate śivaḥ |
śaktiśaktimadutthaṃ tu śāktaṃ śaivamidaṃ jagat || 36 ||

yathā na jāyate putraḥ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ vinā |
tathā bhavaṃ bhavānīṃ ca vinā naitaccarācaram |
strīpuṃsaprabhavaṃ viśvaṃ strīpuṃsātmakameva ca // 37 || 37 ||

strīpuṃsayorvibhūtiśca strīpuṃsābhyāmadhiṣṭhitam |
paramātmā śivaḥ proktaśśivā sā ca prakīrtitā || 38 ||

śivassadāśivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca manonmanī |
śivo maheśvaro jñeyaḥ śivā māyeti kathyate || 39 ||

puruṣaḥ parameśānaḥ prakṛtiḥ parameśvarī |
rudro maheśvarassākṣādrudrāṇī rudravallabhā || 40 ||

viṣṇurviśveśvaro devo lakṣmīrviśveśvarapriyā |
brahmā śivo yadā sraṣṭā brahmāṇī brahmaṇaḥ priyā || 41 ||

bhāskaro bhagavāñchaṃbhuḥ prabhā bhagavatī śivā |
mahendro manmathārātiḥ śacī śailendrakanyakā || 42 ||

jātavedā mahādevaḥ svāhā śarvārddhadehinī |
yamastriyaṃbako devastatpriyā girikanyakā || 43 ||

nirṛtirbhagavānīśo nairṛtī naganandanī |
varuṇo bhagavānrudro vāruṇī bhūdharātmajā || 44 ||

bālenduśekharo vāyuḥ śivā śivamanoharā |
yakṣo yajñaśirohartā ṛddhirhimagirīndrajā || 45 ||

candrārdhaśekharaścandro rohiṇī rudravallabhā |
īśānaḥ parameśānastadāryā parameśvarī || 46 ||

anantavalayo .ananto hyanantānantavallabhā |
kālāgnirudraḥ kālāriḥ kālī kālāntakapriyā || 47 ||

puruṣākhyo manuśśaṃbhuḥ śatarūpā śivapriyā |
dakṣassākṣānmahādevaḥ prasūtiḥ parameśvarī || 48 ||

rucirbhavo bhavānī ca budhairākūtirucyate |
bhṛgurbhagākṣihā devaḥ khyātistrinayanapriyā || 49 ||

marīcibhagavānrudraḥ saṃbhūtiśśarvavallabhā |
gaṃgādharo .aṃgirā jñeyaḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣādumā smṛtā || 50 ||

pulastyaḥ śaśabhṛnmauliḥ prītiḥ kāntā pinākinaḥ |
pulahastripuradhvaṃsī tatpriyā tu śivapriyā || 51 ||

kratudhvaṃsī kratuḥ proktaḥ saṃnatirdayitā vibhoḥ |
trinetro .atrirumā sākṣādanasūyā smṛtā budhaiḥ || 52 ||

kaśyapaḥ kālahā devo devamātā maheśvarī |
vasiṣṭho manmathārātirdevī sākṣādarundhatī || 53 ||

śaṃkaraḥ puruṣāssarve striyassarvā maheśvarī |
sarve strīpuruṣāstasmāttayoreva vibhūtayaḥ || 54 ||

viṣayī bhagavānīśo viṣayaḥ parameśvarī |
śrāvyaṃ sarvamumārūpaṃ śrotā śūlavarāyudhaḥ || 55 ||

praṣṭavyaṃ vastujātaṃ tu dhatte śaṃkaravallabhā |
praṣṭā sa eva viśvātmā bālacandrāvataṃsakaḥ || 56 ||

draṣṭavyaṃ vasturūpaṃ tu bibhartti vaktavallabhā |
draṣṭā viśveśvaro devaḥ śaśikhaṃḍaśikhāmaṇiḥ || 57 ||

rasajātaṃ mahādevī devo rasayitā śivaḥ |
preyajātaṃ ca girijā preyāṃścaiva garāśanaḥ || 58 ||

mantavyavastutāṃ dhatte sadā devī maheśvarī |
mantā sa eva viśvātmā mahādevo maheśvaraḥ || 59 ||

boddhavyavasturūpaṃ tu bibhartti bhavavallabhā |
devassa eva bhagavānboddhā mugdhenduśekharaḥ || 60 ||

prāṇaḥ pinākī sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ bhagavānprabhuḥ |
prāṇasthitistu sarveṣāmaṃbikā cāṃburūpiṇī || 61 ||

bibharti kṣetratāṃ devī tripurāntakavallabhā |
kṣetrajñatvaṃ tadā dhatte bhagavānantakāntakaḥ || 62 ||

ahaḥ śūlāyudho devaḥ śūlapāṇipriyā niśā |
ākāśaḥ śaṃkaro devaḥ pṛthivī śaṃkarapriyā || 63 ||

samudro bhagavānīśo velā śailendrakanyakā |
vṛkṣo vṛṣadhvajo devo latā viśveśvarapriyā || 64 ||

puṃlliṃgamakhilaṃ dhatte bhagavānpuraśāsanaḥ |
striliṃgaṃ cākhilaṃ dhatte devī devamanoramā || 65 ||

śabdajālamaśeṣaṃ tu dhatte sarvasya vallabhā |
arthasvarūpamakhilaṃ dhatte mugdhenduśekharaḥ || 66 ||

yasya yasya padārthasya yā yā śaktirudāhṛtā |
sā sā viśveśvarī devī sa sa sarvo maheśvaraḥ || 67 ||

yatparaṃ yatpavitraṃ ca yatpuṇyaṃ yacca maṃgalam |
tattadāha mahābhāgāstayostejovijṛṃbhitam || 68 ||

yathā dīpasya dīptasya śikhā dīpayate gṛham |
tathā tejastayoretadvyāpya dīpayate jagat || 69 ||

tṛṇādiśivamūrtyantaṃ viśvakhyātiśayakramaḥ |
sannikarṣakramavaśāttayoriti parā śrutiḥ || 70 ||

sarvākārātmakāvetau sarvaśreyovidhāyinau |
pūjanīyau namaskāryau ciṃtanīyau ca sarvadā || 71 ||

yathāprajñamidaṃ kṛṣṇa yāthātmyaṃ parameśayoḥ |
kathitaṃ hi mayā te .adya na tu tāvadiyattayā || 72 ||

tatkathaṃ śakyate vaktuṃ yāthātmyaṃ parameśayoḥ |
mahatāmapi sarveṣāṃ manaso .api bahirgatam || 73 ||

antargatamananyānāmīśvarārpitacetasām |
anyeṣāṃ buddhyanārūḍhamārūḍhaṃ ca yathaiva tat || 74 ||

yeyamuktā vibhūtirvai prākṛtī sā parā matā |
aprākṛtāṃ parāmanyāṃ guhyāṃ guhyavido viduḥ || 75 ||

yato vāco nivarttante manasā cendriyaissaha |
aprākṛtī parā caiṣā vibhūtiḥ pārameśvarī || 76 ||

saiveha paramaṃ dhāma saiveha paramā gatiḥ |
saiveha paramā kāṣṭhā vibhūtiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ || 77 ||

tāṃ prāptuṃ prayatante .atra jitaśvāsā jitendriyāḥ |
garbhakārā gṛhadvāraṃ niśchidraṃ ghaṭituṃ yathā || 78 ||

saṃsārāśīviṣālīḍhamṛtasaṃjīvanauṣadham |
vibhūtiṃ śivayorvidvānna bibheti kutaścana || 79 ||

yaḥ parāmaparāṃ caiva vibhūtiṃ vetti tattvataḥ |
so .aparo bhūtimullaṃghya parāṃ bhūtiṃ samaśnute || 80 ||

etatte kathitaṃ kṛṣṇa yāthātmyaṃ paramātmanoḥ |
rahasyamapi yogyo .asi bhargabhakto bhavāniti || 81 ||

nāśiṣyebhyo .apyaśaivebhyo nābhaktebhyaḥ kadācana |
vyāharedīśayorbhūtimiti vedānuśāsanam || 82 ||

tasmāttvamatikalyāṇaparebhyaḥ kathayenna hi |
tvādṛśebhyo .anurūpebhyaḥ kathayaitanna cānyathā || 83 ||

vibhūtimetāṃ śivayoryogyebhyo yaḥ pradāpayet |
saṃsārasāgarānmuktaḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 84 ||

kīrtanādasya naśyanti mahāntyaḥ pāpakoṭayaḥ |
triścaturdhāsamabhyastairvinaśyanti tato .adhikāḥ || 85 ||

naśyantyaniṣṭaripavo varddhante suhṛdastathā |
vidyā ca varddhate śaivī matissatye pravartate || 86 ||

bhaktiḥ parāḥ śive sāmbe sānuge saparicchide |
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ cānyattattadāpnotyasaṃśayam || 87 ||

antaḥśuciḥ śive bhakto visrabdhaḥ kīrtayedyadi |
prabalaiḥ karmabhiḥ pūrvaiḥ phalaṃ cetpratibadhyate |
punaḥ punaḥ samabhyasyettasya nāstīha durllabham // 88 || 88 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe gaurīśaṃkaravibhūtiyogo nāma caturtho .adhyāyaḥ || 4 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

vigrahaṃ devadevasya viśvametaccarācaram |
tadevaṃ na vijānanti paśavaḥ pāśagauravāt || 1 ||

tamekameva bahudhā vadanti yadunandana |
ajānantaḥ paraṃ bhāvamavikalpaṃ maharṣayaḥ || 2 ||

aparaṃ brahmarūpaṃ ca paraṃ brahmātmakaṃ tathā |
kecidāhurmahādevamanādinidhanaṃ param || 3 ||

bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇapradhānaviṣayātmakam |
aparaṃ brahma nirdiṣṭaṃ paraṃ brahma cidātmakam || 4 ||

bṛhattvādbṛhaṇatvādvā brahma cetyabhidhīyate |
ubhe te brahmaṇo rūpe brahmaṇo .adhipateḥ prabhoḥ |
vidyā .avidyāsvarūpīti kaiścidīśo nigadyate // 5 || 5 ||

vidyāṃ tu cetanāṃ prāhustathāvidyāmacetanām |
vidyā .avidyātmakaṃ caiva viśvaṃ viśvagurorvibhoḥ || 6 ||

rūpameva na saṃdeho viśvaṃ tasya vaśe yataḥ |
bhrāntirvidyā parā ceti śārvaṃ rūpaṃ paraṃ viduḥ || 7 ||

ayathābuddhirartheṣu bahudhā bhrāntirucyate |
yathārthākārasaṃvittirvidyeti parikīrtyate || 8 ||

vikalparahitaṃ tattvaṃ paramityabhidhīyate |
vaiparītyādasacchabdaḥ kathyate vedavādibhiḥ || 9 ||

tayoḥ patitvāttu śivaḥ sadasatpatirucyate |
kṣarākṣarātmakaṃ prāhuḥ kṣarākṣaraparaṃ pare || 10 ||

kṣarassarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭastho .akṣara ucyate |
ubhe te parameśasya rūpe tasya vaśe yataḥ || 11 ||

tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣarākṣarāparassmṛtaḥ |
samaṣṭivyaṣṭhirūpaṃ ca samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam || 12 ||

vadanti munayaḥ kecicchivaṃ paramakāraṇam |
samaṣṭimāhuravyaktaṃ vyaṣṭiṃ vyaktaṃ tathaiva ca || 13 ||

te rūpe parameśasya tadicchāyāḥ pravartanāt |
tayoḥ kāraṇabhāvena śivaṃ paramakāraṇam || 14 ||

kāraṇārthavidaḥ prāhuḥ samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam |
jātivyaktisvarūpīti kathyate kaiścidīśvaraḥ || 15 ||

yā piṃḍepyanuvarteta sā jātiriti kathyate |
vyaktirvyāvṛttirūpaṃ taṃ piṇḍajāteḥ samāśrayam || 16 ||

jātayo vyaktayaścaiva tadājñāparipālitāḥ |
yatastato mahādevo jātivyaktivapuḥ smṛtaḥ || 17 ||

pradhānapuruṣavyaktakālātmā kathyate śivaḥ |
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ prāhuḥkṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ tathā || 18 ||

trayoviṃśatitattvāni vyaktamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ |
kālaḥ kāryyaprapaṃcasya pariṇāmaikakāraṇam || 19 ||

eṣāmīśo .adhipo dhātā pravartakanivartakaḥ |
āvirbhāvatirobhāvaheturekaḥ svarāḍajaḥ || 20 ||

tasmātpradhānapuruṣavyaktakālasvarūpavān |
heturnetādhipasteṣāṃ dhātā coktā maheśvaraḥ || 21 ||

virāḍḍhiraṇyagarbhātmā kaiścidīśo nigadyate |
hiraṇyagarbho lokānāṃ heturviśvātmako virāṭ || 22 ||

antaryāmī paraśceti kathyate kavibhiśśivaḥ |
prājñastaijasaviśvātmetyapare saṃpracakṣate || 23 ||

turīyamapare prāhuḥ saumyameva pare viduḥ |
mātā mānaṃ ca meyaṃ ca matiṃ cāhurathāpare || 24 ||

kartā kriyā ca kāryyaṃ ca karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ pare |
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptyātmetyapare saṃpracakṣate || 25 ||

turīyamapare prāhusturyātītamitītare |
tamāhurviguṇaṃ kecidguṇavantaṃ pare viduḥ || 26 ||

kecitsaṃsāriṇaṃ prāhustamasaṃsāriṇaṃ pare |
svatantramapare prāhurasvatantraṃ pare viduḥ || 27 ||

ghoramityapare prāhuḥ saumyameva pare viduḥ |
rāgavantaṃ pare prāhurvītarāgaṃ tathā pare || 28 ||

niṣkriyaṃ ca pare prāhuḥ sakriyaṃ cetare janāḥ |
nirindriyaṃ pare prāhuḥ sendriyaṃ ca tathāpare || 29 ||

dhruvamityapare prāhustamadhruvāmitīrate |
arūpaṃ kecidāhurvai rūpavantaṃ pare viduḥ || 30 ||

adṛśyamapare prāhurdṛśyamityapare viduḥ |
vācyamityapare prāhuravācyamiti cāpare |
śabdātmakaṃ pare prāhuśśabdātītamathāpare // 31 || 31 ||

keciccintāmayaṃ prāhuścintayā rahitaṃ pare |
jñānātmakaṃ pare prāhurvijñānamiti cāpare || 32 ||

kecicjñeyamiti prāhurajñeyamiti kecana |
parameke tamevāhuraparaṃ ca tathā pare || 33 ||

evaṃ vikalpyamānaṃ tu yāthātmyaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ |
nādhyavasyanti munayo nānāpratyayakāraṇāt || 34 ||

ye punassarvabhāvena prapannāḥ parameśvaram |
te hi jānantyayatnena śivaṃ paramakāraṇam || 35 ||

yāvatpaśurnaiva paśyatyanīśaṃ purāṇaṃ bhuvanasyeśitāram |
tāvadduḥkhe vartate baddhapāśaḥ saṃsāre .asmiñcakranemikrameṇa || 36 ||

yadā paśyaḥ paśyate rukmavarṇaṃ kartāramīśaṃ puruṣaṃ brahmayonim |
tadāvidvānpuṇyapāpe vidhūya niraṃjanaḥ paramamupaiti sāmyam || 37 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe paśupatitvajñānayogo nāma paṃcamo .adhyāyaḥ || 5 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

naśivasyāṇavo bandhaḥ kāryo māyeya eva vā |
prākṛto vātha boddhā vā hyahaṃkārātmakastathā || 1 ||

naivāsya mānaso bandho na caitto nendriyātmakaḥ |
na ca tanmātrabandho .api bhūtabandho na kaścana || 2 ||

na ca kālaḥ kalā caiva na vidyā niyatistathā |
na rāgo na ca vidveṣaḥ śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ || 3 ||

na cāstyabhiniveśo .asya kuśalā .akuśalānyapi |
karmāṇi tadvipākaśca sukhaduḥkhe ca tatphale || 4 ||

āśayairnāpi saṃbandhaḥ saṃskāraiḥ karmaṇāmapi |
bhogaiśca bhogasaṃskāraiḥ kālatritayagocaraiḥ || 5 ||

na tasya kāraṇaṃ kartā nādirantastathāntaram |
na karma karaṇaṃ vāpi nākāryaṃ kāryameva ca || 6 ||

nāsya bandhurabandhurvā niyantā prerako .api vā |
na patirna gurustrātā nādhiko na samastathā || 7 ||

na janmamaraṇe tasya na kāṃkṣitamakāṃkṣitam |
na vidhirna niṣedhaśca na muktirna ca bandhanam || 8 ||

nāsti yadyadakalyāṇaṃ tattadasya kadācana |
kalyāṇaṃ sakalaṃ cāsti paramātmā śivo yataḥ || 9 ||

sa śivassarvamevedamadhiṣṭhāya svaśaktibhiḥ |
apracyutassvato bhāvaḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇurataḥ smṛtaḥ || 10 ||

śivenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yasmājjagatsthāvarajaṃgamam |
sarvarūpaḥ smṛtaśśarvastathā jñātvā na muhyati || 11 ||

śarvo rudro namastasmai puruṣaḥ satparo mahān |
hiraṇyabāhurbhagavānhiraṇyapatirīśvaraḥ || 12 ||

aṃbikāpatirīśānaḥ pinākī vṛṣavāhanaḥ |
eko rudraḥ paraṃ brahma puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇapiṃgalaḥ || 13 ||

bālāgramātro hṛnmadhye viciṃtyo daharāntare |
hiraṇyakeśaḥ padmākṣo hyaruṇastāmra eva ca || 14 ||

yo .avasarpatya sau devo nīlagrīvo hiraṇmayaḥ |
saumyo ghorastathā miśraścākṣāraścāmṛto .avyayaḥ || 15 ||

sa puṃviśeṣaḥ paramo bhagavānantakāntakaḥ |
cetanacetanonmuktaḥ prapaṃcācca parātparaḥ || 16 ||

śivenātiśayatvena jñānaiśvarye vilokite |
lokeśātiśayatvena sthitaṃ prāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ || 17 ||

pratisargaprasūtānāṃ brahmaṇāṃ śāstravistaram |
upadeṣṭā sa evādau kālāvacchedavartinām || 18 ||

kālāvacchedayuktānāṃ gurūṇāmapyasau guruḥ |
sarveṣāmeva sarveśaḥ kālāvacchedavarjitaḥ || 19 ||

śuddhā svābhāvikī tasya śaktissarvātiśāyinī |
jñānamapratimaṃ nityaṃ vapuratyantanirmitam || 20 ||

aiśvaryamapratidvandvaṃ sukhamātyantikaṃ balam |
tejaḥprabhāvo vīryaṃ ca kṣamā kāruṇyameva ca || 21 ||

paripūrṇasya sargādyairnātmano .asti prayojanam |
parānugraha evāsya phalaṃ sarvasya karmaṇaḥ || 22 ||

praṇavo vācakastasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
śivarudrādiśabdānāṃ praṇavo hi parassmṛtaḥ || 23 ||

śaṃbho praṇavavācyasya bhavanāttajjapādapi |
yā siddhissā parā prāpyā bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 24 ||

tasmādekākṣaraṃ devamāhurāgamapāragāḥ |
vācyavācakayoraikyaṃ manyamānā manasvinaḥ || 25 ||

asya mātrāḥ samākhyātāścatasro vedamūrddhani |
akāraścāpyukāraśca makāro nāda ityapi || 26 ||

akāraṃ bahvṛcaṃ prāhurukāro yajurucyate |
makāraḥ sāmanādosya śrutirātharvaṇī smṛtāḥ || 27 ||

akāraśca mahābījaṃ rajaḥ sraṣṭā caturmukhaḥ |
ukāraḥ prakṛtiryoniḥ sattvaṃ pālayitā hariḥ || 28 ||

makāraḥ puruṣo bījaṃ tamaḥ saṃhārako haraḥ |
nādaḥ paraḥ pumānīśo nirguṇo niṣkriyaḥ śivaḥ || 29 ||

sarvaṃ tisṛbhirevedaṃ mātrābhirnikhilaṃ tridhā |
abhidhāya śivātmānaṃ bodhayatyardhamātrayā || 30 ||

yasmātparaṃ nāparamasti kiṃcidyasmānnāṇīyo na jyāyo .asti kiṃcit |
vṛkṣa iva stabdho divi tiṣṭhatyekastenedaṃ pūrṇaṃ puruṣeṇa sarvam || 31 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho .adhyāyaḥ || 6 ||

upamanyuruvaca

śaktissvābhavikī tasya vidyā viśvavilakṣaṇā |
ekānekasya rūpeṇa bhāti bhānoriva prabhā || 1 ||

anantāḥ śaktayo yasyā icchājñānakriyādayaḥ |
māyādyāścābhavanvahnorvisphuliṃgā yathā tathā || 2 ||

sadāśiveśvarādyā hi vidyā .avidyeśvarādayaḥ |
abhavanpuruṣāścāsyāḥ prakṛtiśca parātparā || 3 ||

mahadādiviśeṣāntāstvajādyāścāpi mūrttayaḥ |
yaccānyadasti tatsarvaṃ tasyāḥ kāryyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 4 ||

sā śaktissarvagā sūkṣmā prabodhānandarūpiṇī |
śaktimānucyate devaśśivaśśītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ || 5 ||

vedyaśśivaśśivā vidyā prajñā caiva śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ |
dhṛtireṣā sthitirniṣṭhā jñānecchākarmaśaktayaḥ || 6 ||

ājñā caiva paraṃ brahma dve vidye ca parāpare |
śuddhavidyā śuddhakalā sarvaṃ śaktikṛtaṃ yataḥ || 7 ||

māyā ca prakṛtirjīvo vikāro vikṛtistathā |
asacca sacca yatkiṃcittayā sarvamidaṃ tatam || 8 ||

sā devī māyayā sarvaṃ brahmāṃḍaṃ sacarācaram |
mohayatyaprayatnena mocayatyapi līlayā || 9 ||

anayā saha sarveśaḥ saptaviṃśaprakārayā |
viśvaṃ vyāpya sthitastasmānmuktiratra pravartate || 10 ||

mumukṣavaḥ purā kecinmunayo brahmavādinaḥ |
saṃśayāviṣṭamanaso vismṛśanti yathātatham || 11 ||

kiṃ kāraṇaṃ kuto jātā jīvāmaḥ kena vā vayam |
kutrāsmākaṃ saṃpratiṣṭhā kena vādhiṣṭhitā vayam || 12 ||

kena vartāmahe śaśvatsukheṣvanyeṣu cāniśam |
avilaṃghyā ca viśvasya vyavasthā kena vā kṛtā || 13 ||

kālasya bhāvo niyatiryadṛcchā nātra yujyate |
bhūtāni yoniḥ puruṣo yogī caiṣāṃ paro .atha vā || 14 ||

acetanatvātkālādeścetanatvepi cātmanaḥ |
sukhaduḥkhāni bhūtatvādanīśatvādvicāryate || 15 ||

taddhyānayogānugatāṃ prapaśyañchaktimaiśvarīm |
pāśavicchedikāṃ sākṣānnigūḍhāṃ svaguṇairbhṛśam || 16 ||

tayā vicchinnapāśāste sarvakāraṇakāraṇam |
śaktimantaṃ mahādevamapaśyandivyacakṣuṣā || 17 ||

yaḥ kāraṇānyaśeṣāṇi kālātmasahitāni ca |
aprameyo .anayā śaktyā sakalaṃ yo .adhitiṣṭhati || 18 ||

tataḥ prasādayogena yogena parameṇa ca |
dṛṣṭena bhaktiyogena divyaḥ gatimavāpnuyuḥ || 19 ||

tasmātsaha tathā śaktyā hṛdi paśyanti ye śivam |
teṣāṃ śāśvatikī śāntirnaitareṣāmiti śrutiḥ || 20 ||

na hi śaktimataśśaktyā viprayogo .asti jātucit |
tasmācchakteḥ śaktimatastādātmyānnirvṛtirdvayoḥ || 21 ||

kramo vivakṣito nūnaṃ vimuktau jñānakarmaṇoḥ |
prasāde sati sā mūrtiryasmātkaratale sthitā || 22 ||

devo vā dānavo vāpi paśurvā vihago .api vā |
kīro vātha kṛmirvāpi mucyate tatprasādataḥ || 23 ||

garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇo.pi vā |
vṛddho vā mriyamāṇo vā svargastho vātha nārakī || 24 ||

patito vāpi dharmātmā paṃḍito mūḍha eva vā |
prasāde tatkṣaṇādeva mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 25 ||

ayogyānāṃ ca kāruṇyādbhaktānāṃ parameśvaraḥ |
prasīdati na saṃdeho vigṛhya vividhānmalān || 26 ||

prasadādeva sā bhaktiḥ prasādo bhaktisaṃbhavaḥ |
avasthābhedamutprekṣya vidvāṃstatra na muhyati || 27 ||

prasādapūrvikā yeyaṃ bhuktimuktividhāyinī |
naiva sā śakyate prāptuṃ narairekena janmanā || 28 ||

anekajanmasiddhānāṃ śrautasmārtānuvartinām |
viraktānāṃ prabuddhānāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ || 29 ||

prasanne sati deveśa paśau tasminpravartate |
asti nātho mametyalpā bhaktirbuddhipurassarā || 30 ||

tapasā vividhaiśśaivairdharmaissaṃyujyate naraḥ |
tatra yoge tadabhyāsastato bhaktiḥ parā bhavet || 31 ||

parayā ca tayā bhaktyā prasādo labhyate paraḥ |
prasādātsarvapāśebhyo muktirmuktasya nirvṛtiḥ || 32 ||

alpabhāvo .api yo martyasso .api janmatrayātparam |
nayoniyantrapīḍāyai bhavennaivātra saṃśayaḥ || 33 ||

sāṃgā .anaṃgā ca yā sevā sā bhaktiriti kathyate |
sā punarbhidyate tredhā manovākkāyasādhanaiḥ || 34 ||

śivarūpādiciṃtā yā sā sevā mānasī smṛtā |
japādirvācikī sevā karmapūjādi kāyikī || 35 ||

seyaṃ trisādhanā sevā śivadharmaśca kathyate |
sa tu paṃcavidhaḥ proktaḥ śivena paramātmanā || 36 ||

tapaḥ karma japo dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ceti samāsataḥ |
karmaliGgārcanādyaṃ ca tapaścāndrāyaṇādikam || 37 ||

japastridhā śivābhyāsaścintā dhyānaṃ śivasya tu |
śivāgamoktaṃ yajjñānaṃ tadatra jñānamucyate || 38 ||

śrīkaṃṭhena śivenoktaṃ śivāyai ca śivāgamaḥ |
śivāśritānāṃ kāruṇyācchreyasāmekasādhanam || 39 ||

tasmādvivardhayedbhaktiṃ śive paramakāraṇe |
tyajecca viṣayāsaṃgaṃ śreyo .arthī matimānnaraḥ || 40 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivatattvakathanaṃ nāma saptamo .adhyāyaḥ || 7 ||

kṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavañchrotumicchāmi śivena paribhāṣitam |
vedasāre śivajñānaṃ svāśritānāṃ vimuktaye || 1 ||

abhaktānāmabuddhīnāmayuktānāmagocaram |
arthairdaśarddhaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ gūḍhamaprājñaninditam || 2 ||

varṇāśramakṛtairddharmairviparītaṃ kvacitsamam |
vedātṣaḍaṃgāduddhṛtya sāṃkhyādyogācca kṛtsnaśaḥ || 3 ||

śatakoṭipramāṇena vistīrṇaṃ granthasaṃkhyayā |
kathitaṃ parameśena tatra pūjā kathaṃ prabhoḥ || 4 ||

kasyādhikāraḥ pūjādau jñānayogādayaḥ katham |
tatsarvaṃ vistarādeva vaktumarhasi suvrata || 5 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śaivaṃ saṃkṣipya vedoktaṃ śivena paribhāṣitam |
stutinindādirahitaṃ sadyaḥ pratyayakāraṇam || 6 ||

guruprasādajaṃ divyamanāyāsena muktidam |
kathayiṣye samāsena tasya śakyo na vistaraḥ || 7 ||

sisṛkṣayā purāvyaktācchivaḥ sthāṇurmaheśvaraḥ |
satkāryakāraṇopetassvayamāvirabhūtprabhuḥ || 8 ||

janayāmāsa ca tadā ṛṣirviśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ |
devānāṃ prathamaṃ devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ brahmaṇaspatim || 9 ||

brahmāpi pitaraṃ devaṃ jāyamānaṃ nyavaikṣata |
taṃ jāyamānaṃ janako devaḥ prāpaśyadājñayā || 10 ||

dṛṣṭo rudreṇa devo .asāvasṛjadviśvamīśvaraḥ |
varṇāśramavyavasthāṃ ca cakāra sa pṛthakpṛthak || 11 ||

somaṃ sasarja yajñārthe somāddyaussamajāyata |
dharā ca vahniḥ sūryaśca yajño viṣṇuśśacīpatiḥ || 12 ||

te cānye ca surā rudraṃ rudrādhyāyena tuṣṭuvuḥ |
prasannavadanastasthau devānāmagrataḥ prabhuḥ || 13 ||

apahṛtya svalīlārthaṃ teṣāṃ jñānaṃ maheśvaraḥ |
tamapṛcchaṃstato devāḥ ko bhavāniti mohitāḥ || 14 ||

so .abravīdbhagavānrudro hyahamekaḥ purātanaḥ |
āsaṃ prathamamevāhaṃ vartāmi ca surottamāḥ || 15 ||

bhaviṣyāmi ca mattonyo vyatirikto na kaścana |
ahameva jagatsarvaṃ tarpayāmi svatejasā || 16 ||

matto .adhikaḥ samo nāsti māṃ yo veda sa mucyate |
ityuktvā bhagavānrudrastatraivāntaradhatta sa |
apaśyantastamīśānaṃ stuvantaścaiva sāmabhiḥ // 17 || 17 ||

vrataṃ pāśupataṃ kṛtvā tvatharvaśirasi sthitam |
bhasmasaṃchannasarvāṃgā babhūvuramarāstadā || 18 ||

atha teṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ paśūnāṃ patirīśvaraḥ // 19 |

sagaṇaścomayā sārddhaṃ sānnidhyamakarotprabhuḥ |
yaṃ vinidrā jitaśvāsā yogino dagdhakilbiṣāḥ || 20 ||

hṛdi paśyanti taṃ devaṃ dadṛśurdevapuṃgavāḥ |
yāmāhuḥ paramāṃ śaktimīśvarecchānuvartinīm || 21 ||

tāmapaśyanmaheśasya vāmato vāmalocanām |
ye vinirdhūtasaṃsārāḥ prāptāḥ śaivaṃ paraṃ padam || 22 ||

nityasiddhāśca ye vānyaṃ te ca dṛṣṭā gaṇeśvarāḥ |
atha taṃ tuṣṭuvurdevā devyā saha maheśvaram || 23 ||

stotrairmāheśvarairdivyaiḥ śrotaiḥ paurāṇikairapi |
devo .api devānālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ || 24 ||

tuṣṭo .asmītyāha suprītassvabhāvamadhurāṃ giram |
atha suprītamanasaṃ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam |
arthamahattamaṃ devāḥ papracchurimamādarāt // 25 || 25 ||

devā ūcuḥ |

bhagavankena mārgeṇa pūjanīyo .asi bhūtale |
kasyādhikāraḥ pūjāyāṃ vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ || 26 ||

tataḥ sasmitamālokya devīṃ devavaroharaḥ |
svarūpaṃ darśayāmāsa ghoraṃ sūryātmakaṃ param || 27 ||

sarvaiśvaryaguṇopetaṃ sarvatejomayaṃ param |
śaktibhirmūrtibhiścāṃgairgrahairdevaiśca saṃvṛtam || 28 ||

aṣṭabāhuṃ caturvaktramarddhanārīkamadbhutam |
dṛṣṭvaivamadbhutākāraṃ devā viṣṇupurogamāḥ || 29 ||

buddhvā divākaraṃ devaṃ devīṃ caiva niśākaram |
pañcabhūtāni śeṣāṇi tanmayaṃ ca carācaram || 30 ||

evamuktvā namaścakrustasmai cārghyaṃ pradāya vai || 31 ||

sindūravarṇāya sumaṇḍalāya suvarṇavarṇābharaṇāya tubhyam |
padmābhanetrāya sapaṃkajāya brahmendranārāyaṇakāraṇāya || 32 ||

suratnapūrṇaṃ sasuvarṇatoyaṃ sukuṃkumādyaṃ sakuśaṃ sapuṣpam |
pradattamādāya sahemapātraṃ praśastamarghyaṃ bhagavanprasīda || 33 ||

namaśśivāya śāntāya sagaṇāyādihetave |
rudrāya viṣṇave tubhyaṃ brahmaṇe sūryamūrtaye || 34 ||

yaśśivaṃ maṇḍale saure saṃpūjyaiva samāhitaḥ |
prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhne pradadyādarghyamuttamam || 35 ||

praṇamedvā paṭhedetāñchlokāñchrutimukhānimān |
na tasya durllabhaṃ kiṃcidbhaktaścenmucyate dṛḍham || 36 ||

tasmādabhyarcayenityaṃ śivamādityarūpiṇam |
dharmakāmārthamuktyarthaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā || 37 ||

atha devānsamālokya maṇḍalastho maheśvaraḥ |
sarvāgamottaraṃ dattvā śāstramantaradhāddharaḥ || 38 ||

tatra pūjādhikāro .ayaṃ brahmakṣatraviśāmiti |
jñātvā praṇamya deveśaṃ devā jagmuryathāgatam || 39 ||

atha kālena mahatā tasmiñchāstre tirohite |
bhartāraṃ paripapraccha tadaṃkasthā maheśvarī || 40 ||

tayā sa codito devo devyā candravibhūṣaṇaḥ |
avadatkaramuddhṛtya śāstraṃ sarvāgamottaram || 41 ||

pravartitaṃ ca talloke niyogātparameṣṭhinaḥ |
mayāgastyena guruṇā dadhīcena maharṣiṇā || 42 ||

svayamapyavatīryorvyāṃ yugāvarteṣu śūladhṛk |
svāśritānāṃ vimuktyarthaṃ kurute jñānasantatim || 43 ||

ṛbhussatyo bhārgavaśca hyaṃgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ |
mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmānvasiṣṭho munipuṃgavaḥ || 44 ||

sārasvatastridhāmā ca trivṛto munipuṃgavaḥ |
śatatejāssvayaṃ dharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ || 45 ||

svarakṣaścāruṇirdhīmāṃstathā caiva kṛtaṃjayaḥ |
kṛtaṃjayo bharadvājo gautamaḥ kaviruttamaḥ || 46 ||

vācaḥsravā munissākṣāttathā sūkṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ |
tṛṇabindurmuniḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ || 47 ||

jātūkarṇyo harissākṣātkṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ |
vyāsāvatārāñchṛṇvantu kalpayogeśvarānkramāt || 48 ||

laiṃge vyāsāvatārā hi dvāparāṃ teṣu suvratāḥ |
yogācāryāvatārāśca tathā śiṣyeṣu śūlinaḥ || 49 ||

tatra tatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāścatvāraḥ syurmahaujasaḥ |
śiṣyāsteṣāṃ praśiṣyāśca śataśo .atha sahasraśaḥ || 50 ||

teṣāṃ saṃbhāvanālloke śaivājñākaraṇādibhiḥ |
bhāgyavanto vimucyante bhaktyā cātyantabhāvitāḥ || 51 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivatattvajñāne vyāsāvatāravarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭamo .adhyāyaḥ || 8 ||

kṛṣṇa uvāca |

yugāvarteṣu sarveṣu yogācāryacchalena tu |
avatārānhi śarvasya śiṣyāṃśca bhagavanvada || 1 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śvetaḥ sutāro madanaḥ suhotraḥ kaGka eva ca |
laugākṣiśca mahāmāyo jaigīṣavyastathaiva ca || 2 ||

dadhivāhaśca ṛṣabho munirugro .atrireva ca |
supālako gautamaśca tathā vedaśirā muniḥ || 3 ||

gokarṇaśca guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍī cāparaḥ smṛtaḥ |
jaṭāmālī cāṭṭahāso dāruko lāṃgulī tathā || 4 ||

mahākālaśca śūlī ca ḍaṃḍī muṇḍīśa eva ca |
saviṣṇussomaśarmā ca lakulīśvara eva ca || 5 ||

ete vārāha kalpe .asminsaptamasyāntaro manoḥ |
aṣṭāviṃśatisaṃkhyātā yogācāryā yugakramāt || 6 ||

śiṣyāḥ pratyekameteṣāṃ catvāraśśāntacetasaḥ |
śvetādayaśca ruṣyāntāṃstānbravīmi yathākramam || 7 ||

śvetaśśvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ |
dundubhiśśatarūpaśca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstathā || 8 ||

vikośaśca vikeśaśca vipāśaḥ pāśanāśanaḥ |
sumukho durmukhaścaiva durgamo duratikramaḥ || 9 ||

sanatkumārassanakaḥ sanandaśca sanātanaḥ |
sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṃkhaścāṃḍaja eva ca || 10 ||

sārasvataśca meghaśca meghavāhassuvāhakaḥ |
kapilaścāsuriḥ paṃcaśikho bāṣkala eva ca || 11 ||

parāśarāśca gargaśca bhārgavaścāṃgirāstathā |
balabandhurnirāmitrāḥ ketuśṛṃgastapodhanaḥ || 12 ||

laṃbodaraśca laṃbaśca lambātmā laṃbakeśakaḥ |
sarvajñassamabuddhiśca sādhyasiddhistathaiva ca || 13 ||

sudhāmā kaśyapaścaiva vasiṣṭho virajāstathā |
atrirugro guruśreṣṭhaḥ śravanotha śraviṣṭakaḥ || 14 ||

kuṇiśca kuṇibāhuśca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ |
kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavanaśca bṛhaspatiḥ || 15 ||

utathyo vāmadevaśca mahākālo mahā .anilaḥ |
vācaḥśravāḥ suvīraśca śyāvakaśca yatīśvaraḥ || 16 ||

hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣiḥ kuthumistathā |
sumanturjaiminiścaiva kubandhaḥ kuśakandharaḥ || 17 ||

plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumāngautamastathā |
bhallavī madhupiṃgaśca śvetaketustathaiva ca || 18 ||

uśijo bṛhadaśvaśca devalaḥ kavireva ca |
śālihotraḥ suveṣaśca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ || 19 ||

akṣapādaḥ kaṇādaśca ulūko vatsa eva ca |
kulikaścaiva gargaśca mitrako ruṣya eva ca || 20 ||

ete śiṣyā maheśasya yogācāryasvarūpiṇaḥ |
saṃkhyā ca śatameteṣāṃ saha dvādaśasaṃkhyayā || 21 ||

sarve pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ |
sarvaśāstrārthatattvajñā vedavedāṃgapāragāḥ || 22 ||

śivāśramaratāssarve śivajñānaparāyaṇāḥ |
sarve saṃgavinirmuktāḥ śivaikāsaktacetasaḥ || 23 ||

sarvadvandvasahā dhīrāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ |
ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svasthā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ || 24 ||

rudrākṣamālābharaṇāstripuṃḍrāṃkitamastakāḥ |
śikhājaṭāssarvajaṭā ajaṭā muṃḍaśīrṣakāḥ || 25 ||

phalamūlāśanaprāyāḥ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ |
śivābhimānasaṃpannāḥ śivadhyānaikatatparāḥ || 26 ||

samunmathitasaṃsāraviṣavṛkṣāṃkurodgamāḥ |
prayātumeva sannaddhāḥ paraṃ śivapuraṃ prati || 27 ||

sadeśikānimānmatvā nityaṃ yaśśivamarcayet |
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 28 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpu.. saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivasya yogāvatāravarṇanaṃ nāma navamo .adhyāyaḥ || 9 ||

kṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavansarvayogīndra gaṇeśvara munīśvara |
ṣaḍānanasamaprakhya sarvajñānanidhe guro || 1 ||

prāyastvamavatīryorvyāṃ pāśavicchittaye nṛṇām |
maharṣivapurāsthāya sthito .asi parameśvara || 2 ||

anyathā hi jagatyasmin devo vā dānavo .api vā |
tvattonyaḥ paramaṃ bhāvaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam || 3 ||

tasmāttava mukhodgīrṇaṃ sākṣādiva pinākinaḥ |
śivajñānāmṛtaṃ pītvā na me tṛptamabhūnmanaḥ || 4 ||

sākṣātsarvajagatkarturbharturaṃkaṃ samāśritā |
bhagavankinnu papraccha bhartāraṃ parameśvarī || 5 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

sthāne pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇa tadvakṣyāmi yathātatham |
bhavabhaktasya yuktasya tava kalyāṇacetasaḥ || 6 ||

mahīdharavare divye mandare cārukandare |
devyā saha mahādevo divyo dhyānagato .abhavat || 7 ||

tadā devyāḥ priyasakhī susmitāsyā śubhāvatī |
phullānyatimanojñāni puṣpāṇi samudāharat || 8 ||

tataḥ svamaṃkamāropya devīṃ devavarorahaḥ |
alaṃkṛtya ca taiḥ puṣpairāste hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam || 9 ||

athāntaḥpuracāriṇyo devyo divyavibhūṣaṇāḥ |
antaraṃgā gaṇendrāśca sarvalokamaheśvarīm || 10 ||

bhartāraṃ paripūrṇaṃ ca sarvalokamaheśvaram |
cāmarāsaktahastāśca devīṃ devaṃ siṣevire || 11 ||

tataḥ priyāḥ kathā vṛttā vinodāya maheśayoḥ |
trāṇāya ca nṛṇāṃ loke ye śivaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ || 12 ||

tadāvasaramālokya sarvalokamaheśvarī |
bhartāraṃ paripapraccha sarvalokamaheśvaram || 13 ||

devyuvāca |

kena vaśyo mahādevo martyānāṃ mandacetasām |
ātmatattvādyaśaktānāmātmanāmakṛtātmanām || 14 ||

īśvara uvāca |

na karmaṇā na tapasā na japairnāsanādibhiḥ |
na jñānena na cānyena vaśyo .ahaṃ śraddhayā vinā || 15 ||

śraddhā mayyasti cetpuṃsāṃ yena kenāpi hetunā |
vaśyaḥ spṛśyaśca dṛśyaśca pūjyassaṃbhāṣya eva ca || 16 ||

sādhyā tasmānmayi śaddhā māṃ vaśīkartumicchatā |
śraddhā hetussvadharmasya rakṣaṇaṃ varṇināmiha || 17 ||

svavarṇāśramadharmeṇa vartate yastu mānavaḥ |
tasyaiva bhavati śraddhā mayi nānyasya kasyacit || 18 ||

āmnāyasiddhamakhilaṃ dharmamāśramiṇāmiha |
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ mamaivājñāpurassaram || 19 ||

sa tu paitāmaho dharmo bahuvittakriyānvitaḥ |
nātyanta phalabhūyiṣṭhaḥ kleśāyā sasamanvitaḥ |
tena dharmeṇa mahatāṃ śraddhāṃ prāpya sudurllabhām // 20 || 20 ||

varṇino ye prapadyante māmananyasamāśrayāḥ |
teṣāṃ sukhena mārgeṇa dharmakāmārthamuktayaḥ || 21 ||

varṇāśramasamācāro mayā bhūyaḥ prakalpitaḥ |
tasminbhaktimatāmeva madīyānāṃ tu varṇinām || 22 ||

adhikāro na cānyeṣāmityājñā naiṣṭhikī mama |
tadājñaptena mārgeṇa varṇino madupāśrayāḥ || 23 ||

malamāyādipāśebhyo vimuktā matprasādataḥ |
paraṃ madīyamāsādya punarāvṛttidurlabham |
paramaṃ mama sādharmyaṃ prāpya nirvṛtimāyayuḥ // 24 || 24 ||

tasmāllabdhvāpyalabdhvā vā varṇadharmaṃ mayeritam |
āśritya mama bhaktaścetsvātmanātmānamuddharet || 25 ||

alabdhalābha evaiṣa koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ |
tasmānme mukhato labdhaṃ varṇadharmaṃ samācaret || 26 ||

mamāvatārā hi śubhe yogācāryacchalena tu |
sarvāntareṣu santyārye santatiśca sahasraśaḥ || 27 ||

ayuktānāmabuddhīnāmabhaktānāṃ sureśvari |
durlabhaṃ santatijñānaṃ tato yatnātsamāśrayet || 28 ||

sā hānistanmahacchidraṃ sa mohassāndhamūkatā |
yadanyatra śramaṃ kuryyānmokṣamārgabahiṣkṛtaḥ || 29 ||

jñānaṃ kriyā ca caryā ca yogaśceti sureśvari |
catuṣpādaḥ samākhyāto mama dharmassanātanaḥ || 30 ||

paśupāśapatijñānaṃ jñānamityabhidhīyate |
ṣaḍadhvaśuddhirvidhinā gurvadhīnā kriyocyate || 31 ||

varṇāśramaprayuktasya mayaiva vihitasya ca |
mamārccanādidharmasya caryyā caryyeti kathyate || 32 ||

maduktenaiva mārgeṇa mayyavasthitacetasaḥ |
vṛttyantaranirodho yo yoga ityabhidhīyate || 33 ||

aśvamedhagaṇācchreṣṭhaṃ devi cittaprasādhanam |
muktidaṃ ca tathā hyetadduṣprāpyaṃ viṣayaiṣiṇām || 34 ||

vijitendriyavargasya yamena niyamena ca |
pūrvapāpaharo yogo viraktasyaiva kathyate || 35 ||

vairāgyājjāyate jñānaṃ jñānādyogaḥ pravartate || 36 ||

yogajñaḥ patito vāpi mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |
dayā kāryātha satatamahiṃsā jñānasaṃgrahaḥ || 37 ||

satyamasteyamāstikyaṃ śraddhā cendriyanigrahaḥ |
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ yājanaṃ tathā || 38 ||

dhyānamīśvarabhāvaśca satataṃ jñānaśīlatā |
ya evaṃ varttate vipro jñānayogasya siddhaye || 39 ||

acirādeva vijñānaṃ labdhvā yogaṃ ca vindati |
dagdhvā dehamimaṃ jñānī kṣaṇājjñānāgninā priye || 40 ||

prasādānmama yogajñaḥ karmabandhaṃ prahāsyati |
puṇyaḥpuṇyātmakaṃ karmamuktestatpratibandhakam |
tasmānniyogato yogī puṇyāpuṇyaṃ vivarjayet // 41 || 41 ||

phalakāmanayā karmakaraṇātpratibadhyate |
na karmamātrakaraṇāttasmātkarmaphalaṃ tyajet || 42 ||

prathamaṃ karmayajñena bahiḥ sampūjya māṃ priye |
jñānayogarato bhūtvā paścādyogaṃ samabhyaset || 43 ||

vidite mama yāthātmye karmayajñena dehinaḥ |
na yajanti hi māṃ yuktāḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāṃcanāḥ || 44 ||

nityayukto muniḥ śreṣṭho madbhaktaśca samāhitaḥ |
jñānayogarato yogī mama sāyujyamāpnuyāt || 45 ||

athāviraktacittā ye varṇino madupāśritāḥ |
jñānacaryākriyāsveva te .adhikuryyustadarhakāḥ || 46 ||

dvidhā matpūjanaṃ jñeyaṃ bāhyamābhyantaraṃ tathā |
vāGmanaḥkāyabhedācca tridhā madbhajanaṃ viduḥ || 47 ||

tapaḥ karma japo dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ vetyanupūrvaśaḥ |
paṃcadhā kathyate sadbhistadeva bhajanaṃ punaḥ || 48 ||

anyātmaviditaṃ bāhyamasmadabhyarcanādikam |
tadeva tu svasaṃvedyamābhyantaramudāhṛtam || 49 ||

manomatpravaṇaṃ cittaṃ na manomātramucyate |
mannāmaniratā vāṇī vāGmatā khalu netarā || 50 ||

liṃgairmacchāsanādiṣṭaistripuṃḍrādibhiraṃkitaḥ |
mamopacāranirataḥ kāyaḥ kāyo na cetaraḥ || 51 ||

madarcākarma vijñeyaṃ bāhye yāgādinocyate |
madarthe dehasaṃśoṣastapaḥ kṛcchrādi no matam || 52 ||

japaḥ paṃcākṣarābhyāsaḥ praṇavābhyāsa eva ca |
rudrādhyāyādikābhyāso na vedādhyayanādikam || 53 ||

dhyānammadrūpaciṃtādyaṃ nātmādyarthasamādhayaḥ |
mamāgamārthavijñānaṃ jñānaṃ nānyārthavedanam || 54 ||

bāhye vābhyantare vātha yatra syānmanaso ratiḥ |
prāgvāsanāvaśāddevi tattvaniṣṭhāṃ samācaret || 55 ||

bāhyādābhyantaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhavecchataguṇādhikam |
asaṃkaratvāddoṣāṇāṃ dṛṣṭānāmapyasambhavāt || 56 ||

śaucamābhyantaraṃ vidyānna bāhyaṃ śaucamucyate |
antaḥ śaucavimuktātmā śucirapyaśuciryataḥ || 57 ||

bāhyamābhyantaraṃ caiva bhajanaṃ bhavapūrvakam |
na bhāvarahitaṃ devi vipralaṃbhaikakāraṇam || 58 ||

kṛtakṛtyasya pūtasya mama kiṃ kriyate naraiḥ |
bahirvābhyantaraṃ vātha mayā bhāvo hi gṛhyate || 59 ||

bhāvaikātmā kriyā devi mama dharmassanātanaḥ |
manasā karmaṇā vācā hyanapekṣya phalaṃ kvacit || 60 ||

phaloddeśena deveśi laghurmama samāśrayaḥ |
phalārthī tadabhāve māṃ parityaktuṃ kṣamo yataḥ || 61 ||

phalārthino .api yasyaiva mayi cittaṃ pratiṣṭhitam |
bhāvānurūpaphaladastasyāpyahamanindite || 62 ||

phalānapekṣayā yeṣāṃ mano matpravaṇaṃ bhavet |
prārthayeyuḥ phalaṃ paścādbhaktāste .api mama priyāḥ || 63 ||

prāk saṃskāravaśādeva ye viciṃtya phalāphale |
vivaśā māṃ prapadyante mama priyatamā matāḥ || 64 ||

mallābhānna paro lābhasteṣāmasti yathātatham |
mamāpi lābhastallābhānnāparaḥ parameśvari || 65 ||

madanugrahatasteṣāṃ bhāvo mayi samarpitaḥ |
phalaṃ paramanirvāṇaṃ prayacchati balādiva || 66 ||

mahātmanāmananyānāṃ mayi saṃnyastacetasām |
aṣṭadhā lakṣaṇaṃ prāhurmama dharmādhikāriṇām || 67 ||

madbhaktajanavātsalyaṃ pūjāyāṃ cānumodanam |
svayamabhyarcanaṃ caiva madarthe cāṃgaceṣṭitam || 68 ||

matkathāśravaṇe bhaktiḥ svaranetrāṃgavikriyāḥ |
mamānusmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ yaśca māmupajīvati || 69 ||

evamaṣṭavidhaṃ cihnaṃ yasmin mlecche .api vartate |
sa viprendro muniḥ śrīmānsa yatissa ca paṃḍitaḥ || 70 ||

na me priyaścaturvedī madbhakto śvapaco .api yaḥ |
tasmai deyaṃ tato grāhyaṃ sa ca pūjyo yathā hyaham || 71 ||

patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati |
tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati || 72 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivabhaktivarṇanaṃ nāma daśamo .adhyāyaḥ || 10 ||

īśvara uvāca |

atha vakṣyāmi deveśi bhaktānāmadhikāriṇām |
viduṣāṃ dvijamukhyānāṃ varṇadharmasamāsataḥ || 1 ||

triḥ snānaṃ cāgnikāryaṃ ca liṃgārcanamanukramam |
dānamīśrarabhāvaśca dayā sarvatra sarvadā || 2 ||

satyaṃ santoṣamāstikyamahiṃsā sarvajantuṣu |
hrīśraddhādhyayanaṃ yogassadādhyāpanameva ca || 3 ||

vyākhyānaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca śravaṇaṃ ca tapaḥ kṣamā |
śaucaṃ śikhopavītaṃ ca uṣṇīṣaṃ cottarīyakam || 4 ||

niṣiddhāsevanaṃ caiva bhasmarudrākṣadhāraṇam |
parvaṇyabhyarcanaṃ devi caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ || 5 ||

pānaṃ ca brahmakūrcasya māsi māsi yathāvidhi |
abhyarcanaṃ viśeṣeṇa tenaiva snāpya māṃ priye || 6 ||

sarvakriyānna santyāgaḥ śraddhānnasya ca varjanam |
tathā paryuṣitānnasya yāvakasya viśeṣataḥ || 7 ||

madyasya madyagandhasya naivedyasya ca varjanam |
sāmānyaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ || 8 ||

kṣamā śāntiśca santoṣassatyamasteyameva ca |
brahmacaryaṃ mama jñānaṃ vairāgyaṃ bhasmasevanam || 9 ||

sarvasaṃganivṛttiśca daśaitāni viśeṣataḥ |
liṃgāni yogināṃ bhūyo divā bhikṣāśanaṃ tathā || 10 ||

vānaprasthāśramasthānāṃ samānamidamiṣyate |
rātrau na bhojanaṃ kāryaṃ sarveṣāṃ brahmacāriṇām || 11 ||

adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca kṣatriyasyāpratigrahaḥ |
vaiśyasya ca viśeṣeṇa mayā nātra vidhīyate || 12 ||

rakṣaṇaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ yuddhe śatruvadhastathā |
duṣṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca duṣṭānāṃ śātanaṃ nṛṇām || 13 ||

aviśvāsaśca sarvatra viśvāso mama yogiṣu |
strīsaṃsargaśca kāleṣu camūrakṣaṇameva ca || 14 ||

sadā saṃcāritaiścārairlokavṛttāntavedanam |
sadāstradhāraṇaṃ caiva bhasmakaṃcukadhāraṇam || 15 ||

rājñāṃ mamāśramasthānāmeṣa dharmasya saṃgrahaḥ |
gorakṣaṇaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ kṛṣirvaiśyasya kathyate || 16 ||

śuśrūṣetaravarṇānāṃ dharmaḥ śūdrasya kathyate |
udyānakaraṇaṃ caiva mama kṣetrasamāśrayaḥ || 17 ||

dharmapatnyāstu gamanaṃ gṛhasthasya vidhīyate |
brahmacaryaṃ vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām || 18 ||

strīṇāṃ tu bhartṛśuśrūṣā dharmo nānyassanātanaḥ |
mamārcanaṃ ca kalyāṇi niyogo bharturasti cet || 19 ||

yā nārī bhartṛśuśrūṣāṃ vihāya vratatatparā |
sā nārī narakaṃ yāti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 20 ||

atha bhartṛvihīnāyā vakṣye dharmaṃ sanātanam |
vrataṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śaucaṃ bhūśayyānaktabhojanam || 21 ||

brahmacaryaṃ sadā snānaṃ bhasmanā salilena vā |
śāntirmaunaṃ kṣamā nityaṃ saṃvibhāgo yathāvidhi || 22 ||

aṣṭābhyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ |
ekādaśyāṃ ca vidhivadupavāsomamārcanam || 23 ||

iti saṃkṣepataḥ prokto mayāśramaniṣeviṇām |
brahmakṣatraviśāṃ devi yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām || 24 ||

tathaiva vānaprasthānāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ca sundari |
śūdrāṇāmatha nārīṇāṃ dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ || 25 ||

dhyeyastvayāhaṃ deveśi sadā jāpyaḥ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ |
vedoktamakhilaṃ dharmamiti dharmārthasaṃgrahaḥ || 26 ||

atha ye mānavā loke svecchayā dhṛtavigrahāḥ |
bhāvātiśayasaṃpannāḥ pūrvasaṃskārasaṃyutāḥ || 27 ||

viraktā vānuraktā vā stryādīnāṃ viṣayeṣvapi |
pāpairna te viliṃpante padmapatramivāṃbhasā || 28 ||

teṣāṃ mamātmavijñānaṃ viśuddhānāṃ vivekinām |
matprasādādviśuddhānāṃ duḥkhamāśramarakṣaṇāt || 29 ||

nāsti kṛtyamakṛtyaṃ ca samādhirvā parāyaṇam |
na vidhirna niṣedhaśca teṣāṃ mama yathā tathā || 30 ||

tatheha paripūrṇasya sādhyaṃ mama na vidyate |
tathaiva kṛtakṛtyānāṃ teṣāmapi na saṃśayaḥ || 31 ||

madbhaktānāṃ hitārthāya mānuṣaṃ bhāvamāśritāḥ |
rudralokātparibhraṣṭāste rudrā nātra saṃśayaḥ || 32 ||

mamānuśāsanaṃ yadvadbrahmādīnāṃ pravartakam |
tathā narāṇāmanyeṣāṃ tanniyogaḥ pravartakaḥ || 33 ||

mamājñādhārabhāvena sadbhāvātiśayena ca |
tadālokanamātreṇa sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet || 34 ||

pratyayāśca pravartante praśastaphalasūcakāḥ |
mayi bhāvavatāṃ puṃsāṃ prāgadṛṣṭārthagocarāḥ || 35 ||

kaṃpasvedo .aśrupātaśca kaṇṭhe ca svaravikriyā |
ānandādyupalabdhiśca bhavedākasmikī muhuḥ || 36 ||

sa tairvyastaissamastairvā liṃgairavyabhicāribhiḥ |
mandamadhyottamairbhāvairvijñeyāste narottamāḥ || 37 ||

yathāyognisamāveśānnāyo bhavati kevalam |
sa tathaiva mama sānnidhyānna te kevalamānuṣāḥ || 38 ||

hastapādādisādharmyādrudrānmartyavapurdharān |
prākṛtāniva manvāno nāvajānīta paṃḍitaḥ || 39 ||

avajñānaṃ kṛtaṃ teṣu narairvyāmūḍhacetanaiḥ |
āyuḥ śriyaṃ kulaṃ śīlaṃ hitvā nirayamāvahet || 40 ||

brahmaviṣṇusureśānāmapi tūlāyate padam |
mattonyadanapekṣāṇāmuddhṛtānāṃ mahātmanām || 41 ||

aśuddhaṃ bauddhamaiśvaryaṃ prākṛtaṃ pauruṣaṃ tathā |
guṇeśānāmatastyājyaṃ guṇātītapadaiṣiṇām || 42 ||

atha kiṃ bahunoktena śreyaḥ prāptyaikasādhanam |
mayi cittasamāsaṃgo yena kenāpi hetunā || 43 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

itthaṃ śrīkaṇṭhanāthena śivena paramātmanā |
hitāya jagatāmukto jñānasārārthasaṃgrahaḥ || 44 ||

vijñānasaṃgrahasyāsya vedaśāstrāṇi kṛtsnaśaḥ |
setihāsapurāṇāni vidyā vyākhyānavistaraḥ || 45 ||

jñānaṃ jñeyamanuṣṭheyamadhikāro .atha sādhanam |
sādhyaṃ ceti ṣaḍarthānāṃ saṃgrahatveṣa saṃgrahaḥ || 46 ||

guroradhikṛtaṃ jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ pāśaḥ paśuḥ patiḥ |
liṃgārcanādyanuṣṭheyaṃ bhaktastvadhikṛto .api yaḥ || 47 ||

sādhanaṃ śivamantrādyaṃ sādhyaṃ śivasamānatā |
ṣaḍarthasaṃgrahasyāsya jñānātsarvajñatocyate || 48 ||

prathamaṃ karma yajñāderbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ |
bāhyebhyarcya śivaṃ paścādantaryāgarato bhavet || 49 ||

ratirabhyantare yasya na bāhye puṇyagauravāt |
na karma karaṇīyaṃ hi bahistasya mahātmanāḥ || 50 ||

jñānāmṛtena tṛptasya bhaktyā śaivaśivātmanaḥ |
