nāntarna ca bahiḥ kṛṣṇa kṛtyamasti kadācana || 51 ||

tasmātkrameṇa santyajya bāhyamābhyantaraṃ tathā |
jñānena jñeyamālokyājñānaṃ cāpi parityajet || 52 ||

naikāgraṃ cecchive cittaṃ kiṃ kṛtenāpi karmaṇā |
ekāgrameva ceccittaṃ kiṃ kṛtenāpi karmaṇā || 53 ||

tasmātkarmāṇyakṛtvā vā kṛtvā vāntarbahiḥkramāt |
yena kenāpyupāyena śive cittaṃ niveśayet || 54 ||

śive niviṣṭacittānāṃ pratiṣṭhitadhiyāṃ satām |
paratreha ca sarvatra nirvṛtiḥ paramā bhavet || 55 ||

ihonnamaḥ śivāyeti mantreṇānena siddhayaḥ |
sa tasmādadhigantavyaḥ parāvaravibhūtaye || 56 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṃḍe śivajñānavarṇanaṃ nāmaikādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 11 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

maharṣivara sarvajña sarvajñānamahodadhe |
paṃcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ || 1 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

paṃcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi |
aśakyaṃ vistarādvaktuṃ tasmātsaṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu || 2 ||

vede śivāgame cāyamubhayatra ṣaḍakṣareḥ |
sarveṣāṃ śivabhaktānāmaśeṣārthasādhakaḥ || 3 ||

tadalpākṣaramarthāḍhyaṃ vedasāraṃ vimuktidam |
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam || 4 ||

nānāsiddhiyutaṃ divyaṃ lokacittānuraṃjakam |
suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ tatpārameśvaram || 5 ||

mantraṃ sukhamukoccāryamaśeṣārthaprasiddhaye |
prāhonnamaḥ śivāyeti sarvajñassarvadehinām || 6 ||

tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ ṣaḍakṣaram |
atisūkṣmaṃ mahārthaṃ ca jñeyaṃ tadvaṭabījavat || 7 ||

devo guṇatrayātītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛtprabhuḥ |
omityekākṣare mantre sthitaḥ sarvagataḥ śivaḥ || 8 ||

iśānādyāni sūkṣmāṇi brahmāṇyekākṣarāṇi tu |
mantre namaśśivāyeti saṃsthitāni yathākramam |
mantre ṣaḍakṣare sūkṣme paṃcabrahmatanuḥ śivaḥ // 9 || 9 ||

vācyavācakabhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣātsvabhāvataḥ |
vācyaśśivoprameyatvānmantrastadvācakassmṛtaḥ || 10 ||

vācyavācakabhāvo .ayamanādisaṃsthitastayoḥ |
yathā .anādipravṛttoyaṃ ghorasaṃsārasāgaraḥ || 11 ||

śivo .api hi tathānādisaṃsārānmocakaḥ sthitaḥ |
vyādhīnāṃ bheṣajaṃ yadvatpratipakṣaḥ svabhāvataḥ || 12 ||

tadvatsaṃsāradoṣāṇāṃ pratipakṣaḥ śivassmṛtaḥ |
asatyasmin jagannāthe tamobhūtamidaṃ bhavet || 13 ||

acetanatvātprakṛterajñatvātpuraṣasya ca |
pradhānaparamāṇvādi yāvatkiṃcidacetanam || 14 ||

na tatkartṛ svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ buddhimatkāraṇaṃ vinā |
dharmādharmopadeśaśca bandhamokṣau vicāraṇāt || 15 ||

na sarvajñaṃ vinā puṃsāmādisargaḥ prasiddhyati |
vaidyaṃ vinā nirānandāḥ kliśyante rogiṇo yathā || 16 ||

tasmādanādiḥ sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇassadāśivaḥ |
asti nāthaḥ paritrātā puṃsāṃ saṃsārasāgarāt || 17 ||

ādimadhyāntanirmuktassvabhāvavimalaḥ prabhuḥ |
sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaśca śivo jñeyaśśivāgame || 18 ||

tasyābhidhānamantro .ayamabhidheyaśca sa smṛtaḥ |
abhidhānābhidheyatvānmantrassiddhaḥ paraśśivaḥ || 19 ||

etāvattu śivajñānametāvatparamaṃ padam |
yadoṃnamaśśivāyeti śivavākyaṃ ṣaḍakṣaram || 20 ||

vidhivākyamidaṃ śaivaṃ nārthavādaṃ śivātmakam |
yassarvajñassusaṃpūrṇaḥ svabhāvavimalaḥ śivaḥ || 21 ||

lokānugrahakarttā ca sa mṛṣārthaṃ kathaṃ vadet |
yadyathāvasthitaṃ vastu guṇadoṣaiḥ svabhāvataḥ || 22 ||

yāvatphalaṃ ca tatpūrṇaṃ sarvajñastu yathā vadet |
rāgājñānādibhirdoṣairgrastatvādanṛtaṃ vadet || 23 ||

te ceśvare na vidyete brūyātsa kathamanyathā |
ajñātāśeṣadoṣeṇa sarvajñeya śivena yat |
praṇītamamalaṃ vākyaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ na saṃśayaḥ // 24 || 24 ||

tasmādīśvaravākyāni śraddheyāni vipaścitā |
yathārthapuṇyapāpeṣu tadaśraddho vrajatyadhaḥ || 25 ||

svargāpavargasiddhyarthaṃ bhāṣitaṃ yatsuśobhanam |
vākyaṃ munivaraiḥ śāntaistadvijñeyaṃ subhāṣitam || 26 ||

rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhakāmatṛṣṇānusāri yat |
vākyaṃ nirayahetutvāttaddurbhāṣitamucyate || 27 ||

saṃskṛtenāpi kiṃ tena mṛdunā lalitena vā |
avidyārāgavākyena saṃsārakleśahetunā || 28 ||

yacchrutvā jāyate śreyo rāgādīnāṃ ca saṃśayaḥ |
virūpamapi tadvākyaṃ vijñeyamiti śobhanam || 29 ||

bahutvepi hi mantrāṇāṃ sarvajñena śivena yaḥ |
praṇīto vimalo mantro na tena sadṛśaḥ kvacit || 30 ||

sāṃgāni vedaśāstrāṇi saṃsthitāni ṣaḍakṣare |
na tena sadṛśastasmānmantro .apyastyaparaḥ kvacit || 31 ||

saptakoṭimahāmantrairupamantrairanekadhā |
mantraḥ ṣaḍakṣaro bhinnassūtraṃ vṛtyātmanā yathā || 32 ||

śivajñānāni yāvanti vidyāsthānāpi yāni ca |
ṣaḍakṣarasya sūtrasya tāni bhāṣyaṃ samāsataḥ || 33 ||

kiṃ tasya bahubhirmantraiśśāstrairvā bahuvistaraiḥ |
yasyonnamaḥ śivāyeti mantro .ayaṃ hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ || 34 ||

tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena kṛtaṃ sarvamanuṣṭhitam |
yenonnamaśśivāyeti mantrābhyāsaḥ sthirīkṛtaḥ || 35 ||

namaskārādisaṃyuktaṃ śivāyetyakṣaratrayam |
jihvāgre vartate yasya saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam || 36 ||

antyajo vādhamo vāpi mūrkho vā paṃḍito .api vā |
paṃcākṣarajape niṣṭho mucyate pāpapaṃjarāt || 37 ||

ityuktaṃ parameśena devyā pṛṣṭena śūlinā |
hitāya sarvamartyānāṃ dvijānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ || 38 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma dvādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 12 ||

devyuvāca |

kalau kaluṣite kāle durjaye duratikrame |
apuṇyatamasācchanne loke dharmaparāGmukhe || 1 ||

kṣīṇe varṇāśramācāre saṃkaṭe samupasthite |
sarvādhikāre saṃdigdhe niścite vāpi paryaye || 2 ||

tadopadeśe vihate guruśiṣyakrame gate |
kenopāyena mucyante bhaktāstava maheśvara || 3 ||

īśvara uvāca |

āśritya paramāṃ vidyāṃ hṛdyāṃ paṃcākṣarīṃ mama |
bhaktyā ca bhāvitātmāno mucyante kalijā narāḥ || 4 ||

manovākkāyajairdoṣairvaktuṃ smartumagocaraiḥ |
dūṣitānāṃ kṛtaghnānāṃ nindakānāṃ chalātmanām || 5 ||

lubdhānāṃ vakramanasāmapi matpravaṇātmanām |
mama paṃcākṣarī vidyā saṃsārabhayatāriṇī || 6 ||

mayaivamasakṛddevi pratijñātaṃ dharātale |
patito .api vimucyeta madbhakto vidyayānayā || 7 ||

devyuvāca |

karmāyogyo bhavenmartyaḥ patito yadi sarvathā |
karmāyogena yatkarma kṛtaṃ ca narakāya hi |
tataḥ kathaṃ vimucyeta patito vidyayā .anayā // 8 || 8 ||

īśvara uvāca |

tathyametattvayā proktaṃ tathā hi śṛṇu sundari |
rahasyamiti matvaitadgopitaṃ yanmayā purā || 9 ||

samantrakaṃ māṃ patitaḥ pūjayedyadi mohitaḥ |
nārakī syānna sandeho mama paṃcākṣaraṃ vinā || 10 ||

abbhakṣā vāyubhakṣāśca ye cānye vratakarśitāḥ |
teṣāmetairvratairnāsti mama lokasamāgamaḥ || 11 ||

bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇaiva yo hi māṃ sakṛdarcayet |
so .api gacchenmama sthānaṃ mantrasyāsyaiva gauravāt || 12 ||

tasmāttapāṃsi yajñāśca vratāni niyamāstathā |
paṃcākṣarārcanasyaite koṭyaṃśenāpi no samaḥ || 13 ||

baddho vāpyatha mukto vā pāśātpaṃcākṣareṇa yaḥ |
pūjayenmāṃ sa mucyeta nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 14 ||

arudro vā sarudro vā sakṛtpaṃcākṣareṇa yaḥ |
pūjayetpatito vāpi mūḍho vā mucyate naraḥ || 15 ||

ṣaḍakṣareṇa vā devi tathā paṃcākṣareṇa vā |
sa brahmāṃgena māṃ bhaktyā pūjayedyadi mucyate || 16 ||

patito .apatito vāpi mantreṇānena pūjayet |
mama bhakto jitakrodho salabdho .alabdha eva vā || 17 ||

alabdhālabdha eveha koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ |
tasmāllabdhvaiva māṃ devi mantreṇānena pūjayet || 18 ||

labdhvā saṃpūjayedyastu maitryādiguṇasaṃyutaḥ |
brahmacaryarato bhaktyā matsādṛśyamavāpnuyāt || 19 ||

kimatra bahunoktena bhaktāssarvedhikāriṇaḥ |
mama paṃcākṣare mantre tasmācchreṣṭhataro hi saḥ || 20 ||

paṃcākṣaraprabhāveṇa lokavedamaharṣayaḥ |
tiṣṭhanti śāśvatā dharmā devāssarvamidaṃ jagat || 21 ||

pralaye samanuprāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṃgame |
sarvaṃ prakṛtimāpannaṃ tatra saṃlayameṣyati || 22 ||

eko .ahaṃ saṃsthito devi na dvitīyo .asti kutracit |
tadā vedāśca śāstrāṇi sarve paṃcākṣare sthitāḥ || 23 ||

te nāśaṃ naiva saṃprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ |
tatassṛṣṭirabhūnmattaḥ prakṛtyātmaprabhedataḥ || 24 ||

guṇamūrtyātmanāṃ caiva tatovāntarasaṃhṛtiḥ |
tadā nārāyaṇaśśete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum || 25 ||

āsthāya bhogiparyaṃkaśayane toyamadhyagaḥ |
tannābhipaṃkajājjātaḥ paṃcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ || 26 ||

sisṛkṣamāṇo lokāṃstrīnna sakto hyasahāyavān |
munīndaśa sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ || 27 ||

teṣāṃ siddhivivṛddhyarthaṃ māṃ provāca pitāmahaḥ |
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara || 28 ||

ityevaṃ prārthitastena pañcavaktradharo hyaham |
pañcākṣarāṇi kramaśaḥ proktavānpadmayonaye || 29 ||

sa pañcavadanaistāni gṛhṇAllokapitāmahaḥ |
vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānmāṃ maheśvaram || 30 ||

jñātvā prayogaṃ vividhaṃ siddhamantraḥ prajāpatiḥ |
putrebhyaḥ pradadau mantraṃ mantrārthaṃ ca yathātatham || 31 ||

te ca labdhvā mantraratnaṃ sākṣāllokapitāmahāt |
tadājñaptena mārgeṇa madārādhanakāṃkṣiṇaḥ || 32 ||

merostu śikhare ramye muṃjavānnāma parvataḥ |
matpriyaḥ satataṃ śrīmānmadbhaktai rakṣitassadā || 33 ||

tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokaṃ sraṣṭuṃ samutsukāḥ |
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhakṣāssamācaran || 34 ||

teṣāṃ bhaktimahaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ pratyakṣatāmiyām |
ṛṣiṃ chandaśca kīlaṃ ca bījaśaktiṃ ca daivatam || 35 ||

nyāsaṃ ṣaḍaṃgaṃ digbandhaṃ viniyogamaśeṣataḥ |
proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ jagatsṛṣṭivivṛddhaye || 36 ||

tataste mantramāhātmyādṛṣayastapasedhitāḥ |
sṛṣṭiṃ vitanvate samyaksadevāsuramānuṣīm || 37 ||

asyāḥ paramavidyāyāssvarūpamadhunocyate |
ādau namaḥ prayoktavyaṃ śivāya tu tataḥ param || 38 ||

saiṣā pañcākṣarī vidyā sarvaśrutiśirogatā |
sarvajātasya sarvasya bījabhūtā sanātanī || 39 ||

prathamaṃ manmukhodgīrṇā sā mamaivāsti vācikā |
taptacāmīkaraprakhyā pīnonnatapayodharā || 40 ||

caturbhujā trinayanā bālendukṛtaśekharā |
padmotpalakarā saumyā varadābhayapāṇikā || 41 ||

sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā |
sitapadmāsanāsīnā nīlakuṃcitamūrddhajā || 42 ||

asyāḥ pañcavidhā varṇāḥ prasphuradraśmimaṃḍalāḥ |
pītaḥ kṛṣṇastathā dhūmraḥ svarṇābho rakta eva ca || 43 ||

pṛthakprayojyā yadyete bindunādavibhūṣitāḥ |
arddhacandranibho bindurnādo dīpaśikhākṛtiḥ || 44 ||

bījaṃ dvitīyaṃ bījeṣu mantrasyāsya varānane |
dīrghapūrvaṃ turīyasya pañcamaṃ śaktimādiśet || 45 ||

vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiśchanda udāhṛtam |
devatā śiva evāhaṃ mantrasyāsya varānane || 46 ||

gautamo .atrirvarārohe viśvāmitrastathāṃgirāḥ |
bharadvājaśca varṇānāṃ kramaśaścarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ || 47 ||

gāyatryanuṣṭup triṣṭup ca chandāṃsi bṛhatī virāṭ |
indro rudro harirbrahmā skandasteṣāṃ ca devatāḥ || 48 ||

mama paṃcamukhānyāhuḥ sthāne teṣāṃ varānane |
pūrvādeścorddhvaparyantaṃ nakārādi yathākramam || 49 ||

adāttaḥ prathamo varṇaścaturthaśca dvitīyakaḥ |
paṃcamaḥ svaritaścaiva tṛtīyo nihataḥ smṛtaḥ || 50 ||

mūlavidyā śivaṃ śaivaṃ sūtraṃ paṃcākṣaraṃ tathā |
nāmānyasya vijānīyācchaivaṃ me hṛdayaṃ mahat || 51 ||

nakāraśśira ucyeta makārastu śikhocyate |
śikāraḥ kavacaṃ tadvadvakāro netramucyate || 52 ||

yakāro .astraṃ namassvāhā vaṣaṭ huṃvauṣaḍityapi |
phaḍityapi ca varṇānāmante .aGgatvaṃ yadā tadā || 53 ||

tatrāpi mūlamantro .ayaṃ kiṃcidbhedasamanvayāt |
tatrāpi paṃcamo varṇo dvādaśasvarabhūṣitaḥ || 54 ||

tāsmādanena mantreṇa manovākkāyabhedataḥ |
āvayorarcanaṃ kuryyājjapahomādikaṃ tathā || 55 ||

yathāprajñaṃ yathākālaṃ yathāśāstraṃ yathāmati |
yathāśakti yathāsaṃpadyathāyogaṃ yathārati || 56 ||

yadā kadāpi vā bhaktyā yatra kutrāpi vā kṛtā |
yena kenāpi vā devi pūjā muktiṃ nayiṣyate || 57 ||

mayyāsaktena manasā yatkṛtaṃ mama sundari |
matpriyaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva krameṇāpyakrameṇa vā || 58 ||

tathāpi mama bhaktā ye nātyantavivaśāḥ punaḥ |
teṣāṃ sarveṣu śāstreṣu mayeva niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ || 59 ||

tatrādau saṃpravakṣyāmi mantrasaṃgrahaṇaṃ śubham |
yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ jāpyaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet || 60 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāma trayodaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 13 ||

īśvara uvāca |

ājñāhīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ varānane |
ājñārthaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam || 1 ||

ājñāsiddhaṃ kriyāsiddhaṃ śraddhāsiddhaṃ mamātmakam |
evaṃ ceddakṣiṇāyuktaṃ mantrasiddhirmahatphalam || 2 ||

upagamya guruṃ vipramācāryaṃ tattvavedinam |
jāpitaṃ sadguṇopetaṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇam || 3 ||

toṣayettaṃ prayatnena bhāvaśuddhisamanvitaḥ |
vācā ca manasā caiva kāyena draviṇena ca || 4 ||

ācāryaṃ pūjayedvipraḥ sarvadātiprayatnataḥ |
hastyaśvaratharatnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca || 5 ||

bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni ca dhanāni ca |
etāni gurave dadyādbhaktyā ca vibhave sati || 6 ||

vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ |
paścānnivedya svātmānaṃ gurave saparicchadam || 7 ||

evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivadyathāśaktitvavaṃcayan |
ādadīta gurormantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva krameṇa tu || 8 ||

evaṃ tuṣṭo guruḥ śiṣyaṃ pūjakaṃ vatsaroṣitam |
śuśrūṣumanahaṃkāraṃ snātaṃ śucimupoṣitam || 9 ||

snāpayitvā viśuddhyarthaṃ pūrṇakuṃbhaghṛtena vai |
jalena mantraśuddhena puṇyadravyayutena ca || 10 ||

alaṃkṛtya suveṣaṃ ca gandhasragvastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ |
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā ca brāhmaṇānabhipūjya ca || 11 ||

samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālaye .api vā |
śucau deśe gṛhe vāpi kāle siddhikare tithau || 12 ||

nakṣatre śubhayoge ca sarvadoṣavivarjite |
anugṛhya tato dadyājjñānaṃ mama yathāvidhi || 13 ||

svareṇoccārayetsamyagekānte .atiprasannadhīḥ |
uccāryoccārayitvā tamāvayormantramuttamam || 14 ||

śivaṃ cāstu śubhaṃ cāstu śobhano .astu priyo .astviti |
evaṃ dadyādgururmantramājñāṃ caiva tataḥ param || 15 ||

evaṃ labdhvā gurormantramājñāṃ caiva samāhitaḥ |
saṃkalpya ca japennityaṃ puraścaraṇapūrvakam || 16 ||

yāvajjīvaṃ japennityamaṣṭottarasahasrakam |
ananyastatparo bhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim || 17 ||

japedakṣaralakṣaṃ vai caturguṇitamādarāt |
naktāśī saṃyamī yassa pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ || 18 ||

yaḥ puraścaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nityajāpī bhavetpunaḥ |
tasya nāsti samo loke sa siddhaḥ siddhado bhavet || 19 ||

snānaṃ kṛtvā śucau deśe baddhvā ruciramānasam |
tvayā māṃ hṛdi saṃciṃtya saṃciṃtya svaguruṃ tataḥ || 20 ||

udaGmukhaḥ prāGmukho vā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ |
viśodhya paṃcatattvāni dahanaplāvanādibhiḥ || 21 ||

mantranyāsādikaṃ kṛtvā saphalīkṛtavigrahaḥ |
āvayorvigrahau dhyāyanprāṇāpānau niyamya ca || 22 ||

vidyāsthānaṃ svakaṃ rūpamṛṣiñchando .adhidaivatam |
bījaṃ śaktiṃ tathā vākyaṃ smṛtvā paṃcākṣarīṃ japet || 23 ||

uttamaṃ mānasaṃ jāpyamupāṃśuṃ caivamadhyamam |
adhamaṃ vācikaṃ prāhurāgamārthaviśāradāḥ || 24 ||

uttamaṃ rudradaivatyaṃ madhyamaṃ viṣṇudaivatam |
adhamaṃ brahmadaivatyamityāhuranupūrvaśaḥ || 25 ||

yaduccanīcasvaritaiḥspaṣṭāspaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ |
mantramuccārayedvācā vāciko .ayaṃ japassmṛtaḥ || 26 ||

jihvāmātraparispandādīṣaduccārito .api vā |
aparairaśrutaḥ kiṃcicchruto vopāṃśurucyate || 27 ||

dhiyā yadakṣaraśreṇyā varṇādvarṇaṃ padātpadam |
śabdārthaciṃtanaṃ bhūyaḥ kathyate mānaso japaḥ || 28 ||

vācikastveka eva syādupāṃśuḥ śatamucyate |
sāhasraṃ mānasaḥ proktaḥ sagarbhastu śatādhikaḥ || 29 ||

prāṇāyāmasamāyuktassagarbho japa ucyate |
ādyantayoragarbho .api prāṇāyāmaḥ praśasyate || 30 ||

catvāriṃśatsamāvṛttīḥ prāṇānāyamya saṃsmaret |
mantraṃ mantrārthaviddhīmānaśaktaḥ śaktito japet || 31 ||

paṃcakaṃ trikamekaṃ vā prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret |
agarbhaṃ vā sagarbhaṃ vā sagarbhastatra śasyate || 32 ||

sagarbhādapi sāhasraṃ sadhyāno japa ucyate |
eṣu paṃcavidheṣvekaḥ karttavyaḥ śaktito japaḥ || 33 ||

aGgulyā japasaṃkhyānamekamevamudāhṛtam |
rekhayāṣṭaguṇaṃ vidyātputrajīvairdaśādhikam || 34 ||

śataṃ syācchaṃkhamaṇibhiḥ pravālaistu sahasrakam |
sphaṭikairdaśasāhasraṃ mauktikairlakṣamucyate || 35 ||

padmākṣairdaśalakṣantu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate |
kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣairanantaguṇitaṃ bhavet || 36 ||

triṃśadakṣaiḥ kṛtā mālā dhanadā japakarmaṇi |
saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyātairakṣaiḥ puṣṭipradā bhavet || 37 ||

paṃcaviṃśatisaṃkhyātaiḥ kṛtā muktiṃ prayacchati |
akṣaistu paṃcadaśabhirabhicāraphalapradā || 38 ||

aṃguṣṭhaṃ mokṣadaṃ vidyāttarjjanīṃ śatrunāśinīm |
madhyamāṃ dhanadāṃ śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hyanāmikā || 39 ||

aṣṭottaraśataṃ mālā tatra syāduttamottamā |
śatasaṃkhyottamā mālā paṃcāśadbhistu madhyamā || 40 ||

catuḥ paṃcāśadakṣaistu hṛcchreṣṭhā hi prakīrtitā |
ityevaṃ mālayā kuryājjapaṃ kasmai na darśayet || 41 ||

kaniṣṭhā kṣariṇī proktā japakarmaṇi śobhanā |
aṃguṣṭhena japejjapyamanyairaṃgulibhissaha || 42 ||

aṃguṣṭhena vinā japyaṃ kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ yataḥ |
gṛhe japaṃ samaṃ vidyādgoṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ viduḥ || 43 ||

puṇyāraṇye tathārāme sahasraguṇamucyate |
ayutaṃ parvate puṇye nadyāṃ lakṣamudāhṛtam || 44 ||

koṭiṃ devālaye prāhuranantaṃ mama sannidhau |
sūryasyāgnergurorindordīpasya ca jalasya ca || 45 ||

viprāṇāṃ ca gavāṃ caiva sannidhau śasyate japaḥ |
tatpūrvābhimukhaṃ vaśyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cābhicārikam || 46 ||

paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyādauttaraṃ śātidaṃ bhavet |
sūryyāgnivipradevānāṃ gurūṇāmapi sannidhau || 47 ||

anyeṣāṃ ca prasaktānāṃ mantraṃ na vimukho japet |
uṣṇīṣī kuṃcukī namro muktakeśo galāvṛtaḥ || 48 ||

apavitrakaro .aśuddho vilapanna japetkvacit |
krodhaṃ madaṃ kṣutaṃ trīṇi niṣṭhīvanavijṛṃbhaṇe || 49 ||

darśanaṃ ca śvanīcānāṃ varjayejjapakarmaṇi |
ācametsaṃbhave teṣāṃ smaredvā māṃ tvayā saha || 50 ||

jyotīṃṣi ca prapaśyedvā kuryādvā prāṇasaṃyamam |
anāsanaḥ śayāne vā gacchannutthita eva vā || 51 ||

rathyāyāmaśive sthāne na japettimirāntare |
prasāryya na japetpādau kukkuṭāsana eva vā || 52 ||

yānaśayyādhirūḍho vā ciṃtāvyākulito .atha vā |
śaktaścetsarvamevaitadaśaktaḥ śaktito japet || 53 ||

kimatra bahunoktena samāsena vacaḥ śṛṇu |
sadācāro japañchuddhaṃ dhyāyanbhadraṃ samaśnute || 54 ||

ācāraḥ paramo dharma ācāraḥ paramaṃ dhanaṃ |
ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ || 55 ||

ācārahīnaḥ puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ |
paratra ca sukhī na syāttasmādācāravānbhavet || 56 ||

yasya yadvihitaṃ karma vede śāstre ca vaidikaiḥ |
tasya tena samācāraḥ sadācāro na cetaraḥ || 57 ||

sadbhirācaritatvācca sadācāraḥ sa ucyate |
sadācārasya tasyāhurāstikyaṃ mūlakāraṇam || 58 ||

āstikaścetpramādādyaiḥ sadācārādavicyutaḥ |
na duṣyati naro nityaṃ tasmādāstikatāṃ vrajet || 59 ||

yathehāsti sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ sukṛtairduṣkṛtairapi |
tathā paratra cāstīti matirāstikyamucyate || 60 ||

rahasyamanyadvakṣyāmi gopanīyamidaṃ priye |
na vācyaṃ yasya kasyāpi nāstikasyātha vā paśoḥ || 61 ||

sadācāravihīnasya patitasyāntyajasya ca |
paṃcākṣarātparaṃ nāsti paritrāṇaṃ kalau yuge || 62 ||

gacchatastiṣṭhato vāpi svecchayā karma kurvataḥ |
aśucervā śucervāpi mantro .ayanna ca niṣphalaḥ || 63 ||

anācāravatāṃ puṃsāmaviśuddhaṣaḍadhvanām |
anādiṣṭo .api guruṇā mantro .ayaṃ na ca niṣphalaḥ || 64 ||

antyajasyāpi mūrkhasya mūḍhasya patitasya ca |
nirmaryādasya nīcasya mantro .ayaṃ na ca niṣphalaḥ || 65 ||

sarvāvasthāṃ gatasyāpi mayi bhaktimataḥ param |
sidhyatyeva na saṃdeho nāparasya tu kasyacit || 66 ||

na lagnatithinakṣatravārayogādayaḥ priye |
asyātyantamavekṣyāḥ syurnaiṣa saptassadoditaḥ || 67 ||

na kadācinna kasyāpi ripureṣa mahāmanuḥ |
susiddho vāpi siddho vā sādhyo vāpi bhaviṣyati || 68 ||

siddhena guruṇādiṣṭassusiddha iti kathyate |
asiddhenāpi vā dattassiddhasādhyastu kevalaḥ || 69 ||

asādhitassādhito vā sidhyatvena na saṃśayaḥ |
śraddhātiśayayuktasya mayi mantre tathā gurau || 70 ||

tasmānmantrāntarāṃstyaktvā sāpāyānadhikārataḥ |
āśrametparamāṃ vidyāṃ sākṣātpaṃcākṣarīṃ budhaḥ || 71 ||

mantrāntareṣu siddheṣu mantra eṣa na sidhyati |
siddhe tvasminmahāmantre te ca siddhā bhavantyuta || 72 ||

yathā deveṣvalabdho .asmi labdheṣvapi maheśvari |
mayi labdhe tu te labdhā mantreṣveṣu samo vidhiḥ || 73 ||

ye doṣāssarvamantrāṇāṃ na te .asminsaṃbhavantyapi |
asya mantrasya jātyādīnanapekṣya pravartanāt || 74 ||

tathāpi naiva kṣudreṣu phaleṣu prati yogiṣu |
sahasā viniyuṃjīta tasmādeṣa mahābalaḥ || 75 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

evaṃ sākṣānmahādevyai mahādevena śūlinā |
hitā ya jagatāmuktaḥ pañcākṣaravidhiryathā || 76 ||

ya idaṃ kīrttayedbhaktyā śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prayāti paramāṃ gatim || 77 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṃḍe paṃcākṣaramahimavarṇanaṃ nāma caturdaśodhyāyaḥ || 14 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavānmantramāhātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ prabho |
tatprayogavidhānaṃ ca sākṣācchrutisamaṃ yathā || 1 ||

idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi śivasaṃskāramuttamam |
mantrasaṃgrahaṇe kiṃcitsūcitanna tu vismṛtam || 2 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

hanta te kathayiṣyāmi sarvapāpaviśodhanam |
saṃskāraṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ śivena patibhāṣitam || 3 ||

samyak kṛtādhikāraḥ syātpūjādiṣu naro yataḥ |
saṃskāraḥ kathyate tena ṣaḍadhvapariśodhanam || 4 ||

dīyate yena vijñānaṃ kṣīyate pāśabandhanam |
tasmātsaṃskāra evāyaṃ dīkṣetyapi ca kathyate || 5 ||

śāṃbhavī caiva śāktī ca māntrī caiva śivāgame |
dīkṣopadiśyate tredhā śivena paramātmanā || 6 ||

gurorālokamātreṇa sparśātsaṃbhāṣaṇādapi |
sadyassaṃjñā bhavejjantoḥ pāśopakṣayakāriṇī || 7 ||

sā dīkṣā śāṃbhavī proktā sā punarbhidyate dvidhā |
tīvrā tīvratarā ceti pāśo pakṣayabhedataḥ || 8 ||

yayā syānnirvṛtiḥ sadyassaiva tīvratarā matā |
tīvrā tu jīvatotyantaṃ puṃsaḥ pāpaviśodhikā || 9 ||

śaktī jñānavatī dīkṣā śiṣyadehaṃ praviśya tu |
guruṇā yogamārgeṇa kriyate jñānacakṣuṣā || 10 ||

māntrī kriyāvatī dīkṣā kuṃḍamaṃḍalapūrvikā |
mandamandataroddeśātkartavyā guruṇā bahiḥ || 11 ||

śaktipātānusāreṇa śiṣyo .anugrahamarhati |
śaivadharmānusārasya tanmūlatvātsamāsataḥ || 12 ||

yatra śaktirna patitā tatra śuddhirna jāyate |
na vidyā na śivācāro na muktirna ca siddhayaḥ || 13 ||

tasmālliṃgāni saṃvīkṣya śaktipātasya bhūyasaḥ |
jñānena kriyayā vātha guruśśiṣyaṃ viśodhayet || 14 ||

yo .anyathā kurute mohātsa vinaśyati durmatiḥ |
tasmātsarvaprakāreṇa guruḥ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣayet || 15 ||

lakṣaṇaṃ śaktipātasya prabodhānandasaṃbhavaḥ |
sā yasmātparamā śaktiḥ prabodhānandarūpiṇī || 16 ||

ānandabodhayorliṃgamantaḥkaraṇavikriyāḥ |
yathā syātkaṃparomāṃcasvaranetrāṃgavikriyāḥ || 17 ||

śiṣyopi lakṣaṇairebhiḥ kuryyādguruparīkṣaṇam |
tatsaṃparkaiḥ śivārcādau saṃgatairvātha tadgataiḥ || 18 ||

śiṣyastu śikṣaṇīyatvādgurorgauravakāraṇāt |
tasmātsarvaprayatnena gurorgauravamācaret || 19 ||

yo gurussa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ |
gururvā śiva evātha vidyākāreṇa saṃsthitaḥ || 20 ||

yathā śivastathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ |
śivavidyā gurūṇāṃ ca pūjayā sadṛśaṃ phalam || 21 ||

sarvadevātmakaścāsau sarvamantramayo guruḥ |
tasmātsarvaprayatnena yasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet || 22 ||

śreyo .arthī yadi gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṃghayet |
gurvājñāpālako yasmājjñānasaṃpattimaśnute || 23 ||

gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapanbhuṃjannānyatkarma samācaret |
samakṣaṃ yadi kurvīta sarvaṃ cānujñayā guroḥ || 24 ||

gurorgṛhe samakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet |
gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāttadgṛhaṃ devamandiram || 25 ||

pāpināṃ ca yathā saṃgāttatpāpātpatito bhavet |
yatheha vahnisaṃparkānmalaṃ tyajati kāṃcanam || 26 ||

tathaiva gurusaṃparkkātpāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ |
yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakumbho vilīyate || 27 ||

tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta hyācāryasya samīpataḥ |
yathā prajvalito vahniḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet || 28 ||

tathāyamapi santuṣṭo guruḥ pāpaṃ kṣaṇāddahet |
manasā karmaṇā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet || 29 ||

tasya krodhena dahyante hyāyuḥśrījñānasatkriyāḥ |
tatkrodhakāriṇo ye syusteṣāṃ yajñāśca niṣphalāḥ || 30 ||

yamaśca niyamāścaiva nātra kāryyā vicāraṇā |
gurorviruddhaṃ yadvākyaṃ na vadejjātucinnaraḥ || 31 ||

vadedyadi mahāmohādrauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet |
manasā karmaṇā vācā gurumuddiśya yatnataḥ || 32 ||

śreyorthī cennaro dhīmānna mithyācāramācaret |
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryādādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā || 33 ||

asamakṣaṃ samakṣaṃ vā tasya kāryaṃ samācaret |
itthamācāravānbhakto nityamudyuktamānasaḥ || 34 ||

gurupriyakaraḥ śiṣyaḥ śaivadharmāṃstato .arhati |
guruścedguṇavānprājñaḥ paramānandabhāsakaḥ || 35 ||

tattvavicchivasaṃsakto muktido na tu cāparaḥ |
saṃvitsaṃjananaṃ tattvaṃ paramānandasaṃbhavam || 36 ||

tattattvaṃ viditaṃ yena sa evānandadarśakaḥ |
na punarnāmamātreṇa saṃvidārahitastu yaḥ || 37 ||

anyonyaṃ tārayennaukā kiṃ śilā tārayecchilām |
etasyā nāmamātreṇa muktirvai nāmamātrikā || 38 ||

yaiḥ punarviditaṃ tattvaṃ te muktā mocayantyapi |
tattvahīne kuto bodhaḥ kuto hyātmaparigrahaḥ || 39 ||

parigrahavinirmuktaḥ paśurityabhidhīyate |
paśubhiḥ preritaścāpi paśutvaṃ nātivartate || 40 ||

tasmāttattvavideveha mukto mocaka iṣyate |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaḥ sarvaśāstravidapyayam || 41 ||

sarvopāyavidhijño .api tattvahīnastu niṣphalaḥ |
yasyānubhavaparyantā buddhistattve pravartate || 42 ||

tasyāvalokanādyaiśca parānando .abhijāyate |
tasmādyasyaiva saṃparkātprabodhānandasaṃbhavaḥ || 43 ||

guruṃ tameva vṛṇuyānnāparaṃ matimānnaraḥ |
sa śiṣyairvinayācāracaturairucito guruḥ || 44 ||

yāvadvijñāyate tāvatsevanīyo mumukṣubhiḥ |
jñāte tasminsthirā bhaktiryāvattattvaṃ samāśrayet || 45 ||

na tu tattvaṃ tyajejjātu nopekṣeta kathaṃcana |
yatrānandaḥ prabodho vā nālpamapyupalabhyate || 46 ||

vatsarādapi śiṣyeṇa so .anyaṃ gurumupāśrayet |
gurumanyaṃ prapanne .api nāvamanyeta paurvikam |
gurorbhrātR̥ṃstathā putrānbodhakānprerakānapi // 47 || 47 ||

tatrādāvupasaṃgamya brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam |
gurumārādhayetprājñaṃ śubhagaṃ priyadarśanam || 48 ||

sarvābhayapradātāraṃ karuṇākrāntamānasam |
toṣayettaṃ prayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā || 49 ||

tāvadārādhayecchiṣyaḥ prasannosau bhavedyathā |
tasminprasanne śiṣyasya sadyaḥ pāpakṣayo bhavet || 50 ||

tasmāddhanāni ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca |
bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi yānaśayyāsanāni ca || 51 ||

etāni gurave dadyādbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ |
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetparamāṃ gatim || 52 ||

sa eva janako mātā bhartā bandhurdhanaṃ sukham |
sakhā mitraṃ ca yattasmātsarvaṃ tasmai nivedayet || 53 ||

nivedya paścātsvātmānaṃ sānvayaṃ saparigraham |
samarpya sodakaṃ tasmai nityaṃ tadvaśago bhavet || 54 ||

yadā śivāya svātmānaṃ dattavān deśikātmane |
tadā śaivo bhaveddehī na tato .asti punarbhavaḥ || 55 ||

guruśca svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣamekaṃ parīkṣayet |
brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ dvivarṣaṃ ca trivarṣakam || 56 ||

prāṇadravyapradānādyairādeśaiśca samāsamaiḥ |
uttamāṃścādhame kṛtvā nīcānuttamakarmaṇi || 57 ||

ākruṣṭāstāḍitā vāpi ye viṣādaṃ na yāntyapi |
te yogyāḥ saṃyatāḥ śuddhāḥ śivasaṃskārakarmaṇi || 58 ||

ahiṃsakā dayāvanto nityamudyuktacetasaḥ |
amānino buddhimantastyaktasparddhāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ || 59 ||

ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svacchā vinītāḥ sthiracetasaḥ |
śaucācārasamāyuktāḥ śivabhaktā dvijātayaḥ || 60 ||

evaṃ vṛttasamopetā vāGmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ |
śodhyā bodhyā yathānyāyamiti śāstreṣu niścayaḥ || 61 ||

nādhikāraḥ svato nāryyāḥ śivasaṃskārakarmaṇi |
niyogādbharturastyeva bhaktiyuktā yadīśvare || 62 ||

tathaiva bhartṛhīnāyā putrāderabhyanujñayā |
adhikāro bhavatyeva kanyāyāḥ piturājñayā |
śūdrāṇāṃ martyajātīnāṃ patitānāṃ viśeṣataḥ // 63 || 63 ||

tathā saṃkarajātīnāṃ nādhvaśuddhirvidhīyate |
taipyakṛtrimabhāvaścecchive paramakāraṇe || 64 ||

pādodakapradānādyaiḥ kuryuḥ pāpaviśodhanam |
atrānulomajātā ye yuktā eva dvijātiṣu || 65 ||

teṣāmadhvaviśuddhyādi kuryānmātṛkulocitam |
yā tu kanyā svapitrādyaiśśivadharme niyojitā || 66 ||

sā bhaktāya pradātavyā nāparāya virodhine |
dattā cetpratikūlāya pramādādbodhayetpatim || 67 ||

aśaktā taṃ parityajya manasā dharmamācaret |
yathā munivaraṃ tyaktvā patimatriṃ pativratā || 68 ||

kṛtakṛtyā .abhavatpūrvaṃ tapasārādhya śaGkaram |
yathā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ tapasārādhya pāṃḍavān || 69 ||

patĪllabdhavatī dharme gurubhirna niyojitā |
asvātantryakṛto doṣo nehāsti paramārthataḥ || 70 ||

śivadharme niyuktāyāśśivaśāsanagauravāt |
bahunātra kimuktena yo .api ko .api śivāśrayaḥ || 71 ||

saṃskāryo gurvadhīnaścetsaṃskriyā na prabhidyate |
gurorālokanādeva sparśātsaṃbhāṣaṇādapi || 72 ||

yasya saṃjāyate prajñā tasya nāsti parājayaḥ |
manasā yastu saṃskāraḥ kriyate yogavartmanā || 73 ||

sa neha kathito guhyo guruvaktraikagocaraḥ |
kriyāvānyastu saṃskāraḥ kuṃḍamaṃḍapapūrvakaḥ |
sa vakṣyate samāsena tasya śakyo na vistaraḥ // 74 || 74 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe dīkṣāvidhāne gurumāhātmyaṃ nāma pañcadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 15 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

puṇye .ahani śucau deśe bahudoṣavivarjite |
deśikaḥ prathamaṃ kuryātsaṃskāraṃ samayāhvayam || 1 ||

parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ |
śilpiśāstroktamārgeṇa maṇḍapaṃ tatra kalpayet || 2 ||

kṛtvā vediṃ ca tanmadhye kuṇḍāni parikalpayet |
aṣṭadikṣu tathā dikṣu tatraiśānyāṃ punaḥ kramāt || 3 ||

pradhānakuṃḍaṃ kurvīta yadvā paścimabhāgataḥ |
pradhānamekamevātha kṛtvā śobhāṃ prakalpayet || 4 ||

vitānadhvajamālābhirvividhābhiranekaśaḥ |
vedimadhye tataḥ kuryānmaṃḍalaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam || 5 ||

raktahemādibhiścūrṇairīśvarāvāhanocitam |
sindūraśālinīvāracūrṇairevātha nirddhanaḥ || 6 ||

ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ vā sitaṃ vā raktameva vā |
ekahastasya padmasya karṇikāṣṭāṃgulā matā || 7 ||

kesarāṇi tadarddhāni śeṣaṃ cāṣṭadalādikam |
dvihastasya tu padmasya dviguṇaṃ karṇikādikam || 8 ||

kṛtvā śobhopaśobhāḍhyamaiśānyāṃ tasya kalpayet |
ekahastaṃ tadarddhaṃ vā punarvedyaḥ tu maṃḍalam || 9 ||

vrīhitandulasiddhārthatilapuṣpakuśāstṛte |
tatra lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ śivakuṃbhaṃ prasādhayet || 10 ||

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmrajaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tu vā |
gandhapuṣpākṣatākīrṇaṃ kuśadūrvāṃkurācitam || 11 ||

sitasūtrāvṛtaṃ kaṃṭhe navavastrayugāvṛtam |
śuddhāmbupūrṇamutkūrcaṃ sadravyaṃ sapidhānakam || 12 ||

bhṛGgāraṃ vardhanīṃ cāpi śaṃkhaṃ ca cakrameva vā |
vinā sūtrādikaṃ sarvaṃ padmapatramathāpi vā || 13 ||

tasyāsanāravindasya kalpayeduttare dale |
agrataścandanāṃbhobhirastrarājasya vardhanīm || 14 ||

maṇḍalasya tataḥ prācyāṃ mantrakuṃbhe ca pūrvavat |
kṛtvā vidhivadīśasya mahāpūjāṃ samācaret || 15 ||

athārṇavasya tīre vā nadyāṃ goṣṭhe .api vā girau |
devāgare gṛhe vāpi deśe .anyasminmanohare || 16 ||

kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ sarvaṃ vinā vā maṃḍapādikam |
maṃḍalaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā sthaṃḍilaṃ ca vibhāvasoḥ || 17 ||

praviśya pūjābhavanaṃ prahṛṣṭavadano guruḥ |
sarvamaṃgalasaṃyuktaḥ samācaritanaityakaḥ || 18 ||

mahāpūjāṃ maheśasya kṛtvā maṇḍalamadhyataḥ |
śivakuṃbhe tathā bhūyaḥ śivamāvāhya pūjayet || 19 ||

paścimābhimukhaṃ dhyātvā yajñarakṣakamīśvaram |
arcayedastravarddhanyāmastramīśasya dakṣiṇe || 20 ||

mantrakumbhe ca vinyasya mantraṃ mantraviśāradaḥ |
kṛtvā mudrādikaṃ sarvaṃ mantrayāgaṃ samācaret || 21 ||

tataśśivānale homaṃ kuryāddeśikasattamaḥ |
pradhānakuṇḍe parito juhuyuścāpare dvijāḥ || 22 ||

ācāryātpādamarddhaṃ vā homasteṣāṃ vidhīyate |
pradhānakuṇḍa evātha juhuyāddeśikottamaḥ || 23 ||

svādhyāyamapare kuryuḥ stotraṃ maṃgalavācanam |
japaṃ ca vidhivaccānye śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ || 24 ||

nṛtyaṃ gītaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca maṃgalānyaparāṇi ca |
pūjanaṃ ca sadasyānāṃ kṛtvā samyagvidhānataḥ || 25 ||

puṇyāhaṃ kārayitvātha punaḥ saṃpūjya śaṃkaram |
prārthayeddeśiko devaṃ śiṣyānugrahakāmyayā || 26 ||

prasīda devadeveśa dehamāviśya māmakam |
vimocayainaṃ viśveśa ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇānidhe || 27 ||

atha caivaṃ karomīti labdhānujñastu deśikaḥ |
ānīyopoṣitaṃ śiṣyaṃ haviṣyāśinameva vā || 28 ||

ekāśanaṃ vā virataṃ snātaṃ prātaḥkṛtakriyam |
japantaṃ praṇavaṃ devaṃ dhyāyantaṃ kṛtamaṃgalam || 29 ||

dvārasya paścimasyāgramaṇḍale dakṣiṇasya vā |
darbhāsane samāsīnaṃ vidhāyodaGmukhaṃ śiśum || 30 ||

svayaṃ prāgvadanastiṣṭhannūrdhvakāyaṃ kṛtāṃjalim |
saṃprokṣya prokṣaṇautoyairmūrddhanyastreṇa mudrayā || 31 ||

puṣpakṣepeṇa santāḍya badhnīyāllocanaṃ guruḥ |
dukūlārddhena vastreṇa mantritena navena ca || 32 ||

tataḥ praveśayecchiṣyaṃ gururdvāreṇa maṃḍalam |
so .api teneritaḥ śaṃbhorācarettriḥ pradakṣiṇam || 33 ||

tatassuvarṇasaṃmiśraṃ dattvā puṣpāṃjaliṃ prabhoḥ |
prāGmukhaścodaGmukho vā praṇameddaṃḍavatkṣito || 34 ||

tatassaṃprokṣya mūlena śirasyastreṇa pūrvavat |
santāḍya deśikastasya mocayennetrabandhanam || 35 ||

sa dṛṣṭvā maṃḍalaṃ bhūyaḥ praṇametsāñjaliḥ prabhum |
athāsīnaṃ śivācāryo maṃḍalasya tu dakṣiṇe || 36 ||

upaveśyātmanassavye śiṣyaṃ darbhāsane guruḥ |
ārādhya ca mahādevaṃ śivahastaṃ pravinyaset || 37 ||

śivatejomayaṃ pāṇiṃ śivamantramudīrayet |
śivābhimānasaṃpanno nyasecchiṣyasya mastake || 38 ||

sarvāṃgālaṃbanaṃ caiva kuryāttenaiva deśikaḥ |
śiṣyo .api praṇamedbhūmau deśikākṛtamīśvaram || 39 ||

tataśśivānale devaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi |
hutāhutitrayaṃ śiṣyamupaveśya yathā purā || 40 ||

darbhāgraiḥ saṃspṛśaṃstaṃ ca vidyayātmānamāviśet |
namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānamācaret || 41 ||

śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa kṛtvā prāṇasya nirgamam |
śiṣyadehapraveśaṃ ca smṛtvā mantrāṃstu tarpayet || 42 ||

santarpaṇāya mūlasya tenaivāhutayo daśa |
deyāstisrastathāṃgānāmaṃgaireva yathākramam || 43 ||

tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ |
punardaśāhutīnkuryānmūlamantreṇa mantravit || 44 ||

punaḥ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ samyagācamya deśikaḥ |
hutvā caiva yathānyāyaṃ svajātyā vaiśyamuddharet || 45 ||

tasyaivaṃ janayetkṣātramuddhāraṃ ca tataḥ punaḥ |
kṛtvā tathaiva vipratvaṃ janayedasya deśikaḥ || 46 ||

rājanyaṃ caivamuddhṛtya kṛtvā vipraṃ punastayoḥ |
rudratvaṃ janayedvipre rudranāmaiva sādhayet || 47 ||

prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ kṛtvā śiśossvātmānamātmani |
śivātmakamanusmṛtya sphurantaṃ visphuliṃgavat || 48 ||

nāḍyā yathoktayā vāyuṃ recayenmantrato guruḥ |
nirgamya praviśennāḍyā śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ tathā || 49 ||

praviśya tasya caitanyaṃ nīlabindunibhaṃ smaran |
svatejasāpāstamalaṃ jvalantamanuciṃtayet || 50 ||

tamādāya tayā nāḍyā mantrī saṃhāramudrayā |
na pūrakeṇa niveśyainamekībhāvārthamātmanaḥ || 51 ||

kuṃbhakena tathā nāḍyā recakena yathā purā |
tasmādādāya śiṣyasya hṛdaye tanniveśayet || 52 ||

tamālabhya śivāllabdhaṃ tasmai dattvopavītakam |
hutvā .a.ahutitrayaṃ paścāddadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ || 53 ||

devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyamupaveśyavarāsane |
kuśapuṣpaparistīrṇe baddhāṃjalirudaGmukham || 54 ||

svastikāsanamārūḍhaṃ vidhāya prāGmukhaḥ svayam |
varāsanasthito mantrairmahāmaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ || 55 ||

samādāya ghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ pūrṇameva prasāditam |
dhyāyamānaḥ śivaṃ śiṣyamābhiṣiṃceta deśikaḥ || 56 ||

athāpanudya snānāṃbu paridhāya sitāṃbaram |
ācāntolaṃkṛtaśśiṣyaḥ prāṃjalirmaṃḍapaṃ vrajet || 57 ||

upaveśya yathāpūrvaṃ taṃ gururdarbhaviṣṭare |
saṃpūjya maṃḍalaṃ devaṃ karanyāsaṃ samācaret || 58 ||

tatastu bhasmanā devaṃ dhyāyanmanasi deśikaḥ |
samālabheta pāṇibhyāṃ śiśuṃ śivamudīrayet || 59 ||

atha tasya śivācāryo dahanaplāvanādikam |
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā mātṛkānyāsavartmanā || 60 ||

tataḥ śivāsanaṃ dhyātvā śiṣyamūrddhni deśikaḥ |
tatrāvāhya yathānyāyamarcayenmanasā śivam || 61 ||

prārthayetprāṃjalirdevaṃ nityamatra sthito bhava |
iti vijñāpya taṃ śaṃbhostejasā bhāsuraṃ smaret || 62 ||

saṃpūjyātha śivaṃ śaivīmājñāṃ prāpya śivātmikām |
karṇe śiṣyasya śanakaiśśivamantramudīrayet || 63 ||

sa tu baddhāṃjaliḥ śrutvā mantraṃ tadgatamānasaḥ |
śanaistaṃ vyāharecchiṣyaśivācāryasya śāsanāt || 64 ||

tataḥ śāktaṃ ca saṃdiśya mantraṃ mantravicakṣaṇaḥ |
uccārayitvā ca sukhaṃ tasmai maṃgalamādiśet || 65 ||

tatassamāsānmantrārthaṃ vācyavācakayogataḥ |
samadiśyeśvaraṃ rūpaṃ yogamāsanamādiśet || 66 ||

atha gurvājñayā śiṣyaḥ śivāgnigurusannidhau |
bhaktyaivamabhisaṃdhāya dīkṣāvākyamudīrayet || 67 ||

varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaśchedanaṃ śiraso .api vā |
na tvanabhyarcya bhuṃjīya bhagavantaṃ trilocanam || 68 ||

sa eva dadyānniyato yāvanmohaviparyayaḥ |
tāvadārādhayeddevaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ || 69 ||

tataḥ sa samayo nāma bhaviṣyati śivāśrame |
labdhādhikāro gurvājñāpālakastadvaśo bhavet || 70 ||

ataḥ paraṃ nyastakaro bhasmādāya svahastataḥ |
dadyācchiṣyāya mūlena rudrākṣaṃ cābhimantritam || 71 ||

pratimā vāpi devasya gūḍhadehamathāpi vā |
pūjāhomajapadhyānasādhanāni ca saṃbhave || 72 ||

sopi śiṣyaḥ śivācāryāllabdhāni bahumānataḥ |
ādadītājñayā tasya deśikasya na cānyathā || 73 ||

ācāryādāptamakhilaṃ śirasyādhāya bhaktitaḥ |
rakṣayetpūjayecchaṃbhuṃ maṭhe vā gṛha evavā || 74 ||

ataḥ paraṃ śivācāramādiśedasya deśikaḥ |
bhaktiśraddhānusāreṇa prajñāyāścānusārataḥ || 75 ||

yaduktaṃ yatsamājñātaṃ yaccaivānyatprakīrtitam |
śivācāryeṇa samaye tatsarvaṃ śirasā vahet || 76 ||

śivāgamasya grahaṇaṃ vācanaṃ śravaṇaṃ tathā |
deśikadeśataḥ kuryānna svecchāto na cānyataḥ || 77 ||

iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ saṃskāraḥ samayāhvayaḥ |
sākṣācchivapuraprāptau nṛṇāṃ paramasādhanam || 78 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṃḍe śiṣyasaṃskāravarṇanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 16 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

ataḥ paraṃ samāvekṣya guruḥ śiṣyasya yogyatām |
ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ kurvīta sarvabandhavimuktaye || 1 ||

kalāṃ tattvaṃ ca bhuvanaṃ varṇaṃ padamataḥ param |
mantraśceti samāsena ṣaḍadhvā paripaṭhyate || 2 ||

nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāḥ paṃca kalādhvā kathyate budhaiḥ |
vyāptāḥ kalābhiritare tvadhvānaḥ paṃca paṃcabhiḥ || 3 ||

śivatattvādibhūmyantaṃ tattvādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ |
ṣaḍviṃśatsaṃkhyayopetaḥ śuddhāśuddhobhayātmakaḥ || 4 ||

ādhārādyunmanāntaśca bhuvanādhvā prakīrtitaḥ |
vinā bhedopabhedābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭisaṃkhyāsamanvitaḥ || 5 ||

paṃcāśadrudrarūpāstu varṇā varṇādhvasaṃjñitāḥ |
anekabhedasaṃpannaḥ padādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ || 6 ||

sarvopamantrairmantrādhvā vyāptaḥ paramavidyayā |
yathā śivo na tattveṣu gaṇyate tattvanāyakaḥ || 7 ||

mantrādhvani na gaṇyeta tathāsau mantranāyakaḥ |
kalādhvano vyāpakatvaṃ vyāpyatvaṃ cetarādhvanām || 8 ||

na vetti tattvato yasya naivārhatyadhvaśodhanam |
ṣaḍvidhasyādhvano rūpaṃ na yena viditaṃ bhavet || 9 ||

vyāpyavyāpakatā tena jñātumeva na śakyate |
tasmādadhvasvarūpaṃ ca vyāpyavyāpakatāṃ tathā || 10 ||

yathāvadavagamyaiva kuryyādadhvaviśodhanam |
kuṃḍamaṃḍalaparyantaṃ tatra kṛtvā yathā purā || 11 ||

dvihastamānaṃ kurvīta prācyāṃ kalaśamaṃḍalam |
tataḥ snātaśśivācāryaḥ saśiṣyaḥ kṛtanaityakaḥ || 12 ||

praviśya maṃḍalaṃ śaṃbhoḥ pūjāṃ pūrvavadācaret |
tatrāḍhakāvaraissiddhaṃ tandulaiḥ pāyasaṃ prabhoḥ || 13 ||

arddhaṃ nivedya homārthaṃ śeṣaṃ samupakalpayet |
purataḥ kalpite vātha maṃḍale varṇimaṃḍite || 14 ||

sthāpayetpaṃcakalaśāndikṣu madhye ca deśikaḥ |
teṣu brahmāṇi mūlārṇairbindunādasamanvitaiḥ || 15 ||

namaādyairyakarāntaiḥ kalpayetkalpavittamaḥ |
īśānaṃ madhyame kuṃbhe puruṣaṃ purataḥ sthite || 16 ||

aghoraṃ dakṣiṇe vāme vāmaṃ sadyaṃ ca paścime |
rakṣāṃ vidhāya mudrā ca baddhvā kuṃbhābhimantraṇam || 17 ||

kṛtvā śivānalairhomaṃ prārabhet yathā purā |
yadarddhaṃ pāyasaṃ pūrvaṃ homārthaṃ parikalpitam || 18 ||

hutvā śiṣyasya taccheṣaṃ bhoktuṃ samupakalpayet |
tarpaṇāntaṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ kṛtvā karma yathā purā || 19 ||

hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ teṣāṃ tataḥ kuryyātpradīpanam |
.okārādanu huṃkāraṃ tato mūlaṃ phaḍantakam || 20 ||

svāhāntaṃ dīpane prāhuraṃgāni ca yathākramam |
teṣāmāhutayastisro deyā dīpanakarmaṇi || 21 ||

mantrairekaikaśastaistu vicintyā dīptamūrtayaḥ |
triguṇaṃ triguṇī kṛtya dvijakanyākṛtaṃ sitam || 22 ||

sūtraṃ sūtreṇa saṃmantrya śikhāgre bandhayecchiśoḥ |
caraṇāṃguṣṭhaparyyantamūrddhvakāyasya tiṣṭhataḥ || 23 ||

laṃbayitvā tu tatsūtraṃ suṣumṇāṃ tatra yojayet |
śāntayā mudrayādāya mūlamantreṇa mantravit || 24 ||

hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasyāssānnidhyamupakalpayet |
hṛdi santāḍya śiṣyasya puṣpakṣepeṇa pūrvavat || 25 ||

caitanyaṃ samupādāya dvādaśānte nivedya ca |
sūtraṃ sūtreṇa saṃyojya saṃrakṣyāstreṇa varmaṇā || 26 ||

avaguṃṭhyātha tatsūtraṃ śiṣyadehaṃ viciṃtayet |
mūlatrayamayaṃ pāśaṃ bhogabhogyatvalakṣaṇam || 27 ||

viṣayendriyadehādijanakaṃ tasya bhāvayet |
vyomādibhūtarūpiṇyaḥ śāntyatītādayaḥ kalāḥ || 28 ||

sūtre svanāmabhiryojyaḥ pūjyaścaiva namoyutaiḥ |
athavā bījabhūtaistatkṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ kramāt || 29 ||

tato malādestattvādau vyāptiṃ samalokayet |
kalāvyāptiṃ malādau ca hutvā saṃdīpayetkalāḥ || 30 ||

śiṣyaṃ śirasi santāḍya sūtraṃ dehe yathākramam |
śāntyatītapade sūtraṃ lāñchayenmantramuccaran || 31 ||

evaṃ kṛtvā nivṛttyantaṃ śāntyatītamanukramāt |
hutvāhutitrayaṃ paścānmaṇḍale ca śivaṃ yajet || 32 ||

devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyamupaveśyottarāmukham |
sadarbhe maṇḍale dadyāddhomaśiṣṭaṃ caruṃ guruḥ || 33 ||

śiṣyastadguruṇā dattaṃ satkṛtya śivapūrvakam |
bhuktvā paścāddvirācamya śivamantramudīrayet || 34 ||

apare maṇḍale dadyātpaṃcagavyaṃ tathā guruḥ |
so .api tacchaktitaḥ pītvā dvirācamya śivaṃ smaret || 35 ||

tṛtīye maṇḍale śiṣyamupaveśya yathā purā |
pradadyāddantapavanaṃ yathāśāstroktalakṣaṇam || 36 ||

agreṇa tasya mṛdunā prāGmukho vāpyudaGmukhaḥ |
vācaṃ niyamya cāsīnaśśiṣyo dantānviśodhayet || 37 ||

prakṣālya dantapavanaṃ tyaktvācamya śivaṃ smaret |
praviśeddeśikādiṣṭaḥ prāṃjaliḥ śivamaṇḍalam || 38 ||

tyaktaṃ taddantapavanaṃ dṛśyate guruṇā yadi |
prāgudakpaścime vāgre śivamanyacchivetaram || 39 ||

aśastāśāmukhe tasmingurustaddoṣaśāntaye |
śatamarddhaṃ tadarddhaṃ vājuhuyānmūlamantrataḥ || 40 ||

tataḥ śiṣyaṃ samālabhya japitvā karṇayoḥ śivam |
devasya dakṣiṇe bhāge taṃ śiṣyamadhivāsayet || 41 ||

ahatāstaraṇāstīrṇe sa darbhaśayane śuciḥ |
mantrite .antaḥ śivaṃ dhyāyañśayīta prākchirā niśi || 42 ||

śikhāyāṃ baddhasūtrasya śikhayā tacchikhāṃ guruḥ |
ābadhyāhatavastreṇa tamācchādya ca varmaṇā || 43 ||

rekhātrayaṃ ca parito bhasmanā tilasarṣapaiḥ |
kṛtvāstrajaptaistadvāhye digīśānāṃ baliṃ haret || 44 ||

śiṣyo .api parato .anaśnankṛtvaivamadhivāsanam |
prabudhyotthāya gurave svapnaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nivedayet || 45 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivadīkṣāvidhānavarṇanaṃ nāma saptadaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 17 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

tataḥ snānādikaṃ sarvaṃ samāpyācāryacoditaḥ |
gacchedbaddhāṃjalirdhyāyañchivamaṇḍalapārśvataḥ || 1 ||

atha pūjāṃ vinā sarvaṃ kṛtvā pūrvadine yathā |
netrabandhanaparyyantaṃ darśayenmaṇḍalaṃ guruḥ || 2 ||

baddhanetreṇa śiṣyeṇa puṣpāvakiraṇe kṛte |
yatrāpatanti puṣṇāṇi tasya nāmā .asya saṃdiśet || 3 ||

taṃ copanīya nirmālyamaṇḍale .asminyathā purā |
pūjayeddevamīśānaṃ juhuyācca śivānale || 4 ||

śiṣyeṇa yadi duḥsvapno dṛṣṭastaddoṣaśāntaye |
śatamarddhaṃ tadarddhaṃ vā juhuyānmūlavidyayā || 5 ||

tataḥ sūtraṃ śikhābaddhaṃ laṃbayitvā yathā purā |
ādhārapūjāprabhṛti yannivṛttikalāśrayam || 6 ||

vāgīśvarīpūjanāntaṃ kuryāddhomapurassaram |
atha praṇamya vāgīśaṃ nivṛttervyāpikāṃ satīm || 7 ||

maṇḍale devamabhyarcya hutvā caivāhutitrayam |
prāpayecca śiśoḥ prāptiṃ yugapatsarvayoniṣu || 8 ||

sūtradehe .atha śiṣyasya tāḍanaprokṣaṇādikam |
kṛtvātmānaṃ samādāya dvādaśānte nivedya ca || 9 ||

tato .apyādāya mūlena mudrayā śāstradṛṣṭayā |
yojayenmanasācāryo yugapatsarvayoniṣu || 10 ||

devānāṃ jātayaścāṣṭau tiraścāṃ paṃca jātayaḥ |
jātyaikayā ca mānuṣyā yonayaśca caturdaśa || 11 ||

tāsu sarvāsu yugapatpraveśāya śiśorddhiyā |
vāgīśānyāṃ yathānyāyaṃ śiṣyātmānaṃ niveśayet || 12 ||

garbhaniṣpattaye devaṃ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca |
hutvā caiva yathānyāyaṃ niṣpannaṃ tadanusmaret || 13 ||

niṣpannasyaivamutpattimanuvṛttiṃ ca karmaṇā |
ārjavaṃ bhoganiṣpattiḥ kuryātprītiṃ parāṃ tathā || 14 ||

niṣkṛtyarthaṃ ca jātyāyurbhogasaṃskārasiddhaye |
hutvāhutitrayaṃ devaṃ prārthayeddeśikottamaḥ || 15 ||

bhoktṛtvaviṣayāsaṃgamalaṃ tatkāyaśodhanam |
kṛtvaivameva śiṣyasya chindyātpāśatrayaṃ tataḥ || 16 ||

nikṛtyā pari baddhasya pāśasyātyantabhedataḥ |
kṛtvā śiṣyasya caitanyaṃ svacchaṃ manyeta kevalam || 17 ||

hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ vahnau brahmāṇaṃ pūjayettataḥ |
hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasmai śivājñāmanusaṃdiśet || 18 ||

pitāmaha tvayā nāsya yātuḥ śaivaṃ paraṃ padam |
pratibandho vidhātavyaḥ śaivājñaiṣā garīyasī || 19 ||

ityādiśya tamabhyarcya visṛja ca vidhānataḥ |
samabhyarcya mahādevaṃ juhuyādāhutitrayam || 20 ||

nivṛttyā śuddhamuddhṛtya śiṣyātmānaṃ yathā purā |
niveśyātmani sūtre ca vāgīśaṃ pūjayettataḥ || 21 ||

hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasmai praṇamya ca visṛjya tām |
kuryānnivṛttaḥ saṃdhānaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ kalayā saha || 22 ||

saṃdhāne yugapatpūjāṃ kṛtvā hutvāhutitrayam |
śiṣyātmanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ praveśaṃ tvatha bhāvayet || 23 ||

tataḥ pratiṣṭhāmāvāhya kṛtvāśeṣaṃ puroditam |
tadvyāptiṃ vyāpikāṃ tasya vāgīśānīṃ ca bhāvayet || 24 ||

pūrṇedumaṃḍalaprakhyāṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca pūrvavat |
viṣṇave saṃviśedājñāṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 25 ||

viṣṇorvisarjanādyaṃ ca kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca vidyayā |
pratiṣṭhāmanusaṃdhāya tasyāṃ cāpi yathā purā || 26 ||

kṛtvānucintya tadvyāptiṃ vāgīśāṃ ca yathākramam |
dīptāgnau pūrṇahomāntaṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca pūrvavat || 27 ||

nīlarudramupasthāpya tasmai pūjādikaṃ tathā |
kṛtvā karma śivājñāṃ ca dadyātpūrvoktavartmanā || 28 ||

tapastamapi codvāsya kṛtvā tasyātha śāntaye |
vidyākalāṃ samādhāya tadvyāptiṃ cāvalokayet || 29 ||

svātmano vyāpikāṃ tadvadvāgīśīṃ ca yathā purā |
bālārkasadṛśākārāṃ bhāsayantīṃ diśo daśa || 30 ||

tataḥ śeṣaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā devaṃ maheśvaram |
āvāhyārādhya hutvāsmai śivājñāṃ manasā diśet || 31 ||

maheśvaraṃ tathotsṛjya kṛtvānyāṃ ca kalāmimām |
śāntyatītāṃ kalāṃ nītvā tadvyāptimavalokayet || 32 ||

svātmano vyāpikāṃ tadvadvāgīśāṃ ca viciṃtayet |
nabhomaṃḍalasaṃkāśāṃ pūrṇāntaṃ cāpi pūrvavat || 33 ||

kṛtvā śeṣavidhānena samabhyarcya sadāśivam |
tasmai samādiśedājñāṃ śaṃbhoramitakarmaṇaḥ || 34 ||

tatrāpi ca yathāpūrvaṃ śivaṃ śirasi pūrvavat |
samabhyarcya ca vāgīśaṃ praṇamya ca visarjayet || 35 ||

tataśśivena samprokṣya śiṣyaṃ śirasi pūrvavat |
vilayaṃ śāntyatītāyāḥ śaktitattve .atha ciṃtayet || 36 ||

ṣaḍadhvanaḥ pare pāre sarvādhvavyāpinī parām |
koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ śaivīṃ śaktiñca cintayet || 37 ||

tadagre śiṣyamānīya śuddhasphaṭikanirmalam |
prakṣālya karttarīṃ paścācchivaśāstroktamārgataḥ || 38 ||

kuryāttasya śikhācchedaṃ saha sūtreṇa deśikaḥ |
tatastāṃ gomaye nyasya śivāgnau juhuyācchikhām || 39 ||

vauṣaḍantena mūlena punaḥ prakṣālya kartarīm |
haste śiṣyasya caitanyaṃ taddehe vinivartayet || 40 ||

tataḥ snātaṃ samācāntaṃ kṛtasvastyayanaṃ śiśum |
praveśya maṃḍalābhyāsaṃ praṇipatya ca daṃḍavat || 41 ||

pūjāṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ kriyāvaikalyaśuddhaye |
vācakenaiva mantreṇa juhuyādāhutitrayam || 42 ||

upāṃśūccārayogena juhuyādāhutitrayam |
punassaṃpūjya deveśaṃ mantravaikalyaśuddhaye || 43 ||

mānasoccārayogena juhuyādāhutitrayam |
tatra śaṃbhuṃ samārādhya maṃḍalasthaṃ sahāṃbayā |
hutvāhutitrayaṃ paścātprārthayetprāṃjalirguruḥ // 44 || 44 ||

bhagavaṃstvatprasādena śuddhirasya ṣaḍadhvanaḥ |
kṛtā tasmātparaṃ dhāma gamayainaṃ tavāvyayam || 45 ||

iti vijñāpya devāya nāḍīsaṃdhānapūrvakam |
pūrṇāntaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā tato bhūtāni śodhayet || 46 ||

sthirāsthire tataḥ śuddhyai śītoṣṇe ca tataḥ pade |
dhyāyedvyāptyaikatākāre bhūtaśodhanakarmaṇi || 47 ||

bhūtānāṃ granthivicchedaṃ kṛtvā tyaktvā sahādhipaiḥ |
bhūtāni sthitayogena yo japetparame śive || 48 ||

viśodhyāsya tanuṃ dagdhvā plāvayitvā sudhākaṇaiḥ |
sthāpyātmānaṃ tataḥ kuryādviśuddhādhvamayaṃ vapuḥ || 49 ||

tatrādau śāntyatītāṃ tu vyāpikāṃ svādhvanaḥ kalām |
śuddhāmeva śiśormūrdhni nyasecchāntimukhe tathā || 50 ||

vidyāṃ galādinābhyantaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ tadadhaḥ kramāt |
jānvantaṃ tadadho nyasyennivṛttiṃ cānuciṃtayet || 51 ||

svabījaissūtramantraṃ ca nyasyāṃ gaistaṃ śivātmakam |
buddhvā taṃ hṛdayāṃbhoje devamāvāhya pūjayet || 52 ||

āśāsya nityasāṃnidhyaṃ śivasvātmyaṃ śiśau guruḥ |
śivatejomayasyāsya śiśorāpādayedguṇān || 53 ||

aṇimādīnprasīdeti pradadyādāhutitrayam |
tathaiva tu guṇāneva punarasyopapādayet || 54 ||

sarvajñātāṃ tathā tṛptiṃ bodhaṃ cādyantavarjitam |
aluptaśaktiṃ svātantryamanantāṃ śaktimeva ca || 55 ||

tato devamanujñāpya sadyādikalaśaistu tam |
abhiṣiṃceta deveśaṃ dhyāyanhṛdi yathākramam || 56 ||

athopaveśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivamabhyarcya pūrvavat |
labdhānujñaḥ śivācchaivīṃ vidyāmasmai samādiśet || 57 ||

oṃkārapūrvikāṃ tatra saṃpuṭāntu namo .antagām |
śivaśaktiyutāñcaiva śaktividyāṃ ca tādṛśīm || 58 ||

ṛṣiṃ chandaśca devaṃ ca śivatāṃ śivayostathā |
pūjāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ śambhorāsanāni ca sandiśet || 59 ||

punaḥ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ yanmayā samanuṣṭhitam |
sukṛtaṃ kuru tatsarvamiti vijñāpayecchivam || 60 ||

sahaśiṣyo gururdevaṃ daṇḍavatkṣitimaṃḍale |
praṇamyodvāsayettasmānmaṃḍalātpāvakādapi || 61 ||

tataḥ sadasikāḥ sarve pūjyāḥ pūjārhakāḥ kramāt || 62 ||

sevyā vittānusāreṇa sadasyāśca sahartvijaḥ |
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ || 63 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe ṣaḍadhvaśuddhyādikathanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo .adhyāyaḥ || 18 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sādhakaṃ nāma nāmataḥ |
saṃskāramantramāhātmyaṃ kathane sūcitaṃ mayā || 1 ||

saṃpūjya maṃḍale devaṃ sthāpya kumbhe ca pūrvavat |
hutvā śiṣyamanuṣṇīṣaṃ prāpayedbhuvi maṃḍale || 2 ||

pūrvāntaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā hutvāhutiśataṃ tathā |
santarpya mūlamantreṇa kalaśairdeśikottamaḥ || 3 ||

sandīpya ca yathāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ kramāt |
abhiṣicya yathāpūrvaṃ pradadyānmantramuttamam || 4 ||

tatra vidyopadeśāntaṃ kṛtvā vistaraśaḥ kramāt |
puṣpāmbunā śiśoḥ pāṇau vidyāṃ śaivīṃ samarpayet || 5 ||

tavaihikāmuṣmikayoḥ sarvasiddhiphalapradaḥ |
bhavatyeva mahāmantraḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ || 6 ||

ityutvā devamabhyarcya labdhānujñaḥ śivādguruḥ |
sādhanaṃ śivayogaṃ ca sādhakāya samādiśet || 7 ||

tacchrutvā gurusaṃdeśaṃ kramaśo mantrasādhakaḥ |
purato viniyogasya mantrasādhanamācaret || 8 ||

sādhanaṃ mūlamantrasya puraścaraṇamucyate |
purataścaraṇīyatvādviniyogākhyakarmaṇaḥ || 9 ||

nātyantaṃ karaṇīyantu mumukṣormantrasādhanam |
kṛtantu tadihānyatra tāsyāpi śubhadaṃ bhavet || 10 ||

śubhe .ahani śubhe deśe kāle vā doṣavarjite |
śukladantanakhaḥ snātaḥ kṛtapūrvāhṇikakriyaḥ || 11 ||

alaṃkṛtya yathā labdhairgandhamālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ |
soṣṇīṣaḥ sottarāsaṃgaḥ sarvaśuklasamāhitaḥ || 12 ||

devālaye gṛhe .anyasmindeśe vā sumanohare |
sukhenābhyastapūrveṇa tvāsanena kṛtāsanaḥ || 13 ||

tanuṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ śaivīṃ śivaśāstroktavartmanā |
saṃpūjya devadeveśaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram || 14 ||

nivedya pāyasaṃ tasmai samapyārādhanaṃ kramāt |
praṇipatya ca taṃ devaṃ prāptānujñaśca tanmukhāt || 15 ||

koṭivāraṃ tadarddhaṃ vā tadarddhaṃ vā japecchivam |
lakṣaviṃśatikaṃ vāpi daśalakṣamathāpi vā || 16 ||

tataśca pāyasākṣāralavaṇaikamitāśanaḥ |
ahiṃsakaḥ kṣamī śānto dāntaścaiva sadā bhavet || 17 ||

alābhe pāyasasyāśnanphalamūlādikāni vā |
vihitāni śivenaiva viśiṣṭānyuttarottaram || 18 ||

caruṃ bhakṣyamatho saktukaṇānyāvakameva ca |
śākaṃ payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ mūlaṃ phalamathodakam || 19 ||

abhimantrya ca mantreṇa bhakṣyabhojyādikāni ca |
sādhane .asminviśeṣeṇa nityaṃ bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ || 20 ||

mantrāṣṭaśatapūtena jalena śucinā vratī |
snāyānnadīnadotthena prokṣayedvātha śaktitaḥ || 21 ||

tarpayecca tathā nityaṃ juhuyācca śivānale |
saptabhiḥ pañcabhirdravyaistribhirvātha ghṛtena vā || 22 ||

itthaṃ bhaktyā śivaṃ śaivo yaḥ sādhayati sādhakaḥ |
tasyehāmutra duṣprāpaṃ na kiṃcidapi vidyate || 23 ||

athavā .aharaharmantraṃ japedekāgramānasaḥ |
anaśnanneva sāhasraṃ vinā mantrasya sādhanam || 24 ||

na tasya durlabhaṃ kiṃcinna tasyāstyaśubhaṃ kvacit |
iha vidyāṃ śriyaṃ saukhyaṃ labdhvā muktiṃ ca vindati || 25 ||

sādhane viniyoge ca nitye naimittike tathā |
japejjalairbhasmanā ca snātvā mantreṇa ca kramāt || 26 ||

śucirbaddhaśikhassūtrī sapavitrakarastathā |
dhṛtatripuṃḍrarudrākṣo vidyāṃ pañcākṣarīṃ japet || 27 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṃḍe sādhakasaṃskāramantramāhātmyaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 19 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

athaivaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ śiṣyaṃ kṛtapāśupatavratam |
ācāryatve .abhiṣiṃceta tadyogatvena cānyathā || 1 ||

maṇḍalaṃ pūrvavatkṛttvā saṃpūjya parameśvaram |
sthāpayatpaṃcakalaśāndikṣu madhye ca pūrvavat || 2 ||

nivṛttiṃ purato nyasya pratiṣṭhāṃ paścime ghaṭe |
vidyāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ śāntimuttare madhyataḥ parām || 3 ||

kṛtvā rakṣādikaṃ tatra baddhvā mudrāṃ ca dhainavīm |
abhimantrya ghaṭānhutvā pūrṇāntaṃ ca yathā purā || 4 ||

praveśya maṃḍale śiṣyamanuṣṇīṣaṃ ca deśikaḥ |
tarpaṇādyaṃ tu mantrāṇāṃ kuryātpūrvāvasānakam || 5 ||

tataḥ saṃpūjya deveśamanujñāpya ca pūrvavat |
abhiṣekāya taṃ śiṣyamāsanaṃ tvadhirohayet || 6 ||

sakalīkṛtya taṃ paścātkalāpaṃcakarūpiṇam |
nyastamantratanuṃ baddhvā śivaṃ śiṣyaṃ samarpayet || 7 ||

tato nivṛttikuṃbhādighaṭānuddhṛtya vai kramāt |
madhyamāntācchivenaiva śiṣyaṃ tamabhiṣecayat || 8 ||

śivahastaṃ samarpyātha śiśoḥ śirasi deśikaḥ |
śivabhāvasamāpannaḥ śivācāryaṃ tamādiśet || 9 ||

athālaṃkṛtya taṃ devamārādhya śivamaṇḍale |
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ hutvā dadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ || 10 ||

punaḥ sampūjya deveśaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat |
śirasyaṃjalimādhāya śivaṃ vijñāpayedguruḥ || 11 ||

bhagavaṃstvatprasādena deśiko.yaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ |
anugṛhya tvayā deva divyājñāsmai pradīyatām || 12 ||

evaṃ vijñāpya śiṣyeṇa saha bhūyaḥ praṇamya ca |
śivaṃ śivāgamaṃ divyaṃ pūjayecchivavadguruḥ || 13 ||

punaḥ śivamanujñāpya śivajñānasya pustakam |
ubhābhyāmatha pāṇibhyāṃ dadyācchiṣyāya deśikaḥ || 14 ||

sa tāmmūrdhni samādhāya vidyāṃ vidyāsanopari |
adhiropya yathānyāyamabhivandya samarcayet || 15 ||

atha tasmai gururdadyādrājopakaraṇānyapi |
ācāryapadavīṃ prāpto rājyaṃ cāpi yato .arhati || 16 ||

athānuśāsanaṃ kuryātpūrvairācaritaṃ yathā |
yathā ca śivaśāstroktaṃ yathā lokeṣu pūjyate || 17 ||

śiṣyānparikṣya yatnena śivaśāstroktalakṣaṇaiḥ |
saṃskṛtya ca śivajñānaṃ tebhyo dadyācca deśikaḥ || 18 ||

evaṃ sarvamanāyāsaṃ śaucaṃ kṣāntiṃ dayāṃ tathā |
aspṛhāmapyasūyāṃ ca yatnena ca vibhāvayet || 19 ||

itthamādiśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivamudvāsya maṃḍalāt |
śivakuṃbhānalādīṃśca sadasyānapi pūjayet || 20 ||

yugapadvātha saṃskārānkurvīta sagaṇo guruḥ |
tatra yatra dvayaṃ vāpi prayogasyopadiśyate || 21 ||

tadādāveva kalaśānkalpayedadhvaśuddhivat |
kṛtvā samayasaṃskāramabhiṣekaṃ vinākhilam || 22 ||

samabhyarcya śivaṃ bhūyaḥ kṛtvā cādhvaviśodhanam |
tasminparisamāpte tu punardevaṃ prapūjayet || 23 ||

hutvā mantrantu santarpya saṃdīpyāśāsya ceśvaram |
samarpya mantraṃ śiṣyasya pāṇau śeṣaṃ samāpayet || 24 ||

athavā mantrasaṃskāramanuciṃtyākhilaṃ kramāt |
adhvaśuddhiṃ guruḥ kuryādabhiṣekāvasānikam || 25 ||

tatra yaḥ śāntyatītādikalāsu vihito vidhiḥ |
sa sarvo .api vidhātavyastattvatrayaviśodhane || 26 ||

śivavidyātmatattvākhyaṃ tattvatrayamudāhṛtam |
śaktau śivastato vidyāttasyāstvātmā samudbabhau || 27 ||

śivena śāntyatītādhvā vyāptastadaparaḥ paraḥ |
vidyayā pariśiṣṭo .adhvā hyātmanā nikhilaḥ kramāt || 28 ||

durlabhaṃ śāṃbhavaṃ matvā mantramūlaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ |
śāktaṃ śaṃsīta saṃskāraṃ śivaśāstrārthapāragāḥ || 29 ||

iti te sarvamākhyātaṃ saṃskārākhyasya karmaṇaḥ |
cāturvidhyamidaṃ kṛṣṇa kiṃ bhūya śrotumicchasi || 30 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe viśeṣādisaṃskṛtirnāma viṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 20 ||

kṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavañchrotumicchāmi śivāśramaniṣeviṇām |
śivaśāstroditaṃ karma nityanaimittikaṃ tathā || 1 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

prātarutthāya śayanāddhyātvā devaṃ sahāmbayā |
vicārya kāryaṃ nirgacchedgṛhādabhyudite .aruṇe || 2 ||

abādhe vijane deśe kuryādāvaśyakaṃ tataḥ |
kṛtvā śaucaṃ vidhānena dantadhāvanamācaret || 3 ||

alābhe dantakāṣṭhānāmaṣṭamyādidineṣu ca |
apāṃ dvādaśagaṇḍūṣaiḥ kuryādāsyaviśodhanam || 4 ||

ācamya vidhivatpaścādvāruṇaṃ snānamācaret |
nadyāṃ vā devakhāte vā hrade vātha gṛhe .api vā || 5 ||

snānadravyāṇi tattīre sthāpayitvā bahirmalam |
vyāpohya mṛdamālipya snātvā gomayamālipet || 6 ||

snātvā punaḥ punarvastraṃ tyaktvāvātha viśodhya ca |
susnāto nṛpavadbhūyaḥ śuddhaṃ vāso vasīta ca || 7 ||

malasnānaṃ sugandhādyaiḥ snānaṃ dantaviśodhanam |
na kuryādbrahmacārī ca tapasvī vidhavā tathā || 8 ||

sopavītaśśikhāṃ baddhā praviśya ca jalāntaram |
avagāhya samācānto jale nyasyettrimaṃḍalam || 9 ||

saumye magnaḥ punarmantraṃ japecchaktyā śivaṃ smaret |
utthāyācamya tenaiva svātmānamabhiṣecayet || 10 ||

gośṛṃgeṇa sadarbheṇa pālāśena dalena vā |
pādmena vātha pāṇibhyāṃ paṃcakṛtvastrireva vā || 11 ||

udyānādau gṛhe caiva varddhanyā kalaśena vā |
avagāhanakāle .adbhirmantritairabhiṣecayet || 12 ||

atha cedvāruṇaṃ kartumaśaktaḥ śuddhavāsasā |
ārdreṇa śodhayeddehamāpādatalamastakam || 13 ||

āgneyaṃ vātha vā māntraṃ kuryātsnānaṃ śivena vā |
śivaciṃtāparaṃ snānaṃ yuktasyātmīyamucyate || 14 ||

svasūtroktavidhānena mantrācamanapūrvakam |
ācaredbrahmayajñāntaṃ kṛtvā devāditarpaṇam || 15 ||

maṃḍalasthaṃ mahādevaṃ dhyātvābhyarcya yathāvidhi |
dadyādarghyaṃ tatastasmai śivāyādityarūpiṇe || 16 ||

atha vaitatsvasūtroktaṃ kṛtvā hastau viśodhayet |
karanyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ || 17 ||

vāmahastagatāṃbhobhirgandhasiddhārthakānvitaiḥ |
kuśapuṃjena vābhyukṣya mūlamantrasamanvitaiḥ || 18 ||

āpohiṣṭhādibhirmantraiḥ śeṣamāghrāya vai jalam |
vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva devaṃ saṃbhāvayetsitam || 19 ||

arghamādāya dehasthaṃ savyanāsāpuṭena ca |
kṛṣṇavarṇena bāhyasthaṃ bhāvayecca śilāgatam || 20 ||

tarpayedatha devebhya ṛṣibhiśca viśeṣataḥ |
bhūtebhyaśca pitṛbhyaśca dadyādarghyaṃ yathāvidhi || 21 ||

raktacandanatoyena hastamātreṇa maṃḍalam |
suvṛttaṃ kalpayedbhūmau raktacūrṇādyalaṃkṛtam || 22 ||

tatra saṃpūjayedbhānuṃ svakīyāvaraṇaiḥ saha |
svakholkāyeti mantreṇa sāṃgatassukhasiddhaye || 23 ||

punaśca maṃḍalaṃ kṛtvā tadaṃgaiḥ paripūjya ca |
tatra sthāpya hemapātraṃ māgadhaprasthasaṃmitam || 24 ||

pūrayedgandhatoyena raktacandanayoginā |
raktapuṣpaistilaiścaiva kuśākṣatasamanvitaiḥ || 25 ||

dūrvāpāmārgagavyaiśca kevalena jalena vā |
jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā natvā devaṃ ca maṃḍale || 26 ||

kṛtvā śirasi tatpātraṃ dadyādarghyaṃ śivāya tat |
athavāṃjalinā toyaṃ sadarbhaṃ mūlavidyayā || 27 ||

utkṣipedambarasthāya śivāyādityamūrtaye |
kṛtvā punaḥ karanyāsaṃ karaśodhanapūrvakam || 28 ||

buddhveśānādisadyāntaṃ paṃcabrahmamayaṃ śivam |
gṛhītvā bhasitaṃ mantrairvimṛjyāGgāni saṃspṛśet || 29 ||

yā dināntaiśśirovaktrahṛdguhyacaraṇānkramāt |
tato mūlena sarvāṃgamālabhya vasanāntaram || 30 ||

paridhāya dvirācamya prokṣyaikādaśamantritaiḥ |
jalairācchādya vāso .ayaddvirācamya śivaṃ smaret || 31 ||

punarnyastakaro mantrī tripuṃḍraṃ bhasmanā likhet |
avakramāya taṃ vyaktaṃ lalāṭe gandhavāriṇā || 32 ||

vṛttaṃ vā caturasraṃ vā bindumarddhendumeva vā |
lalāṭe yādṛśaṃ puṇḍraṃ likhitaṃ bhasmanā punaḥ || 33 ||

tādṛśaṃ bhujayormūrdhni stanayorantare likhet |
sarvāṃgoddhūlanaṃ caiva na samānaṃ tripuṇḍrakaiḥ || 34 ||

tasmāttripuṇḍramevaikaṃ likheduddhūlanaṃ vinā |
rudrākṣāndhārayedmūrdhni kaṃṭhe śrote kare tathā || 35 ||

suvarṇavarṇamacchinnaṃ śubhaṃ nānyairdhṛtaṃ śubham |
viprādīnāṃ kramācchreṣṭhaṃ pītaṃ raktamathāsitam || 36 ||

tadalābhe yathālābhaṃ dhāraṇīyamadūṣitam |
tatrāpi nottaraṃ nīcairdhāryaṃ nīcamathottaraiḥ || 37 ||

nāśucirdhārayedakṣaṃ sadā kāleṣu dhārayet |
itthaṃ trisandhyamathavā dvisandhyaṃ sakṛdeva vā || 38 ||

kṛtvā snānādikaṃ śaktyā pūjayetparameśvaram |
prajāsthānaṃ samāsādya baddhvā ruciramāsanam || 39 ||

dhyāyeddevaṃ ca devīṃ ca prāGmukho vāpyudaGmukhaḥ |
śvetādīnnakulīśāntāṃstacchiṣyānpraṇamedgurum || 40 ||

punardevaṃ śivaṃ natvā tato nāmāṣṭakaṃ japet |
śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ || 41 ||

saṃsāravaidyassarvajñaḥ paramātmeti cāṣṭakam |
athavā śivamevaikaṃ japitvaikādaśādhikam || 42 ||

jihvāgre tejaso rāśiṃ dhyātvāvyādhyādiśāntaye |
prakṣālya caraṇau kṛtvā karau candanacarcitau |
prakurvīta karanyāsaṃ karaśodhanapūrvakam // 43 || 43 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe nityanaimittikakarmavarṇanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 21 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

nyāsastu trividhaḥ proktaḥ sthityutpattilayakramāt |
sthitirnyāso gṛhasthānāmutpattirbrahmacāriṇām || 1 ||

yatīnāṃ saṃhṛtinyāso vanasthānāṃ tathaiva ca |
sa eva bhartṛhīnāyāḥ kuṭuṃbinyāḥ sthitirbhavet || 2 ||

kanyāyāḥ punarutpattiṃ vakṣye nyāsasya lakṣaṇam |
aṃguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ || 3 ||

dakṣiṇāṃguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṃguṣṭhāntameva ca |
utpattinyāsa ākhyāto viparītastu saṃhṛtiḥ || 4 ||

sabindukānnakārādīnvarṇānnyasyedanukramāt |
aṃgulīṣu śivaṃ nyasyettalayorapyanāmayoḥ || 5 ||

astranyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā daśadikṣvastramantrataḥ |
nivṛttyādikalāḥ paṃca paṃcabhūtasvarūpiṇīḥ || 6 ||

paṃcabhūtādhipaissārddhaṃ tataccihnasamanvitāḥ |
hṛtkaṇṭatālubhrūmadhyabrahmarandhrasamāśrayāḥ || 7 ||

tattadbījena saṃgranthīstattadbījeṣu bhāvayet |
tāsāṃ viśodhanārthāya vidyāṃ paṃcākṣarīṃ japet || 8 ||

niruddhvā prāṇavāyuṃ ca guṇasaṃkhyānusārataḥ |
bhūtagranthiṃ tataśchidyādastreṇaivāstramudrayā || 9 ||

nāḍyā suṣumnayātmānaṃ preritaṃ prāṇavāyunā |
nirgataṃ brahmarandhreṇa yojayecchivatejasā || 10 ||

viśoṣya vāyunā paścāddehaṃ kālāgninā dahet |
tataścoparibhāvena kalāssaṃhṛtya vāyunā || 11 ||

dehaṃ saṃhṛtya vai dagdhaṃ kalāsspṛṣṭvā sahābdhinā |
plāvayitvāmṛtairdehaṃ yathāsthānaṃ niveśayet || 12 ||

atha saṃhṛtya vai dagdhaḥ kalāsargaṃ vinaiva tu |
amṛtaplāvanaṃ kuryādbhasmībhūtasya vai tataḥ || 13 ||

tato vidyāmaye tasmindehe dīpaśikhākṛtim |
śivānnirgatamātmānaṃ brahmarandhreṇa yojayet || 14 ||

dehasyāntaḥ praviṣṭaṃ taṃ dhyātvā hṛdayapaṃkaje |
punaścāmṛtavarṣeṇa siṃcedvidyāmayaṃ vapuḥ || 15 ||

tataḥ kuryātkaranyāsaṃ karaśodhanapūrvakam |
dehanyāsaṃ tataḥ paścānmahatyā mudrayā caret || 16 ||

aṃganyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā śivoktena tu vartmanā |
varṇanyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryyāddhastapādādisaṃdhiṣu || 17 ||

ṣaḍaṃgāni tato nyasya jātiṣaṭkayutāni ca |
digbandhamācaretpaścādāgneyādi yathākramam || 18 ||

yadvā mūrddhādipaṃcāṃgaṃ nyāsameva samācaret |
tathā ṣaḍaṃganyāsaṃ ca bhūtaśuddhyādikaṃ vinā || 19 ||

evaṃ samāsarūpeṇa kṛtvā dehātmaśodhanam |
śivabhāvamupāgamya pūjayetparameśvaram || 20 ||

atha yasyāstyavasaro nāsti vā mativibhramaḥ |
sa vistīrṇena kalpena nyāsakarma samācaret || 21 ||

tatrādyo mātṛkānyāso brahmanyāsastataḥ paraḥ |
tṛtīyaḥ praṇavanyāso haṃsanyāsastaduttaraḥ || 22 ||

paṃcamaḥ kathyate sadbhirnyāsaḥ paṃcākṣarātmakaḥ |
eteṣvekamanekaṃ vā kuryātpūjādi karmasu || 23 ||

akāraṃ mūrdhni vinyasya ākāraṃ ca lalāṭake |
iṃ īṃ ca netrayostadvat uṃ ūṃ śravaṇayostathā || 24 ||

ṛṃ R̥ṃ kapolayoścaiva Lṃ LLṃ nāsāpuṭadvaye |
ememoṣṭhadvayoromauṃ dantapaṅktidvayoḥ kramāt || 25 ||

aṃ jihvāyāmatho tālunyaḥ prayojyo yathākramam |
kavargaṃ dakṣiṇe haste nyasetpaṃcasu sandhiṣu || 26 ||

cavargaṃ ca tathā vāmahastasandhiṣu vinyaset |
ṭavargaṃ ca tavargaṃ ca pādayorubhayorapi || 27 ||

paphau tu pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhe nābhau cāpi babhau tataḥ |
nyasenmakāraṃ hṛdaye tvagādiṣu yathākramam || 28 ||

yakarādisakārāntānnyasetsaptasu dhātuṣu |
haṃkāraṃ hṛdayasyāntaḥ kṣakāraṃ bhrūyugāntare || 29 ||

evaṃ varṇānpravinyasya pañcāśadrudravartmanā |
aṃgavaktrakalābhedātpaṃca brahmāṇi vinyaset || 30 ||

karanyāsādyamapi taiḥ kṛtvā vātha na vā kramāt |
śirovadanahṛdguhyapādeṣvetāni kalpayet || 31 ||

tataścorddhvādivaktrāṇi paścimāntāni kalpayet |
īśānasya kalāḥ pañca pañcasveteṣu ca kramāt || 32 ||

tataścaturṣu vaktreṣu puruṣasya kalā api |
catasraḥ praṇidhātavyāḥ pūrvādikramayogataḥ || 33 ||

hṛtkaṃṭhāṃseṣu nābhau ca kukṣau pṛṣṭhe ca vakṣasi |
aghorasya kalāścāṣṭau pādayorapi hastayoḥ || 34 ||

paścāttrayoḥdaśakalāḥ pāyumeḍhrorujānuṣu |
jaṃghāsphikkaṭipārśveṣu vāmadevasya bhāvayet || 35 ||

ghrāṇe śirasi bāhvośca kalpayetkalpavittamaḥ |
aṣṭatriṃśatkalānyāsamevaṃ kṛtvānupūrvaśaḥ || 36 ||

paścātpraṇavaviddhīmānpraṇavanyāsamācaret |
bāhudvaye kūrparayostathā ca maṇibandhayoḥ || 37 ||

pārśvodarorujaṃgheṣu pādayoḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā |
itthaṃ praṇavavinyāsaṃ kṛtvā nyāsavicakṣaṇaḥ || 38 ||

haṃsanyāsaṃ prakurvīta śivaśāstre yathoditam |
bījaṃ vibhajya haṃsasya netrayorghrāṇayorapi || 39 ||

vibhajya bāhunetrāsyalalāṭe ghrāṇayorapi |
kakṣayoḥ skandhayoścaiva pārśvayostanayostathā || 40 ||

kaṭhyoḥ pāṇyorgulphayośca yadvā paṃcāṃgavartmanā |
haṃsanyāsamimaṃ kṛtvā nyasetpañcākṣarīṃ tataḥ || 41 ||

yathā pūrvoktamārgeṇa śivatvaṃ yena jāyate |
nāśivaḥ śivamabhyasyennāśivaḥ śivamarcayet || 42 ||

nāśivastu śivaṃ dhyāyennāśivamprāpnuyācchivam |
tasmācchaivīṃ tanuṃ kṛtvā tyaktvā ca paśubhāvanām || 43 ||

śivo .ahamiti saṃcintya śaivaṃ karma samācaret |
karmayajñastapoyajño japayajñastaduttaraḥ |
dhyānayajño jñānayajñaḥ pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // 44 || 44 ||

karmayajñaratāḥ kecittapoyajñaratāḥ pare |
japayajñaratāścānye dhyānayajñaratāstathā || 45 ||

jñānayajñaratāścānye viśiṣṭāścottarottaram |
kramayajño dvidhā proktaḥ kāmākāmavibhedataḥ || 46 ||

kāmānkāmī tato bhuktvā kāmāsaktaḥ punarbhavet |
akāme rudrabhavane bhogānbhuktvā tataścyutaḥ || 47 ||

tapoyajñarato bhūtvā jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |
tapasvī ca punastasminbhogān bhuktvā tataścyutaḥ || 48 ||

japadhyānarato bhūtvā jāyate bhuvi mānavaḥ |
japadhyānarato martyastadvaiśiṣṭyavaśādiha || 49 ||

jñānaṃ labdhvācirādeva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt |
tasmānmukto śivājñaptaḥ karmayajño .api dehinām || 50 ||

akāmaḥ kāmasaṃyukto bandhāyaiva bhaviṣyati |
tasmātpañcasu yajñeṣu dhyānajñānaparo bhavet || 51 ||

dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ca yasyāsti tīrṇastena bhavārṇavaḥ |
hiṃsādidoṣanirmukto viśuddhaścittasādhanaḥ || 52 ||

dhyānayajñaḥ parastasmādapavargaphalapradaḥ |
bahiḥ karmakarā yadvannātīva phalabhāginaḥ || 53 ||

dṛṣṭvā narendrabhavane tadvadatrāpi karmiṇaḥ |
dhyānināṃ hi vapuḥ sūkṣmaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamaiśvaram || 54 ||

yatheha karmaṇāṃ sthūlaṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam |
dhyānayajñaratāstasmāddevānpāṣāṇamṛṇmayān || 55 ||

nātyantaṃ pratipadyante śivayāthātmyavedanāt |
ātmasthaṃ yaḥ śivaṃ tyaktvā bahirabhyarcayennaraḥ || 56 ||

hastasthaṃ phalamutsṛjya lihetkūrparamātmanaḥ |
jñānāddhyānaṃ bhaveddhyānājjñānaṃ bhūyaḥ pravartate || 57 ||

tadubhābhyāṃ bhavenmuktistasmāddhyānarato bhavet |
dvādaśānte tathā mūrdhni lalāṭe bhrūyugāntare || 58 ||

nāsāgre vā tathāsye vā kandhare hṛdaye tathā |
nābhau vā śāśvatasthāne śraddhāviddhena cetasā || 59 ||

bahiryāgopacāreṇa devaṃ devīṃ ca pūjayet |
athavā pūjayennityaṃ liṃge vā kṛtakepi vā || 60 ||

vahnau vā sthaṇḍile vātha bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ |
athavāntarbahiścaiva pūjayetparameśvaram |
antaryāgarataḥ pūjāṃ bahiḥ kurvīta vā na vā // 61 || 61 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivaśāstroktanityanaimittikakarmavarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 22 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

vyākhyāṃ pūjāvidhānasya pravadāmi samāsataḥ |
śivaśāstre śivenaiva śivāyai kathitasya tu || 1 ||

aṃgamabhyantaraṃ yāgamagnikāryāvasānakam |
vidhāya vā na vā paścādbahiryāgaṃ samācaret || 2 ||

tatra dravyāṇi manasā kalpayitvā viśodhya ca |
dhyātvā vināyakaṃ devaṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ || 3 ||

dakṣiṇe cottare caiva nandīśaṃ suyaśaṃ tathā |
ārādhya manasā samyagāsanaṃ kalpayedbudhaḥ || 4 ||

ārādhanādikairyuktassiṃhayogāsanādikam |
padmāsanaṃ vā vimalaṃ tattvatrayasamanvitam || 5 ||

tasyopari śivaṃ dhyāyetsāṃbaṃ sarvamanoharam |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ sarvāvayavaśobhanam || 6 ||

sarvātiśayasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |
raktāsyapāṇicaraṇaṃ kundacandrasmitānanam || 7 ||

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ phullapadmatrilocanam |
caturbhujamudārāGgaṃ cārucandrakalādharam || 8 ||

varadābhayahastaṃ ca mṛgaṭaṃkadharaṃ haram |
bhujaṃgahāravalayaṃ cārunīlagalāntaram || 9 ||

sarvopamānarahitaṃ sānugaṃ saparicchadam |
tataḥ saṃciṃtayettasya vāmabhāge maheśvarīm || 10 ||

praphullotpalapatrābhāṃ vistīrṇāyatalocanām |
pūrṇacandrābhavadanāṃ nīlakuṃcitamūrdhajām || 11 ||

nīlotpaladalaprakhyāṃ candrārddhakṛtaśekharām |
ativṛttaghanottuṃgasnigdhapīnapayodharām || 12 ||

tanumadhyāṃ pṛthuśroṇīṃ pītasūkṣmavarāmbarām |
sarvābharaṇasaṃpannāṃ lalāṭatilakojjvalām || 13 ||

vicitrapuṣpasaṃkīrṇakeśapāśopaśobhitām |
sarvato .anuguṇākārāṃ kiṃcillajjānatānanām || 14 ||

hemāravindaṃ vilasaddadhānāṃ dakṣiṇe kare |
daṃḍavaccāparaṃ haste nyasyāsīnāṃ mahāsane || 15 ||

pāśavicchedikāṃ sākṣātsaccidānandarūpiṇīm |
evaṃ devaṃ ca devīṃ ca dhyātvāsanavare śubhe || 16 ||

sarvopacāravadbhaktyā bhāvapuṣpaissamarcayet |
athavā parikalpyaivaṃ mūrtimanyatamāṃ vibhoḥ || 17 ||

śaivīṃ sadāśivākhyāṃ vā tathā māheśvarīṃ parām |
ṣaḍviṃśakābhidhānāṃ vā śrīkaṃṭhākhyāmathāpi vā || 18 ||

mantranyāsādikāṃ cāpi kṛtvā svasyāṃ tanau yathā |
asyāṃ mūrtau mūrtimantaṃ śivaṃ sadasataḥ param || 19 ||

dhyātvā bāhyakrameṇaiva pūjāṃ nirvarttayeddhiyā |
samidājyādibhiḥ paścānnābhau homaṃ ca bhāvayet || 20 ||

bhrūmadhye ca śivaṃ dhyāyecchuddhadīpaśikhākṛtim |
itthamaṃge svatantre vā yoge dhyānamaye śubhe || 21 ||

agnikāryyāvasānaṃ ca sarvatraiva samo vidhiḥ |
atha ciṃtāmayaṃ sarvaṃ samāpyārādhanakramam || 22 ||

liṃge ca pūjayeddevaṃ sthaṃḍile vānale .api vā |

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe pūjāvidhānavyākhyānavarṇanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 23 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

prokṣayenmūlamantreṇa pūjāsthānaṃ viśuddhaye |
gandhacandanatoyena puṣpaṃ tatra vinikṣipet || 1 ||

astreṇotsārya vai vighnānavaguṇṭhya ca varmaṇā |
astraṃ dikṣu pravinyasya kalpayedarcanābhuvam || 2 ||

tatra darbhānparistīrya kṣālayetprokṣaṇādibhiḥ |
saṃśodhya sarvapātrāṇi dravyaśuddhiṃ samācaret || 3 ||

prokṣaṇīmardhyapātraṃ ca pādyapātramataḥ param |
tathaivācamanīyasya pātraṃ ceti catuṣṭayam || 4 ||

prakṣālya prokṣya vīkṣyātha kṣipetteṣu jalaṃ śivam |
puṇyadravyāṇi sarvāṇi yathālābhaṃ vinikṣipet || 5 ||

ratnāni rajataṃ hema gandhapuṣpākṣatādayaḥ |
phalapallavadarbhāṃśca puṇyadravyāṇyanekadhā || 6 ||

snānodake sugandhādi pānīye ca viśeṣataḥ |
śītalāni manojñānī kusumādīni nikṣipet || 7 ||

uśīraṃ candanaṃ caiva pādye tu parikalpayet |
jātikaṃkolakarpūrabahumūlatamālakān || 8 ||

kṣipedācamanīye ca cūrṇayitvā viśeṣataḥ |
elāṃ pātreṣu sarveṣu karpūraṃ candanaṃ tathā || 9 ||

kuśāgrāṇyakṣatāṃścaiva yavavrīhitilānapi |
ājyasiddhārthapuṣpāṇi bhasitañcārghyapātrake || 10 ||

kuśapuṣpayavavrīhibahumūlatamālakān |
prakṣipetprokṣaṇīpātre bhasitaṃ ca yathākramam || 11 ||

sarvatra mantraṃ vinyasya varmaṇāveṣṭya bāhyataḥ |
paścādastreṇa saṃrakṣya dhenumudrāṃ pradarśayet || 12 ||

pūjādravyāṇi sarvāṇi prokṣaṇīpātravāriṇā |
samprokṣya mūlamantreṇa śodhayedvidhivattataḥ || 13 ||

pātrāṇāṃ prokṣaṇīmekāmalābhe sarvakarmasu |
sādhayedarghyamadbhistatsāmānyaṃ sādhakottamaḥ || 14 ||

tato vināyakaṃ devaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ kramāt |
pūjayitvā vidhānena dvārapārśve .atha dakṣiṇe || 15 ||

antaḥpurādhipaṃ sākṣānnandinaṃ samyagarcayet |
cāmīkarācalaprakhyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 16 ||

bālendumukuṭaṃ saumyaṃ trinetraṃ ca caturbhujam |
dīptaśūlamṛgīṭaṃkatigmavetradharaṃ prabhum || 17 ||

candrabimbābhavadanaṃ harivaktramathāpi vā |
uttare dvārapārśvasya bhāryyāṃ ca marutāṃ sutām || 18 ||

suyaśāṃ suvratāmambāṃ pādamaṇḍanatatparām |
pūjayitvā praviśyāntarbhavanaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ || 19 ||

saṃpūjya liGgaṃ tairdravyairnirmālyamapanodayet |
prakṣālya puṣpaṃ śirasi nyasettasya viśuddhaye || 20 ||

puṣpahasto japecchaktyā mantraṃ mantraviśuddhaye |
aiśānyāṃ caṇḍamārādhya nirmālyaṃ tasya dāpayet || 21 ||

kalpayedāsanaṃ paścādādhārādi yathākramam |
ādhāraśaktiṃ kalyāṇīṃ śyāmāṃ dhyāyedadho bhuvi || 22 ||

tasyāḥ purastādutkaṃṭhamanantaṃ kuṇḍalākṛtim |
dhavalaṃ paṃcaphaṇinaṃ lelihānamivāmbaram || 23 ||

tasyoparyāsanaṃ bhadraṃ kaṇṭhīravacatuṣpadam |
dharmmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryañca padāni vai || 24 ||

āgneyādiśvetaraktapītaśyāmāni varṇataḥ |
adharmādīni pūrvādīnyuttarāntānyanukramāt || 25 ||

rājāvartamaṇiprakhyānnyasya gātrāṇi bhāvayet |
asyordhvacchādanaṃ padmamāsanaṃ vimalaṃ sitam || 26 ||

aṣṭapatrāṇi tasyāhuraṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam |
kesarāṇi ca vāmādyā rudrāvāmādiśaktibhiḥ || 27 ||

bījānyapi ca tā eva śaktayoṃtarmanonmanīḥ |
karṇikāparavairāgyaṃ nālaṃ jñānaṃ śivātmakam || 28 ||

kandaśca śivadharmātmā karṇikānte trimaṇḍale |
trimaṇḍaloparyātmādi tattvatritayamāsanam || 29 ||

sarvāsanopari sukhaṃ vicitrāstaraṇāstṛtam |
āsanaṃ kalpayeddivyaṃ śuddhavidyāsamujjvalam || 30 ||

āvāhanaṃ sthāpanaṃ ca sannirodhaṃ nirīkṣaṇam |
namaskāraṃ ca kurvīta badhvā mudrāḥ pṛthakpṛthak || 31 ||

pādyamācamanaṃ cārghyaṃ gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tataḥ param |
dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca tāṃbūlaṃ dattvātha svāpayecchivau || 32 ||

athavā parikalpyaivamāsanaṃ mūrtimeva ca |
sakalīkṛtya mūlena brahmābhiścāparaistathā || 33 ||

āvāhayettato devyā śivaṃ paramakāraṇam |
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ devaṃ niścalamakṣaram || 34 ||

kāraṇaṃ sarvalokānāṃ sarvalokamayaṃ param |
antarbahiḥsthitaṃ vyāpya hyaṇoraṇu mahattaram || 35 ||

bhaktānāmaprayatnena dṛśyamīśvaramavyayam |
brahmendraviṣṇurudrādyairapi devairagocaram || 36 ||

devasāraṃ ca vidvadbhiragocaramiti śrutam |
ādimadhyāntarahitaṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavarogiṇām || 37 ||

śivatattvamiti khyātaṃ śivārthaṃ jagati sthiram |
paṃcopacāravadbhaktyā pūjayelliṃgamuttamam || 38 ||

liṃgamūrttirmaheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
snānakāle prakurvīta jayaśabdādimaṃgalam || 39 ||

pañcagavyaghṛtakṣīradadhimadhvādipūrvakaiḥ |
mūlaiḥ phalānāṃ sāraiśca tilasarṣapasaktubhiḥ || 40 ||

bījairyavādibhiśśastaiścūrṇairmāṣādisaṃbhavaiḥ |
saṃsnāpyālipya piṣṭādyaiḥ snāpayeduṣṇavāribhiḥ || 41 ||

gharṣayedvilvapatrādyairlepagandhāpanuttaye |
punaḥ saṃsnāpya salilaiścakravarttyupacārataḥ || 42 ||

sugandhāmalakaṃ dadyāddharidrāṃ ca yathākramam |
tataḥ saṃśodhya salilairliṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā || 43 ||

snāpayedgandhatoyena kuśapuṣpodakena ca |
hiraṇyaratnatoyaiśca mantrasiddhairyathākramam || 44 ||

asaṃbhave tu dravyāṇāṃ yathāsaṃbhavasaṃbhṛtaiḥ |
kevalairmantratoyairvā snāpayecchraddhayā śivam || 45 ||

kalaśenātha śaṃkhena varddhanyā pāṇinā tathā |
sakuśena sapuṣpeṇa snāpayenmantrapūrvakam || 46 ||

pavamānena rudreṇa nīlena tvaritena ca |
liṃgasūktādisūktaiśca śirasātharvaṇena ca || 47 ||

ṛgbhiśca sāmabhiḥ śaivairbrahmabhiścāpi paṃcabhiḥ |
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ śivena praṇavena ca || 48 ||

yathā devasya devyāśca kuryātsnānādikaṃ tathā |
na tu kaścidviśeṣo .asti tatra tau sadṛśau yataḥ || 49 ||

prathamaṃ devamuddiśya kṛtvā snānādikāḥ kriyāḥ |
devyaiḥ praścātprakurvīta devadevasya śāsanāt || 50 ||

arddhanārīśvare pūjye paurvāparyaṃ na vidyate |
tatra tatropacārāṇāṃ liṃge vānyatra vā kvacit || 51 ||

kṛtvā .abhiṣekaṃ liṃgasya śucinā ca sugandhinā |
saṃmṛjya vāsasā dadyādaṃbaraṃ copavītakam || 52 ||

pādyamācamanaṃ cārghyaṃ gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ ca bhūṣaṇam |
dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca naivedyaṃ pānīyaṃ mukhaśodhanam || 53 ||

punaścācamanīyaṃ ca mukhavāsaṃ tataḥ param |
mukuṭaṃ ca śubhaṃ bhadraṃ sarvaratnairalaṃkṛtam || 54 ||

bhūṣaṇāni pavitrāṇi mālyāni vividhāni ca |
vyajane cāmare chatraṃ tālavṛṃtaṃ ca darpaṇam || 55 ||

dattvā nīrājanaṃ kuryātsarvamaṃgalanisvanaiḥ |
gītanṛtyādibhiścaiva jayaśabdasamanvitaḥ || 56 ||

haime ca rājate tāmre pātre vā mṛnmaye śubhe |
padmakaiśśobhitaiḥ puṣpairbījairdadhyakṣatādibhiḥ || 57 ||

triśūlaśaṃkhayugmābjanandyāvartaiḥ karīṣajaiḥ |
śrīvatsasvastikādarśavajrairvahnyādicihnitaiḥ || 58 ||

aṣṭau pradīpānparito vidhāyaikaṃ tu madhyame |
teṣu vāmādikāścintyāḥ pūjyāśca nava śaktayaḥ || 59 ||

kavacena samācchādya saṃrakṣyāstreṇa sarvataḥ |
dhenumudrāṃ ca saṃdarśya pāṇibhyāṃ pātramuddharet || 60 ||

athavāropayetpātre paṃcadīpānyathākramam |
vidikṣvapi ca madhye ca dīpamekamathāpi vā || 61 ||

tatastatpātramuddhṛtya liṃgāderupari kramāt |
triḥ pradakṣiṇayogena bhrāmayenmūlavidyayā || 62 ||

dadyādarghyaṃ tato mūrdhni bhasitaṃ ca sugandhitam |
kṛtvā puṣpāṃjaliṃ paścādupahārānnivedayet || 63 ||

pānīyaṃ ca tato dadyāddattvā vācamanaṃ punaḥ |
paṃcasaugandhikopetaṃ tāmbūlaṃ ca nivedayet || 64 ||

prokṣayetprokṣaṇīyāni gānanāṭyāni kārayet |
liṃgādau śivayościntāṃ kṛtvā śaktyajapecchivam || 65 ||

pradakṣiṇaṃ praṇāmaṃ ca stavaṃ cātmasamarpaṇam |
vijñāpanaṃ ca kāryāṇāṃ kuryādvinayapūrvakam || 66 ||

arghyaṃ puṣpāṃjaliṃ dattvā baddhvā mudrāṃ yathāvidhi |
paścātkṣamāpayeddevamudvāsyātmani ciṃtayet || 67 ||

pādyādimukhavāsāntamarghyādyaṃ cātisaṃkaṭe |
puṣpavikṣepamātraṃ vā kuryādbhāvapurassaram || 68 ||

tāvataiva paro dharmo bhāvane sukṛto bhavet |
asaṃpūjya na bhuñjīta śivamāprāṇasaṃcarāt || 69 ||

yadi pāpastu bhuṃjīta svairaṃ taysa na niṣkṛtiḥ |
pramādena tu bhuṅkte cettadudgīrya prayatnataḥ || 70 ||

snātvā dviguṇamabhyarcya devaṃ devīmupoṣya ca |
śivasyāyutamabhyasyedbrahmacaryapurassaram || 71 ||

paredyuśśaktito dattvā suvarṇādyaṃ śivāya ca |
śivabhaktāya vā kṛtvā mahāpūjāṃ śucirbhavet || 72 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śāstroktaśivapūjanavarṇanaṃ nāma caturviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 24 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

anuktaṃ cātra pūjāyāḥ kamalopabhayādiva |
yattadanyatpravakṣyāmi samāsānna tu vistarāt || 1 ||

havirnivedanātpūrvaṃ dīpadānādanantaram |
kuryādāvaraṇābhyarcāṃ prāpte nīrājane .atha vā || 2 ||

tatreśānādisadyāntaṃ rudrādyastrāntameva ca |
śivasya vā śivāyāśca prathamāvaraṇe japet || 3 ||

aiśānyāṃ pūrvabhāge ca dakṣiṇe cottare tathā |
paścime ca tathāgneyyāmaiśānyāṃ nairṛte tathā || 4 ||

vāyavyāṃ punaraiśānyāṃ caturdikṣu tataḥ param |
garbhāvaraṇamākhyātaṃ mantrasaṃghātameva vā || 5 ||

hṛdayādyastraparyantamathavāpi samarcayet |
tadbahiḥ pūrvataḥ śakraṃ yamaṃ dakṣiṇato yajet || 6 ||

varuṇaṃ vāruṇe bhāge dhanadaṃ cottare budhaḥ |
īśamaiśe .analaṃ svīye nairṛte nirṛtiṃ yajet || 7 ||

mārute mārutaṃ viṣṇuṃ nairṛte vidhimaiśvare |
bahiḥpadmasya vajrādyānyabjāntānyāyudhānyapi || 8 ||

prasiddharūpāṇyāśāsu lokeśānāṃ kramādyajet |
devaṃ devīṃ ca saṃprekṣya sarvāvaraṇadevatāḥ || 9 ||

baddhāṃjalipuṭā dhyeyāḥ samāsīnā yathāsukham |
sarvāvaraṇadevānāṃ svābhidhānairnamoyutaiḥ || 10 ||

puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjanaṃ kuryānnatvā sarvānyathākramam |
garbhāvaraṇamevāpi yajetsvāvaraṇena vā || 11 ||

yoge dhyāne jape home vāhye vābhyantare .api vā |
haviśca ṣaḍvidhaṃ deyaṃ śuddhaṃ mudgānnameva ca || 12 ||

pāyasaṃ dadhisaṃmiśraṃ gauḍaṃ ca madhunāplutam |
eteṣvekamanekaṃ vā nānāvyaṃjanasaṃyutam || 13 ||

guḍakhaṃḍanvitaṃ dadyānmathitaṃ dadhi cottamam |
bhakṣyāṇyapūpamukhyāni svādumanti phalāni ca || 14 ||

raktacandanapuṣpāḍhyaṃ pānīyaṃ cātiśītalam |
mṛdu elārasāktaṃ ca khaṇḍaṃ pūgaphalasya ca || 15 ||

dalāni nāgavallyāśca yuktāni khadirādibhiḥ |
gaurāṇi svarṇavarṇāni vihitāni śivāni ca |
śailameva sitaṃ cūrṇaṃ nātirūkṣaṃ na dūṣitam // 16 || 16 ||

karpūraṃ cātha kaṃkolaṃ jātyādi ca navaṃ śubham |
ālepanaṃ candanaṃ syānmūlakāṣṭhaṃrajomayam || 17 ||

kastūrikā kuṃkumaṃ ca raso mṛgamadātmakaḥ |
puṣpāṇi surabhīṇyeva pavitrāṇi śubhāni ca || 18 ||

nirgandhānyugragandhāni dūṣitānyuṣitāni ca |
svayameva viśīrṇāni na deyāni śivārcane || 19 ||

vāsāṃsi ca mṛdūnyeva tapanīyamayāni ca |
vidyudvalayakalpāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ || 20 ||

sarvāṇyetāni karpūraniryāsāgurucandanaiḥ |
ādhūpitāni puṣpaughairvāsitāni samantataḥ || 21 ||

candanāgurukarpūrakāṣṭhaguggulucūrṇikaiḥ |
ghṛtena madhunā caiva siddho dhūpaḥ praśasyate || 22 ||

kapilāsambhavenaiva ghṛtenātisugandhinā |
nityaṃ pradīpitā dīpāḥ śastāḥ karpūrasaṃyutāḥ || 23 ||

pañcagavyaṃ ca madhuraṃ payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ tathā |
kapilāsambhavaṃ śambhoriṣṭaṃ snāne ca pānake || 24 ||

āsanāni ca bhadrāṇi gajadantamayāni ca |
suvarṇaratnayuktāni citrāṇyāstaraṇāni ca || 25 ||

mṛdūpadhānayuktāni sūkṣmatūlamayāni ca |
uccāvacāni ramyāṇi śayanāni sukhāni ca || 26 ||

nadyassamudragāminyā naṭādvāmbhaḥ samāhṛtam |
śītañca vastrapūtaṃ tadviśiṣṭaṃ snānapānayoḥ || 27 ||

chatraṃ śaśinibhaṃ cāru muktādāmavirājitam |
navaratnacitaṃ divyaṃ hemadaṇḍamanoharam || 28 ||

cāmare ca site sūkṣme cāmīkarapariṣkṛte |
rājahaṃsadvayākāre ratnadaṃḍopaśobhite || 29 ||

darpaṇaṃ cāpi susnigdhaṃ divyagandhānulepanam |
samantādratnasañchannaṃ sragvairaiścāpi bhūṣitam || 30 ||

gambhīraninadaḥ śaṃkho haṃsakundendusannibhaḥ |
āsvapṛṣṭhādideśeṣu ratnacāmīkarācitaḥ || 31 ||

kāhalāni ca ramyāṇi nānānādakarāṇi ca |
suvarṇanirmitānyeva mauktikālaṃkṛtāni ca || 32 ||

bherīmṛdaṃgamurajatimicchapaṭahādayaḥ |
samudrakalpasannādāḥ kalpanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ || 33 ||

bhāṃḍānyapi ca ramyāṇi patrāṇyapi ca kṛtsnaśaḥ |
tadādhārāṇi sarvāṇi sauvarṇānyeva sādhayet || 34 ||

ālayaṃ ca maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ |
rājāvasathavatkalpyaṃ śilpaśāstroktalakṣaṇam || 35 ||

uccaprākārasaṃbhinnaṃ bhūdharākāragopuram |
anekaratnasaṃcchannaṃ hemadvārakapāṭakam || 36 ||

taptajāṃbūnadamayaṃ ratnastambhaśatāvṛtam |
muktādāmavitānāḍhyaṃ vidrumadvāratoraṇam || 37 ||

cāmīkaramayairdivyairmukuṭaiḥ kumbhalakṣaṇaiḥ |
alaṃkṛtaśirobhāgamastrarājena cihnitam || 38 ||

rājanyārhanivāsaiśca rājavīthyādiśobhitaiḥ |
procchritaprāṃśuśikharaiḥ prāsādaiśca samantataḥ || 39 ||

āsthānasthānavaryaiśca sthitairdikṣu vidikṣu ca |
atyantālaṃkṛtaprāntamantarāvaraṇairiva || 40 ||

uttamastrīsahasraiśca nṛtyageyaviśāradaiḥ |
veṇuvīṇāvidagdhaiśca puruṣairbahubhiryutam || 41 ||

rakṣitaṃ rakṣibhirvīrairgajavājirathānvitaiḥ |
anekapuṣpavāṭībhiranekaiśca sarovaraiḥ || 42 ||

dīrghikābhiranekābhirdigvidikṣu virājitam |
vedavedāntatattvajñaiśśivaśāstraparāyaṇaiḥ || 43 ||

śivāśramaratairbhaktaiḥ śivaśāstroktalakṣaṇaiḥ |
śāntaiḥ smitamukhaiḥ sphītaiḥ sadācāraparāyaṇaiḥ || 44 ||

śaivairmāheśvaraiścaiva śrīmadbhissevitadvijaiḥ |
evamantarbahirvāthayathāśaktivinirmitaiḥ || 45 ||

sthāne śilāmaye dānte dārave ceṣṭakāmaye |
kevalaṃ mṛnmaye vāpi puṇyāraṇye .atha vā girau || 46 ||

nadyāṃ devālaye .anyatra deśe vātha gṛhe śubhe |
āḍhyo vātha daridro vā svakāṃ śaktimavaṃcayan |
dravyairnyāyārjitaireva bhaktyā devaṃ samarccayet // 47 || 47 ||

athānyāyārjjitaiścāpi bhaktyā cecchivamarccayet |
na tasya pratyavāyo .asti bhāvavaśyo yataḥ prabhuḥ || 48 ||

nyāyārjitairapi dravyairabhaktyā pūjayedyadi |
na tatphalamavāpnoti bhaktirevātra kāraṇam || 49 ||

bhaktyā vittānusāreṇa śivamuddiśya yatkṛtam |
alpe mahati vā tulyaṃ phalamāḍhyadaridrayoḥ || 50 ||

bhaktyā pracoditaḥ kuryādalpavittopi mānavaḥ |
mahāvibhavasāropi na kuryādbhaktivarjitaḥ || 51 ||

sarvasvamapi yo dadyācchive bhaktivivarjitaḥ |
na tena phalabhāksa syādbhaktirevātra kāraṇam || 52 ||

na tattapobhiratyugrairna ca sarvairmahāmakhaiḥ |
gacchecchivapuraṃ divyaṃ muktvā bhaktiṃ śivātmakam || 53 ||

guhyādguhyataraṃ kṛṣṇa sarvatra parameśvare |
śive bhaktirna saṃdehastayā bhakto vimucyate || 54 ||

śivamantrajapo dhyānaṃ homo yajñastapaḥśrutam |
dānamadhyayanaṃ sarve bhāvārthaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ || 55 ||

bhāvahīno narassarvaṃ kṛtvāpi na vimucyate |
bhāvayuktaḥ punassarvamakṛtvāpi vimucyate || 56 ||

cāndrāyaṇasahasraiśca prājāpatyaśataistathā |
māsopavāsaiścānyaiśca śivabhaktasya kiṃ punaḥ || 57 ||

abhaktā mānavāścāsmiṃlloke giriguhāsu ca |
tapanti cālpabhogārthaṃ bhakto bhāvena mucyate || 58 ||

sāttvikaṃ muktidaṃ karma sattve vai yoginaḥ sthitāḥ |
rājasaṃ siddhidaṃ kuryuḥ karmiṇo rajasāvṛtāḥ || 59 ||

asurā rākṣasāścaiva tamoguṇasamanvitāḥ |
aihikārthaṃ yajantīśaṃ narāścānye .api tādṛśāḥ || 60 ||

tāmasaṃ rājasaṃ vāpi sāttvikaṃ bhāvameva ca |
āśritya bhaktyā pūjādyaṃ kurvanbhadraṃ samaśnute || 61 ||

yataḥ pāpārṇavāttrātuṃ bhaktirnauriva nirmitā |
tasmādbhaktyupapannasya rajasā tamasā ca kim || 62 ||

antyajo vādhamo vāpi mūrkho vā patito .api vā |
śivaṃ prapannaścetkṛṣṇa pūjyassarvasurāsuraiḥ || 63 ||

tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhaktyaiva śivamarcayet |
abhuktānāṃ kvacidapi phalaṃ nāsti yatastataḥ || 64 ||

vakṣyāmyatirahasyaṃ te śṛṇu kṛṣṇa vaco mama |
vedaiśśāstrairvedavidbhirvicārya suviniścitam || 65 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivaśāstroktapūjanavarṇanaṃ nāma paṃcaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 25 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

brahmaghno vā surāpo vā steyīvā gurutalpagaḥ |
mātṛhā pitṛhā vāpi vīrahā bhrūṇahāpi vā || 1 ||

saṃpūjyāmantrakaṃ bhaktyā śivaṃ paramakāraṇam |
