taistaiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyeta varṣairdvādaśabhiḥ kramāt || 2 ||

tasmātsarvaprayatnena patito .api yajecchivam |
bhaktaścennāparaḥ kaścidbhikṣāhāro jitendriyaḥ || 3 ||

kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpaṃ bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇa tu |
pūjayedyadi deveśaṃ tasmātpāpātpramucyate || 4 ||

abbhakṣā vāyubhakṣāśca ye cānye vratakarśitāḥ |
teṣāmetairvratairnāsti śivalokasamāgamaḥ || 5 ||

bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇaiva yaḥ śivaṃ sakṛdarcayet |
sopi gacchecchivasthānaṃ śivamantrasya gauravāt || 6 ||

tasmāttapāṃsi yajñāṃśca sarve sarvasvadakṣiṇāḥ |
śivamūrtyarcanasyaite koṭyaṃśenāpi no samāḥ || 7 ||

baddho vāpyatha mukto vā paścātpañcākṣareṇa cet |
pūjayanmucyate bhakto nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 8 ||

arudro vā sarudro vā sūktena śivamarcayet |
yaḥ sakṛtpatito vāpimūḍho vā mucyate naraḥ || 9 ||

ṣaḍakṣareṇa vā devaṃ sūktamantreṇa pūjayet |
śivabhakto jitakrodho hyalabdho labdha eva ca || 10 ||

alabdhāllabdha evātra viśiṣṭo nātra saṃśayaḥ |
sa brahmāṃgena vā tena sahaṃsena vimucyate || 11 ||

tasmānnityaṃ śivaṃ bhaktyā sūktamantreṇa pūjayet |
ekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ nityameva vā || 12 ||

ye .arcayanti mahādevaṃ vijñeyāste maheśvarāḥ |
jñānenātmasahāyena nārcito bhagavāñchivaḥ || 13 ||

sa ciraṃ saṃsaratyasminsaṃsāre duḥkhasāgare |
durllabhaṃ prāpya mānuṣyaṃ mūḍho nārcayate śivam || 14 ||

niṣphalaṃ tasya tajjanma mokṣāya na bhavedyataḥ |
durllabhaṃ prāpya mānuṣyaṃ ye .arcayanti pinākinam || 15 ||

teṣāṃ hi saphalaṃ janma kṛtārthāste narottamāḥ |
bhavabhaktiparā ye ca bhavapraṇatacetasaḥ || 16 ||

bhavasaṃsmaraṇodyuktā na te duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ |
bhavanāni manojñāni vibhramābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ || 17 ||

dhanaṃ cātṛptiparyyantaṃ śivapūjāvidheḥ phalam |
ye vāñchanti mahābhogānrājyaṃ ca tridaśālaye || 18 ||

te vāñchanti sadākālaṃ harasya caraṇāmbujam |
saubhāgyaṃ kāntimadrūpaṃ sattvaṃ tyāgārdrabhāvatā || 19 ||

śauryaṃ vai jagati khyātiśśivamarcayato bhavet |
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya śivaikāhitamānasaḥ || 20 ||

śivapūjāvidhiṃ kuryādyadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ |
tvaritaṃ jīvitaṃ yāti tvaritaṃ yāti yauvanam || 21 ||

tvaritaṃ vyādhirabhyeti tasmātpūjyaḥ pinākadhṛk |
yāvannāyāti maraṇaṃ yāvannākramate jarā || 22 ||

yāvannendriyavaikalyaṃ tāvatpūjaya śaṃkaram |
na śivārcanatulyo .asti dharmo .anyo bhuvanatraye || 23 ||

iti vijñāya yatnena pūjanīyassadāśivaḥ |
dvārayāgaṃ javanikāṃ parivārabalikriyām || 24 ||

nityotsavaṃ ca kurvīta prasāde yadi pūjayet |
havirnivedanādūrddhvaṃ svayaṃ cānucaro .api vā || 25 ||

prasādaparivārebhyo baliṃ dadyādyathākramam |
nirgamya saha vāditraistadāśābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ || 26 ||

puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ ca dīpañca dadyādannaṃ jalaiḥ saha |
tato dadyānmahāpīṭhe tiṣṭhanbalimudaGmukhaḥ || 27 ||

tato niveditaṃ deve yattadannādikaṃ purā |
tatsarvaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ vā caṇḍāya vinivedayet || 28 ||

hutvā ca vidhivatpaścātpūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet |
kṛtvā prayogaṃ vidhivadyāvanmantraṃ japaṃ tataḥ || 29 ||

nityotsavaṃ prakurvīta yathoktaṃ śivaśāsane |
vipule taijase pātre raktapadmopaśobhite || 30 ||

astraṃ pāśupataṃ divyaṃ tatrāvāhya samarcayet |
śivasyāropyaḥ tatpātraṃ dvijasyālaṃkṛtasya ca || 31 ||

nyastāstravapuṣā tena dīptayaṣṭidharasya ca |
prāsādaparivārebhyo bahirmaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ || 32 ||

nṛtyageyādibhiścaiva saha dīpadhvajādibhiḥ |
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā na drutaṃ cāvilambitam || 33 ||

mahāpīṭhaṃ samāvṛtya triḥpradakṣiṇayogataḥ |
punaḥ praviṣṭo dvārastho yajamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ |
ādāyābhyantaraṃ nītvā hyastramudvāsayet tataḥ // 34 || 34 ||

pradakṣiṇādikaṃ kṛtvā yathāpūrvoditaṃ kramāt |
ādāya cāṣṭapuṣpāṇi pūjāmatha samāpayet || 35 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe sāṃgopāṃgapūjāvidhānavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 26 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

athāgnikāryaṃ vakṣyāmi kuṇḍe vā sthaṃḍile .api vā |
vedyāṃ vā hyāyase pātre mṛnmaye vā nave śubhe || 1 ||

ādhāyāgniṃ vidhānena saṃskṛtya ca tataḥ param |
tatrārādhya mahādevaṃ homakarma samācaret || 2 ||

kuṇḍaṃ dvihastamānaṃ vā hastamātramathāpi vā |
vṛttaṃ vā caturasraṃ vā kuryādvediṃ ca maṇḍalam || 3 ||

kuṇḍaṃ vistāravannimnaṃ tanmadhye .aṣṭadalāmbujam |
caturaṃgulamutsedhaṃ tasya dvyaṃgulameva vā || 4 ||

vitastidviguṇonnatyā nābhimantaḥ pracakṣate |
madhyaṃ ca madhyamāṃgulyā madhyamottamaparvaṇoḥ || 5 ||

aṃgulaiḥ kathyate sadbhiścaturviṃśatibhiḥ karaḥ |
mekhalānāṃ trayaṃ vāpi dvayamekamathāpi vā || 6 ||

yathāśobhaṃ prakurvīta ślakṣṇamiṣṭaṃ mṛdā sthiram |
aśvatthapatravadyoniṃ gajādhāravadeva vā || 7 ||

mekhalāmadhyataḥ kuryātpaścime dakṣiṇe .api vā |
śobhanāmagnitaḥ kiṃcinnimnāmunmīlikāṃ śanaiḥ || 8 ||

agreṇa kuṇḍābhimukhīṃ kiṃcidutsṛjya mekhalām |
notsedhaniyamo vedyāḥ sā mārdī vātha saikatī || 9 ||

maṃḍalaṃ gośakṛttoyairmānaṃ pātrasya noditam |
kuṇḍaṃ ca mṛnmayaṃ vedimālipedgomayāṃbunā || 10 ||

prakṣālya tāpayetpātraṃ prokṣayedanyadaṃbhasā |
svasūtroktaprakāreṇa kuṇḍādau villikhettataḥ || 11 ||

saṃprokṣya kalpayeddarbhaiḥ puṣpairvā vahniviṣṭaram |
arcanārthaṃ ca homārthaṃ sarvadravyāṇi sādhayet || 12 ||

prakṣālyakṣālanīyāni prokṣaṇyā prokṣya śodhayet |
maṇijaṃ kāṣṭhajaṃ vātha śrotriyāgārasambhavam || 13 ||

anyaṃ vābhyarhitaṃ vahniṃ tataḥ sādhāramānayet |
triḥ pradakṣiṇamāvṛtya kuṇḍāderupari kramāt || 14 ||

vahnibījaṃ samuccārya tvādadhītāgnimāsane |
yonimārgeṇa vā tadvadātmanaḥ saṃmukhena vā || 15 ||

niyogaḥ pradeśa sarvaṃ kuṃḍaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ |
svanābhyantaḥsthitaṃ vahniṃ tadrandhrādvisphuliṃgavad || 16 ||

nirgamya pāvake bahye līnaṃ biṃbākṛti smaret |
ājyasaṃskāraparyantamanvādhānapurassaram || 17 ||

svasūtroktakramātkuryānmūlamantreṇa mantravit |
śivamūrtiṃ samabhyarcya tato dakṣiṇapārśvataḥ || 18 ||

nyasya mantraṃ ghṛte mudrāṃ darśayeddhenusaṃjñitām |
sruksruvau taijasau grāhyau na kāṃsyāyasasaisakau || 19 ||

yajñadārumayau vāpi smārtau vā śilpasammatau |
parṇe vā brahmavṛkṣāderacchidre madhya utthite || 20 ||

saṃsṛjya darbhaistau vahnau santāpya prokṣayetpunaḥ |
pārārṣarcyasvasūtroktakrameṇa śivapūrvakaiḥ || 21 ||

juhuyādaṣṭabhirbījairagnisaṃskārasiddhaye |
bhruṃstuṃbruśruṃ krameṇaiva puṃḍrandramityataḥ param || 22 ||

bījāni sapta saptānāṃ jihvānāmanupūrvaśaḥ |
triśikhā madhyamā jihvā bahurūpasamāhvayā || 23 ||

raktāgneyī nairṛtī ca kṛṣṇānyā suprabhā matā |
atiriktā marujjihvā svanāmānuguṇaprabhā || 24 ||

svabijānantaraṃ vācyā svāhāntañca yathākramam |
jihvāmantraistu tairhutvājyaṃ jihvāstvekaikaśa kramāt || 25 ||

raṃ vahnayeti svāheti madhye hutvāhutitrayam |
sarpiṣā vā samidbhirvā pariṣecanamācaret || 26 ||

evaṃ kṛte śivāgniḥ syātsmarettatra śivāsanam |
tatrāvāhya yajeddevamardhanārīśvaraṃ śivam |
dīpāntaṃ pariṣicyātha samiddhomaṃ samācaret // 27 || 27 ||

tāḥ pālāśyaḥ parā vāpi yājñiyā dvādaśāṃgulāḥ |
avakrā na svayaṃ śuṣkāssatvaco nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ || 28 ||

daśāṃgulā vā vihitāḥ kaniṣṭhāṃgulisaṃmitāḥ |
prādeśamātrā vālābhe hotavyāḥ sakalā api || 29 ||

dūrvāpatrasamākārāṃ caturaṃgulamāyatām |
dadyādājyāhutiṃ paścādannamakṣapramāṇataḥ || 30 ||

lājāṃstathā sarṣapāṃśca yavāṃścaiva tilāṃstathā |
sarpiṣāktāni bhakṣyāṇi lehyacoṣyāṇi sambhave || 31 ||

daśaivāhutayastatra pañca vā tritayaṃ ca vā |
hotavyāḥ śaktito dadyādekamevātha vāhutim || 32 ||

śruveṇājyaṃ samityādyāsrucāśeṣātkareṇa vā |
tatra divyena hotavyaṃ tīrthenārṣeṇa vā tathā || 33 ||

dravyeṇaikena vā .alābhe juhuyācchraddhayā punaḥ |
prāyaścittāya juhuyānmantrayitvāhutitrayam || 34 ||

tato homaviśiṣṭena ghṛtenāpūryya vai srucam |
nidhāya puṣpaṃ tasyāgre śruveṇādhomukhena tām || 35 ||

sadarbhena samācchādya mūlenāṃjalinotthitaḥ |
vauṣaḍantena juhuyāddhārāṃ tu yavasaṃmitām || 36 ||

itthaṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ kṛtvā pariṣiṃcecca pūrvavat |
tata udvāsya deveśaṃ gopayettu hutāśanam || 37 ||

tamapyudvāsya vā nābhau yajetsaṃdhāya nityaśaḥ |
athavā vahnimānīya śivaśāstroktavartmanā || 38 ||

vāgīśīgarbhasaṃbhūtaṃ saṃskṛtya vidhivadyajet |
anvādhānaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā paridhīn paridhāya ca || 39 ||

pātrāṇi dvandvarūpeṇa nikṣipyeṣṭvā śivaṃ tataḥ |
saṃśodhya prokṣaṇīpātraṃ prokṣyatāni tadaṃbhasā || 40 ||

praṇītāpātramaiśānyāṃ vinyasyā pūritaṃ jalaiḥ |
ājyasaṃskāraparyantaṃ kṛtvā saṃśodhya sraksruvau || 41 ||

garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmantonnayanaṃ tataḥ |
kṛtvā pṛthakpṛthagghutvā jātamagniṃ vicintayet || 42 ||

tripādaṃ saptahastaṃ ca catuḥśṛṃgaṃ dviśīrṣakam |
madhupiṃgaṃ trinayanaṃ sakapardenduśekharam || 43 ||

raktaṃ raktāmbarālepaṃ mālyabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ sopavītaṃ trimekhalam || 44 ||

śaktimantaṃ sruksruvau ca dadhānaṃ dakṣiṇe kare |
tomaraṃ tālavṛṃtaṃ ca ghṛtapātraṃ tathetaraiḥ || 45 ||

jātaṃ dhyātvaivamākāraṃ jātakarma samācaret |
nālāpanayanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ saṃśodhya sūtakam || 46 ||

śivāgnirucināmāsya kṛtvāhutipurassaram |
pitrorvisarjanaṃ kṛtvā caulopanayanādikam || 47 ||

aptoryāmāvasānāntaṃ kṛtvā saṃskāramasya tu |
ājyadhārādihomaṃ ca kṛtvā sviṣṭakṛtaṃ tataḥ || 48 ||

ramityanena bījena pariṣiṃcettataḥ param |
brahmaviṣṇuśiveśānāṃ lokeśānāṃ tathaiva ca || 49 ||

tadastrāṇāṃ ca paritaḥ kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathākramam |
dhūpadīpādisiddhyarthaṃ vahnimuddhṛtya kṛtyavit || 50 ||

sādhayitvājyapūrvāṇi dravyāṇi punareva ca |
kalpayitvāsanaṃ vahnau tatrāvāhya yathāpurā || 51 ||

saṃpūjya devaṃ devīṃ ca tataḥ pūrṇāntamācaret |
atha vā svāśramoktaṃ tu vahnikarma śivārpaṇam || 52 ||

buddhvā śivāśramī kuryānna ca tatrāparo vidhiḥ |
śivāgnerbhasmasaṃgrāhyamagnihotrodbhavaṃ tu vā || 53 ||

vaivāhognibhavaṃ vāpi pakvaṃ śuci sugandhi ca |
kapilāyāḥ śakṛcchastaṃ gṛhītaṃ gagane patat || 54 ||

na klinnaṃ nātikaṭhinaṃ na durgandhaṃ na śoṣitam |
uparyadhaḥ parityajya gṛhṇīyātpatitaṃ yadi || 55 ||

piṃḍīkṛtya śivāgnyādau tatkṣipenmūlamantrataḥ |
apakvamatipākvaṃ ca santyajya bhasitaṃ sitam || 56 ||

ādāya vā samāloḍya bhasmādhāre vinikṣipet |
taijasaṃ dāravaṃ vāpi mṛnmayaṃ śailameva ca || 57 ||

anyadvā śobhanaṃ śuddhaṃ bhasmādhāraṃ prakalpayet |
same deśe śubhe śuddhe dhanavadbhasma nikṣipet || 58 ||

na cāyuktakare dadyānnaivāśucitale kṣipet |
na saṃspṛśecca nīcāṃgairnopekṣeta na laṃghayet || 59 ||

tasmādbhasitamādāya viniyuṃjīta mantrataḥ |
kāleṣūkteṣu nānyatra nāyogyebhyaḥ pradāpayet || 60 ||

bhasmasaṃgrahaṇaṃ kuryāddeve .anudvāsite sati |
udvāsane kṛte yasmāccaṇḍabhasma prajāpate || 61 ||

agnikārye kṛte paścācchivaśāstroktamārgataḥ |
svasūtroktaprakārādvā balikarma samācaret || 62 ||

atha vidyāsanaṃ nyasya supralipte tu maṇḍale |
vidyākośaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yajetpuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt || 63 ||

vidyāyāḥ purataḥ kṛtvā gurorapi ca maṇḍalam |
tatrāsanavaraṃ kṛtvā puṣpādyai gurumarcayet || 64 ||

tatonupūjayetpūjyān bhojayecca bubhukṣitān |
tatassvayaṃ ca bhuṃjīta śuddhamannaṃ yathāsukham || 65 ||

niveditaṃ ca vā deve taccheṣaṃ cātmaśuddhaye |
śraddadhāno na lobhena na caṇḍāya samarpitam || 66 ||

gandhamālyādi yaccānyattatrāpyeṣa samo vidhiḥ |
na tu tatra śivosmīti buddhiṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ || 67 ||

bhuktvācamya śivaṃ dhyātvā hṛdaye mūlamuccaret |
kālaśeṣaṃ nayedyogyaiḥ śivaśāstrakathādibhiḥ || 68 ||

rātrau vyatīte pūrvāṃśe kṛtvā pūjāṃ manoharām |
śivayoḥ śayanaṃ tvekaṃ kalpayedatiśobhanam || 69 ||

bhakṣyabhojyāṃbarālepapuṣpamālādikaṃ tathā |
manasā karmaṇā vāpi kṛtvā sarvaṃ manoharam || 70 ||

tato devasya devyāśca pādamūle śucissvapet |
gṛhastho bhāryayā sārddhaṃ tadanye .api tu kevalāḥ || 71 ||

pratyūṣasamayaṃ buddhvā mātrāmādyāmudīrayet |
praṇamya manasāṃ devaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam || 72 ||

deśakālocitaṃ kṛtvā śaucādyamapi śaktitaḥ |
śaṃkhādininadairdivyairdevaṃ devīṃ ca bodhayet || 73 ||

tatastatsamayonnidraiḥ puṣpairatisugandhibhiḥ |
nirvartya śivayoḥ pūjāṃ prārabheta puroditam || 74 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe agnikāryavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 27 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śivāśramaniṣeviṇām |
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa naimittikavidhikramam || 1 ||

sarveṣvapi ca māseṣu pakṣayorubhayorapi |
aṣṭābhyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tathā parvāṇi ca kramāt || 2 ||

ayane viṣuve caiva grahaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ |
kartavyā mahatī pūjā hyadhikā vāpi śaktitaḥ || 3 ||

māsimāsi yathānyāyaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ prasādhya tu |
snāpayitvā śivaṃ tena pibeccheṣamupoṣitaḥ || 4 ||

brahmahatyādidoṣāṇāmatīva mahatāmapi |
niṣkṛtirbrahmakūrcasya pānānnānyā viśiṣyate || 5 ||

pauṣe puṣyanakṣatre kuryānnīrājanaṃ vibhoḥ |
māghe maghākhye nakṣatre pradadyād ghṛtakaṃbalam || 6 ||

phālgune cottarānte vai prārabheta mahotsavam |
caitre citrāpaurṇamāsyāṃ dolāṃ kuryādyathāvidhi || 7 ||

vaiśākhyāṃ tu viśākhāyāṃ kuryātpuṣpamahālayam |
jyeṣṭhe mūlākhyanakṣatre śītakumbhaṃ pradāpayet || 8 ||

āṣāḍhe cottarāṣāḍhe pavitrāropaṇaṃ tathā |
śrāvaṇe prākṛtānyāpi maṇḍalāni prakalpayet || 9 ||

śraviṣṭhākhye tu nakṣatre prauṣṭhapadyāṃ tataḥ param |
prokṣayecca jalakrīḍāṃ pūrvāṣāḍhāśraye dine || 10 ||

āśvayujyāṃ tato dadyātpāyasaṃ ca navodanam |
agnikāryaṃ ca tenaiva kuryācchatabhiṣagdine || 11 ||

kārtikyāṃ kṛtikāyoge dadyāddīpasahasrakam |
mārgaśīrṣe tathārdrāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayecchivam || 12 ||

aśaktasteṣu kāleṣu kuryādutsavameva vā |
āsthānaṃ vā mahāpūjāmadhikaṃ vā samarcanam || 13 ||

āvṛtte .api ca kalyāṇe praśasteṣvapi karmasu |
daurmanasye durācāre duḥsvapne duṣṭadarśane || 14 ||

utpāte vāśubhenyasminroge vā prabale .atha vā |
snānapūjājapadhyānahomadānādikāḥ kriyaḥ || 15 ||

nirmitānuguṇāḥ kāryyāḥ puraścaraṇapūrvikāḥ |
śivānale ca vihate punassandhānamācaret || 16 ||

ya evaṃ śarvadharmiṣṭho vartate nityamudyataḥ |
tasyaikajanmanā muktiṃ prayacchati maheśvaraḥ || 17 ||

etadyathottaraṃ kuryānnityanaimittikeṣu yaḥ |
divyaṃ śrīkaṃṭhanāthasya sthānamādyaṃ sa gacchati || 18 ||

tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpakoṭiśatannaraḥ |
kālāntarecyutastasmādaumaṃ kaumārameva ca || 19 ||

saṃprāpya vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ rudralokaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
tatroṣitvā ciraṃ kālaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathoditān || 20 ||

punaścordhvaṃ gatastasmādatītya sthānapañcakam |
śrīkaṇṭhājjñānamāsādya tasmācchaivapuraṃ vrajet || 21 ||

arddhacaryyārataścāpi dvirāvṛttyaivameva tu |
paścājjñānaṃ samāsādya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 22 ||

arddhārddhacarito yastu dehī dehakṣayātparam |
aṃḍāntaṃ vorddhvamavyaktamatītya bhuvanadvayam || 23 ||

saṃprāpya pauruṣaṃ raudrasthānamadrīndrajāpateḥ |
anekayugasāhasraṃ bhuktvā bhogānanekadhā || 24 ||

puṇyakṣaye kṣitiṃ prāpya kule mahati jāyate |
tatrāpi pūrvasaṃskāravaśena sa mahādyutiḥ || 25 ||

paśudharmānparityajya śivadharmarato bhavet |
taddharmagauravādeva dhyātvā śivapuraṃ vrajet || 26 ||

bhogāṃśca vividhānbhuktvā vidyeśvarapadaṃ vrajet |
tatra vidyeśvaraissārddhaṃ bhuktvā bhogānbahūnkramāt || 27 ||

aṇḍasyāntarbahirvātha sakṛdāvartate punaḥ |
tato labdhvā śivajñānaṃ parāṃ bhaktimavāpya ca || 28 ||

śivasādharmyamāsādya na bhūyo vinivartate |
yaścātīva śive bhakto viṣayāsaktacittavat || 29 ||

śivadharmānasau kurvannakurvanvāpi mucyate |
ekāvṛtto dvirāvṛttastrirāvṛtto nivartakaḥ || 30 ||

na punaścakravartī syācchivadharmādhikāravān |
tasmāccchivāśrito bhūtvā yena kenāpi hetunā || 31 ||

śivadharme matiṃ kuryācchreyase cetkṛtodyamaḥ |
nātra nirbandhayiṣyāmo vayaṃ kecana kenacit || 32 ||

nirbandhebhyo .ativādebhyaḥ prakṛtyaitanna rocate |
rocate vā parebhyastu puṇyasaṃskāragauravāt || 33 ||

saṃsārakāraṇaṃ yeṣāṃ na praroḍhumalaṃ bhavet |
prakṛtyanuguṇaṃ tasmādvimṛśyaitadaśeṣataḥ || 34 ||

śivadharme .adhikurvīta yadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ || 35 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe nityanaimittikavidhivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 28 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavaṃstvanmukhādeva śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ mayā |
svāśritānāṃ śivaproktaṃ nityanaimittikaṃ tathā || 1 ||

idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi śivadharmādhikāriṇām |
kāmyamapyasti cetkarma vaktumarhasi sāmpratam || 2 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

astyaihikaphalaṃ kiñcidāmuṣmikaphalaṃ tathā |
aihikāmuṣmikañcāpi tacca pañcavidhaṃ punaḥ || 3 ||

kiṃcitkriyāmayaṃ karma kiṃcitkarma tapo mayam || 4 ||

japadhyānamayaṃ kiṃcitkiṃcitsarvamayaṃ tathā |
kriyāmayaṃ tathā bhinnaṃ homadānārcanakramāt || 5 ||

sarvaśaktimatāmeva nānyeṣāṃ saphalaṃ bhavet |
śaktiścājñā madeśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 6 ||

tasmātkāmyāni karmāṇi kuryādājñādharodvijaḥ |
atha vakṣyāmi kāmyaṃ hi cehāmutra phalapradam || 7 ||

śaivairmāheśvaraiścaiva kāryamantarbahiḥ kramāt |
śivo maheśvaraśceti nātyantamiha bhidyate || 8 ||

yathā tathā na bhidyante śaivā māheśvarā api |
śivāśritā hi te śaivā jñānayajñaratā narāḥ || 9 ||

māheśvarāssamākhyātā karmayajñaratā bhuvi |
tasmādābhyantare kuryuḥ śaivā māheśvarā vahiḥ || 10 ||

na tu prayogo bhidyeta vakṣyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ |
parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ || 11 ||

manobhilaṣite tatra vitānavitatāṃbare |
supralipte mahīpṛṣṭhe darpaṇodarasaṃnibhe || 12 ||

prācīmutpādayetpūrvaṃ śāstradṛṣṭena vartmanā |
ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ vā maṇḍalaṃ parikalpayet || 13 ||

ālikhedvimalaṃ padmamaṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam |
ratnahemādibhiścūrṇairyathāsaṃbhavasaṃbhṛtaiḥ || 14 ||

pañcāvaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ bahuśobhāsamanvitam |
daleṣu siddhayaḥ kalpyāḥ kesareṣu saśaktikāḥ || 15 ||

rudrā vāmādayastvaṣṭau pūrvādidalataḥ kramāt |
karṇikāyāṃ ca vairāgyaṃ bījeṣu nava śaktayaḥ || 16 ||

skande śivātmako dharmo nāle jñānaṃ śivāśrayam |
karṇikopari cāgneyaṃ maṃḍalaṃ sauramaindavam || 17 ||

śivavidyātmatattvākhyaṃ tattvatrayamataḥ param |
sarvāsanopari sukhaṃ vicitrakusumānvitam || 18 ||

paṃcāvaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ pūjayedaṃbayā saha |
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ prasannaṃ śītaladyutim || 19 ||

vidyudvalayasaṃkāśajaṭāmukuṭabhūṣitam |
śārdūlacarmavasanaṃ kiñcitsmitamukhāṃbujam || 20 ||

raktapadmadalaprakhyapādapāṇitalādharam |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam || 21 ||

divyāyudhavarairyuktaṃ divyagandhānulepanam |
paṃcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ candrakhaṇḍaśikhāmaṇim || 22 ||

asya pūrvamukhaṃ saumyaṃ bālārkasadṛśaprabham |
trilocanāravindāḍhyaṃ kṛtabālenduśekharam || 23 ||

dakṣiṇaṃ nīlajīmūtasamānaruciraprabham |
bhrukuṭīkuṭilaṃ ghoraṃ raktavṛttekṣaṇatrayam || 24 ||

daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ durddharṣaṃ sphuritādharapallavam |
uttaraṃ vidrumaprakhyaṃ nīlālakavibhūṣitam || 25 ||

savilāsaṃ trinayanaṃ candrābharaṇaśekharam |
paścimaṃ pūrṇacandrābhaṃ locanatritayojjvalam || 26 ||

candrarekhādharaṃ saumyaṃ mandasmitamanoharam |
paṃcamaṃ sphaṭikaprakhyamindurekhāsamujjvalam || 27 ||

atīva saumyamutphullalocanatritayojjvalam |
dakṣiṇe śūlaparaśuvajrakhaḍgānalojjvalam || 28 ||

savye ca nāganārācaghaṇṭāpāśāṃkuśojjvalam |
nivṛttyājānusaṃbaddhamānābheśca pratiṣṭhayā || 29 ||

ākaṃṭhaṃ vidyayā tadvadālalāṭaṃ tu śāntayā |
tadūrddhvaṃ śāntyatītākhyakalayā parayā tathā || 30 ||

paṃcādhvavyāpinaṃ sākṣātkalāpaṃcakavigraham |
īśānamukuṭaṃ devaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ purātanam || 31 ||

aghorahṛdayaṃ tadvadvāmaguhyaṃ maheśvaram |
sadyapādaṃ ca tanmūrtimaṣṭatriṃśatkalāmayam || 32 ||

mātṛkāmayamīśānaṃ paṃcabrahmamayaṃ tathā |
.okārākhyamayaṃ caiva haṃsaśaktyā samanvitam || 33 ||

tathecchātmikayā śaktyā samārūḍhāṃkamaṃḍalam |
jñānākhyayā dakṣiṇato vāmataśca kriyākhyayā || 34 ||

tattvatrayamayaṃ sākṣādvidyāmūrtiṃ sadāśivam |
mūrtimūlena saṃkalpya sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt || 35 ||

saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyamarghāntaṃ mūlavidyayā |
mūrtimantaṃ śivaṃ sākṣācchaktyā paramayā saha || 36 ||

tatrāvāhya mahādevaṃ sadasadvyaktivarjitam |
paṃcopakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pūjayetparameśvaram || 37 ||

brahmabhiśca ṣaḍaGgaiśca tato mātṛkayā saha |
praṇavena śivenaiva śaktiyuktena ca kramāt || 38 ||

śāntena vā tathānyaiśca vedamantraiśca kṛtsnaśaḥ |
pūjayetparamaṃ devaṃ kevalena śivena vā || 39 ||

pādyādimukhavāsāntaṃ kṛtvā prasthāpanaṃ vinā |
paṃcāvaraṇapūjāṃ tu hyārabheta yathākramam || 40 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe kāmyakarmavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśattamo .adhyāyaḥ || 29 ||

tatrādau śivayoḥ pārśve dakṣiṇe vāmataḥ kramāt |
gandhādyairarcayetpūrvaṃ devau heraṃbaṣaṇmukhau || 1 ||

tato brahmāṇi parita īśānādi yathākramam |
saśaktikāni sadyāntaṃ prathamāvaraṇe yajet || 2 ||

ṣaḍaṃgānyapi tatraiva hṛdayādīnyanukramāt |
śivasya ca śivāyāśca vāhneyādi samarcayet || 3 ||

tatra vāmādikānrudrānaṣṭau vāmādiśaktibhiḥ |
arcayedvā na vā paścātpūrvādiparitaḥ kramāt || 4 ||

prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ mayā te yadunandana |
dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ prītyā procyate śraddhayā śṛṇu || 5 ||

anantaṃ pūrvādikpatre tacchaktiṃ tasya vāmataḥ |
sūkṣmaṃ dakṣiṇadikpatre saha śaktyā samarcayet || 6 ||

tataḥ paścimadikpatre saha śaktyā śivottamam |
tathaivottaradikpatre caikanetraṃ samarcayet || 7 ||

ekarudraṃ ca tacchaktiṃ paścādīśadale .arcayet |
trimūrtiṃ tasya śaktiṃ ca pūjayedagnidigdale || 8 ||

śrīkaṇṭhaṃ nairṛte patre tacchaktiṃ tasya vāmataḥ |
tathaiva mārute patre śikhaṃḍīśaṃ samarcayet || 9 ||

dvitīyāvaraṇe cejyāssarvartaścakravarttinaḥ |
tṛtīyāvaraṇe pūjyāḥ śaktibhiścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ || 10 ||

aṣṭasu kramaśo dikṣu pūrvādiparitaḥ kramāt |
bhavaḥ śarvastatheśāno rudraḥ paśupatistataḥ || 11 ||

ugro bhīmo mahādeva ityaṣṭau mūrtayaḥ kramāt |
anantaraṃ tataścaiva mahādevādayaḥ kramāt |
śaktibhissaha saṃpūjyāstatraikādaśamūrttayaḥ // 12 || 12 ||

mahādevaḥ śivo rudraḥ śaṃkaro nīlalohitaḥ |
īśāno vijayo bhīmo devadevo bhavodbhavaḥ || 13 ||

kapardīśaśca kathyante tathaikādaśaśaktayaḥ |
tatrāṣṭau prathamaṃ pūjyāḥ vāhneyādi yathākramam || 14 ||

devadevaḥ pūrvapatre īśānaṃ cāgnigocare |
bhavodbhavastayormadhye kapālīśastataḥ param || 15 ||

tasminnāvaraṇe bhūyo vṛṣendraṃ purato yajet |
nandinaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya mahākālaṃ tathottare || 16 ||

śāstāraṃ vahnidikpatre mātR̥rdakṣiṇadigdale |
gajāsyaṃ nairṛte patre ṣaṇmukhaṃ vāruṇe punaḥ || 17 ||

jyeṣṭhāṃ vāyudale gaurīmuttare caṃḍamaiśvare |
śāstṛnandīśayormadhye munīndraṃ vṛṣabhaṃ yajet || 18 ||

mahākālasyottarataḥ piṃgalaṃ tu samarcayet |
śāstṛmātṛsamūhasya madhye bhṛṃgīśvaraṃ tataḥ || 19 ||

mātṛvighneśamadhye tu vīrabhadraṃ samarcayet |
skandavighneśayormadhye yajeddevīṃ sarasvatīm || 20 ||

jyeṣṭhākumārayormadhye śriyaṃ śivapadārccitām |
jyeṣṭhāgaṇāmbayormadhye mahāmoṭīṃ samarcayet || 21 ||

gaṇāmbācaṇḍayormadhye devīṃ durgāṃ prapūjayet |
atraivāvaraṇe bhūyaḥ śivānucarasaṃhatim || 22 ||

rudraprathamabhūtākhyāṃ vividhāṃ ca saśaktikām |
śivāyāśca sakhīvarggaṃ japeddhyātvā samāhitaḥ || 23 ||

evaṃ tṛtīyāvaraṇe vitate pūjite sati |
caturthāvaraṇaṃ dhyātvā bahistasya samarccayet || 24 ||

bhānuḥ pūrvadale pūjyo dakṣiṇe caturānanaḥ |
rudro varuṇadikpatre viṣṇuruttaradigdale || 25 ||

caturṇāmapi devānāṃ pṛthagāvaraṇānyatha |
tasyāṃgāni ṣaḍevādau dīptādyābhiśca śaktibhiḥ || 26 ||

dīptā sūkṣmā jayā bhadrā vibhūtirvimalā kramāt |
amoghā vidyutā caiva pūrvādi paritaḥ sthitāḥ || 27 ||

dvitīyāvaraṇe pūjyāścatasro mūrtayaḥ kramāt |
pūrvādyuttaraparyantāḥ śaktayaśca tataḥ param || 28 ||

ādityo bhāskaro bhānū raviścetyanupūrvaśaḥ |
arko brahmā tathā rudro viṣṇuścaite vivasvataḥ || 29 ||

vistārā pūrvadigbhāge sutarāṃ dakṣiṇe sthitāḥ |
bodhanī paścime bhāge āpyāyinyuttare punaḥ || 30 ||

uṣāṃ prabhāṃ tathā prājñāṃ sandhyāmapi tataḥ param |
aiśānādiṣu vinyasya dvitīyāvaraṇe yajet || 31 ||

somamaṃgārakaṃ caiva budhaṃ buddhimatāṃ varam |
bṛhaspatiṃ bṛhadbuddhiṃ bhārgavaṃ tejasāṃ nidhim || 32 ||

śanaiścaraṃ tathā rāhuṃ ketuṃ dhūmraṃ bhayaṃkaram |
samantato yajedetāṃstṛtīyāvaraṇe kramāt || 33 ||

athavā dvādaśādityā dvitīyāvaraṇe yajet |
tṛtīyāvaraṇe caiva rāśīndvādaśa pūjayet || 34 ||

saptasapta gaṇāṃścaiva bahistasya samantataḥ |
ṛṣīndevāṃśca gandharvānpannagānapsarogaṇān || 35 ||

grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣānyātudhānāṃstathā hayān |
saptacchandomayāṃścaiva vālakhilyāṃśca pūjayet || 36 ||

evaṃ tṛtīyāvaraṇe samabhyarcya divākaram |
brahmāṇamarcayetpaścāttribhirāvaraṇaiḥ sahaḥ || 37 ||

hiraṇyagarbhaṃ pūrvasyāṃ virājaṃ dakṣiṇe tataḥ |
kālaṃ paścimadigbhāge puruṣaṃ cottare yajet || 38 ||

hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prathamo brahmā kamalasannibhaḥ |
kālo jātyaṃjanaprakhyaḥ puruṣaḥ sphaṭikopamaḥ || 39 ||

triguṇo rājasaścaiva tāmasaḥ sāttvikastathā |
catvāra ete kramaśaḥ prathamāvaraṇe sthitāḥ || 40 ||

dvitīyāvaraṇe pūjyāḥ pūrvādiparitaḥ kramāt |
sanatkumāraḥ sanakaḥ sanandaśca sanātanaḥ || 41 ||

tṛtīyāvaraṇe paścādarcayecca prajāpatīn |
aṣṭau pūrvāṃśca pūrvvādau trīnprākpaścādanukramāt || 42 ||

dakṣo rucirbhṛguścaiva marīciśca tathāṃgirāḥ |
pulastyaḥ pulahaścaiva kraturatriśca kaśyapaḥ || 43 ||

vasiṣṭhaśceti vikhyātāḥ prajānāṃ patayastvime |
teṣāṃ bhāryyāśca taissārddhaṃ pūjanīyā yathākramam || 44 ||

prasūtiśca tathā .a.akūtiḥ khyātiḥ sambhūtireva ca |
dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ kṣamā caiva sannatiścānasūyakā || 45 ||

devamātārundhatī ca sarvāḥ khalu pativratāḥ |
śivārcanarato nityaṃ śrīmatyaḥ priyadarśanāḥ || 46 ||

prathamāvaraṇe vedāṃścaturo vā prapūjayet |
itihāsapurāṇāni dvitīyāvaraṇe punaḥ || 47 ||

tṛtīyāvaraṇe paścāddharmaśāstrapurassarāḥ |
vaidikyo nikhilā vidyāḥ pūjyā eva samantataḥ || 48 ||

pūrvādipurato vedāstadanye tu yathāruci |
aṣṭadhā vā caturdhā vā kṛtvā pūjāṃ samantataḥ || 49 ||

evaṃ brahmāṇamabhyarcya tribhirāvaraṇairyutam |
dakṣiṇe paścime paścādrudraṃ sāvaraṇaṃ yajet || 50 ||

tasya brahmaṣaḍaṃgāni prathamāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam |
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva vidyeśvaramayaṃ tathā || 51 ||

tṛtīyāvaraṇe bhedo vidyate sa tu kathyate |
catasro mūrtayastasya pūjyāḥ pūrvāditaḥ kramāt || 52 ||

triguṇāssakalo devaḥ purastācchivasaṃjñakaḥ |
rājaso dakṣiṇe brahmā sṛṣṭikṛtpūjyate bhavaḥ || 53 ||

tāmasaḥ paścime cāgniḥ pūjyassaṃhārako haraḥ |
sāttvikassukhakṛtsaumye viṣṇurviśvapatirmṛḍaḥ || 54 ||

evaṃ paścimadigbhāge śambhoḥ ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ śivam |
samabhyarcyottare pārśve tato vaikuṃṭhamarcayet || 55 ||

vāsudevaṃ puraskṛtvā prathamāvaraṇe yajet |
aniruddhaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pradyumnaṃ paścime tataḥ || 56 ||

saumye saṃkarṣaṇaṃ paścādvyatyastau vā yajedimau |
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śubham || 57 ||

matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca narasiṃhotha vāmanaḥ |
rāmaścānyatamaḥ kṛṣṇo bhavānaśvamukhopi ca || 58 ||

tṛtīyāvaraṇe cakruḥ pūrvabhāge samarcayet |
nārāyaṇākhyāṃ yāmyestraṃ kvacidavyāhataṃ yajet || 59 ||

paścime pāṃcajanyaṃ ca śārGgandhanurathottare |
evaṃ tryāvaraṇaiḥ sākṣādviśvākhyāṃ paramaṃ harim || 60 ||

mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāviṣṇuṃ mūrtīkṛtya samarcayet |
itthaṃ viṣṇoścaturvyūhakramānmūrticatuṣṭayam |
pūjayitvā ca tacchaktīścatasraḥ pujayetkramāt // 61 || 61 ||

prabhāmāgneyadigbhāge nairṛte tu sarasvatīm |
gaṇāṃbikā ca vāyavye lakṣmīṃ raudre samarcayet || 62 ||

evaṃ bhānvādimūrttīnāṃ tacchaktīnāmanantaram |
pūjāṃ vidhāya lokeśāṃstatraivāvaraṇe yajet || 63 ||

indramagniṃ yamaṃ caiva nirṛtiṃ varuṇaṃ tathā |
vāyuṃ somaṃ kuberaṃ ca paścādīśānamarcayet || 64 ||

evaṃ caturthāvaraṇaṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ |
āyudhāni maheśasya paścādbāṃhyaṃ samarcayet || 65 ||

śrīmantriśūlamaiśāne vajraṃ māhendradiGmukhe |
paraśuṃ vahnidigbhāge yāmye sāyakamarcayet || 66 ||

nairṛte tu yajetkhaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ vāruṇagocare |
aṃkuśaṃ mārute bhāge pinākaṃ cottare yajet || 67 ||

paścimābhimukhaṃ raudraṃ kṣetrapālaṃ samarcayet |
pañcamāvaraṇaṃ caiva sampūjyānantaraṃ bahiḥ || 68 ||

sarvāvaraṇadevānāṃ bahirvā pañcame .athavā |
pañcame mātṛbhissārddhaṃ mahokṣa purato yajet || 69 ||

tataḥ samantataḥ pūjyāssarvā vai devayonayaḥ |
khecarā ṛṣayassiddhā daityā yakṣāśca rākṣasāḥ || 70 ||

anantādyāśca nāgendrā nāgaistattatkulodbhavaiḥ |
ḍākinībhūtavetālapretabhairavanāyakāḥ || 71 ||

pātālavāsinaścānye nānāyonisamudbhavāḥ |
nadyassamudrā girayaḥ kānanāni sarāṃsi ca || 72 ||

paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo vṛkṣāḥ kīṭādyāḥ kṣudrayonayaḥ |
narāśca vividhākārā mṛgāśca kṣudrayonayaḥ || 73 ||

bhuvanānyantaraṇḍasya tato brahmāṇḍakoṭayaḥ |
bahiraṃḍānyasaṃkhyāni bhuvanāni sahādhipaiḥ || 74 ||

brahmāṃḍādhārakā rudrā daśadikṣu vyavasthitāḥ |
yadgauḍa yacca māmeyaṃ yadvā śāktaṃ tataḥ param || 75 ||

yatkiñcidasti śabdasya vācyaṃ cidacidātmakam |
tatsarvaṃ śivayoḥ pārśve buddhvā sāmānyato yajet || 76 ||

kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve .aciṃtyāḥ smitamukhāstathā |
prītyā saṃprekṣamāṇāśca devaṃ devīṃ ca sarvadā || 77 ||

itthamāvaraṇābhyarcāṃ kṛtvāvikṣepaśāntaye |
punarabhyarcya deveśaṃ paktvākṣaramudīrayet || 78 ||

nivedayettataḥ paścācchivayoramṛtopamam |
suvyañjanasamāyuktaṃ śuddhaṃ cāru mahācarum || 79 ||

dvātriṃśadāḍhakairmukhyamadhamaṃ tvāḍhakāvaram |
sādhayitvā yathāsaṃpacchraddhayā vinivedayet || 80 ||

tato nivedya pānīyaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ copadaṃśakaiḥ |
nīrājanādikaṃ kṛtvā pūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet || 81 ||

bhogopayogyadravyāṇi viśiṣṭānyeva sādhayet |
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta bhaktimānvibhave sati || 82 ||

śaṭhasyopekṣakasyāpi vyaṃgyaṃ caivānutiṣṭhataḥ |
na phalantyeva karmāṇi kāmyānīti satāṃ kathā || 83 ||

tasmātsamyagupekṣāṃ ca tyaktvā sarvāṃgayogataḥ |
kuryātkāmyāni karmāṇi phalasiddhiṃ yadīcchati || 84 ||

itthaṃ pūjāṃ samāpyātha devaṃ devīṃ praṇamya ca |
bhaktyā manassamādhāya paścātstotramudīrayet || 85 ||

tataḥ stotramupāsyānte tvaṣṭottaraśatāvarām |
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ sahasrottaramutsukaḥ || 86 ||

vidyāpūjāṃ guroḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā paścādyathākramam |
yathodayaṃ yathāśrāddhaṃ sadasyānapi pūjayet || 87 ||

tataḥ udvāsya deveśaṃ sarvairāvaraṇaiḥ saha |
maṇḍalaṃ gurave dadyādyāgopakaraṇaissaha || 88 ||

śivāśritebhyo vā dadyātsarvamevānupūrvaśaḥ |
athavā tacchivāyaiva śivakṣetre samarpayet || 89 ||

śivāgnau vā yajeddevaṃ homadravyaiśca saptabhiḥ |
samabhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ sarvāvaraṇadevatāḥ || 90 ||

eṣa yogeśvaro nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ |
na tasmādadhikaḥ kaścidyāgo .asti bhuvane kvacit || 91 ||

na tadasti jagatyasminnasadhyaṃ yadanena tu |
aihikaṃ vā phalaṃ kiṃcidāmuṣmikaphalaṃ tu vā || 92 ||

idamasya phalaṃ nedamiti naiva niyamyate |
śreyorūpasya kṛtsnasya tadidaṃ śreṣṭasādhanam || 93 ||

idaṃ na śakyate vaktuṃ puruṣeṇa yadarcyate |
ciṃtāmaṇerivaitasmāttattena prāpyate phalam || 94 ||

tathāpi kṣudramuddiśya phalaṃ naitatprayojayet |
laghvarthī mahato yasmātsvayaṃ laghutaro bhavet || 95 ||

mahadvā phalamalpaṃ vā kṛtaṃ cetkarma sidhyati |
mahādevaṃ samuddiśya kṛtaṃ karma prayujyatām || 96 ||

tasmādananyalabhyeṣu śatrumṛtyuṃjayādiṣu |
phaleṣu dṛṣṭādṛṣṭeṣu kuryyādetadvicakṣaṇaḥ || 97 ||

mahatsvapi ca pāteṣu mahārāgabhayādiṣu |
durbhikṣādiṣu śāntyarthaṃ śāntiṃ kuryyādanena tu || 98 ||

bahunā kiṃ pralāpena mahāvyāpannivārakam |
ātmīyamastraṃ śaivānāmidamāha maheśvaraḥ || 99 ||

tasmāditaḥ paraṃ nāsti paritrāṇamihātmanaḥ |
iti matvā prayuṃjānaḥ karmedaṃ śubhamaśnute || 100 ||

stotramātraṃ śucirbhūtvā yaḥ paṭhetsusamāhitaḥ |
sopyabhīṣṭatamādarthādaṣṭāṃśaphalamāpnuyāt || 101 ||

arthaṃ tasyānusandhāya parvaṇyanaśanaḥ paṭhet |
aṣṭābhyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ phalamarddhaṃ samāpnuyāt || 102 ||

yastvarthamanusaṃdhāya parvādiṣu tathā vratī |
māsamekaṃ japetstotraṃ sa kṛtsnaṃ phalamāpnuyāt || 103 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śaivānāṃ kāmyakavarṇanaṃ nāma triṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 30 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

stotraṃ vakṣyāmi te kṛṣṇa paṃcāvaraṇamārgataḥ |
yogeśvaramidaṃ puṇyaṃ karma yena samāpyate || 1 ||

jaya jaya jagadekanātha śaṃbho prakṛtimanohara nityacitsvabhāva |
atigatakaluṣaprapañcavācāmapi manasāṃ padavīmatītatattvam || 2 ||

svabhāvanirmalābhoga jaya sundaraceṣṭita |
svātmatulyamahāśakte jaya śuddhaguṇārṇava || 3 ||

anantakāntisaṃpanna jayāsadṛśavigraha |
atarkyamahimādhāra jayānākulamaṃgala || 4 ||

niraṃjana nirādhāra jaya niṣkāraṇodaya |
nirantaraparānanda jaya nirvṛtikāraṇa || 5 ||

jayātiparamaiśvarya jayātikaruṇāspada |
jaya svatantrasarvasva jayāsadṛśavaibhava || 6 ||

jayāvṛtamahāviśva jayānāvṛta kenacit |
jayottara samastasya jayātyantaniruttara || 7 ||

jayādbhuta jayākṣudra jayākṣata jayāvyaya |
jayāmeya jayāmāya jayābhāva jayāmala || 8 ||

mahābhuja mahāsāra mahāguṇa mahākatha |
mahābala mahāmāya mahārasa mahāratha || 9 ||

namaḥ paramadevāya namaḥ paramahetave |
namaśśivāya śāntāya namaśśivatarāya te || 10 ||

tvadadhīnamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagaddhi sasurāsuram |

atastvadvihitāmājñāṃ kṣamate ko .ativartitum |

ayaṃ punarjano nityaṃ bhavadekasamāśrayaḥ |
bhavānato .anugṛhyāsmai prārthitaṃ saṃprayacchatu || 13 ||

jayāṃbike jaganmātarjaya sarvajaganmayi |
jayānavadhikaiśvarye jayānupamavigrahe || 14 ||

jaya vāGmanasātīte jayāciddhvāntabhaṃjike |
jaya janmajarāhīne jaya kālottarottare || 15 ||

jayānekavidhānasthe jaya viśveśvarapriye |
jaya viśvasurārādhye jaya viśvavijṛṃbhiṇi || 16 ||

jaya maṃgaladivyāṃgi jaya maṃgaladīpike |
jaya maṃgalacāritre jaya maṃgaladāyini || 17 ||

namaḥ paramakalyāṇaguṇasaṃcayamūrtaye |
tvattaḥ khalu samutpannaṃ jagattvayyeva līyate || 18 ||

tvadvinātaḥ phalaṃ dātumīśvaropi na śaknuyāt |
janmaprabhṛti deveśi janoyaṃ tvadupāśritaḥ || 19 ||

ato .asya tava bhaktasya nirvartaya manoratham |
paṃcavaktro daśabhujaḥ śuddhasphaṭikasannibhaḥ || 20 ||

varṇabrahmakalādeho devassakalaniṣkalaḥ |
śivabhaktisamārūḍhaḥ śāntyatītassadāśivaḥ |
bhaktyā mayārcito mahyaṃ prārthitaṃ śaṃ prayacchatu // 21 || 21 ||

sadāśivāṃkamārūḍhā śaktiricchā śivāhvayā |
jananī sarvalokānāṃ prayacchatu manoratham || 22 ||

śivayordayitā putrau devau heraṃbaṣaṇmukhau |
śivānubhāvau sarvajñau śivajñānāmṛtāśinau || 23 ||

tṛptau parasparaṃ snigdhau śivābhyāṃ nityasatkṛtau |
satkṛtau ca sadā devau brahmādyaistridaśairapi || 24 ||

sarvalokaparitrāṇaṃ kartumabhyuditau sadā |
svecchāvatāraṃ kurvantau svāṃśabhedairanekaśaḥ || 25 ||

tāvimau śivayoḥ pārśve nityamitthaṃ mayārcitau |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya prārthitaṃ me prayacchatām || 26 ||

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśamīśānākhyaṃ sadāśivam |
mūrddhābhimāninī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 27 ||

śivārcanarataṃ śāntaṃ śāntyatītaṃ makhāsthitam |
paṃcākṣarāntimaṃ bījaṃ kalābhiḥ paṃcabhiryutam || 28 ||

prathamāvaraṇe pūrvaṃ śaktyā saha samarcitam |
pavitraṃ paramaṃ brahma prārthitaṃ me prayacchatu || 29 ||

bālasūryapratīkāśaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ purātanam |
pūrvavaktrābhimānaṃ ca śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ || 30 ||

śāntyātmakaṃ marutsaṃsthaṃ śambhoḥ pādārcane ratam |
prathamaṃ śivabījeṣu kalāsu ca catuṣkalam || 31 ||

pūrvabhāge mayā bhaktyā śaktyā saha samarcitam |
pavitraṃ paramaṃ brahma prārthitaṃ me prayacchatu || 32 ||

añjanādipratīkāśamaghoraṃ ghoravigraham |
devasya dakṣiṇaṃ vaktraṃ devadevapadārcakam || 33 ||

vidyāpādaṃ samārūḍhaṃ vahnimaṇḍalamadhyagam |
dvitīyaṃ śivabījeṣu kalāsvaṣṭakalānvitam || 34 ||

śaṃbhordakṣiṇadigbhāge śaktyā saha samarcitam |
pavitraṃ madhyamaṃ brahma prārthitaṃ me prayacchatu || 35 ||

kuṃkumakṣodasaṃkāśaṃ vāmākhyaṃ varaveṣadhṛk |
vaktramuttaramīśasya pratiṣṭhāyāṃ pratiṣṭhitam || 36 ||

vārimaṃḍalamadhyasthaṃ mahādevārcane ratam |
turīyaṃ śivabījeṣu trayodaśakalānvitam || 37 ||

devasyottaradigbhāge śaktyā saha samarcitam |
pavitraṃ paramaṃ brahma prārthitaṃ me prayacchatu || 38 ||

śaṃkhakundendudhavalaṃ sandhyākhyaṃ saumyalakṣaṇam |
śivasya paścimaṃ vaktraṃ śivapādārcane ratam || 39 ||

nivṛttipadaniṣṭhaṃ ca pṛthivyāṃ samavasthitam |
tṛtīyaṃ śivabījeṣu kalābhiścāṣṭabhiryutam || 40 ||

devasya paścime bhāge śaktyā saha samarcitam |
pavitraṃ paramaṃ brahma prārthitaṃ me prayacchatu || 41 ||

śivasya tu śivāyāśca hṛnmūrtiśivabhāvite |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya te me kāmaṃ prayacchatām || 42 ||

śivasya ca śivāyāśca śikhāmūrtiśivāśrite |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ prayacchatām || 43 ||

śivasya ca śivāyāśca varmaṇā śivabhāvite |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ prayacchatām || 44 ||

śivasya ca śivāyāśca netramūrtiśivāśrite |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ prayacchatām || 45 ||

astramūrtī ca śivayornityamarcanatatpare |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ prayacchatām || 46 ||

vāmau jyeṣṭhastathā rudraḥ kālo vikaraṇastathā |
balo vikaraṇaścaiva balapramathanaḥ paraḥ || 47 ||

sarvabhūtasya damanastādṛśāścāṣṭaśaktayaḥ |
prārthitaṃ me prayacchantu śivayoreva śāsanāt || 48 ||

athānantaśca sūkṣmaśca śivaścāpyekanetrakaḥ |
eka rudrākhyamartiśca śrīkaṇṭhaśca śikhaṃḍakaḥ || 49 ||

tathāṣṭau śaktayasteṣāṃ dvitīyāvaraṇe .arcitāḥ |
te me kāmaṃ prayacchantu śivayoreva śāsanāt || 50 ||

bhavādyā mūrtayaścāṣṭau tāsāmapi ca śaktayaḥ |
mahādevādayaścānye tathaikādaśamūrtayaḥ || 51 ||

śaktibhissahitāssarve tṛtīyāvaraṇe sthitāḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ diśantu phalamīpsitam || 52 ||

vṛkṣarājo mahātejā mahāmeghasamasvanaḥ |
merumandarakailāsahimādriśikharopamaḥ || 53 ||

sitābhraśikharākāraḥ kakudā pariśobhitaḥ |
mahābhogīndrakalpena vālena ca virājitaḥ || 54 ||

raktāsyaśṛṃgacaraṇau raktaprāyavilocanaḥ |
pīvaronnatasarvāṃgassucārugamanojjvalaḥ || 55 ||

praśastalakṣaṇaḥ śrīmānprajvalanmaṇibhūṣaṇaḥ |
śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivayordhvajavāhanaḥ || 56 ||

tathā taccaraṇanyāsapāvitāparavigrahaḥ |
gorājapuruṣaḥ śrīmāñchrīmacchūlavarāyudhaḥ |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu // 57 || 57 ||

nandīśvaro mahātejā nagendratanayātmajaḥ |
sanārāyaṇakairdevairnityamabhyarcya vanditaḥ || 58 ||

śarvasyāntaḥpuradvāri sārddhaṃ parijanaiḥ sthitaḥ |
sarveśvarasamaprakhyassarvāsuravimardanaḥ || 59 ||

sarveṣāṃ śivadharmāṇāmadhyakṣatve .abhiṣecitaḥ |
śivapriyaśśivāsaktaśśrīmacchūlavarāyudhaḥ || 60 ||

śivāśriteṣu saṃsaktastvanuraktaśca tairapi |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu || 61 ||

mahākālo mahābāhurmahādeva ivāparaḥ |
mahādevāśritānāṃ tu nityamevābhirakṣatu || 62 ||

śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaśśivayorarcakassadā |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 63 ||

sarvaśāstrārthatattvajñaḥ śāstā viṣṇoḥ parā tanuḥ |
mahāmohātmatanayo madhumāṃsāsavapriyaḥ |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu // 64 || 64 ||

brahmāṇī caiva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā |
vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṃḍā caṃḍavikramā || 65 ||

etā vai mātaraḥ sapta sarvalokasya mātaraḥ |
prārthitaṃ me prayacchantu parameśvaraśāsanāt || 66 ||

mattamātaṃgavadano gaṃgomāśaṃkarātmajaḥ |
ākāśadeho digbāhussomasūryāgnilocanaḥ || 67 ||

airāvatādibhirdivyairdiggajairnityamarcitaḥ |
śivajñānamadodbhinnarstridaśānāmavighnakṛt || 68 ||

vighnakṛccāsurādīnāṃ vighneśaḥ śivabhāvitaḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 69 ||

ṣaṇmukhaśśivasambhūtaḥ śaktivajradharaḥ prabhuḥ |
agneśca tanayo devo hyaparṇātanayaḥ punaḥ || 70 ||

gaṃgāyāśca gaṇāṃbāyāḥ kṛttikānāṃ tathaiva ca |
viśākhena ca śākhena naigameyena cāvṛtaḥ || 71 ||

indrajiccandrasenānīstārakāsurajittathā |
śailānāṃ merumukhyānāṃ vedhakaśca svatejasā || 72 ||

taptacāmīkaraprakhyaḥ śatapatradalekṣaṇaḥ |
kumārassukumārāṇāṃ rūpodāharaṇaṃ mahat || 73 ||

śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapadārcakassadā |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 74 ||

jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā varadā śivayoryajaneratā |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 75 ||

trailokyavanditā sākṣādulkākārā gaṇāṃbikā |
jagatsṛṣṭivivṛddhyarthaṃ brahmaṇā .abhyarthitā śivāt || 76 ||

śivāyāḥ pravibhaktāyā bhruvorantaranissṛtāḥ |
dakṣāyaṇī satī menā tathā haimavatī hyumā || 77 ||

kauśikyāścaiva jananī bhadrakālyāstathaiva ca |
aparṇāyāśca jananī pāṭalāyāstathaiva ca || 78 ||

śivārcanaratā nityaṃ rudrāṇī rudravallabhā |
satkṛṭya śivayorājñāṃ sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 79 ||

caṃḍaḥ sarvagaṇeśānaḥ śaṃbhorvadanasaṃbhavaḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 80 ||

piṃgalo gaṇapaḥ śrīmāñchivāsaktaḥ śivapriyaḥ |
ājñayā śivayoreva sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu || 81 ||

bhṛṃgīśo nāma gaṇapaḥ śivarādhanatatparaḥ |
prayacchatu sa me kāmaṃ patyurājñā puraḥsaram || 82 ||

vīrabhadro mahātejā himakundendusannibhaḥ |
bhadrakālīpriyo nityaṃ mātR̥ṇāṃ cābhirakṣitā || 83 ||

yajñasya ca śirohartā dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ |
upendrendrayamādīnāṃ devānāmaṃgatakṣakaḥ || 84 ||

śivasyānucaraḥ śrīmāñchivaśāsanapālakaḥ |
śivayoḥ śāsanādeva sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 85 ||

sarasvatī maheśasya vāksarojasamudbhavā |
śivayoḥ pūjane saktā sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 86 ||

viṣṇorvakṣaḥsthitā lakṣmīḥ śivayoḥ pūjane ratā |
śivayoḥ śāsanādeva sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 87 ||

mahāmoṭī mahādevyāḥ pādapūjāparāyaṇā |
tasyā eva niyogena sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 88 ||

kauśikī siṃhamārūḍhā pārvatyāḥ paramā sutā |
viṣṇornidrāmahāmāyā mahāmahiṣamardinī || 89 ||

niśaṃbhaśuṃbhasaṃhatrī madhumāṃsāsavapriyā |
satkṛtya śāsanaṃ mātussā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam || 90 ||

rudrā rudrasamaprakhyāḥ prathamāḥ prathitaujasaḥ |
bhūtākhyāśca mahāvīryyā mahādevasamaprabhāḥ || 91 ||

nityamuktā nirupamā nirdvandvā nirupaplavāḥ |
saśaktayassānucarāssarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ || 92 ||

sarveṣāmeva lokānāṃ sṛṣṭisaṃharaṇakṣamāḥ |
parasparānuraktāśca parasparamanuvratāḥ || 93 ||

parasparamatisnigdhāḥ parasparanamaskṛtāḥ |
śivapriyatamā nityaṃ śivalakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ || 94 ||

saumyādhārāstathā miśrāścāntarāladvayātmikāḥ |
virūpāśca surūpāśca nānārūpadharāstathā || 95 ||

satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ diśantu vai |
devyā priyasakhīvargo devīlakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ || 96 ||

sahito rudrakanyābhiḥ śaktibhiścāpyanekaśaḥ |
tṛtīyāvaraṇe śaṃbhorbhaktyā nityaṃ samarcitaḥ || 97 ||

satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam |
divākaro maheśasya mūrtirdīptisumaṃḍalaḥ || 98 ||

nirguṇo guṇasaṃkīrṇastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ |
avikārātmakaścādya ekassāmānyavikriyaḥ || 99 ||

asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt |
evaṃ tridhā caturddhā ca vibhaktāḥ paṃcadhā punaḥ || 100 ||

caturthāvaraṇe śaṃbhoḥ pūjitaścānugaiḥ saha |
śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ || 101 ||

satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam |
divākaraṣaḍaṃgāni dīptādyāścāṣṭaśaktayaḥ || 102 ||

ādityo bhāskaro bhānū raviścetyanupūrvaśaḥ |
arko brahmā tathā rudro viṣṇuścādityamūrtayaḥ || 103 ||

vistarāsutarābodhinyāpyāyinyaparāḥ punaḥ |
uṣā prabhā tathā prājñā sandhyā cetyapi śaktayaḥ || 104 ||

somādiketuparyantā grahāśca śivabhāvitāḥ |
śivayorājñayānunnā maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me || 105 ||

athavā dvādaśādityāstathā dvādaśa śaktayaḥ |
ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ || 106 ||

grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā rākṣasāścāsurāstathā |
saptasaptagaṇāścaite saptacchandomayā hayāḥ || 107 ||

vālakhilyā dayaścaiva sarve śivapadārcakāḥ |
satkṛtyaśivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me || 108 ||

brahmātha devadevasya mūrtirbhūmaṇḍalādhipaḥ |
catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaiśvaryo buddhitattve pratiṣṭhitaḥ || 109 ||

nirguṇo guṇasaṃkīrṇastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ |
avikārātmako devastatassādhāraṇaḥ puraḥ || 110 ||

asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt |
bhuvaṃ tridhā caturddhā ca vibhaktaḥ paṃcadhā punaḥ || 111 ||

caturthāvaraṇe śaṃbho pūjitaśca sahānugaiḥ |
śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaśśivapādārcane rataḥ || 112 ||

satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam |
hiraṇyagarbho lokeśo virāṭ kālaśca pūruṣaḥ || 113 ||

sanatkumāraḥ sanakaḥ sanandaśca sanātanaḥ |
prajānāṃ patayaścaiva dakṣādyā brahmasūnavaḥ || 114 ||

ekādaśa sapatnīkā dharmassaṃkalpa eva ca |
śivārcanaratāścaite śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ || 115 ||

śivājñāvaśagāssarve diśantu mama maṃgalam |
catvāraśca tathā vedāssetihāsapurāṇakāḥ || 116 ||

dharmaśāstrāṇi vidyābhirvaidikībhissamanvitāḥ |
parasparaviruddhārthāḥ śivaprakṛtipādakāḥ || 117 ||

satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me |
atha rudro mahādevaḥ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī || 118 ||

vāhneyamaṇḍalādhīśaḥ pauruṣaiśvaryavānprabhuḥ |
śivābhimānasaṃpanno nirguṇastriguṇātmakaḥ || 119 ||

kevalaṃ sāttvikaścāpi rājasaścaiva tāmasaḥ |
avikārarataḥ pūrvaṃ tatastu samavikriyaḥ || 120 ||

asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭyādikaraṇātpṛthak |
brahmaṇopi śiraśchettā janakastasya tatsutaḥ || 121 ||

janakastanayaścāpi viṣṇorapi niyāmakaḥ |
bodhakaśca tayornityamanugrahakaraḥ prabhuḥ || 122 ||

aṃḍasyāntarbahirvartī rudro lokadvayādhipaḥ |
śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ || 123 ||

śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam |
tasya brahma ṣaḍaṃgāni vidyeśāntaṃ tathāṣṭakam || 124 ||

catvāro mūrtibhedāśca śivapūrvāḥ śivārcakāḥ |
śivo bhavo haraścaiva mṛḍaścaiva tathāparaḥ |
śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me // 125 || 125 ||

atha viṣṇurmaheśasya śivasyaiva parā tanuḥ |
vāritattvādhipaḥ sākṣādavyaktapadasaṃsthitaḥ || 126 ||

nirguṇassattvabahulastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ |
avikārābhimānī ca trisādhāraṇavikriyaḥ || 127 ||

asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭyādikaraṇātpṛthak |
dakṣiṇāṃgabhavenāpi sparddhamānaḥ svayaṃbhuvā || 128 ||

ādyena brahmaṇā sākṣātsṛṣṭaḥ sraṣṭā ca tasya tu |
aṃḍasyāntarbahirvartī viṣṇurlokadvayādhipaḥ || 129 ||

asurāntakaraścakrī śakrasyāpi tathānujaḥ |
prādurbhūtaśca daśadhā bhṛguśāpacchalādiha || 130 ||

bhūbhāranigrahārthāya svecchayāvātarakṣitau |
aprameyabalo māyī māyayā mohayañjagat || 131 ||

mūrtiṃ kṛtvā mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāśiṣṇumathāpi vā |
vaiṣṇavaiḥ pūjito nityaṃ mūrtitrayamayāsane || 132 ||

śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ |
śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam || 133 ||

vāsudevo .aniruddhaśca pradyumnaśca tataḥ paraḥ |
saṃkarṣaṇassamākhyātāścatasro mūrtayo hareḥ || 134 ||

matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca nārasiṃho .atha vāmanaḥ |
rāmatrayaṃ tathā kṛṣṇo viṣṇusturagavaktrakaḥ || 135 ||

cakraṃ nārāyaṇasyāstraṃ pāṃcajanyaṃ ca śārGgakam |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me || 136 ||

prabhā sarasvatī gaurī lakṣmīśca śivabhāvitā |
śivayoḥ śāsanādetā maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me || 137 ||

indro .agniśca yamaścaiva nirṛtirvaruṇastathā |
vāyuḥ somaḥ kuberaśca tatheśānastriśūladhṛk || 138 ||

sarve śivārcanaratāḥ śivasadbhāvabhāvitāḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśantu me || 139 ||

triśūlamatha vajraṃ ca tathā paraśusāyakau / |
khaḍgapāśāṃkuśāścaiva pinākaścāyudhottamaḥ || 140 ||

divyāyudhāni devasya devyāścaitāni nityaśaḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ rakṣāṃ kurvantu me sadā || 141 ||

vṛṣarūpadharo devaḥ saurabheyo mahābalaḥ |
vaḍavākhyānalasparddhāṃ pañcagomātṛbhirvṛtaḥ || 142 ||

vāhanatvamanuprāptastapasā parameśayoḥ |
tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu || 143 ||

nandā sunandā surabhiḥ suśīlā sumanāstathā |
paṃcagomātarastvetāśśivaloke vyavasthitāḥ || 144 ||

śivabhaktiparā nityaṃ śivārcanaparāyaṇāḥ |
śivayoḥ śāsanādeva diśantu mama vāṃchitam || 145 ||

kṣetrapālo mahātejā nīla jīmūtasannibhaḥ |
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaḥ sphuradraktādharojjvalaḥ || 146 ||

raktorddhvamūrddhajaḥ śrīmānbhrukuṭīkuṭilekṣaṇaḥ |
raktavṛttatrinayanaḥ śaśipannagabhūṣaṇaḥ || 147 ||

nagnastriśūlapāśāsikapālodyatapāṇikaḥ |
bhairavo bhairavaiḥ siddhairyoginībhiśca saṃvṛtaḥ || 148 ||

kṣetrekṣetre samāsīnaḥ sthito yo rakṣakassatām |
śivapraṇāmaparamaḥ śivasadbhāvabhāvitaḥ || 149 ||

śivaśritānviśeṣeṇa rakṣanputrānivaurasān |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maGgalam || 150 ||

tālajaGghādayastasya prathamāvaraṇercitāḥ |
satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ catvāraḥ samavantu mām || 151 ||

bhairavādyāśca ye cānye samantāttasya veṣṭitāḥ |
te .api māmanugṛhṇantu śivaśāsanagauravāt || 152 ||

nāradādyāśca munayo divyā devaiśca pūjitāḥ |
sādhyā māgāśca ye devā janalokanivāsinaḥ || 153 ||

vinivṛttādhikārāśca maharlokanivāsinaḥ |
saptarṣayastathānye vai vaimānikaguṇaissaha || 154 ||

sarve śivārcanaratāḥ śivājñāvaśavartinaḥ |
śivayorājñayā mahyaṃ diśantu mama kāṃkṣitam || 155 ||

gandharvādyāḥ piśācāntāścatasro devayonayaḥ |
siddhā vidyādharādyāśca ye .api cānye nabhaścarāḥ || 156 ||

asurā rākṣasāścaiva pātālatalavāsinaḥ |
anantādyāśca nāgendrā vainateyādayo dvijāḥ || 157 ||

kūṣmāṃḍāḥ pretavetālā grahā bhūtagaṇāḥ pare |
ḍākinyaścāpi yoginyaḥ śākinyaścāpi tādṛśāḥ || 158 ||

kṣetrārāmagṛhādīni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca |
dvīpāḥ samudrā nadyaśca nadāścānye sarāṃsi ca || 159 ||

girayaśca sumervādyāḥ kananāni samantataḥ |
paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo vṛkṣāḥ kṛmikīṭādayo mṛgāḥ || 160 ||

bhuvanānyapi sarvāṇi bhuvanānāmadhīśvaraḥ |
aṇḍānyāvaraṇaissārddhaṃ māsāśca daśa diggajāḥ || 161 ||

varṇāḥ padāni mantrāśca tattvānyapi sahādhipaiḥ |
brahmāṃḍadhārakā rudrā rudrāścānye saśaktikāḥ || 162 ||

yacca kiṃcijjagatyasmindṛṣṭaṃ cānumitaṃ śrutam |
sarve kāmaṃ prayacchantu śivayoreva śāsanāt || 163 ||

atha vidyā parā śaivī paśupāśavimocinī |
paṃcārthasaṃjñitā divyā paśuvidyābahiṣkṛtā || 164 ||

śāstraṃ ca śivadharmākhyaṃ dharmākhyaṃ ca taduttaram |
śaivākhyaṃ śivadharmākhyaṃ purāṇaṃ śrutisaṃmitam || 165 ||

śaivāgamāśca ye cānye kāmikādyāścaturvidhāḥ |
śivābhyāmaviśeṣeṇa satkṛtyeha samarcitāḥ || 166 ||

tābhyāmeva samājñātā mamābhipretasiddhaye |
karmedamanumanyantāṃ saphalaṃ sādhvanuṣṭhitam || 167 ||

śvetādyā nakulīśāntāḥ saśiṣyāścāpi deśikāḥ |
tatsantatīyā guravo viśeṣādguravo mama || 168 ||

śaivā māheśvarāścaiva jñānakarmaparāyaṇāḥ |
karmedamanumanyantāṃ saphalaṃ sādhvanuṣṭhitam || 169 ||

laukikā brāhmaṇāssarve kṣatriyāśca viśaḥ kramāt |
vedavedāṃgatattvajñāḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradāḥ || 170 ||

sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikāścaiva yaugā naiyāyikā narāḥ |
saurā brahmāstathā raudrā vaiṣṇavāścāpare narāḥ || 171 ||

śiṣṭāḥ sarve viśiṣṭā ca śivaśāsanayantritāḥ |
karmedamanumanyantāṃ mamābhipretasādhakam || 172 ||

śaivāḥ siddhāntamārgasthāḥ śaivāḥ pāśupatāstathā |
śaivā mahāvratadharāḥ śaivāḥ kāpālikāḥ pare || 173 ||

śivājñāpālakāḥ pūjyā mamāpi śivaśāsanāt |
sarve mamānugṛhṇantu śaṃsantu saphalakriyām || 174 ||

dakṣiṇajñānaniṣṭhāśca dakṣiṇottaramārgagāḥ |
avirodhena vartantāṃ mantraśreyo .arthino mama || 175 ||

nāstikāśca śaṭhāścaiva kṛtaghnāścaiva tāmasāḥ |
pāṣaṃḍāścātipāpāśca vartantāṃ dūrato mama || 176 ||

bahubhiḥ kiṃ stutairatra ye .api ke .apicidāstikāḥ |
sarve māmanugṛhṇantu santaḥ śaṃsantu maṃgalam || 177 ||

namaśśivāya sāṃbāya sasutāyādihetave |
paṃcāvaraṇarūpeṇa prapaṃcenāvṛtāya te || 178 ||

ityuktvā daṃḍavadbhūmau praṇipatya śivaṃ śivām |
japetpaṃcākṣarīṃ vidyāmaṣṭottaraśatāvarām || 179 ||

tathaiva śaktividyāṃ ca japitvā tatsamarpaṇam |
kṛtvā taṃ kṣamayitveśaṃ pūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet || 180 ||

etatpuṇyatamaṃ stotraṃ śivayorhṛdayaṃgamam |
sarvābhīṣṭapradaṃ sākṣādbhuktimuktyaikasādhanam || 181 ||

ya idaṃ kīrtayennityaṃ śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ |
sa vidhūyāśu pāpāni śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 182 ||

goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaśca vīrahā bhrūṇahāpi vā |
śaraṇāgataghātī ca mitraviśraṃbhaghātakaḥ || 183 ||

duṣṭapāpasamācāro mātṛhā pitṛhāpi vā |
stavenānena japtena tattatpāpātpramucyate || 184 ||

duḥsvapnādimahānarthasūcakeṣu bhayeṣu ca |
yadi saṃkīrtayedetanna tato nārthabhāgbhavet || 185 ||

āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ yaccānyadapi vāñchitam |
stotrasyāsya jape tiṣṭhaṃstatsarvaṃ labhate naraḥ || 186 ||

asaṃpūjya śivastotraṃ japātphalamudāhṛtam |
saṃpūjya ca jape tasya phalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate || 187 ||

āstāmiyaṃ phalāvāptirasminsaṃkīrtite sati |
sārddhamaṃbikayā devaḥ śrutyaivaṃ divi tiṣṭhati || 188 ||

tasmānnabhasi saṃpūjya devaṃ devaṃ sahomayā |
kṛtāṃjalipuṭastiṣṭhaṃstotrametadudīrayet || 189 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śivamahāstotravarṇanaṃ nāmaikatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 31 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

etatte kathitaṃ kṛṣṇa karmehāmutra siddhidam |
kriyātapojapadhyānasamuccayamayaṃ param || 1 ||

atha vakṣyāmi śaivānāmihaiva phaladaṃ nṛṇām |
pūjāhomajapadhyānatapodānamayaṃ mahat || 2 ||

tatra saṃsādhayetpūrvaṃ mantraṃ mantrārthavittamaḥ |
dṛṣṭasiddhikaraṃ karma nānyathā phaladaṃ yataḥ || 3 ||

siddhamantro .apyadṛṣṭena prabalena tu kenacit |
pratibandhaphalaṃ karma na kuryātsahasā budhaḥ || 4 ||

tasya tu pratibandhasya kartuṃ śakyeha niṣkṛtiḥ |
parīkṣya śakunādyaistadādau niṣkṛtimācaret || 5 ||

yo .anyathā kurute mohātkarmaihikaphalaṃ naraḥ |
na tena phalabhāksa syātprāpnuyāccopahāsyatām || 6 ||

abisrabdho na kurvīta karma dṛṣṭaphalaṃ kvacit |
sa khalvaśraddhadhānaḥ syānnāśraddhaḥ phalamṛcchati || 7 ||

nāparādhosti devasya karmaṇyapi tu niṣphale |
yathoktakāriṇāṃ puṃsāmihaiva phaladarśanāt || 8 ||

sādhakaḥ siddhamantraśca nirastapratibandhakaḥ |
viśvastaḥ śraddhadhānaśca kurvannāpnoti tatphalam || 9 ||

athavā tatphalāvāptyai brahmacaryarato bhavet |
rātrau haviṣyamaśnīyātpāyasaṃ vā phalāni vā || 10 ||

hiṃsādi yanniṣiddhaṃ syānna kuryānmanasāpi tat |
sadā bhasmānuliptāṃ gassuveṣaśca śucirbhavet || 11 ||

itthamācāravānbhūtvā svānukūle śubhe .ahani |
pūrvoktalakṣaṇe deśe puṣpadāmādyalaṃkṛte || 12 ||

ālipya śakṛtā bhūmiṃ hastamānāvarāṃ yathā |
vilikhetkamale bhadre dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā || 13 ||

taptajāṃbūnadamayamaṣṭapatraṃ sakesaram |
madhye karṇikayā yuktaṃ sarvaratnairalaṃkṛtam || 14 ||

svākārasadṛśenaiva nālena ca samanvitam |
tādṛśe svarṇanirmāṇe kande samyagvidhānataḥ || 15 ||

tatrāṇimādikaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkalpya manasā punaḥ |
ratnajaṃ vātha sauvarṇaṃ sphaṭikaṃ vā salakṣaṇam |
liGgaṃ savedikaṃ caiva sthāpayitvā vidhānataḥ // 16 || 16 ||

tatrāvāhya yajeddevaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam |
tatra māheśvarī kalpyā mūrtirmūrtimataḥ prabhoḥ || 17 ||

caturbhujā caturvaktrā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā |
śārdūlacarmavasanā kiṃcidvihasitānanā || 18 ||

varadābhayahastā ca mṛgaṭaṃkadharā tathā |
atha vāṣṭabhujā ciṃtyā ciṃtakasya yathāruci || 19 ||

tadā triśūlaparaśukhaḍgavajrāṇi dakṣiṇe |
vāme pāśāṃkuśau tadvatkheṭaṃ nāgaṃ ca bibhratī || 20 ||

bālārkasadṛśaprakhyā prativaktraṃ trilocanā |
tasyāḥ pūrvamukhaṃ saumyaṃ svākārasadṛśaprabham || 21 ||

dakṣiṇaṃ nīlajīmūtasadṛśaṃ ghoradarśanam |
uttaraṃ vidrumaprakhyaṃ nīlālakavibhūṣitam || 22 ||

paścimaṃ pūrṇacandrābhaṃ saumyamindukalādharam |
tadaṃkamaṃḍalārūḍhā śaktirmāheśvarī parā || 23 ||

mahālakṣmīriti khyātā śyāmā sarvamanoharā |
mūrtiṃ kṛtvaivamākārāṃ sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt || 24 ||

mūrtimantamathāvāhya yajetparamakāraṇam |
snānārthe kalpayettatra paṃcagavyaṃ tu kāpilam || 25 ||

paṃcāmṛtaṃ ca pūrṇāni bījāni ca viśeṣataḥ |
purastānmaṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā ratnacūrṇādyalaṃkṛtam || 26 ||

karṇikāyāṃ pravinyasyedīśānakalaśaṃ punaḥ |
sadyādikalaśānpaścātparitastasya kalpayet || 27 ||

tato vidyeśakalaśānaṣṭau pūrvādivatkramāt |
tīrthāmbupūritānkṛtvā sūtreṇāveṣṭya pūrvavat || 28 ||

puṇyadravyāṇi nikṣipya samantraṃ savidhānakam |
dukūlādyena vastreṇa samācchādya samantataḥ || 29 ||

sarvatra mantraṃ vinyasya tattanmantrapurassaram |
snānakāle tu saṃprāpte sarvamaGgalanisvanaiḥ || 30 ||

paṃcagavyādibhiścaiva snāpayetparameśvaram |
tataḥ kuśodakādyāni svarṇaratnodakānyapi || 31 ||

gandhapuṣpādisiddhāni mantrasiddhāni ca kramāt |
uddhṛtyoddhṛtya mantreṇa taistaissnāpya maheśvaram || 32 ||

gandhaṃ puṣpādidīpāṃśca pūjākarma samācaret |
palāvaraḥ syādālepa ekādaśapalottaraḥ || 33 ||

suvarṇaratnapuṣpāṇi śubhāni surabhīṇi ca |
nīlotpalādyutpalāni bilvapatrāṇyanekaśaḥ || 34 ||

kamalāni ca raktāni śvetānyapi ca śaṃbhave |
kṛṣṇāgurūdbhavo dhūpaḥ sakarpūrājyaguggulaḥ || 35 ||

kapilāghṛtasaṃsiddhā dīpāḥ karpūravartijāḥ |
paṃcabrahmaṣaḍaṃgāni pūjyānyāvaraṇāni ca || 36 ||

naivedyaḥ payasā siddhaḥ sa guḍājyo mahācaruḥ |
pāṭalotpalapadmādyaiḥ pānīyaṃ ca sugandhitam || 37 ||

paṃcasaugandhikopetaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ ca susaṃskṛtam |
suvarṇaratnasiddhāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ || 38 ||

vāsāṃsi ca vicitrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi ca navāni ca |
darśanīyāni deyāni gānavādyādibhissaha || 39 ||

japaśca mūlamantrasya lakṣaḥ paramasaṃkhyayā |
ekāvarā tryuttarā ca pūjā phalavaśādiha || 40 ||

daśasaṃkhyāvaro homaḥ pratidravyaṃ śatottaraḥ |
ghorarūpaśśivaściṃtyo māraṇoccāṭanādiṣu || 41 ||

śivaliṃge śivāgnau ca hyanyāsu pratimāsu ca |
ciṃtyassaumyatanuśśaṃbhuḥ kārye śāntikapauṣṭike || 42 ||

āyasau sruksruvau kāryau māraṇādiṣu karmasu |
tadanyatra tu sauvarṇau śāntikādyeṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ || 43 ||

dūrvayā ghṛtagokṣīramiśrayā madhunā tathā |
caruṇā saghṛtenaiva kevalaṃ payasāpi vā || 44 ||

juhuyānmṛtyuvijaye tilai rogopaśāntaye |
ghṛtena payasā caiva kamalairvātha kevalaiḥ || 45 ||

samṛddhikāmo juhuyānmahādāridryaśāntaye |
jātīpuṣpeṇa vaśyārthī juhuyātsaghṛtena tu || 46 ||

ghṛtena karavīraiśca kuryādākarṣaṇaṃ dvijaḥ |
tailenoccāṭanaṃ kuryātstaṃbhanaṃ madhunā punaḥ || 47 ||

staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi laśunena tu pātanam |
tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa syātkharasyoṣṭrasya cobhayoḥ || 48 ||

māraṇoccāṭane kuryādrohibījaistilānvitaiḥ |
vidveṣaṇaṃ ca tailena kuryāllāṃgalakasya tu || 49 ||

bandhanaṃ rohibījena senāstaṃbhanameva ca |
raktasarṣapasaṃmiśrairhomadravyairaśeṣataḥ || 50 ||

hastayantrodbhavaistailairjuhuyādābhicārike |
kaṭukītuṣasaṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsāsthibhireva ca || 51 ||

sarṣapaistailasaṃmiśrairjuhuyādābhicārike |
jvaropaśāntidaṃ kṣīraṃ saubhāgyaphaladaṃ tathā || 52 ||

sarvasiddhikaro homaḥ kṣaudrājyadadhibhiryutaiḥ |
kṣīreṇa tandulaiścaiva caruṇā kevalena vā || 53 ||

śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ vāpi saptabhiḥ samidādibhiḥ |
dravyairviśeṣato home vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ tathā / || 54 ||

vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ caiva śrīpadaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
bilvapatraistu havanaṃ śatrorvijayadaṃ tathā || 55 ||

samidhaḥ śāntikāryeṣu pālāśakhadirādikāḥ |
karavīrārkajāḥ kraurye kaṇṭakinyaśca vigrahe || 56 ||

praśāntaḥ śāntikaṃ kuryātpauṣṭikaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
nirghṛṇaḥ kruddhacittastu prakuryādābhicārikam || 57 ||

atīvaduravasthāyāṃ pratīkārāntaraṃ na cet |
ātatāyinamuddiśya prakuryādābhicārikam || 58 ||

svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya na kuryādābhicārikam |
yadyāstikassudharmiṣṭho mānyo vā yo .api kopi vā || 59 ||

tamuddiśyāpi no kuryādātatāyinamapyuta |
manasā karmmaṇā vācā yo .api kopi śivāśritaḥ || 60 ||

svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya śivā śritamathāpi vā |
kṛtvābhicārikaṃ karma sadyo vinipatennaraḥ || 61 ||

svarāṣṭrapālakaṃ tasmācchivabhaktaṃ ca kañcana |
na hiṃsyādabhicārādyairyadīcchetsukhamātmanaḥ || 62 ||

anyaṃ kamapi coddiśya kṛtvā vai māraṇādikam |
paścāttāpena saṃyuktaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samācaret || 63 ||

bāṇaliṃge .api vā kuryānnirdhano dhanavānapi |
svayaṃbhūte .atha vā liṃge ārṣake vaidike .api vā || 64 ||

abhāve hemaratnānāmaśaktau ca tadarjane |
manasaivācaredetaddravyairvā pratirūpakaiḥ || 65 ||

kvacidaṃśe tu yaḥ śaktastvaśaktaḥ kvacidaṃśake |
so .api śaktyanusāreṇa kurvaṃścetphalamṛcchati || 66 ||

karmaṇyanuṣṭhite .apyasminphalaṃ yatra na dṛśyate |
dvistrirvāvarttayettatra sarvathā dṛśyate phalam || 67 ||

pūjopayuktaṃ yaddravyaṃ hemaratnādyanuttamam |
tatsarvaṃ gurave dadyāddakṣiṇāṃ ca tataḥ pṛthak || 68 ||

sa cennecchati tatsarvaṃ śivāya vinivedayet |
athavā śivabhaktebhyo nānyebhyastu pradīyate || 69 ||

yaḥ svayaṃ sādhayecchaktyā gurvādinirapekṣayā |
so .apyevamācaredatra na gṛhṇīyātsvayaṃ punaḥ || 70 ||

svayaṃ gṛhṇāti yo lobhātpūjāṃgadravyamuttamam |
kāṃkṣitaṃ na labhenmūḍho nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 71 ||

arcitaṃ yattu talliṃgaṃ gṛhṇīyādvā navā svayam |
gṛhṇīyādyadi tannityaṃ svayaṃ vānyo .api vārcayet || 72 ||

yathoktameva karmaitadācaredyo .anapāyataḥ |
phalaṃ vyabhicarennaivamityataḥ kiṃ prarocakam || 73 ||

tathāpyuddeśato vakṣye karmaṇaḥ siddhimuttamam |
api śatrubhirākrānto vyādhibhirvāpyanekaśaḥ || 74 ||

mṛtyorāsyagataścāpi mucyate nirapāyataḥ |
pūjāyate .atikṛpaṇo rikto vaiśravaṇāyate || 75 ||

kāmāyate virūpo .api vṛddho .api taruṇāyate |
śatrurmitrāyate sadyo virodhī kiṃkarāyate || 76 ||

viṣāyate yadamṛtaṃ viṣamapyamṛtāyate |
sthalāyate samudro .api sthalamapyarṇavāyate || 77 ||

mahīdharāyate śvabhraṃ sa ca śvabhrāyate giriḥ |
padmākarāyate vahniḥ saro vaiśvānarāyate || 78 ||

vanāyate yadudyānaṃ tadudyānāyate vanam |
siṃhāyate mṛgaḥ kṣudraḥ siṃhaḥ krīḍāmṛgāyate || 79 ||

striyo .abhisārikāyante lakṣmīḥ sucaritāyate |
svairapreṣyāyate vāṇī kīrtistu gaṇikāyate || 80 ||

svairācārāyate medhā vajrasūcīyate manaḥ |
mahāvātāyate śaktirbalaṃ mattagajāyate || 81 ||

stambhāyate samudyogaiḥ śatrupakṣe sthitā kriyā |
śatrupakṣāyate .arīṇāṃ sarva eva suhṛjjanaḥ || 82 ||

śatravaḥ kuṇapāyante jīvantopi sabāndhavāḥ |
āpanno .api gatāriṣṭaḥ svayaṃ khalvamṛtāyate || 83 ||

rasāya nāyate nityamapathyamapi sevitam |
aniśaṃ kriyamāṇāpi ratistvabhinavāyate || 84 ||

anāgatādikaṃ sarvaṃ karasthāmalakāyate |
yādṛcchikaphalāyante siddhayo .apyaṇimādayaḥ || 85 ||

bahunātra kimuktena sarvakāmārthasiddhiṣu |
asminkarmaṇi nirvṛtte tvanavāpyaṃ na vidyate || 86 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe aihikasiddhikarmavarṇanaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 32 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kevalāmuṣmikaṃ vidhim |
naitena sadṛśaṃ kiṃcitkarmāsti bhuvanatraye || 1 ||

puṇyātiśayasaṃyuktaḥ sarvairdevairanuṣṭhitaḥ |
brahmaṇā viṣṇunā caiva rudreṇa ca viśeṣataḥ || 2 ||

indrādilokapāraiśca sūryādyairnavabhirgrahaiḥ |
viśvāmitravasiṣṭhādyairbrahmavidbhirmaharṣibhiḥ || 3 ||

śvetāgastyadadhīcādyairasmābhiśca śivāśritaiḥ |
nandīśvaramahākālabhṛṃgīśādyairgaṇeśvaraiḥ || 4 ||

pātālavāsibhirdaityaiḥ śeṣādyaiśca mahoragaiḥ |
siddhairyakṣaiśca gandharvai rakṣobhūtapiśācakaiḥ || 5 ||

svaṃsvaṃ padamanuprāptaṃ sarvairayamanuṣṭhitaḥ |
anena vidhinā sarve devā devatvamāgatāḥ || 6 ||

brahmā brahmatvamāpanno viṣṇurviṣṇutvamāgataḥ |
rudro rudratvamāpanna indraścendratvamāgataḥ || 7 ||

gaṇeśaśca gaṇeśatvamanena vidhinā gataḥ |
sitacandanatoyena liṃgaṃ snāpya śivaṃ śivām |
śvetairvikasitaiḥ padmaiḥ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca // 8 || 8 ||

tatra padmāsanaṃ ramyaṃ kṛtvā lakṣaṇasaṃyutam |
vibhave sati hemādyai ratnādyairvā svaśaktitaḥ || 9 ||

madhye kesarajālāsya sthāpya liṃgaṃ kanīyasam |
aṃguṣṭhapratimaṃ ramyaṃ sarvagandhamayaṃ śubham || 10 ||

dakṣiṇe sthāpayitvā tu bilvapatraiḥ samarcayet |
aguruṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve paścime tu manaḥśilām || 11 ||

uttare candanaṃ dadyāddharitālaṃ tu pūrvataḥ |
sugandhaiḥ kusumai ramyairvicitraiścāpi pūjayet || 12 ||

dhūpaṃ kṛṣṇāguruṃ dadyātsarvataśca saguggulam |
vāsāṃsi cātisūkṣmāṇi vikāśāni nivedayet || 13 ||

pāyasaṃ ghṛtasaṃmiśraṃ ghṛtadīpāṃśca dāpayet |
sarvaṃ nivedya mantreṇa tato gacchetpradakṣiṇām || 14 ||

praṇamya bhaktyā deveśaṃ stutvā cānte kṣamāpayet |
sarvopahārasaṃmiśraṃ tato liṃgaṃ nivedayet || 15 ||

śivāya śivamantreṇa dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ |
evaṃ yo .arcayate nityaṃ pañcagandhamayaṃ śubham || 16 ||

sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate |
etadvratottamaṃ guhyaṃ śivaliṃgamahāvratam || 17 ||

bhaktasya te samākhyātaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit |
deyaṃ ca śivabhaktebhyaḥ śivena kathitaṃ purā || 18 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe āmuṣmikakarmavidhivarṇanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 33 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

nityanaimittikātkāmyādyā siddhiriha kīrtitā |
sā sarvā labhyeta sadyo liṃgaberapratiṣṭhayā || 1 ||

sarvo liṃgamayo lokassarvaṃ liṃge pratiṣṭhitam |
tasmātpratiṣṭhite liṃge bhavetsarvaṃ patiṣṭhitam || 2 ||

brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vāpi rudreṇānyena kena vā |
liṃgapratiṣṭhāmutsṛjya kriyate svapadasthitiḥ || 3 ||

kimanyadiha vaktavyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ prati kāraṇam |
partiṣṭhitaṃ śivenāpi liṃgaṃ vaiśveśvaraṃ yataḥ || 4 ||

tasmātsarvaprayatnena paratreha ca śarmaṇe |
sthāpayetparameśasya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā || 5 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

kimidaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ kathaṃ liṃgī maheśvaraḥ |
kathaṃ ca liṃgabhāvo .asya kasmādasmiñchivo .arcyate || 6 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

avyaktaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ triguṇaprabhavāpyayam |
anādyanantaṃ viśvasya yadupādānakāraṇam || 7 ||

tadeva mūlaprakṛtirmāyā ca gaganātmikā |
tata eva samutpannaṃ jagadetaccarācaram || 8 ||

aśuddhaṃ caiva śuddhaṃ yacchuddhāśuddhaṃ ca tattridhā |
tataḥ śivo maheśaśca rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ || 9 ||

bhūtāni cendriyairjātā līyante .atra śivājñayā |
ata eva śivo liṃgo liṃgamājñāpayedyataḥ || 10 ||

yato na tadanājñātaṃ kāryāya prabhavetsvataḥ |
tato jātasya viśvasya tatraiva vilayo yataḥ || 11 ||

anena liṃgatāṃ tasya bhavennānyena kenacit |
liṃgaṃ ca śivayordehastābhyāṃ yasmādadhiṣṭhitam || 12 ||

atastatra śivaḥ sāmbo nityameva samarcayet |
liṃgavedī mahādevī liṃgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ || 13 ||

tayoḥ saṃpūjanādeva sa ca sā ca samarcitau |
na tayorliṃgadehatvaṃ vidyate paramārthataḥ || 14 ||

yatastvetau viśuddhau tau dehastadupacārataḥ |
tadeva paramā śaktiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 15 ||

śaktirājñāṃ yadādatte prasūte taccarācaram |
na tasya mahimā śakyo vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi || 16 ||

yenādau mohitau syātāṃ brahmanārāyaṇāvapi |
purā tribhuvanasyāsya pralaye samupasthite || 17 ||

vāriśayyāgato viṣṇuḥ suṣvāpānākulaḥ sukham |
yadṛcchayā gatastatra brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ || 18 ||

dadarśa puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ svapantaṃ tamanākulam |
māyayā mohitaḥ śambhorviṣṇumāha pitāmahaḥ || 19 ||

kastvaṃ vadetyamarṣeṇa prahṛtyotthāpya mādhavam |
sa tu hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇābhihataḥ kṣaṇāt || 20 ||

prabuddhotthāya śayanāddadarśa parameṣṭhinam |
tamāha cāntassaṃkruddhaḥ svayamakruddhavaddhariḥ || 21 ||

kutastvamāgato vatsa kasmāttvaṃ vyākulo vada |
iti viṣṇuvacaḥ śrutvā prabhutvaguṇasūcakam || 22 ||

rajasā baddhavairastaṃ brahmā punarabhāṣata |
vatseti māṃ kuto brūṣe guruḥ śiṣyamivātmanaḥ || 23 ||

māṃ na jānāsi kiṃ nāthaṃ prapaṃco yasya me kṛtiḥ |
tridhātmānaṃ vibhajyedaṃ sṛṣṭvātha paripālyate || 24 ||

saṃharāmi name kaścitsraṣṭā jagati vidyate |
ityukte sati so .apyāha brahmāṇaṃ viṣṇuravyayaḥ || 25 ||

ahamevādikartāsya hartā ca paripālakaḥ |
bhavānapi mamaivāṃgādavatīrṇaḥ purāvyayāt || 26 ||

manniyogāttvamātmānaṃ tridhā kṛtvā jagattrayam |
sṛjasyavasi cānte tatpunaḥ pratisṛjasyapi || 27 ||

vismṛtosi jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam |
tavāpi janakaṃ sākṣānmāmevamavamanyase || 28 ||

tavāparādho nāstyatra bhrāntosi mama māyayā |
matprasādādiyaṃ bhrāntirapaiṣyati tavācirāt || 29 ||

śṛṇu satyaṃ caturvaktra sarvadeveśvaro hyaham |
kartā bhartā ca hartā ca na mayāsti samo vibhuḥ || 30 ||

evameva vivādobhūdbrahmaviṣṇvoḥ parasparam |
abhavacca mahāyuddhaṃ bhairavaṃ romaharṣaṇam || 31 ||

muṣṭibhirnnighnatostīvraṃ rajasā baddhavairayoḥ |
tayordarpāpahārāya prabodhāya ca devayoḥ || 32 ||

madhye samāvirabhavalliṃgamaiśvaramadbhutam |
jvālāmālāsahasrāḍhyamaprameyamanaupamam || 33 ||

kṣayavṛddhivinirmuktamādimadhyāntavarjitam |
tasya jvālāsahasreṇa brahmaviṣṇū vimohitau || 34 ||

visṛjya yuddhaṃ kiṃ tvetadityaciṃtayatāṃ tadā |
na tayostasya yāthātmyaṃ prabuddhamabhavadyadā || 35 ||

tadā samudyatau syātāṃ tasyādyantaṃ parīkṣitum || 36 ||

tatra haṃsākṛtirbrahmā viśvataḥ pakṣasaṃyutaḥ |
manonilajavo bhūtvā gatastūrddhvaṃ prayatnataḥ || 37 ||

nārāyaṇopi viśvātmā līlāñjanacayopamam |
vārāhamamitaṃ rūpamasthāya gatavānadhaḥ || 38 ||

evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaran viṣṇuradhogataḥ |
nāpaśyadalpamapyasya mūlaṃ liṃgasya sūkaraḥ || 39 ||

tāvatkālaṃ gataścorddhvaṃ tasyāntaṃ jñātumicchayā |
śrāntotyantamadṛṣṭvāntaṃ pāpatādhaḥ pitāmahaḥ || 40 ||

tathaiva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃvignalocanaḥ |
kleśena mahatā tūrṇamadhastādutthito .abhavat || 41 ||

samāgatāvathānyonyaṃ vismayasmeravīkṣaṇau |
māyayā mohitau śaṃbhoḥ kṛtyākṛtyaṃ na jagmatuḥ || 42 ||

pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvatastasya cāgrataśca sthitāvubhau |
praṇipatya kimātmedamityaciṃtayatāṃ tadā || 43 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe harividhimohavarṇanaṃ nāma catustriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 34 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

athāvirabhavattatra sanādaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam |
omityekākṣaraṃ brahma brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakam || 1 ||

tadapyaviditaṃ tāvadbrahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā |
rajasā tamasā cittaṃ tayoryasmāttiraskṛtam || 2 ||

tadā vibhaktamabhavaccaturddhaikaṃ tadakṣaram |
a u meti trimātrābhiḥ parastāccārddhamātrayā || 3 ||

tatrākāraḥ śrito bhāge jvalalliṃgasya dakṣiṇe |
ukāraścottare tadvanmakārastasya madhyataḥ || 4 ||

arddhamātrātmako nādaḥ śrūyate liṃgamūrddhani |
vibhakte .api tadā tasminpraṇave paramākṣare || 5 ||

vibhāvārthaṃ ca tau devau na kiṃcidavajagmatuḥ |
vedātmanā tadāvyaktaḥ praṇavo vikṛtiṃ gataḥ || 6 ||

tatrākāro ṛgabhavadukāro yajuravyayaḥ |
makārassāma saṃjāto nādastvātharvaṇī śrutiḥ || 7 ||

ṛgayaṃ sthāpayāmāsa samāsāttvarthamātmanaḥ |
rajoguṇeṣu brahmāṇaṃ mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsvapi || 8 ||

sṛṣṭiṃ lokeṣu pṛthivīṃ tattveṣvātmānamavyayam |
kalādhvani nivṛttiṃ ca sadyaṃ brahmasu paṃcasu || 9 ||

liṃgabhāgeṣvadhobhāgaṃ bījākhyaṃ kāraṇatraye |
catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaiśvaryaṃ bauddhaṃ yadaṇimādiṣu || 10 ||

taditthamarthairdaśabhirvyāptaṃ viśvamṛcā jagat |
athopasthāpayāmāsa svārthaṃ daśavidhaṃ yajuḥ || 11 ||

sattvaṃ guṇeṣu viṣṇuṃ ca mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsvapi |
sthitiṃ lokeṣvantarikṣaṃ vidyāṃ tattveṣu ca triṣu || 12 ||

kalādhvasu pratiṣṭhāṃ ca vāmaṃ brahmasu paṃcasu |
madhyaṃ tu liṃgabhāgeṣu yoniṃ ca triṣu hetuṣu || 13 ||

prākṛtaṃ ca yathaiśvaryaṃ tasmādviśvaṃ yajurmayam |
tatopasthāpayāmāsa sāmārthaṃ daśadhātmanaḥ || 14 ||

tamoguṇeṣvatho rudraṃ mūrtiṣvādyaṃ kriyāsu ca |
saṃhṛtiṃ triṣu lokeṣu tattveṣu śivamuttamam || 15 ||

vidyākalāsvaghoraṃ ca tathā brahmasu paṃcasu |
liṃgabhāgeṣu pīṭhorddhvaṃ bījinaṃ kāraṇatraye || 16 ||

pauruṣaṃ ca tathaiśvaryamitthaṃ sāmnā tataṃ jagat |
athātharvāha nairguṇyamarthaṃ prathamamātmanaḥ || 17 ||

tato maheśvaraṃ sākṣānmūrtiṣvapi sadāśivam |
kriyāsu niṣkriyasyāpi śivasya paramātmanaḥ || 18 ||

bhūtānugrahaṇaṃ caiva mucyante yena jantavaḥ |
lokeṣvapi yato vāco nivṛttā manasā saha || 19 ||

tadūrddhvamunmanā lokātsomalokamalaukikam |
somassahomayā yatra nityaṃ nivasatīśvaraḥ || 20 ||

tadūrddhvamunmanā lokādyaṃ prāpto na nivartate |
śāntiṃ ca śāntyatītāṃ ca vyāpikāṃ cai kalāsvapi || 21 ||

tatpūruṣaṃ tatheśānaṃ brahma brahmasu paṃcasu |
mūrddhānamapi liṃgasya nādabhāgeṣvanuttamam || 22 ||

yatrāvāhya samārādhyaḥ kevalo niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ |
tatteṣvapi tadā bindornādācchaktestataḥ parāt || 23 ||

tattvādapi paraṃ tattvamatattvaṃ paramārthataḥ |
kāraṇeṣu trayātītānmāyāvikṣobhakāraṇāt || 24 ||

anantācchuddhavidyāyāḥ parastācca maheśvarāt |
sarvavidyeśvarādhīśānna parācca sadāśivāt || 25 ||

sarvamantratanordevācchaktitrayasamanvitāt |
paṃcavaktrāddaśabhujātsākṣātsakalaniṣkalāt || 26 ||

tasmādapi parādbindorarddhedośca tataḥ parāt |
tataḥ parānniśādhīśānnādākhyācca tataḥ parāt || 27 ||

tataḥ parātsuṣumneśādbrahmarandhreśvarādapi |
tataḥ parasmācchakteśca parastācchivatattvataḥ || 28 ||

paramaṃ kāraṇaṃ sākṣātsvayaṃ niṣkāraṇaṃ śivam |
kāraṇānāṃ ca dhātāraṃ dhyātārāṃ dhyeyamavyayam || 29 ||

paramākāśamadhyasthaṃ paramātmopari sthitaṃ |
sarvaiśvaryeṇa saṃpannaṃ sarveśvaramanīśvaram || 30 ||

aiśvaryāccāpi māyeyādaśuddhānmānuṣādikāt |
aparācca parāttyājyādadhiśuddhādhvagocarāt || 31 ||

tatparācchuddhavidyādyādunmanāntātparātparāt |
paramaṃ paramaiśvaryamunmanādyamanādi ca || 32 ||

apāramaparādhīnaṃ nirastātiśayaṃ sthiram |
itthamarthairdaśavidhairiyamātharvaṇī śrutiḥ || 33 ||

yasmādgarīyasī tasmādviśvaṃ vyāptamatharvaṇāt |
ṛgvedaḥ punarāhedaṃ jāgradrūpaṃ mayocyate || 34 ||

yenāhamātmatattvasya nityamasmyabhidhāyakaḥ |
yajurvedo .avadattadvatsvapnāvasthā mayocyate || 35 ||

bhogyātmanā pariṇatā vidyāvedyā yato mayi |
sāma cāha suṣuptyākhyamevaṃ sarvaṃ mayocyate || 36 ||

mamārthena śivenedaṃ tāmasenābhidhīyate |
atharvāha turāyākhyaṃ turīyātītameva ca || 37 ||

mayābhidhīyate tasmādadhvātītapadosmyaham |
adhvātmakaṃ tu tritayaṃ śivavidyātmasaṃjñitam || 38 ||

tattraiguṇyaṃ trayīsādhyaṃ saṃśodhyaṃ ca padaiṣiṇā |
adhvātītaṃ turīyākhyaṃ nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ padam || 39 ||

tadatītaṃ ca nairguṇyādadhvanosya viśodhakam |
dvayoḥ pramāpako nādo nadāntaśca madātmakaḥ || 40 ||

tasmānmamārthasvātantryātpradhānaḥ parameśvaraḥ |
yadasti vastu tatsarvaṃ guṇapradhānyayogataḥ || 41 ||

samastaṃ vyastamapi ca praṇavārthaṃ pracakṣate |
savārthavācakaṃ tasmādekaṃ brahmaitadakṣaram || 42 ||

tenomiti jagatkṛtsnaṃ kurute prathamaṃ śivaḥ |
śivo hi praṇavo hyeṣa praṇavo hi śivaḥ smṛtaḥ || 43 ||

vācyavācakayorbhedo nātyantaṃ vidyate yataḥ |
ciṃtayā rahito rudro vācoyanmanasā saha || 44 ||

aprāpya tannivartante vācyastvekākṣareṇa saḥ |
ekākṣarādakārākhyādātmā brahmābhidhīyate || 45 ||

ekākṣarādukārākhyāddvidhā viṣṇurudīryate |
ekākṣarānmakārākhyācchivo rudra udāhṛtaḥ || 46 ||

dakṣiṇāṃgānmaheśasya jāto brahmātmasaṃjñikaḥ |
vāmāṃgādabhavadviṣṇustato vidyeti saṃjñitaḥ || 47 ||

hṛdayānnīlarudro bhūcchivasya śivasaṃjñikaḥ |
sṛṣṭeḥ pravartako brahmā sthiterviṣṇurvimohakaḥ || 48 ||

saṃhārasya tathā rudrastayornityaṃ niyāmakaḥ || 49 ||

tasmāttrayaste kathyante jagataḥ kāraṇāni ca |
kāraṇatrayahetuśca śivaḥ paramakāraṇam || 50 ||

arthametamavijñāya rajasā baddhavairayoḥ |
yuvayoḥ pratibodhāya madhye liṃgamupasthitam || 51 ||

evamomiti māṃ prāhuryadihoktamatharvaṇā |
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni śākhāścānyāḥ sahasraśaḥ || 52 ||

vedeṣvevaṃ svayaṃ vaktrairvyaktamityavadatsvapi |
svapnānubhūtamiva tattābhyāṃ nādhyavasīyate || 53 ||

tayostatra prabodhāya tamopanayanāya ca |
liṃgepi mudritaṃ sarvaṃ yathā vedairudāhṛtam || 54 ||

taddṛṣṭvā mudritaṃ liṃge prasādālliṃginastadā |
praśāntamanasau devau prabuddhau saṃbabhūvatuḥ || 55 ||

utpattiṃ vilayaṃ caiva yathātmyaṃ ca ṣaḍadhvanām |
tataḥ parataraṃ dhāma dhāmavantaṃ ca pūruṣam || 56 ||

niruttarataraṃ brahma niṣkalaṃ śivamīśvaram |
paśupāśamayasyāsya prapaṃcasya sadā patim || 57 ||

akutobhayamatyantamavṛddhikṣayamavyayam |
vāhyamābhyantaraṃ vyāptaṃ vāhyābhyantaravarjitam || 58 ||

nirastātiśayaṃ śaśvadviśvalokavilakṣaṇam |
alakṣaṇamanirdeśyamavāGmanasagocaram || 59 ||

prakāśaikarasaṃ śāntaṃ prasannaṃ satatoditam |
sarvakalyāṇanilayaṃ śaktyā tādṛśayānvitam || 60 ||

jñātvā devaṃ virūpākṣaṃ brahmanārāyaṇau tadā |
racayitvāṃjaliṃ mūrdhni bhītau tau vācamūcatuḥ || 61 ||

brahmovāca |

ajño vāhamabhijño vā tvayādau deva nirmitaḥ |
īdṛśīṃ bhrāntimāpanna iti ko .atrāparādhyati || 62 ||

āstāṃ mamedamajñānaṃ tvayi sannihate prabho |
nirbhayaḥ ko .abhibhāṣeta kṛtyaṃ svasya parasya vā || 63 ||

āvayordevadevasya vivādo .api hi śobhanaḥ |
pādapraṇāmaphalado nāthasya bhavato yataḥ || 64 ||

viṣṇuruvāca |

stotuṃ deva na vāgasti mahimnaḥ sadṛśī tava |
prabhoragre vidheyānāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvo vyatikramaḥ || 65 ||

kimatra saṃghaṭetkṛtyamityevāvasarocitam |
ajānannapi yatkiṃcitpralapya tvāṃ nato .asmyaham || 66 ||

kāraṇatvaṃ tvayā dattaṃ vismṛtaṃ tava māyayā |
mohito .ahaṃkṛtaścāpi punarevāsmi śāsitaḥ || 67 ||

vijñāpitaiḥ kiṃ bahubhirbhītosmi bhṛśamīśvara |
yato .ahamaparicchedyaṃ tvāṃ paricchettumudyataḥ || 68 ||

tvāmuśanti mahādevaṃ bhītānāmārtināśanam |
ato vyatikramaṃ me .adya kṣantumarhasi śaṃkara || 69 ||

iti vijñāpitastābhyāmīśvarābhyāṃ maheśvaraḥ |
prīto .anugṛhya tau devau smitapūrvamabhāṣata || 70 ||

īśvara uvāca |

vatsavatsa vidhe viṣṇo māyayā mama mohitau |
yuvāṃ prabhutve .ahaṃkṛtya buddhavairo parasparam || 71 ||

vivādaṃ yuddhaparyantaṃ kṛtvā noparatau kila |
tataścchinnā prajāsṛṣṭirjagatkāraṇabhūtayoḥ || 72 ||

ajñānamānaprabhavādvaimatyādyuvayorapi |
tannivartayituṃ yuṣmaddarppamohau mayaiva tu || 73 ||

evaṃ nivāritāvadyaliṃgāvirbhāvalīlayā |
tasmādbhūyo vivādaṃ ca vrīḍāṃ cotsṛjya kṛtsnaśaḥ || 74 ||

yathāsvaṃ karma kuryātāṃ bhavantau vītamatsarau |
purā mamājñayā sārddhaṃ samastajñānasaṃhitāḥ || 75 ||

yuvābhyāṃ hi mayā dattā kāraṇatvaprasiddhaye |
mantraratnaṃ ca sūtrākhyaṃ paṃcākṣaramayaṃ param || 76 ||

mayopadiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ tadyuvayoradya vismṛtam |
dadāmi ca punaḥ sarvaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ mamājñayā || 77 ||

yato vinā yuvāṃ tena na kṣamau sṛṣṭirakṣaṇe |
evamuktvā mahādevo nārāyaṇapitāmahau || 78 ||

mantrarājaṃ dadau tābhyāṃ jñānasaṃhitayā saha |
tau labdhvā mahatīṃ divyāmājñāṃ māheśvarīṃ parām || 79 ||

mahārthaṃ mantraratnaṃ ca tathaiva sakalāḥ kalāḥ |
daṃḍavatpraṇatiṃ kṛtvā devadevasya pādayoḥ || 80 ||

atiṣṭhatāṃ vītabhayāvānandāstimitau tadā |
etasminnantare citramindrajālavadaiśvaram || 81 ||

liṃgaṃ kvāpi tirobhūtaṃ na tābhyāmupalabhyate |
tato vilapya hāheti sadyaḥpraṇayabhaṃgataḥ || 82 ||

kimasatyamidaṃ vṛttamiti coktvā parasparam |
aciṃtyavaibhavaṃ śaṃbhorviciṃtya ca gatavyathau || 83 ||

abhyupetya parāṃ maitrīmāliṃgya ca parasparam |
jagadvyāpāramuddiśya jagmaturdevapuṃgavau || 84 ||

tataḥ prabhṛti śakrādyāḥ sarva eva surāsurāḥ |
ṛṣayaśca narā nāgā nāryaścāpi vidhānataḥ |
liṃgapratiṣṭhā kurvanti liṃge taṃ pūjayanti ca // 85 || 85 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe harividhimohanivāraṇaṃ nāma paṃcatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 35 ||

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

bhagavañchrotumicchāmi pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam |
liṃgasyāpi ca berasya śivena vihitaṃ yathā || 1 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

anātmapratikūle tu divase śuklapakṣake |
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa kuryālliṃgaṃ pramāṇavat || 2 ||

svīkṛtyātha śubhasthānaṃ bhūparīkṣāṃ vidhāya ca |
daśopacārānkurvīta lakṣaṇoddhārapūrvakān || 3 ||

teṣāṃ daśopacārāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ pūjya vināyakam |
sthānaśuddhyādikaṃ kṛtvāliṃgaṃ snānālayaṃ nayet || 4 ||

śalākayā kāṃcanayā kuṃkumādirasāktayā |
lakṣitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śilpaśāstreṇa vilikhettataḥ || 5 ||

aṣṭamṛtsalilairvātha paṃcamṛtsalilaistathā |
liGgaṃ piṃḍikayā sārddhaṃ paṃcagavyaiśca śodhayet || 6 ||

savedikaṃ samabhyarcya divyādyaṃ tu jalāśayam |
nītvādhivāsayettatra liṃgaṃ piṃḍikayā saha || 7 ||

adhivāsālaye śuddhe sarvaśobhāsamanvite |
satoraṇe sāvaraṇe darbhamālāsamāvṛte || 8 ||

diggajāṣṭakasaṃpanne dikpālāṣṭaghaṭānvite |
aṣṭamaṃgalakairyukte kṛtadikpālakārcite || 9 ||

tejasaṃ dāravaṃ vāpi kṛtvā padmāsanāṃkitam |
vinyasenmadhyatastatra vipulaṃ pīṭhakālayam || 10 ||

dvārapālānsamabhyarcya bhadrādīṃścaturaḥkramāt |
samudraśca vibhadraśca sunandaśca vinandakaḥ || 11 ||

snāpayitvā samabhyarcya liṃgaṃ vedikayā saha |
sakūrcābhyāṃ tu vastrābhyāṃ samāveṣṭyaṃ samantataḥ || 12 ||

prāpayya śanakaistoyaṃ pīṭhikopari śāyayet |
prākśiraskamadhaḥsūtraṃ piṃḍikāṃ cāsya paścime || 13 ||

sarvamaṃgalasaṃyuktaṃ liṃgaṃ tatrādhivāsayet |
paṃcarātraṃ trirātraṃ vāpyekarātramathāpi vā || 14 ||

visṛjya pūjitaṃ tatra śodhayitvā ca pūrvavat |
saṃpūjyotsavamārgeṇa śayanālayamānayet || 15 ||

tatrāpi śayanasthānaṃ kuryānmaṃḍalamadhyataḥ |
śuddhairjalaiḥ snāpayitvā liṃgamabhyarcayetkramāt || 16 ||

aiśānyāṃ padmamālikhya śuddhalipte mahītale |
śivakuṃbhaṃ śodhayitvā tatrāvāhya śivaṃ yajet || 17 ||

vedīmadhye sitaṃ padmaṃ parikalpya vidhānataḥ |
tasya paścimataścāpi caṃḍikāpadmamālikhet || 18 ||

kṣaumādyairvāhatairvastraiḥ puṣpairdarbhairathāpi vā |
prakalpya śayanaṃ tasminhemapuṣpaṃ vinikṣipet || 19 ||

tatra liṃgaṃ samānīya sarvamaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ |
raktena vastrayugmena sakūrcena samantataḥ || 20 ||

saha piṃḍikayāveṣṭya śāyayecca yathā purā |
purastātpadmamālikhya taddaleṣu yathākramam || 21 ||

vidyeśakalaśānnyasyenmadhye śaivīṃ ca varddhanīm |
parītya padmatritayaṃ juhuyurdvijasattamāḥ || 22 ||

te cāṣṭamūrttayaḥ kalpyāḥ pūrvādiparitaḥ sthitāḥ |
catvāraścātha vā dikṣu svadhyetārassajāpakāḥ || 23 ||

juhuyuste viraṃcyādyāścatasro mūrtayaḥ smṛtāḥ |
daiśikaḥ prathamaṃ teṣāmaiśānyāṃ paścime .atha vā || 24 ||

pradhānahomaṃ kurvīta saptadravyairyathākramam |
ācāryyātpādamarddhaṃ vā juhuyuścāpare dvijāḥ || 25 ||

pradhānamekamevātra juhuyādatha vā guruḥ |
pūrvaṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā ghṛtenāṣṭottaraṃ śatam || 26 ||

mūrdhni mūlena liṃgasya śivahastaṃ pravinyaset |
śatamarddhaṃ tadarddhaṃ vā kramāddravyaiśca saptabhiḥ || 27 ||

hutvāhutvā spṛśelliṃgaṃ vedikāṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ |
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato hutvā kramāddadyācca dakṣiṇām || 28 ||

ācāryātpādamarddhaṃ vā hotR̥ṇāṃ sthapaterapi |
tadarddhaṃ deyamanyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca śaktitaḥ || 29 ||

tataḥ śvabhre vṛṣaṃ haimaṃ kūrcaṃ vāpi niveśya ca |
mṛdaṃbhasā paṃcagavyaiḥ punaḥ śuddhajalena ca || 30 ||

śodhitāṃ candanāliptāṃ śvabhre brahmaśilāṃ kṣipet |
karanyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā navabhiḥ śaktināmabhiḥ || 31 ||

haritālādidhātūṃśca bījagandhauṣadhairapi |
śivaśāstroktavidhinā kṣipedbrahmaśilopari || 32 ||

pratiliṃgaṃ tu saṃsthāpya kṣīraṃ vṛkṣasamudbhavam |
sthitaṃ buddhvā tadutsṛjya liṃgaṃ brahmaśilopari || 33 ||

prāgudakpravarāṃ kiṃcitsthāpayenmūlavidyayā |
piṃḍikāṃ cātha saṃyojya śāktaṃ mūlamanusmaran || 34 ||

bandhanaṃ bandhakadravyaiḥ kṛtvā sthānaṃ viśodhya ca |
dattvā cārghyaṃ ca puṣpāṇi kuryuryavanikāṃ punaḥ || 35 ||

yathāyogyaṃ niṣekādi liṃgasya puratastadā |
ānīya śayanasthānātkalaśānvinyasetkramāt || 36 ||

mahāpūjāmathārabhya saṃpūjya kalaśāndaśa |
śivamantramanusmṛtya śivakuṃbhajalāntare || 37 ||

aṃguṣṭhānāmikāyogādādāya tamudīrayet |
nyasedīśānabhāgasya madhye liṃgasya mantravit || 38 ||

śaktiṃ nyasettathā vidyāṃ vidyeśāṃśca yathākramam |
liGgamūle śivajalaistato liṃgaṃ niṣecayet || 39 ||

varddhanyāṃ piṃḍikāliṃgaṃ vidyeśakalaśaiḥ punaḥ |
abhiṣicyāsanaṃ paścādādhārādyaṃ prakalpayet || 40 ||

kṛtvā paṃcakalānyāsaṃ dīptaṃ liṃgamanusmaret |
āvāhayecchivau sākṣātprāñjaliḥ prāgudaGmukhaḥ || 41 ||

vṛṣādhirājamāruhya vimānaṃ vā nabhastalāt |
alaṃkṛtaṃ sahāyāntaṃ devyā devamanusmaran |
sarvābharaṇaśobhāḍhyaṃ sarvamaṃgalanisvanaiḥ // 42 || 42 ||

brahmaviṣṇumaheśārkaśakrādyairdevadānavaiḥ |
ānandaklinnasarvāṃgairvinyastāṃjalimastakaiḥ || 43 ||

stuvadbhireva nṛtyadbhirnāmadbhirabhito vṛtam |
tataḥ paṃcopacārāṃśca kṛtvā pūjāṃ samāpayet || 44 ||

nātaḥ parataraḥ kaścidvidhiḥ pañcopacārakāt |
pratiṣṭhāṃ liṃgavatkuryātpratimāsvapi sarvataḥ || 45 ||

lakṣaṇoddhārasamaye kāryaṃ nayanamocanam |
jalādhivāse śayane śāyayettāntvadhomukhīm || 46 ||

kumbhodaśāyitāṃ mantrairhṛdi tāṃ sanniyojayet |
kṛtālayāṃ parāmāhuḥ pratiṣṭhāmakṛtālayāt || 47 ||

śaktaḥ kṛtālayaḥ paścātpratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret |
aśaktaścetpratiṣṭhāpya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā || 48 ||

śakteranuguṇaṃ paścātprakurvīta śivālayam |
gṛhārcāṃ ca punarvakṣye pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam || 49 ||

kṛtvā kanīyasaṃberaṃ liṃgaṃ vā lakṣaṇānvitam |
ayane cottare prāpte śuklapakśe śubhe dine || 50 ||

devīṃ kṛtvā śubhe deśe tatrābjaṃ pūrvavallikhet |
vikīrya patrapuṣpādyairmadhye kuṃbhaṃ nidhāya ca || 51 ||

paritastasya caturaḥ kalaśān dikṣu vinyaset |
paṃca brahmāṇi tadbījaisteṣu paṃcasu paṃcabhiḥ || 52 ||

nyasya saṃpūjya mudrādi darśayitvābhirakṣya ca |
viśodhya liṃgaṃ beraṃ vā mṛttoyādyairyathā purā || 53 ||

sthāpayetpuṣpasaṃchannamuttarasthe varāsane |
nidhāya puṣpaṃ śirasi prokṣayetprokṣaṇījalaiḥ || 54 ||

samabhyarcya punaḥ puṣpairjayaśabdādipūrvakam |
kumbhairīśānavidyāntaiḥ snāpayenmūlavidyayā || 55 ||

tataḥ paṃcakalānyāsaṃ kṛtvā pūjāṃ ca pūrvavat |
nityamārādhayettatra devyā devaṃ trilocanam || 56 ||

ekamevātha vā kuṃbhaṃ mūrtimantrasamanvitam |
nyasya padmāntare sarvaṃ śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret || 57 ||

atyantopahataṃ liṃgaṃ viśodhya sthāpayetpunaḥ |
saṃprokṣayedupahatamanāgupahataṃ yajet || 58 ||

liṃgāni bāṇasaṃjñāni sthāpanīyāni vā na vā |
tāni pūrvaṃ śivenaiva saṃskṛtāni yatastataḥ || 59 ||

śeṣāṇi sthāpanīyāni yāni dṛṣṭāni bāṇavat |
svayamudbhūtaliṃge ca divye cārṣe tathaiva ca || 60 ||

apīṭhe pīṭhamāveśya kṛtvā saṃprokṣaṇaṃ vidhim |
yajettatra śivaṃ teṣāṃ pratiṣṭhā na vidhīyate || 61 ||

dagdhaṃ ślathaṃ kṣatāṃgaṃ ca kṣipelliṃgaṃ jalāśaye |
saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdhāya pratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret || 62 ||

berādvā vikalālliṃgāddevapūjāpurassaram |
udvāsya hṛdi saṃdhānaṃ tyāgaṃ vā yuktamācaret || 63 ||

ekāhapūjāvihatau kuryāddviguṇamarcanam |
dvirātre ca mahāpūjāṃ saṃprokṣaṇamataḥ param || 64 ||

māsādūrdhvamanekāhaṃ pūjā yadi vihanyate |
pratiṣṭhā procyate kaiścitkaiścitsaṃprokṣaṇakramaḥ || 65 ||

saṃprokṣaṇe tu liṃgāderdevamudvāsya pūrvavat |
aṣṭapañcakrameṇaiva snāpayitvā mṛdaṃbhasā || 66 ||

gavāṃ rasaiśca saṃsnāpya darbhatoyairviśodhya ca |
prokṣayetprokṣaṇītoyairmūlenāṣṭottaraṃ śatam || 67 ||

sapuṣpaṃ sakuśaṃ pāṇiṃ nyasya liṃgasya mastake |
paṃcavāraṃ japenmūlamaṣṭottaraśataṃ tataḥ || 68 ||

tato mūlena mūrddhādipīṭhāntaṃ saṃspṛśedapi |
pūjāṃ ca mahatīṃ kuryāddevamāvāhya pūrvavat || 69 ||
