alabdhe sthāpite liṃge śivasthāne jale .atha vā |
vahnau ravau tathā vyomni bhagavantaṃ śivaṃ yajet || 70 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe ptatiṣṭhāvidhivarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 36 ||

śīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

jñāne kriyāyāṃ caryāyāṃ sāramuddhṛtya saṃgrahāt |
uktaṃ bhagavatā sarvaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ mayā || 1 ||

idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham |
sādhikāraṃ ca sāṃgaṃ ca savidhiṃ saprayojanam || 2 ||

yadyasti maraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ yogādyanupamardataḥ |
sadyaḥ sādhayituṃ śakyaṃ yena syānnātmahā naraḥ || 3 ||

tacca tatkāraṇaṃ caiva tatkālakaraṇāni ca |
tadbhedatāratamyaṃ ca vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ || 4 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

sthāne pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇa sarvapraśnārthavedinā |
tataḥ krameṇa tatsarvaṃ vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ || 5 ||

niruddhavṛttyantarasyaṃ śive cittasya niścalā |
yā vṛttiḥ sa samāsena yogaḥ sa khalu paṃcadhā || 6 ||

mantrayogaḥsparśayogo bhāvayogastathāparaḥ |
abhāvayogas sarvebhyo mahāyogaḥ paro mataḥ || 7 ||

mantrābhyāsavaśenaiva mantravācyārthagocaraḥ |
avyākṣepā manovṛttir mantrayoga udāhṛtaḥ || 8 ||

prāṇāyāmamukhā saiva sparśe yogobhidhīyate |
sa mantrasparśanirmukto bhāvayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 9 ||

vilīnāvayavaṃ viśvaṃ rūpaṃ saṃbhāvyate yataḥ |
abhāvayogaḥ saṃprokto .anābhāsād vastunaḥ sataḥ || 10 ||

śivasvabhāva evaikaściṃtyate nirupādhikaḥ |
yathā śaivamanovṛttirmahāyoga ihocyate || 11 ||

dṛṣṭe tathānuśravike viraktaṃ viṣaye manaḥ |
yasya tasyādhikārosti yoge nānyasya kasyacit || 12 ||

viṣayadvayadoṣāṇāṃ guṇānāmīśvarasya ca |
darśanādeva satataṃ viraktaṃ jāyate manaḥ || 13 ||

aṣṭāṃgo vā ṣaḍaṃgo vā sarvayogaḥ samāsataḥ |
yamaśca niyamaścaiva svastikādyaṃ tathāsanam || 14 ||

prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāro dhāraṇā dhyānameva ca |
samādhiriti yogāṃgānyaṣṭāvuktāni sūribhiḥ || 15 ||

āsanaṃ prāṇasaṃrodhaḥ pratyāhārotha dhāraṇā |
dhyānaṃ samādhiryogasya ṣaḍaṃgāni samāsataḥ || 16 ||

pṛthaglakṣaṇameteṣāṃ śivaśāstre samīritam |
śivāgameṣu cānyeṣu viśeṣātkāmikādiṣu || 17 ||

yogaśāstreṣvapi tathā purāṇeṣvapi keṣu ca |
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahaḥ |
yama ityucyate sadbhiḥ paṃcāvayavayogataḥ // 18 || 18 ||

śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapaścaiva japaḥ praṇidhireva ca |
iti paṃcaprabhedassyānniyamaḥ svāṃśabhedataḥ || 19 ||

svastikaṃ padmamadhyenduṃ vīraṃ yogaṃ prasādhitam |
paryaṃkaṃ ca yatheṣṭaṃ ca proktamāsanamaṣṭadhā || 20 ||

prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyustasyāyāmo nirodhanam |
tadrocakaṃ pūrakaṃ ca kuṃbhakaṃ ca tridhocyate || 21 ||

nāsikāpuṭamaṃgulyā pīḍyaikamapareṇa tu |
audaraṃ recayedvāyuṃ tathāyaṃ recakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 22 ||

bāhyena marutā dehaṃ dṛtivatparipūrayet |
nāsāpuṭenāpareṇa pūraṇātpūrakaṃ matam || 23 ||

na muṃcati na gṛhṇāti vāyumantarbahiḥ sthitam |
saṃpūrṇaṃ kuṃbhavattiṣṭhedacalaḥ sa tu kuṃbhaka || 24 ||

recakādyaṃ trayamidaṃ na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam |
tadyataḥ kramayogena tvabhyasedyogasādhakaḥ || 25 ||

recakādiṣu yobhyāso nāḍīśodhanapūrvakaḥ |
svecchotkramaṇaparyantaḥ prokto yogānuśāsane || 26 ||

kanyakādikramavaśātprāṇāyāmanirodhanam |
taccaturddhopadiṣṭaṃ syānmātrāguṇavibhāgataḥ || 27 ||

kanyakastu caturddhā syātsa ca dvādaśamātrakaḥ |
madhyamastu dviruddhātaścaturviṃśatimātrakaḥ || 28 ||

uttamastu triruddhātaḥ ṣaḍviṃśanmātrakaḥ paraḥ |
svedakaṃpādijanakaḥ prāṇāyāmastaduttaraḥ || 29 ||

ānandodbhavaromāṃcanetrāśrūṇāṃ vimocanam |
jalpabhramaṇamūrcchādyaṃ jāyate yoginaḥ param || 30 ||

jānuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam |
aṃgulīsphoṭanaṃ kuryātsā mātreti prakīrtitā || 31 ||

mātrākrameṇa vijñeyāścodvātakramayogataḥ |
nāḍīviśuddhipūrvaṃ tu prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret || 32 ||

agarbhaśca sagarbhaśca prāṇāyāmo dvidhā smṛtaḥ |
japaṃ dhyānaṃ vināgarbhaḥ sagarbhastatsamanvayāt || 33 ||

agarbhādgarbhasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥśatādhikaḥ |
tasmātsagarbhaṃ kurvanti yoginaḥ prāṇasaṃyamam || 34 ||

prāṇasya vijayādeva jīyante dehavāyavaḥ |
prāṇo .apānaḥ samānaśca hyudāno vyāna eva ca || 35 ||

nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkalo devadatto dhanaṃjayaḥ |
prayāṇaṃ kurute yasmāttasmātprāṇo .abhidhīyate || 36 ||

avāGnayatyapānākhyo yadāhārādi bhujyate |
vyāno vyānaśayatyaṃgānyaśeṣāṇi vivardhayan || 37 ||

udvejayati marmāṇītyudāno vāyurīritaḥ |
samaṃ nayati sarvāṃgaṃ samānastena gīyate || 38 ||

udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane sthitaḥ |
kṛkalaḥ kṣavathau jñeyo devadatto vijṛṃbhaṇe || 39 ||

na jahāti mṛtaṃ cāpi sarvavyāpī dhanaṃjayaḥ |
krameṇābhyasyamānoyaṃ prāṇāyāmapramāṇavān || 40 ||

nirdahatyakhilaṃ doṣaṃ karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati |
prāṇe tu vijite samyak taccihnānyupalakṣayet || 41 ||

viṇmūtraśleṣmaṇāṃ tāvadalpabhāvaḥ prajāyate |
bahubhojanasāmarthyaṃ cirāducchvāsanaṃ tathā || 42 ||

laghutvaṃ śīghragāmitvamutsāhaḥ svarasauṣṭhavam |
sarvarogakṣayaścaiva balaṃ tejaḥ surūpatā || 43 ||

dhṛtirmedhā yuvatvaṃ ca sthiratā ca prasannatā |
tapāṃsi pāpakṣayatā yajñadānavratādayaḥ || 44 ||

prāṇāyāmasya tasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm |
indriyāṇi prasaktāni yathāsvaṃ viṣayeṣviha || 45 ||

āhatya yannigṛhṇāti sa pratyāhāra ucyate |
namaḥpūrvāṇīndriyāṇi svargaṃ narakameva ca || 46 ||

nigṛhītanisṛṣṭāni svargāya narakāya ca |
tasmātsukhārthī matimāñjñānavairāgyamāsthitaḥ || 47 ||

indriyāśvānnigṛhyāśu svātmanātmānamuddharet |
dhāraṇā nāma cittasya sthānabandhassamāsataḥ || 48 ||

sthānaṃ ca śiva evaiko nānyaddoṣatrayaṃ yataḥ |
kālaṃ kaṃcāvadhīkṛtya sthāne .avasthāpitaṃ manaḥ || 49 ||

na tu pracyavate lakṣyāddhāraṇā syānna cānyathā |
manasaḥ prathamaṃ sthairyaṃ dhāraṇātaḥ prajāyate || 50 ||

tasmāddhīraṃ manaḥ kuryāddhāraṇābhyāsayogataḥ |
dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ || 51 ||

avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānaṃ nāma taducyate |
dhyeyāvasthitacittasya sadṛśaḥ pratyayaśca yaḥ || 52 ||

pratyayāntaranirmuktaḥ pravāho dhyānamucyate |
sarvamanyatparityajya śiva eva śivaṃkaraḥ || 53 ||

paro dhyeyo .adhideveśaḥ samāptātharvaṇī śrutiḥ |
tathā śivā parā dhyeyā sarvabhūtagatau śivau || 54 ||

tau śrutau smṛtiśāstrebhyaḥ sarvagau sarvadoditau |
sarvajñau satataṃ dhyeyau nānārūpavibhedataḥ || 55 ||

vimuktiḥ pratyayaḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaścāṇimādikam |
ityetaddvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ dhyānasyāsya prayojanam || 56 ||

dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yacca dhyānaprayojanam |
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit || 57 ||

jñānavairāgyasaṃpannaḥ śraddadhānaḥ kṣamānvitaḥ |
nirmamaśca sadotsāhī dhyātetthaṃ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ || 58 ||

japācchrāntaḥ punardhyāyeddhyānācchrāntaḥ punarjapet |
japadhyanābhiyuktasya kṣipraṃ yogaḥ prasiddhyati || 59 ||

dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśadhāraṇam |
dhyānadvādaśakaṃ yāvatsamādhirabhidhīyate || 60 ||

samādhirnnāma yogāṃgamantimaṃ parikīrtitam |
samādhinā ca sarvatra prajñālokaḥ pravartate || 61 ||

yadarthamātranirbhāsaṃ stimito dadhivatsthitam |
svarūpaśūnyavadbhānaṃ samādhirabhidhīyate || 62 ||

dhyeye manaḥ samāveśya paśyedapi ca susthiram |
nirvāṇānalavadyogī samādhisthaḥ pragīyate || 63 ||

na śṛṇoti na cāghrāti na jalpati na paśyati |
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ || 64 ||

navābhimanyate kiṃcidbadhyate na ca kāṣṭavat |
evaṃ śive vilīnātmā samādhistha ihocyate || 65 ||

yathā dīpo nivātasthaḥ spandate na kadācana |
tathā samādhiniṣṭho .api tasmānna vicaletsudhīḥ || 66 ||

evamabhyasataścāraṃ yogino yogamuttamam |
tadantarāyā naśyanti vighnāḥ sarve śanaiḥśanaiḥ || 67 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ vāyunaimiṣeyarṣisaṃvāde uttarakhaṇḍe yogagativarṇanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 37 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

ālasyaṃ vyādhayastīvrāḥ pramādaḥ sthānasaṃśayaḥ |
anavasthitacittatvamaśraddhā bhrāntidarśanam || 1 ||

duḥkhāni daurmanasyaṃ ca viṣayeṣu ca lolatā |
daśaite yuñjatāṃ puṃsāmantarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 2 ||

ālasyamalasattvaṃ tu yogināṃ dehacetanoḥ |
dhātuvaiṣamyajā doṣā vyādhayaḥ karmadoṣajāḥ || 3 ||

pramādo nāma yogasya sādhanā nāma bhāvanā |
idaṃ vetyubhayākrāntaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ || 4 ||

apratiṣṭhā hi manasastvanavasthitirucyate |
aśraddhā bhāvarahitā vṛttirvai yogavartmani || 5 ||

viparyastā matiryā sā bhrāntirityabhidhīyate |
duḥkhamajñānajaṃ puṃsāṃ cittasyādhyātmikaṃ viduḥ || 6 ||

ādhibhautikamaṃgotthaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ purā kṛtaiḥ |
ādhidaivikamākhyātamaśanyastraviṣādikam || 7 ||

icchāvighātajaṃ mokṣaṃ daurmanasyaṃ pracakṣate |
viṣayeṣu vicitreṣu vibhramastatra lolatā || 8 ||

śānteṣveteṣu vighneṣu yogāsaktasya yoginaḥ |
upasargāḥ pravartante divyāste siddhisūcakāḥ || 9 ||

pratibhā śravaṇaṃ vārtā darśanāsvādavedanāḥ |
upasargāḥ ṣaḍityete vyaye yogasya siddhayaḥ || 10 ||

sūkṣme vyavahite .atīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate |
pratibhā kathyate yo .arthe pratibhāso yathātatham || 11 ||

śravaṇaṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ śravaṇe cāprayatnataḥ |
vārttā vārttāsu vijñānaṃ sarveṣāmeva dehinām || 12 ||

darśanaṃ nāma divyānāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ |
tathāsvādaśca divyeṣu raseṣvāsvāda ucyate || 13 ||

sparśanādhigamastadvadvedanā nāma viśrutā |
gandhādīnāṃ ca divyānāmābrahmabhuvanādhipāḥ || 14 ||

santiṣṭhante ca ratnāni prayacchanti bahūni ca |
svacchandamadhurā vāṇī vividhāsyātpravartate || 15 ||

rasāyanāni sarvāṇi divyāścauṣadhayastathā |
sidhyanti praṇipatyainaṃ diśanti surayoṣitaḥ || 16 ||

yogasiddhyaikadeśe .api dṛṣṭe mokṣe bhavenmatiḥ |
dṛṣṭametanmayā yadvattadvanmokṣo bhavediti || 17 ||

kṛśatā sthūlatā bālyaṃ vārddhakyaṃ caiva yauvanam |
nānācātisvarūpaṃ ca caturṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam || 18 ||

pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhirgandhasaṃgrahaḥ |
evamaṣṭaguṇaṃ prāhuḥ paiśācaṃ pārthivaṃ padam || 19 ||

jale nivasanaṃ caiva bhūmyāmevaṃ vinirgamaḥ |
icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ || 20 ||

yatrecchati jagatyasmiṃstatraiva jaladarśanam |
vinā kumbhādikaṃ pāṇau jalasañcayadhāraṇam || 21 ||

yadvastu virasañcāpi bhoktumicchati tatkṣaṇāt |
rasādikaṃ bhaveccānyattrayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam || 22 ||

nirvraṇatvaṃ śarīrasya pārthivaiśca samanvitam |
tadidaṃ ṣoḍaśaguṇamāpyamaiśvaryamadbhutam || 23 ||

śarīrādagninirmāṇaṃ tattāpabhayavarjjanam |
śaktirjagadidaṃ dagdhuṃ yadīcchedaprayatnataḥ || 24 ||

sthāpanaṃ vānalasyā .apsu pāṇau pāvakadhāraṇam |
dagdhe sarge yathāpūrvvaṃ mukhe cānnādipācanam |
dvābhyāṃ dehavinirmāṇamāpyaiśvaryasamanvitam // 25 || 25 ||

etaccaturviṃśatidhā taijasaṃ paricakṣate |
manojavatvaṃ bhūtānāṃ kṣaṇādantaḥpraveśanam || 26 ||

parvvatādimahābhāradhāraṇañcāprayatnataḥ |
gurutvañca laghutvañca pāṇāvaniladhāraṇam || 27 ||

aṃgulyagranipātādyairbhūmerapi ca kampanam |
ekena dehaniṣpattiryuktaṃ bhogaiśca taijasaiḥ || 28 ||

dvātriṃśadguṇamaiśvaryyaṃ mārutaṃ kavayo viduḥ |
chāyāhīnaviniṣpattirindriyāṇāmadarśanam || 29 ||

khecaratvaṃ yathākāmamindriyārthasamanvayaḥ |
ākāśalaṃghanaṃ caiva svadehe tanniveśanam || 30 ||

ākāśapiṇḍīkaraṇamaśarīratvameva ca |
anilaiśvaryasaṃyuktaṃ catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ mahat || 31 ||

aindramaiśvaryamākhyātamāmbaraṃ tatpracakṣate |
yathākāmopalabdhiśca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ || 32 ||

sarvasyābhibhavaścaiva sarvaguhyārthadarśanam |
karmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam || 33 ||

saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva bhogairaindraissamanvitam |
etaccāndramasaiśvaryaṃ mānasaṃ guṇato .adhikam || 34 ||

chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ caiva bandhanaṃ mocanaṃ tathā |
grahaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃsāravaśavartinām || 35 ||

prasādaścāpi sarveṣāṃ mṛtyukālajayastathā |
ābhimānikamaiśvaryaṃ prājāpatyaṃ pracakṣate || 36 ||

etaccāndramasairbhogaiḥ ṣaṭpañcāśadguṇaṃ mahat |
sargaḥ saṃkalpamātreṇa trāṇaṃ saṃharaṇaṃ tathā || 37 ||

svādhikāraśca sarveṣāṃ bhūtacittapravartanam |
asādṛśyaṃ ca sarvasya nirmāṇaṃ jagataḥ pṛthak || 38 ||

śubhāśubhasya karaṇaṃ prājāpatyaiśca saṃyutam |
catuṣṣaṣṭhiguṇaṃ brāhmamaiśvaryaṃ ca pracakṣate || 39 ||

bauddhādasmātparaṃ gauṇamaiśvaryaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ |
vaiṣṇavaṃ tatsamākhyātaṃ tasyaiva bhuvanasthitiḥ |
brahmaṇā tatpadaṃ sarvaṃ vaktumanyairna śakyate // 40 || 40 ||

tatpauruṣaṃ ca gauṇaṃ ca gaṇeśaṃ padamaiśvaram |
viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ kiṃcijjñātumanyairna śakyate || 41 ||

vijñānasiddhayaścaiva sarvā evaupasargikāḥ |
niroddhavyā prayatnena varrāgyeṇa pareṇa tu || 42 ||

pratibhāseṣvaśuddheṣu guṇeṣvāsaktacetasaḥ |
na sidhyetparamaiśvaryamabhayaṃ sārvakāmikam || 43 ||

tasmādguṇāṃśca bhogāṃśca devāsuramahībhṛtām |
tṛṇavadyastyajettasya yogasiddhiḥ parā bhavet || 44 ||

athavānugrahecchāyāṃ jagato vicarenmuniḥ |
yathākāmaṃguṇānbhogānbhuktvā muktiṃ prayāsyati || 45 ||

atha prayogaṃ yogasya vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ |
śubhe kāle śubhe deśe śivakṣetrādike punaḥ |
vijane janturahite niḥśabde bādhavarjite // 46 || 46 ||

supralipte sthale saumye gandhadhūpādivāsite |
muktapuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānādi vicitrite || 47 ||

kuśapuṣpasamittoyaphalamūlasamanvite |
nāgnyabhyāśe jalābhyāśe śuṣkaparṇacaye .api vā || 48 ||

na daṃśamaśakākīrṇe sarpaśvāpadasaṃkule |
na ca duṣṭamṛgākīrṇe na bhaye durjanāvṛte || 49 ||

śmaśāne caityavalmīke jīrṇāgāre catuṣpathe |
nadīnadasamudrāṇāṃ tīre rathyāntare .api vā || 50 ||

na jīrṇodyānagoṣṭhādau nāniṣṭe na ca nindite |
nājīrṇāmlarasodgāre na ca viṇmūtradūṣite || 51 ||

nacchardyāmātisāre vā nātibhuktau śramānvite |
na cāticiṃtākulito na cātikṣutpipāsitaḥ || 52 ||

nāpi svagurukarmādau prasakto yogamācaret |
yuktāhāravihāraśca yuktaceṣṭaśca karmasu || 53 ||

yuktanidrāprabodhaśca sarvāyāsavivarjitaḥ |
āsanaṃ mṛdulaṃ ramyaṃ vipulaṃ susamaṃ śuci || 54 ||

padmakasvastikādīnāmabhyasedāsaneṣu ca |
abhivandya svagurvantānabhivādyānanukramāt || 55 ||

ṛjugrīvaśirovakṣā nātiṣṭhecchiṣṭalocanaḥ |
kiṃcidunnāmitaśirā dantairdantānna saṃspṛśet || 56 ||

dantāgrasaṃsthitā jihvāmacalāṃ sanniveśya ca |
pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃstathā prajananaṃ punaḥ || 57 ||

ūrvorupari saṃsthāpya bāhū tiryagayatnataḥ |
dakṣiṇaṃ karapṛṣṭhaṃ tu nyasya vāmatalopari || 58 ||

unnāmya śanakaiḥ pṛṣṭhamuro viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ |
saṃprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan || 59 ||

saṃbhṛtaprāṇasaṃcāraḥ pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ |
svadehāyatanasyāntarviciṃtya śivamaṃbayā || 60 ||

hṛtpadmapīṭhikāmadhye dhyānayajñena pūjayet |
mūle nāsāgrato nābhau kaṃṭhe vā tālurandhrayoḥ || 61 ||

bhrūmadhye dvāradeśe vā lalāṭe mūrdhni vā smaret |
parikalpya yathānyāyaṃ śivayoḥ paramāsanam || 62 ||

tatra sāvaraṇaṃ vāpi nirāvaraṇameva vā |
dvidaleṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre yathāvidhi || 63 ||

daśāre vā ṣaḍasre vā caturasre śivaṃ smaret |
bhruvorantarataḥ padmaṃ dvidalaṃ taḍidujjvalam || 64 ||

bhrūmadhyasthāravindasya kramādvai dakṣiṇottare |
vidyutsamānavarṇe ca parṇe varṇāvasānake || 65 ||

ṣoḍaśārasya patrāṇi svarāḥ ṣoḍaśa tāni vai |
pūrvādīni kramādetatpadmaṃ kandasya mūlataḥ || 66 ||

kakārādiṭakārāntā varṇāḥ parṇānyanukramāt |
bhānuvarṇasya padmasya dhyeyaṃ taddhṛdayāntare || 67 ||

gokṣīradhavalasyoktā ḍādiphāntā yathākramam |
adho dalasyāmbujasya etasya ca dalāni ṣaṭ || 68 ||

vidhūmāṃgāravarṇasya varṇā vādyāśca lāntimāḥ |
mūlādhārāravindasya hemābhasya yathākramam |
vakārādisakārāntā varṇāḥ parṇamayāḥ sthitāḥ // 69 || 69 ||

eteṣvathāravindeṣu yatraivābhirataṃ manaḥ |
tatraiva devaṃ devīṃ ca ciṃtayeddhīrayā dhiyā || 70 ||

aṃguṣṭhamātramamalaṃ dīpyamānaṃ samantataḥ |
śuddhadīpaśikhākāraṃ svaśaktyā pūrṇamaṇḍitam || 71 ||

indurekhāsamākāraṃ tārārūpamathāpi vā |
nīvāraśūkassadṛśaṃ bisasutrābhameva vā || 72 ||

kadambagolakākāraṃ tuṣārakaṇikopamam |
kṣityāditattvavijayaṃ dhyātā yadyapi vāñchati || 73 ||

tattattattvādhipāmeva mūrtiṃ sthūlāṃ viciṃtayet |
sadāśivāntā brahmādyabhavādyāścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ || 74 ||

śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ |
ghorā miśrā praśāntāśca mūrtayastā munīśvaraiḥ || 75 ||

phalābhilāṣarahitaiścintyāścintāviśāradaiḥ |
ghorāścecciṃtitāḥ kuryuḥ pāparogaparikṣayam || 76 ||

cireṇa miśre saumye tu na sadyo na cirādapi |
saumye muktirviśeṣeṇa śāntiḥ prajñā prasidhyati || 77 ||

sidhyanti siddhayaścātra kramaśo nātra saṃśayaḥ || 78 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 38 ||

upamanyuruvāca |

śrīkaṃṭhanāthaṃ smaratāṃ sadyaḥ sarvārthasiddhayaḥ |
prasidhyantīti matvaike taṃ vai dhyāyanti yoginaḥ || 1 ||

sthityarthaṃ manasaḥ kecitsthūladhyānaṃ prakurvate |
sthūlaṃ tu niścalaṃ ceto bhavetsūkṣme tu tatsthiram || 2 ||

śive tu ciṃtite sākṣātsarvāḥ sidhyanti siddhayaḥ |
mūrtyantareṣu dhyāteṣu śivarūpaṃ viciṃtayet || 3 ||

lakṣayenmanasaḥ sthairyaṃ tattaddhyāyetpunaḥ punaḥ |
dhyānamādau saviṣayaṃ tato nirviṣayaṃ jaguḥ || 4 ||

tatra nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ nāstītyeva satāṃ matam |
buddherhi santatiḥ kāciddhyānamityabhidhīyate || 5 ||

tena nirviṣayā buddhiḥ kevaleha pravartate |
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ bālārkakiraṇāśrayam || 6 ||

sūkṣmāśrayaṃ nirviṣayaṃ nāparaṃ paramārthataḥ |
yadvā saviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ tatsākārasamāśrayam || 7 ||

nirākārātmasaṃvittirdhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ matam |
nirbījaṃ ca sabījaṃ ca tadeva dhyānamucyate || 8 ||

nirākāraśrayatvena sākārāśrayatastathā |
tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānamādau kṛtvā sabījakam || 9 ||

ante nirviṣayaṃ kuryānnirbījaṃ sarvasiddhaye |
prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti devyāḥ śāntyādayaḥ kramāt || 10 ||

śāntiḥ praśāntirdīptiśca prasādaśca tataḥ param |
śamaḥ sarvāpadāṃ caiva śāntirityabhidhīyate || 11 ||

tamaso .antabahirnāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate |
bahirantaḥprakāśo yo dīptirityabhidhīyate || 12 ||

svasthatā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi sabāhyābhyantarāṇi ca || 13 ||

buddheḥ prasādataḥ kṣipraṃ prasannāni bhavantyuta |
dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yadvā dhyānaprayojanam |
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samācaret // 14 / || 14 ||

jñānavairāgyasaṃpanno nityamavyagramānasaḥ |
śraddadhānaḥ prasannātmā dhyātā sadbhirudāhṛtaḥ || 15 ||

dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ || 16 ||

yogābhyāsastathālpe .api yathā pāpaṃ vināśayet |
dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram || 17 ||

avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānamityabhidhīyate |

buddhipravāharūpasya dhyānasyāsyāvalaṃbanam |
dhyeyamityucyate sadbhistacca sāṃbaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ || 19 ||

vimuktipratyayaṃ pūrṇamaiśvaryaṃ cāṇimādikam |
śivadhyānasya pūrṇasya sākṣāduktaṃ prayojanam || 20 ||

yasmātsaukhyaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca dhyānādabhayamāpnuyāt |
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya dhyānayukto bhavennaraḥ || 21 ||

nāsti dhyānaṃ vinā jñānaṃ nāsti dhyānamayoginaḥ |
dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ca yasyāsti tīrṇastena bhavārṇavaḥ || 22 ||

jñānaṃ prasannamekāgramaśeṣopādhivarjjitam |
yogābhyāsena yuktasya yoginastveva sidhyati || 23 ||

prakṣīṇāśeṣapāpānāṃ jñāne dhyāne bhavenmatiḥ |
pāpopahatabuddhīnāṃ tadvārtāpi sudurlabhā || 24 ||

yathāvahnirmahādīptaḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet |
tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma dhyānāgnirdahate kṣaṇāt || 25 ||

atyalpo .api yathā dīpaḥ sumahannāśayettamaḥ |
yogābhyāsastathālpo .api mahāpāpaṃ vināśayet || 26 ||

dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ vā śraddhayā parameśvaram |
yadbhavetsumahacchreyastasyānto naiva vidyate || 27 ||

nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tīrthaṃ nāsti dhyānasamaṃ tapaḥ |
nāsti dhyānasamo yajñastasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret || 28 ||

tīrthāni toyapūrṇāni devānpāṣāṇamṛnmayān |
yogino na prapadyante svātmapratyayakāraṇāt || 29 ||

yogināṃ ca vapuḥ sūkṣmaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamaiśvaram |
yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam || 30 ||

yathehāntaścarā rājñaḥ priyāḥ syurna bahiścarāḥ |
tathāntardhyānaniratāḥ priyāśśaṃbhorna karmiṇaḥ || 31 ||

bahiskarā yathā loke nātīva phalabhoginaḥ |
dṛṣṭvā narendrabhavane tadvadatrāpi karmiṇaḥ || 32 ||

yadyantarā vipadyante jñānayogārthamudyataḥ |
yogasyodyogamātreṇa rudralokaṃ gamiṣyati || 33 ||

anubhūya sukhaṃ tatra sa jāto yogināṃ kule |
jñānayogaṃ punarlabdhvā saṃsāramativarttate || 34 ||

jijñāsurapi yogasya yāṃ gatiṃ labhate naraḥ |
na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti sarvairapi mahāmakhaiḥ || 35 ||

dvijānāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ koṭiṃ saṃpūjya yatphalam |
bhikṣāmātrapradānena tatphalaṃ śivayogine || 36 ||

yajñāgnihotradānena tīrthahomeṣu yatphalam |
yogināmannadānena tatsamastaṃ phalaṃ labhet || 37 ||

ye cāpavādaṃ kurvanti vimūḍhāśśivayoginām |
śrotṛbhiste prapadyante narakeṣvāmahīkṣayāt || 38 ||

sati śrotari vaktāsyādapavādasya yoginām |
tasmācchrotā ca pāpīyāndaṇḍyassumahatāṃ mataḥ |
ye punaḥ satataṃ bhaktyā bhajanti śavayoginaḥ // 39 || 39 ||

te vidanti mahābhogānante yogaṃ ca śāṃkaram |
bhogārthibhirnaraistasmātsaṃpūjyāḥ śivayoginaḥ || 40 ||

pratiśrayānnapānādyaiḥ śayyāprāvaraṇādibhiḥ |
yogadharmaḥ sasāratvādabhedyaḥ pāpamudgaraiḥ || 41 ||

vajratandulavajjñeyaṃ tathā pāpena yoginaḥ |
na lipyante ca tāpaughaiḥ padmapatraṃ yathāṃbhasā || 42 ||

yasmindeśe vasennityaṃ śivayogarato muniḥ |
so .api deśo bhavetpūtaḥ sapūta iti kiṃ punaḥ || 43 ||

tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya kṛtyamanyadvicakṣaṇaḥ |
sarvaduḥkhaprahāṇāya śivayogaṃ samabhyaset || 44 ||

siddhayogaphalo yogī lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā |
bhogānbhuktvā yathākāmaṃ viharedvātra vartatām || 45 ||

athavā kṣudramityeva matvā vaiṣayikaṃ sukham |
tyaktvā virāgayogena svecchayā karma mucyatām || 46 ||

yastvāsannāṃ mṛtiṃ martyo dṛṣṭāriṣṭaṃ ca bhūyasā |
sa yogārambhanirataḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśrayet || 47 ||

sa tatra nivasanneva yadi dhīramanā naraḥ |
prāṇānvināpi rogādyaiḥ svayameva parityajet || 48 ||

kṛtvāpyanaśanaṃ caiva hutvā cāṃgaṃ śivānale |
kṣiptvā vā śivatīrtheṣu svadehamavagāhanāt || 49 ||

śivaśāstroktavidhivatprāṇānyastu parityajet |
sadya eva vimucyeta nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 50 ||

rogādyairvātha vivaśaḥ śivakṣetraṃ samāśritaḥ |
mriyate yadi sopyevaṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 51 ||

yathā hi maraṇaṃ śreṣṭhamuśantyanaśanādibhiḥ |
śāstraviśraṃbhadhīreṇa manasā kriyate yataḥ || 52 ||

śivanindārataṃ hatvā pīḍitaḥ svayameva vā |
yastyajeddustyajānprāṇānna sa bhūyaḥ prajāyate || 53 ||

śivanindārataṃ hantumaśakto yaḥ svayaṃ mṛtaḥ |
sadya eva pramucyeta triḥ saptakulasaṃyutaḥ || 54 ||

śivārthe yastyajetprāṇāñchivabhaktārthameva vā |
na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścinmuktimārgasthito naraḥ || 55 ||

tasmācchīghratarā muktistasya saṃsāramaṃḍalāt |
eteṣvanyatamopāyaṃ kathamapyavalambya vā || 56 ||

ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ vidhivatprāpto vā mriyate yadi |
paśūnāmiva tasyeha na kuryādaurdhvadaihikam || 57 ||

naivāśaucaṃ prapadyeta tatputrādiviśeṣataḥ |
śivacārārthamathavā śivavidyārthameva vā |
khanedvā bhuvi taddehaṃ dahedvā śucināgninā // 58 || 58 ||

kṣipedvāpsu śivāsveva tyajedvā kāṣṭhaloṣṭavat |
athainamapi coddiśya karma cetkartumīpsitam || 59 ||

kalyāṇameva kurvīta śaktyā bhaktāṃśca tarpayet |
dhanaṃ tasya bhajecchaivaḥ śaivī cetasya santatiḥ |
nāsti cettacchive dadyānnadadyātpaśusantatiḥ // 60 || 60 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe śaivayogavarṇanaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 39 ||

śrīsūta uvāca |

iti sa vijitamanyoryādavenopamanyoradhigatamabhidhāya jñānayogaṃ munibhyaḥ |
praṇatimupagatebhyastebhya udbhāvitātmā sapadi viyati vāyuḥ sāyamantarhito .abhūt || 1 ||

tataḥ prabhātasamaye naimiṣīyāstapodhanāḥ |
satrānte .avabhṛthaṃ kartuṃ sarva eva samudyayuḥ || 2 ||

tadā brahmasamādeśāddevī sākṣātsarasvatī |
prasannā svādusalilā prāvartata nadīśubhā || 3 ||

sarasvatīṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ |
samāpya satraṃ prārabdhaṃ cakrustatrāvagāhanam || 4 ||

atha santarpya devādīṃstadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ |
smarantaḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ yayurvārāṇasīṃ prati || 5 ||

tadā te himavatpādātpantatīṃ dakṣiṇāmukhīm |
dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tattīrato yayuḥ || 6 ||

tato vārāṇasīṃ prāpya muditāssarva eva te |
tadottarapravāhāyāṃ gaṃgāyāmavagāhya ca || 7 ||

avimukteśvaraṃ liṃgaṃ dṛṣṭvābhyarcya vidhānataḥ |
prayātumudyatāstatra dadṛśurdivi bhāsvaram || 8 ||

sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ tejo divyaṃ mahādbhutam |
ātmaprabhāvitānena vyāptasarvadigantaram || 9 ||

atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasmasañchannavigrahāḥ |
munayo .abhyetya śataśo līnāḥ syustatra tejasi || 10 ||

tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu |
sadyastirodadhe tejastadadbhutamivābhavat || 11 ||

taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ naimiṣīyā maharṣayaḥ |
kimetadityajānanto yayurbrahmavanaṃ prati || 12 ||

prāgevaiṣāṃ tu gamanātpavano lokapāvanaḥ |
darśanaṃ naimiṣīyāṇāṃ saṃvādastairmahātmanaḥ || 13 ||

śuddhāṃ buddhiṃ tatasteṣāṃ sāmbe sānucare śive |
samāptiṃ cāpi satrasya dīrghapūrvasya satriṇām || 14 ||

vijñāpya jagatāṃ dhātre brahmaṇe brahmayonaye |
svakārye tadanujñāto jagāma svapuraṃ prati || 15 ||

atha sthānagato brahmā tumburornāradasya ca |
paraspara sparddhitayorgāne vivadamānayoḥ || 16 ||

tadudbhāvitagānottharasairmādhyasthamācaran |
gandharvairapsarobhiśca sukhamāste niṣevitaḥ || 17 ||

tadānavasarādeva dvāḥsthairdvāri nivāritāḥ |
munayo brahmabhavanādbahiḥ pārśvamupāviśan || 18 ||

atha tumburuṇā gāne samatāṃ prāpya nāradaḥ |
sāhacaryeṣvanujñāto brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā || 19 ||

tyaktvā parasparasparddhāṃ maitrīṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ |
saha tenāpsarobhiśca gandharvaiśca samāvṛtaḥ || 20 ||

upavīṇayituṃ devaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram |
bhavanānniryayau dhāturjaladādaṃśumāniva || 21 ||

taṃ dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāste nāradaṃ munigovṛṣam |
praṇamyāvasaraṃ śaṃbhoḥ papracchuḥ paramādarāt || 22 ||

sa cāvasara evāyamitoṃtargamyatāmiti |
vadanyayāvanyaparastvarayā parayā yutaḥ || 23 ||

tato dvāri sthitā ye vai brahmaṇe tānnyavedayan |
tena te viviśurveśma piṃḍībhūyāṃḍajanmanaḥ || 24 ||

praviśya dūrato devaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat |
samīpe tadanujñātāḥ parivṛtyopatasthire || 25 ||

tāṃstatrāvasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalaṃ kamalāsanaḥ |
vṛttāntaṃ vo mayā jñātaṃ vāyurevāha no yataḥ || 26 ||

bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ paścānmāruteṃtarhite sati |
ityuktavati deveśe munayo .avabhṛthātparam || 27 ||

gaṃgātīrthesya gamanaṃ yātrāṃ vārāṇasīṃ prati |
darśanaṃ tatra liṃgānāṃ sthāpitānāṃ sureśvaraiḥ || 28 ||

avimukteśvarasyāpi liṃgasyābhyarcanaṃ sakṛt |
ākāśe mahatastasya tejorāśeśca darśanam || 29 ||

munīnāṃ vilayaṃ tatra nirodhaṃ tejasastataḥ |
yāthātmyavedanaṃ tasya ciṃtitasyāpi cātmabhiḥ || 30 ||

sarvaṃ savistaraṃ tasmai praṇamyāhurmuhurmuhuḥ |
munibhiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ || 31 ||

kaṃpayitvā śiraḥ kiṃcitprāha gaṃbhīrayā girā |
pratyāsīdati yuṣmākaṃ siddhirāmuṣmikī parā || 32 ||

bhavadbhirdīrghasatreṇa ciramārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ |
prasādābhimukho bhūta iti bhūtārthasūcitam || 33 ||

vārāṇasyāṃ tu yuṣmābhiryaddṛṣṭaṃ divi dīptimat |
talliṃgasaṃjñitaṃ sākṣāttejo māheśvaraṃ param || 34 ||

tatra līnāśca munayaḥ śrautapāśupatavratāḥ |
muktā babhūvuḥ svasthāśca naiṣṭhikā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ || 35 ||

prāpyānena yathā muktiracirādbhavatāmapi |
sa cāyamarthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmaddṛṣṭena tejasā || 36 ||

tatra vaḥ kāla evaiṣa daivādupanataḥ svayam |
prayāta dakṣiṇaṃ meroḥ śikharaṃ devasevitam || 37 ||

sanatkumāro yatrāste mama putraḥ paro muniḥ |
pratīkṣyāgamanaṃ sākṣādbhūtanāthasya nandinaḥ || 38 ||

purā sanatkumāropi dṛṣṭvāpi parameśvaram |
ajñānātsarvayogīndramānī vinayadūṣitaḥ || 39 ||

abhyutthānādikaṃ yuktamakurvannatinirbhayaḥ |
tato .aparādhātkruddhena mahoṣṭro nandinā kṛtaḥ || 40 ||

atha kālena mahatā tadarthe śocatā mayā |
upāsya devaṃ devīñca nandinaṃ cānunīya vai || 41 ||

kathaṃciduṣṭratā tasya prayatnena nivāritā |
prāpito hi yathāpūrvaṃ sanatpūrvāṃ kumāratām || 42 ||

tadāha ca mahādevaḥ smayanniva gaṇādhipam |
avajñāya hi māmeva tathāhaṃkṛtavānmuniḥ || 43 ||

atastvameva yāthātmyaṃ mamāsmai kathayānagha |
brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putro māṃ mūḍha iva saṃsmaran || 44 ||

mayaiva śiṣyate datto mama jñānapravartakaḥ |
dharmādhyakṣābhiṣekaṃ ca tava nirvarttayiṣyati || 45 ||

sa evaṃ vyāhṛto bhūyassarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ |
yatparājñāpanaṃ mūrdhnā prātaḥ pratigṛhītavān || 46 ||

tathā sanatkumāro .api merau madanuśāsanāt |
prasādārthaṃ gaṇasyāsya tapaścarati duścaram || 47 ||

draṣṭavyaśceti yuṣmābhiḥ prāggaṇeśasamāgamāt |
tatprasādārthamacirānnandī tatrāgamiṣyati || 48 ||

iti satvaramādiśya preṣitā viśvayoginā |
kumāraśikharaṃ merordakṣiṇaṃ munayo yayuḥ || 49 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe naimiṣarṣiyātrāvarṇanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 40 ||

sūta uvāca |

tatra skandasaro nāma sarassāgarasannibham |
amṛtasvāduśiśirasvacchā gādhalaghūdakam || 1 ||

samantataḥ saṃghaṭitaṃ sphaṭiko palasaṃcayaiḥ |
sarvartukusumaiḥ phullaiśchāditākhiladiGmukham || 2 ||

śaivalairutpalaiḥ padmaiḥ kumudaistārakopamaiḥ |
taraṃgairabhrasaṃkāśairākāśamiva bhūmigam || 3 ||

sukhāvataraṇārohaiḥ sthalairnīlaśilāmayaiḥ |
sopānamārgau ruciraiśśobhamānāṣṭadiGmukham || 4 ||

tatrāvatīrṇaiśca yathā tatrottīrṇaśca bhūyasā |
snātaiḥ sitopavītaiśca śuklākaupīnavalkalaiḥ || 5 ||

jaṭāśikhāyanairmuṃḍaistripuṃḍrakṛtamaṃḍanaiḥ |
virāgavivaśasmeramukhairmunikumārakaiḥ || 6 ||

ghaṭaiḥ kamalinīpatrapuṭaiśca kalaśaiḥ śivaiḥ |
kamaṇḍalubhiranyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ karakādibhiḥ || 7 ||

ātmārthaṃ ca parārthaṃ ca devatārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
ānīyamānasalilamāttapuṣpaṃ ca nityaśaḥ || 8 ||

antarjalaśilārūḍhairnīcānāṃ sparśaśaṃkayā |
ācāravadbhirmunibhiḥ kṛtabhasmāṃgadhūsaraiḥ || 9 ||

itastato .apsu majjadbhiriṣṭaśiṣṭaiḥ śilāgataiḥ |
tilaiśca sākṣataiḥ puṣpaistyaktadarbhapavitrakaiḥ || 10 ||

devādyamṛṣimadhyaṃ ca nirvartya pitṛtarpaṇam |
nivedayedabhijñebhyo nityasnānagatān dvijān || 11 ||

sthānesthāne kṛtānekabalipuṣpasamīraṇaiḥ |
saurārghyapūrvaṃ kurvadbhiḥsthaṃḍalebhyarcanādikam || 12 ||

kvacinnimajjadunmajjatprasrastagajayūthapam |
kvacicca tṛṣayāyātamṛgīmṛgaturaṃgamam || 13 ||

kvacitpītajanottīrṇamayūravaravāraṇam |
kvacitkṛtataṭāghātavṛṣaprativṛṣojjvalam || 14 ||

kvacitkāraṃḍavaravaiḥ kvacitsārasakūjitaiḥ |
kvacicca kokaninadaiḥ kvacidbhramaragītibhiḥ || 15 ||

snānapānādikaraṇaiḥ svasaṃpaddrumajīvibhiḥ |
praṇayātprāṇibhistaistairbhāṣamāṇamivāsakṛt || 16 ||

kūlaśākhiśikhālīnakokilākulakūjitaiḥ |
ātapopahatānsarvānnāmantrayadivāniśam || 17 ||

uttare tasya sarasastīre kalpataroradhaḥ |
vedyāṃ vajraśilāmayyāṃ mṛdule mṛgacarmaṇi || 18 ||

sanatkumāramāsīnaṃ śaśvadbālavapurddharam |
tatkālamātroparataṃ samādheracalātmanaḥ || 19 ||

upāsyamānaṃ munibhiryogīndrairapi pūjitam |
dadṛśurnaimiṣeyāste praṇatāścopatasthire || 20 ||

yāvatpṛṣṭavate tasmai procuḥ svāgatakāraṇam |
tumulaḥ śuśruve tāvaddivi dundubhinisvanaḥ || 21 ||

dadṛśe tatkṣaṇe tasminvimānaṃ bhānusannibham |
gaṇeśvarairasaṃkhyeyaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ ca samantataḥ || 22 ||

apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ rudrakanyābhirāvṛtam |
mṛdaṃgamurajodghuṣṭaṃ veṇuvīṇāravānvitam || 23 ||

citraratnavitānāḍhyaṃ muktādāmavirājitam |
munibhissiddhagandharvairyakṣacāraṇakinnaraiḥ || 24 ||

nṛtyadbhiścaiva gāyadbhirvādayadbhiśca saṃvṛtam |
vīragovṛṣacihnena vidramadrumayaṣṭinā || 25 ||

kṛtagopurasatkāraṃ ketunā mānyahetunā |
tasya madhye vimānasya cāmaradvitayāntare || 26 ||

chattrasya maṇidaṃḍasya candrasyeva śuceradhaḥ |
divyasiṃhāsanārūḍhaṃ devyā suyaśayā saha || 27 ||

śriyā ca vapuṣā caiva tribhiścāpi vilocanaiḥ |
prākārairabhikṛtyānāṃ pratyabhijñāpakaṃ prabhoḥ || 28 ||

avilaṃghya jagatkarturājñāpanamivāgatam |
sarvānugrahaṇaṃ śaṃbhoḥ sākṣādiva puraḥsthitam || 29 ||

śilādatanayaṃ sākṣācchrīmacchūlavarāyudham |
viśveśvaragaṇādhyakṣaṃ viśveśvaramivāparam || 30 ||

viśvasyāpi vidhātR̥ṇāṃ nigrahānugrahakṣamam |
caturbāhumudārāṃgaṃ candrarekhāvibhūṣitam || 31 ||

kaṃṭhe nāgena maulau ca śaśāṃkenāpyalaṃkṛtam |
savigrahamivaiśvaryaṃ sāmarthyamiva sakriyam || 32 ||

samāptamiva nirvāṇaṃ sarvajñamiva saṃgatam |
dṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭavadano brahmaputraḥ saharṣibhiḥ || 33 ||

tasthau prāñjalirutthāya tasyātmānamivārpayan |
atha tatrāntare tasminvimāne cāvaniṃ gate || 34 ||

praṇamya daṇḍavaddevaṃ stutvā vyajñāpayanmunīm |
ṣaṭkulīyā ime dīrghaṃ naimiṣe satramāsthitāḥ |
āgatā brahmaṇādiṣṭāḥ pūrvamevābhikāṃkṣayā // 35 || 35 ||

śrutvā vākyaṃ brahmaputrasya nandīchittvā pāśāndṛṣṭipātena sadyaḥ |
śaivaṃ dharmaṃ caiśvaraṃ jñānayogaṃ dattvā bhūyo devapārśvaṃ jagāma || 36 ||

sanatkumāreṇa ca tatsamastaṃ vyāsāya sākṣādgurave mamoktam |
vyāsena coktaṃ mahitena mahyaṃ mayā ca tadvaḥ kathitaṃ samāsāt || 37 ||

nāvedavidbhyaḥ kathanīyametatpurāṇaratnaṃ puraśāsanasya |
nābhaktaśiṣyāya ca nāstikebhyo dattaṃ hi mohānnirayaṃ dadāti || 38 ||

mārgeṇa sevānugatena yaistaddattaṃ gṛhītaṃ paṭhitaṃ śrutaṃ vā |
tebhyaḥ sukhaṃ dharmamukhaṃ trivargaṃ nirvāṇamante niyataṃ dadāti || 39 ||

parasparasyopakṛtaṃ bhavadbhirmayā ca paurāṇikamārggayogāt |
ato gamiṣye .ahamavāptakāmaḥ samastamevāstu śivaṃ sadā naḥ || 40 ||

sūte kṛtāśiṣi gate munayaḥ suvṛttā yāge ca paryavasite mahati prayoge |
kāle kalau ca viṣayaiḥ kaluṣāyamāṇe vārāṇasīparisare vasatiṃ vinetuḥ || 41 ||

atha ca te paśupāśamumukṣayākhilatayā kṛtapāśupatavratāḥ |
adhikṛtākhilabodhasamādhayaḥ paramanirvṛtimāpuraninditāḥ || 42 ||

vyāsa uvāca |

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi samāptaṃ hitamādarāt |
paṭhitavyaṃ prayatnena śrotavyaṃ ca tathaiva hi || 43 ||

nāstikāya na vaktavyamaśraddhāya śaṭhāya ca |
abhaktāya maheśasya tathā dharmadhvajāya ca || 44 ||

etacchrutyā hyekavāraṃ bhavetpāpaṃ hi bhasmasāt |
abhakto bhaktimāpnoti bhakto bhaktisamṛddhibhāk || 45 ||

punaḥ śrute ca sadbhaktirmuktissyācca śruteḥ punaḥ |
tasmātpunaḥpunaścaiva śrotavyaṃ hi mumukṣubhiḥ || 46 ||

pañcāvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasyāsya saddhiyā |
paraṃ phalaṃ samuddiśya tatprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ || 47 ||

purātanāśca rājāno viprā vaiśyāśca sattamāḥ |
saptakṛtvastadāvṛttyālabhanta śivadarśanam || 48 ||

śroṣyatyathāpi yaścedaṃ mānavo bhaktitatparaḥ |
iha bhuktvākhilānbhogānante muktiṃ labhecca saḥ || 49 ||

etacchivapurāṇaṃ hi śivasyātipriyaṃ param |
bhuktimuktipradaṃ brahmasaṃmitaṃ bhaktivarddhanam || 50 ||

etacchivapurāṇasya vaktuḥ śrotuśca sarvadā |
sagaṇassasutassāṃbaśśaṃ karotu sa śaṃkaraḥ || 51 ||

iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe vyāsopadeśaśrīśivamahāpurāṇamāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo .adhyāyaḥ || 41 ||

samāpto .ayaṃ granthaḥ
